### [1] [Beyond Topological Invariants: Order Parameters from Dominant Fock-state Patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10320)
*Tsz Hin Hui,Xiaodan Xia,Pedro D. Sacramento,Wing Chi Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过提取多体基态中主导Fock态的通用模式来构建序参量（order parameter, OP）的通用方案。该方案不仅能区分传统拓扑不变量（如缠绕数）无法区分的隐藏相结构，还能量化相的“深度”，并在无序系统和Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）相变中提供有效的表征与有限尺寸诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统拓扑相通常利用非局域不变量（如缠绕数）进行表征，但这些不变量有时不足以完全区分所有相。本文旨在开发一种更精细、可操作且具有普适性的序参量构造方案，以揭示隐藏的相结构并适用于相互作用与非相互作用的多体系统。

Method: 从多体基态的主导Fock态中提取通用模式，据此构造实空间序参量（real-space order parameter）。该方法不依赖非局域拓扑不变量，而是基于基态波函数的局部结构信息。

Result: 在扩展的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型中，标准缠绕数不足以区分所有相，而所提出的序参量揭示了每个拓扑扇区（topological sector）分裂为两个不同相的隐藏子结构。这些序参量还能量化相深度，并在无序系统中稳健地表征相变。此外，该方法为相互作用的自旋-1/2 XXZ模型中的Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）相变提供了实用的有限尺寸诊断。

Conclusion: 本文提出的序参量构造框架是一种广泛适用的工具，可用于揭示各类相互作用及非相互作用量子多体系统的相图，尤其适用于传统拓扑不变量分辨率不足的情形。

Abstract: We introduce a general scheme for constructing order parameters (OPs) by extracting generic patterns from the dominant Fock states of many-body ground states. While topological phases are traditionally characterized by non-local invariants, we demonstrate that our real-space OPs provide a more refined classification. In the extended Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model, we show that the standard winding number is insufficient to fully distinguish all phases; our OPs reveal a hidden sub-structure where each topological sector splits into two distinct phases. Beyond identifying the phase boundaries, these OPs quantify the depth of a phase, and remain robust in characterizing transitions in disordered systems. Furthermore, our approach provides a practical finite-size diagnostic for the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition in the interacting spin-1/2 XXZ model. The presented framework offers a broadly applicable tool for uncovering the phase diagrams of diverse interacting and non-interacting quantum many-body systems.

</details>


### [2] [Pulse, polarization and topology shaping of polariton fuids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10403)
*Lorenzo Dominici,David Colas,Stefano Donati,Galbadrakh Dagvadorj,Antonio Gianfrate,Carlos Sánchez Muñoz,Dario Ballarini,Milena De Giorgi,Giuseppe Gigli,Marzena H. Szymańska,Fabrice P. Laussy,Daniele Sanvitto*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文基于激子-极化激元（exciton-polariton）的量子流体平台，提出了多种超快脉冲与偏振整形方法。通过利用二维极化激元流体的正规模（normal modes）及其亚皮秒拉比振荡（Rabi oscillations），结合双共振激发脉冲的相干控制（coherent control）与数字离轴全息（digital off-axis holography）超快成像技术，实现了布洛赫球（Bloch sphere）上的相干控制、庞加莱球（Poincaré sphere）上的超快偏振扫描、斯格明子（skyrmion）的动态扭转，以及带有螺旋相位奇点（phase singularity）管的超快旋涡（swirling vortices）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于极化激元的量子流体平台，探索超快脉冲和偏振整形的新方法，以实现对极化激元四分量态（两个正规模×两个偏振自由度）的相干控制与拓扑态操控。

Method: 利用强耦合量子阱激子与微腔光子形成的二维极化激元流体的正规模及其亚皮秒拉比振荡；采用双共振激发脉冲进行相干控制；结合基于数字离轴全息术的超快成像技术，实现极化激元复波函数（complex wavefunction）的时空分辨测量。

Result: 实现了布洛赫球上的极化激元相干控制、庞加莱球上的超快偏振扫描、全庞加莱态（如斯格明子）的动态扭转；通过向双脉冲方案加入角动量自由度，实现了新型超快旋涡——其特征为一个或多个内相位奇点管沿传播轴螺旋运动。

Conclusion: 极化激元量子流体平台能够实现多种超快相干操控与拓扑态构建，旋涡在上、下极化激元分支之间的分裂导致了能量与角动量的振荡交换，并产生时空结构化的光子包。

Abstract: Here we present different approaches to ultrafast pulse and polarization shaping, based on a ``quantum fluid'' platform of polaritons. Indeed we exploit the normal modes of two dimensional polariton fluids made of strong coupled quantum well excitons and microcavity photons, by rooting different polarization and topological states into their sub-picosecond Rabi oscillations. Coherent control of two resonant excitation pulses allows us to prepare the desired state of the polariton, taking benefit from its four-component features given by the combination of the two normal modes with the two degrees of polarization. An ultrafast imaging based on the digital off-axis holography technique is implemented to study the polariton complex wavefunction with time and space resolution. We show in order coherent control of the polariton state on the Bloch sphere, an ultrafast polarization sweeping of the Poincaré sphere, and the dynamical twist of full Poincaré states such as the skyrmion on the sphere itself. Finally, we realize a new kind of ultrafast swirling vortices by adding the angular momentum degree of freedom to the two-pulse scheme. These oscillating topology states are characterized by one or more inner phase singularities tubes which spirals around the axis of propagation. The mechanism is devised in the splitting of the vortex into the upper and lower polaritons, resulting in an oscillatory exchange of energy and angular momentum and in the emitted time and space structured photonic packets.

</details>

### [3] [Criticality in optical properties of the Drude and Drude-Sommerfeld metals around the plasma frequencies for high carrier concentrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08107)
*Bikram Keshari Behera,Rhitabrata Bhattacharyya,Shyamal Biswas*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在经典电动力学框架内解析地确定了 Drude 金属在整个电磁波频率范围（0<ω<∞）内的衰减常数，特别在高载流子浓度（ω_pτ≫1）条件下得到了衰减常数的简洁形式，并揭示了光学性质在等离子体频率（ω=ω_p）附近的临界行为，包括临界指数以及基于 Drude-Sommerfeld 模型和 Thomas-Fermi 屏蔽的量子修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对 Drude 金属的衰减常数缺乏全频率范围内的统一解析描述，尤其在等离子体频率（plasma frequency, ω_p）附近的临界行为尚未被充分刻画。本文旨在填补这一空白，在一个统一的经典电动力学框架下获得完整的衰减常数表达式，并揭示其光学性质的临界现象与量子修正。

Method: 基于经典电动力学（classical electrodynamics）框架，对服从 Drude 模型（Drude model）的导电体进行解析求解，考虑背景束缚电荷和束缚电流的线性介电性与磁性质（ε>ε_0, μ>μ_0）。在高载流子浓度条件（ω_pτ≫1）下简化得到衰减常数的解析形式，并进一步引入 Drude-Sommerfeld 模型（Drude-Sommerfeld model）与 Thomas-Fermi 屏蔽（Thomas-Fermi screening）获得量子修正。

Result: 得到了贯穿整个频率区间（0<ω<∞）的衰减常数解析表达式；在高载流子浓度（ω_pτ≫1）条件下，得到了衰减常数在高于和低于等离子体频率的宽广高频范围内的简洁形式：$k_-\simeq+\sqrt{\frac{με}{2}}\sqrt{ω_p^2-ω^2+|ω_p^2-ω^2|}$。该结果导致衰减常数、群速度和复介电常数在 ω=ω_p 附近表现出临界性，文中给出了这些量的临界指数（critical exponents）。此外，还获得了基于 Drude-Sommerfeld 模型和 Thomas-Fermi 屏蔽的量子修正。

Conclusion: 该工作首次在单一经典电动力学框架内完整描述了 Drude 金属全频率范围的衰减常数，揭示了等离子体频率附近光学性质的临界现象及对应的临界指数，并通过量子修正拓展了理论适用性，为理解导体光学行为提供了更为统一的理论基础。

Abstract: We have analytically determined the attenuation constant of the Drude metal for the entire range of frequency ($0<ω<\infty$) of an electromagnetic (plane) wave incident on it within a single framework of classical electrodynamics. Here, by the Drude metal, we mean an electrical conductor that obeys the Drude model for the conduction electrons. We further consider the conductor to have linear dielectric and magnetic properties (i.e. permittivity $ε>ε_0$ and permeability $μ>μ_0$) due to the bound charges and bound currents in the background. Interestingly, for such a conductor with a high carrier concentration ($ω_pτ\gg1$), we have obtained a simple form of the attenuation constant $k_-\simeq+\sqrt{\frac{με}{2}}\sqrt{ω_p^2-ω^2+|ω_p^2-ω^2|}$ for a wide range of high frequencies below and above plasma frequency $ω_p$. Such a result gives rise to criticality in the conductor's optical properties, such as -- the attenuation constant, group velocity, and complex dielectric constant near around $ω=ω_p$. We have obtained the critical exponents for these quantities. We also have obtained a quantum correction to the optical properties within the Drude-Sommerfeld model with the Thomas-Fermi screening.

</details>


### [4] [Bound-State Spectra of a Lifshitz-Type Dirac Equation in (2+1) Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09249)
*Lucas K. R. Queiroz,Van Sérgio Alves,Nilberto Bezerra,Luis Fernández,Francisco Peña*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了由 Lifshitz 空间导数修正的 (2+1) 维 Dirac 方程（动力学指数 z=2），在径向约束下通过解析和数值方法获得了硬壁、谐振子及对数势三种束缚态能谱，揭示了 Lifshitz 参数 b 调控的标度律，为具有二次低能色散（如双层石墨烯）的二维 Dirac 系统提供了有效描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究 Lifshitz 空间导数（Lifshitz spatial derivatives）对 (2+1) 维 Dirac 方程束缚态谱的影响，特别是动力学指数 z=2 情形下束缚态能谱的标度行为，以理解高阶空间导数如何修正二维 Dirac 系统（如双层石墨烯及相关各向异性二维材料）中的束缚态光谱特性。

Method: 对常数背景、硬壁约束和谐振子势（harmonic potentials）采用解析求解；对数约束（logarithmic confinement）则通过 Numerov 方法（Numerov method）进行数值处理，并辅以半经典 WKB 分析（semiclassical WKB analysis）予以补充。

Result: 硬壁约束下能谱满足 $E - M \propto b/R_0^2$；谐振子束缚下 $E - M \propto \sqrt{2b}\,ω$；对数约束的半经典区域中 $E - M \sim α\ln\sqrt{b}$。三种标度律均由 Lifshitz 参数 b 主导。

Conclusion: 结果系统地刻画了高阶空间导数对二维 Dirac 系统束缚态能谱的修正机制，可为具有二次低能色散（quadratic low-energy dispersion）的材料（如双层石墨烯 bilayer graphene 及相关各向异性二维系统）的有效模型描述提供参考。

Abstract: We investigate a Dirac-type equation in (2+1) dimensions modified by Lifshitz spatial derivatives with dynamical exponent $z=2$, focusing on the spectral properties of bound states under radial confinement. Analytical solutions are obtained for constant backgrounds, hard-wall confinement, and harmonic potentials, while logarithmic confinement is treated numerically via the Numerov method and complemented by a semiclassical WKB analysis. The resulting spectra exhibit characteristic scaling laws governed by the Lifshitz parameter $b$, including $E - M \propto b/R_0^2$ for hard-wall confinement, $E - M \propto \sqrt{2b}\,ω$ for harmonic trapping, and $E - M \sim α\ln\sqrt{b}$ in the semiclassical regime of logarithmic confinement. These results provide a consistent characterization of how higher-order spatial derivatives modify bound-state spectra in two-dimensional Dirac systems and may be relevant for effective descriptions of materials with quadratic low-energy dispersion, such as bilayer graphene and related anisotropic 2D systems.

</details>


### [5] [Microscopic resonant-shell mechanism for slow Liouvillian sectors in an open correlated lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09274)
*X. Z. Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个微观理论框架，通过一个局域相互作用的复合壳层轨道（shell orbital）及其Schur投影机制，解释了开放关联晶格中慢Liouvillian扇区（slow Liouvillian sectors）的选择与涌现行为，涵盖边缘记忆、临界双重态及缺陷动力学等关键现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解开放量子多体系统中慢弛豫扇区（slow relaxation sectors）的微观选择机制，尤其是非厄米能带（non-Hermitian band）假设之外的结构性起源。

Method: 从局域相互作用共振出发：在位双占（on-site doublon）与支分辨最近邻键（branch-resolved nearest-neighbor bond）的耦合构成复合壳层轨道；通过Schur投影（Schur projection）将微观跃迁投影到该壳层，得到支选择性二聚化通道（branch-selective dimerized channel），并在不同填充与边界条件下解析求解。

Result: 在稀薄区域，边界双占消失通道通过Zeno型返回产生指数慢的边缘记忆极点（edge-memory pole）；在壳层临界点，该极点被具有代数相干间距的近零驻波双态（near-zero standing-wave doublet）取代；在有限壳层填充下，壳层发生密度重整；数守恒锁相跳变移除亮失配扇区（bright mismatch sector），缺陷成为渐近慢变量并产生扩散型有限尺寸能隙。

Conclusion: 储层工程化的快块（fast block）作为慢扇区的选择器，而微观母壳层（parent shell）保持不变；该Schur投影框架统一描述了壳层、支拓扑、边缘记忆、临界双重态、密度重整哈密顿量及缺陷生成器。

Abstract: We develop a microscopic theory for how slow Liouvillian sectors are selected in an open correlated lattice. The starting point is not a postulated non-Hermitian band, but a local interacting resonance between an on-site doublon and a branch-resolved nearest-neighbor bond. This resonance defines a composite shell orbital whose doublon weight controls reservoir visibility and whose mixed doublon-bond character controls shell mobility. Projecting the microscopic hopping onto the selected shell yields a branch-selective dimerized channel. In the dilute regime, a boundary doublon-loss channel yields an exponentially slow edge-memory pole through a Zeno-type return. At the shell-critical point, the edge pole is replaced by a near-zero standing-wave doublet with an algebraic coherent spacing. At finite shell filling, the same local shell becomes density dressed. A number-conserving phase-locking jump removes a bright mismatch sector, leaving defects as the asymptotic slow variables and producing a diffusive finite-size gap. We derive the local shell, the projected branch topology, the edge-memory law, the shell-critical doublet, the density-dressed shell Hamiltonian, and the defect generator within one Schur-projection framework. The resulting mechanism identifies the reservoir-engineered fast block as the selector of the observable slow sector, while the microscopic parent shell remains fixed.

</details>


### [6] [Spin Quadrupolar orders in $d$-wave Unconventional Magnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09499)
*Jian-Keng Yuan,Zhiming Pan,Congjun Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过线性响应理论（linear response theory）计算了在弱非磁性周期晶格势下d波非常规磁态的自旋-电荷交叉磁化率，揭示了动量空间中的自旋四极有序（spin quadrupolar ordering）如何转化为实空间中的交错磁分布，建立了动量空间偶分波通道多极矩与实空间自旋多极序之间的物理联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管d波α相非常规磁态（即交变磁体，altermagnet）在动量空间中展现出明显的各向异性d波特征，但这种微观拓扑结构如何转化为实空间中的自旋分布尚不清楚。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 将弱非磁性周期性晶格势引入d波非常规磁态，利用线性响应理论（linear response theory）计算自旋-电荷交叉磁化率（spin-charge cross susceptibility）。

Result: 发现晶格势与内禀d波自旋劈裂（d-wave spin-splitting）之间的相互作用自然诱导出实空间自旋四极分布（spatial spin quadrupole distribution），且无需扩大原胞（unit cell）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了动量空间偶分波通道中的多极矩（multipoles）与实空间自旋多极序（spin multipole orders）之间的物理联系，为理解非常规磁态中微观拓扑与实空间结构的关系提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Unconventional magnetism represents a class of metallic states whose Fermi surfaces exhibit spin-dependent splittings under the non-trivial representations of the rotation group. The $d$-wave $α$-phase unconventional magnetic state, commonly known as altermagnet, recently, has attracted significant attention. While these systems exhibit distinct anisotropic $d$-wave characteristics in momentum space, how this microscopic topology translates into the spin distributions in real space remains a question. In this work, we bridge the intrinsic spin quadrupolar ordering in momentum space to the real-space staggered magnetic distribution. By introducing a weak, non-magnetic periodic crystal potential into a $d$-wave unconventional magnetic state, the spin-charge cross susceptibility is calculated by using the linear response theory. We reveal that the interplay between the crystal potential and the intrinsic $d$-wave spin-splitting naturally induces a spatial spin quadrupole distribution without enlarging the unit cell. Our study thus provides a physical connection between momentum-space multipoles in the even partial wave channel and real-space spin multipole orders.

</details>


### [7] [Boundary-dependent topological degeneracy in an Ising chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09510)
*E. S. Ma,Z. Song*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了存在非零温度时横向场伊辛链（Ising chain with transverse field）的相图，通过引入一种去除两端耦合及横向场的替代边界条件，将系统精确映射为两条独立的Kitaev链。该映射导致相图中拓扑Kramers简并（topological Kramers-like degeneracy）的存在性发生切换。借助马约拉纳表示（Majorana representation）分析，揭示这种切换源于SSH链中规范依赖的绕数（winding number）。有限温度下体-边对应（bulk-boundary correspondence）的体现通过数值模拟得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑简并（topological degeneracy）是量子相图的重要特征，本文旨在考察非零温度下横向场伊辛链在不同边界条件下的相图行为，尤其关注一种新型边界条件对拓扑简并存在性的影响。

Method: 采用精确映射方法，将系统转化为两条独立的Kitaev链，其中无自旋费米子（spinless fermions）对应畴壁激发（domain-wall excitations）；在此基础上利用马约拉纳表示分析切换机制，并通过有限尺寸系统的数值模拟验证体-边对应关系。

Result: 发现替代边界条件导致相图中拓扑Kramers简并的存在性发生切换；该切换的底层机制来自SSH链中绕数的规范依赖性；非零温度下体-边对应的表现由数值模拟证实。

Conclusion: 该发现为量子自旋链（quantum spin chain）的拓扑性质提供了新的见解。

Abstract: The topological degeneracy is a characteristic of quantum phase diagram in an Ising chain with transverse field. We revisit the phase diagram at nonzero temperature of an Ising chain with two types of open boundary conditions. In this work, we focus on an alternative boundary condition that not only removes the coupling between the two end sites but also eliminates the transverse field on them. We show that such a system can be exactly mapped onto two independent Kitaev chains, where spinless fermions correspond to domain-wall excitations. This results in a switch in the existence of the topological Kramers-like degeneracy in the phase diagram. The underlying mechanism is analyzed within the Majorana representation, which indicates that such a switch arises from the gauge dependence of the winding number in an SSH chain. The manifestation of bulk-boundary correspondence at nonzero temperature is demonstrated by numerical simulations on finite-size systems. This finding provides insight into the quantum spin chain.

</details>


### [8] [Spin-charge separation in two-leg t-J ladders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09705)
*Luhang Yang,Elbio Dagotto*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究利用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法及其时间依赖扩展，分析两腿t-J梯子模型中的自旋-电荷分离现象。通过研究基态关联和单粒子移除谱，发现合适的参数（plaquette对角跳跃、自旋交换和空穴掺杂）可使系统从Luther-Emery相转变为Luttinger液体相，从而出现自旋-电荷分离特征。结合先前精确对角化研究，结果表明自旋-电荷分离可能在更宽的梯子系统中持续存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋-电荷分离（spin-charge separation）是一维费米子系统的标志性现象，但在更高维度中是否能够实现仍是一个悬而未决的问题。本文旨在探索该现象在准一维梯子系统中的存在性。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法及其时间依赖扩展，对两腿t-J梯子（t-J ladder）模型进行数值计算。通过分析基态关联（ground-state correlations）和单粒子移除谱（single-particle removal spectra），系统考察plaquette对角跳跃（plaquette diagonal hopping）、自旋交换（spin exchange）和空穴掺杂（hole doping）等参数的影响。

Result: 在适当的参数区间内，系统从Luther-Emery相（Luther Emery phase，自旋能隙打开、电荷模式无能隙）转变为Luttinger液体相（Luttinger liquid phase，自旋和电荷激发均无能隙），并在后者中观察到自旋-电荷分离特征。

Conclusion: 结合先前基于精确对角化（exact diagonalization）的研究结果，本工作为自旋-电荷分离可能在更宽梯子系统中持续存在提供了证据。

Abstract: Spin-charge separation is a hallmark of one-dimensional fermionic systems, yet its realization in higher dimensions remains an open question. To address this issue, we investigate a two-leg t-J ladder using the density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) method and its time-dependent extension. By analyzing ground-state correlations and single-particle removal spectra, we systematically examine the effects of plaquette diagonal hopping, spin exchange, and hole doping. Within appropriate parameter regimes, these factors drive the system from the well-known Luther Emery phase, with gapped spin and gapless charge modes, into a Luttinger liquid phase characterized by gapless spin and charge excitations, where signatures of spin-charge separation emerge. In combination with previous studies using exact diagonalization, our results provide evidence that spin-charge separation may persist in wider ladder systems.

### [9] [Non-magnetic insulating phase induced by Jahn-Teller effect in RNiO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09713)
*Sangeeta Rajpurohit,Liang Z. Tan,Tadashi Ogitsu,Peter E. Blöchl*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个三维多轨道紧束缚模型（three-dimensional multi-orbital tight-binding model），统一处理稀土镍酸盐RNiO₃中的电荷、自旋、轨道和晶格自由度。模型参数来自混合泛函密度泛函理论（hybrid-functional DFT）计算，揭示了三种竞争绝缘相，其稳定性由U−3J与电子-声子耦合（el-ph coupling）之间的竞争决定，并预言了一个非磁性电荷有序的新亚稳态（metastable state）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解稀土镍酸盐RNiO₃中金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator transition）的微观机制，特别是电荷、自旋、轨道和晶格自由度之间的耦合如何导致不同的竞争绝缘相。

Method: 提出一个三维多轨道紧束缚模型，将电荷、自旋、轨道和晶格自由度统一纳入考量。所有模型参数，包括在位相互作用U和J以及呼吸模的电子-声子耦合，均源自对小带宽镍酸盐LuNiO₃的混合泛函DFT计算。

Result: 模型描述了三种竞争绝缘相：大U−3J时，高自旋Ni³⁺位上的局域Jahn-Teller（JT）畸变稳定绝缘态；较小U−3J时，体系发生电荷歧化（charge disproportionation）2Ni³⁺→Ni²⁺+Ni⁴⁺，形成实验观察到的自旋极化电荷有序态；当Ni²⁺位上的JT能量超过Hund交换3J时，出现一种新的电荷和轨道有序绝缘相，两个e_g电子占据同一轨道且自旋相反。

Conclusion: 通过在完整三维紧束缚模型中的自洽计算，进一步确认了新预言的亚稳态相（非磁性电荷有序RNiO₃相中由JT畸变驱动）的稳定性。该结果表明，RNiO₃中金属-绝缘体转变的发生并不需要磁有序的出现。

Abstract: We propose a three-dimensional multi-orbital tight-binding model for rare-earth nickelates RNiO$_3$ that treats charge, spin, orbital, and lattice degrees of freedom on equal footing. All model parameters, including the on-site interactions $U$ and $J$ and the electron-phonon (el-ph) coupling to the breathing mode, are extracted from hybrid-functional DFT calculations for the small-bandwidth nickelate LuNiO$_3$. The model describes three competing insulating phases governed by the interplay of $U{-}3J$ and el-ph coupling to the breathing and Jahn--Teller (JT) modes. For large $U{-}3J$, the insulating state is stabilized by local JT distortions on high-spin Ni$^{3+}$ sites. For smaller $U{-}3J$, the system undergoes charge disproportionation, $2\mathrm{Ni}^{3+}\rightarrow\mathrm{Ni}^{2+}+\mathrm{Ni}^{4+}$, resulting in the spin-polarized charge-ordered state observed experimentally below the Néel temperature in small-bandwidth RNiO$_3$. When the JT energy on the Ni$^{2+}$ site exceeds Hund's exchange $3J$, a distinct charge- and orbital-ordered insulating phase emerges in which the two $e_g$-electrons occupy the same orbital with opposite spin. The stability of this phase is further confirmed by self-consistent calculations within the full three-dimensional tight-binding model. This newly predicted metastable state, characterized by JT distortions in a nonmagnetic charge-ordered RNiO$_3$ phase, shows that the onset of magnetic order is not required for the metal-insulator transition in RNiO$_3$.

### [10] [Magnetic structure in the two-dimensional van der Waals ferromagnet Fe$_3$GaTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09729)
*Po-Chun Chang,Sabreen Hammouda,Yung-Hsiang Tung,Yishui Zhou,Iurii Kibalin,Bachir Ouladdiaf,Chao-Hung Du,Yixi Su*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文采用化学气相输运法成功生长了二维范德华铁磁体Fe₃GaTe₂（FGaT）的高质量单晶，并通过结构及磁性表征证实其具有六方P6₃/mmc结构，Fe占据两种不等价位点，磁易轴沿c轴方向，居里温度（T_C）约为355–360 K。与Fe₃GeTe₂（FGT）相比，FGaT的c轴收缩导致Feⁱ-Feⁱⁱ原子间距减小，增强了Fe–Fe交换相互作用，这是其T_C显著升高的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维范德华铁磁体（two-dimensional van der Waals ferromagnet）在自旋电子学（spintronics）中具有重要应用前景，但现有材料如Fe₃GeTe₂（FGT）的居里温度（Curie temperature, T_C）较低，限制了实际应用。因此，探索具有更高T_C的同构材料并理解其微观机制至关重要。

Method: 采用化学气相输运法（chemical vapour transport method）生长Fe₃GaTe₂（FGaT）单晶，以降低表面杂质；利用单晶X射线衍射（single-crystal X-ray diffraction）和中子衍射（neutron diffraction）进行结构与磁性表征。

Result: FGaT结晶为六方P6₃/mmc结构，Fe占据Feⁱ和Feⁱⁱ两种不等价位点，磁矩分别为1.9(2) μ_B和1.4(6) μ_B；磁易轴（magnetic easy axis）沿c轴方向，T_C约为355–360 K。与FGT相比，FGaT的a轴轻微膨胀、c轴收缩，Feⁱ-Feⁱⁱ沿c轴的原子间距减小。

Conclusion: FGaT中c轴方向的显著收缩缩小了Feⁱ-Feⁱⁱ原子间距，可能增强Fe–Fe交换相互作用（exchange interaction），这是其T_C显著高于FGT的关键原因。

Abstract: High-quality single crystals of the two-dimensional van der Waals ferromagnet Fe$_3$GaTe$_2$ (FGaT) were successfully grown using the chemical vapour transport method, which effectively reduced surface impurities compared with conventional self-flux growth. Structural and magnetic characterizations were performed using single-crystal X-ray and neutron diffraction. The results confirm that FGaT crystallizes in the hexagonal $P6_3/mmc$ structure, with Fe occupying two inequivalent sites (Fe$^{i}$ and Fe$^{ii}$), where the magnetic moment of Fe$^{i}$ [1.9(2) $μ_B$] is larger than that of Fe$^{ii}$ [1.4(6) $μ_B$]. The magnetic easy axis is oriented along the $c$ axis and the Curie temperature ($T_C$) is approximately 355-360 K. Compared with Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$ (FGT), FGaT exhibits a slightly expanded $a$ axis and a contracted $c$ axis, resulting in a reduction in the Fe$^{i}$-Fe$^{ii}$ interatomic distance along the $c$ axis. This pronounced contraction could strengthen the Fe$-$Fe exchange interaction, which is believed to be the key factor responsible for the significantly higher $T_C$ in FGaT relative to FGT.

### [11] [Correlation-Driven Orbital-Selective Fermiology and Superconductivity in the Bilayer Nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10101)
*Yong-Yue Zong,Shun-Li Yu,Jian-Xin Li*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于时间依赖变分原理（TDVP）团簇微扰理论（CPT）与密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）计算，研究了La₃Ni₂O₇中电子关联驱动的轨道选择性费米面重构：dz²谱权重被耗尽，γ带沉入费米能级以下，α和β带出现赝能隙（pseudogap），强耦合下费米弧（Fermi arcs）由dx²-y²轨道主导；超导配对从dz²主导转向dx²-y²主导的层间自旋单态配对，且保持s±结构，表明γ口袋消失并非不利于超导，而是配对通道的关联驱动转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近对La₃Ni₂O₇的角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）测量揭示，dz²衍生的γ带可位于费米能级以下，这与基于密度泛函理论（DFT）的三个费米面（Fermi surfaces）图像相矛盾。该实验-理论分歧促使作者采用超越DFT的强关联方法，重新考察该材料的电子结构与超导配对机制。

Method: 采用基于时间依赖变分原理（time-dependent variational principle, TDVP）的团簇微扰理论（cluster perturbation theory, CPT），在最多16个物理位的团簇上进行计算；同时结合大规模密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）计算，研究一个双层的双轨道（bilayer two-orbital）Hubbard模型。

Result: TDVP-CPT计算表明，电子关联导致轨道选择性的低能谱重构：dz²谱权重逐渐耗尽，γ带沉入费米能级以下，α和β带打开赝能隙（pseudogap），强耦合下费米弧（Fermi arcs）由dx²-y²轨道主导。DMRG计算显示，主导的超导配对从dz²主导转变为dx²-y²主导的层间自旋单态（interlayer spin-singlet）配对，同时保持s±结构。

Conclusion: γ口袋的消失并不损害超导电性；相反，它标志着配对通道发生关联驱动的转变，这一转变由层间反铁磁性（interlayer antiferromagnetism）、Hund耦合（Hund's coupling）和轨道间杂化（inter-orbital hybridization）共同中介。

Abstract: Recent angle-resolved photoemission measurements on La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ have challenged the density-functional-theory-based picture of three Fermi surfaces by revealing that the $d_{z^2}$-derived $γ$ band can reside below the Fermi level. Motivated by this discrepancy, we investigate a realistic bilayer two-orbital Hubbard model using time-dependent variational principle (TDVP)-based cluster perturbation theory (CPT), alongside large-scale density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) calculations. Our TDVP-CPT calculations, performed on clusters of up to 16 physical sites, reveal that electronic correlations drive a pronounced orbital-selective reconstruction of the low-energy spectrum: the $d_{z^2}$ spectral weight is progressively depleted, the $γ$ band sinks below the Fermi level, and pseudogaps open on the remaining $α$ and $β$ bands, leaving Fermi arcs dominated by the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital at strong coupling. Furthermore, large-scale DMRG calculations demonstrate that the leading superconducting correlations evolve consistently with this Fermi surface reconstruction, transitioning from $d_{z^2}$-dominated to $d_{x^2-y^2}$-dominated interlayer spin-singlet pairing while retaining an $s_{\pm}$ structure. Consequently, our results indicate that the disappearance of the $γ$ pocket is not detrimental to superconductivity; rather, it signals a correlation-driven shift of the pairing channel mediated by interlayer antiferromagnetism, Hund's coupling, and inter-orbital hybridization.

</details>


### [12] [B-H hysteresis in itinerant Feromagnetism from Chern-Simons Gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10104)
*Kenzo Ishikawa*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多电子系统自由能中log H项的来源，并解释对称单畴系统中观测到的一级相变（first order transition）和B-H磁滞回线（B-H hysteresis）的物理机制。

Method: 基于陈-西蒙斯规范场论（Chern-Simons gauge theory）推导多电子系统的自由能，从中提取出log H项。

Result: 自由能中存在的log H项在H=0处具有奇异性（singularity），导致对称单畴（symmetric and single domain）的多电子系统出现一级相变和B-H磁滞回线。

Conclusion: 该一级相变和磁滞现象的起源在于量子力学（quantum mechanics），与畴壁的非可逆运动（non-invertible motions of domains）无关，且仅出现在对称单畴系统中。

Abstract: The log H term is derived in the free energy of many-electron system from Chern-Simons gauge theory. Owing to the singularity at $H=0$, this leads the first order transition and B-H hysteresis to many-electron systems of symmetric and single domain. This has the origin in quantum mechanics and is irrelevant to non-invertible motions of domains. This transition appears in single and symmetric domain.

### [13] [Cavity-Induced Excitonic Insulation and Non-Fermi-Liquid Behavior in Dirac Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10652)
*Yuxuan Guo,Ashida Yuto*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文研究了嵌入高阻抗超表面（high-impedance metasurface）形成的深亚波长腔（deep-subwavelength cavity）中的二维狄拉克费米子（two-dimensional Dirac fermions）。超表面支持的准静电磁横模（quasielectrostatic transverse-magnetic modes）介导了电子间长程相互作用，该作用可驱动激子绝缘相变（excitonic insulating phase）或非费米液体临界态（non-Fermi-liquid critical regime），并在磁场下动态解除第零朗道能级简并，表明该腔平台可用于工程化关联狄拉克物质（correlated Dirac matter）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索新型边界条件（即高阻抗超表面腔）对二维狄拉克费米子基态性质的影响，尤其是能否通过工程化长程相互作用实现强关联量子相变。

Method: 采用静态电子屏蔽（static electronic screening）与戴森-施温格方程（Dyson-Schwinger equation）分析方法，研究超表面腔所介导的长程相互作用对狄拉克材料的影响。

Result: 当费米子味道数$N_{f} < 16/\pi$时，相互作用驱动激子绝缘相，发生无穷阶量子相变（infinite-order quantum phase transition），并自发产生质量隙；当$N_{f} > 16/\pi$时，系统保持无能隙但进入非费米液体临界区，准粒子权重奇异地被压制为零，狄拉克锥呈现非解析色散关系。垂直磁场下，腔波动在所有$N_{f}$下动态解除第零朗道能级简并。

Conclusion: 高阻抗超表面腔是实现工程化关联狄拉克物质的有效平台，能够通过调节腔结构控制电子间相互作用，从而调控狄拉克材料的量子相。

Abstract: We investigate two-dimensional Dirac fermions embedded in a deep-subwavelength cavity formed by high-impedance metasurfaces. We point out that, unlike conventional metallic boundaries, these metasurfaces support quasielectrostatic transverse-magnetic modes that mediate a long-range interaction between two-dimensional electrons. Combining static electronic screening with a Dyson-Schwinger analysis, we show that this engineered interaction can qualitatively alter the ground-state properties of Dirac materials. For a fermion flavor number $N_{f}$ below a critical value $N_{c}=16/π$, the interaction drives an excitonic insulating phase through an infinite-order quantum phase transition and spontaneously generates a mass gap. At $N_{f}>N_{c}$, the system remains gapless but enters a non-Fermi-liquid critical regime where the quasiparticle residue is singularly suppressed to zero, and the Dirac cone exhibits a nonanalytic dispersion relation. Furthermore, under a perpendicular magnetic field, the cavity fluctuations dynamically lift the zeroth Landau level degeneracy across all $N_{f}$. These results identify high-impedance metasurface cavities as promising platforms for engineering correlated Dirac matter.

</details>

### [14] [Completely asymptotically free chiral theories with scalars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08294)
*Giacomo Cacciapaglia,Francesco Sannino,Sophie Wagner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了手征规范理论（chiral gauge theories）中包括标量场时的完全渐近自由条件，分析了Georgi-Glashow和Bars-Yankielowicz两类推广模型中标量场处于基础表示（fundamental representation）或伴随表示（adjoint representation）下的情况，发现对于特定颜色数和矢量-手征族（vector-like and chiral families）多重性，可以实现完全渐近自由。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大统一模型（grand unified models）中手征规范理论需要满足完全渐近自由条件，以确保所有相互作用在短距离下保持渐近自由，但包含标量场时该条件的系统性分析尚不充分。

Method: 系统分析了规范耦合（gauge coupling）、Yukawa耦合（Yukawa coupling）和四次耦合（quartic coupling）之间的相互作用，在标量场处于基础表示和伴随表示两种情形下，针对多手征费米子族（multiple chiral fermion families）的情况进行渐近自由条件的推导与检验。

Result: 两种标量表示下，完全渐近自由模型均可在特定的颜色数以及矢量-手征族多重性组合下实现。

Conclusion: 指出了在大统一框架下实现手征规范理论完全渐近自由所需的参数条件，为构建自洽的高能标模型提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We provide the conditions for complete asymptotic freedom for chiral gauge theories including scalars, as motivated by grand unified models. These are generalised Georgi-Glashow and Bars-Yankielowicz theories that feature a scalar field transforming either in the fundamental or in the adjoint of the gauge group. In both scenarios, we consider the addition of multiple chiral fermion families. We systematically analyse the interplay between gauge, Yukawa, and quartic couplings required for all interactions to remain asymptotically free at short distances. We find that for both scalar representations, complete asymptotic free models can be obtained for a specific number of colours and multiplicity of vector-like and chiral families.

### [15] [Inner Horizon Saddles and a Spectral KSW Criterion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08335)
*Jacqueline Caminiti,Aidan Herderschee*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于JT引力（JT gravity）标准结果，指出带电黑洞在接近极端（extremality）时，Bekenstein-Hawking熵公式会收到一个修正项，该修正项半经典地等于内视界面积指数负值；这两个指数项相互抵消导致了趋向极端时态密度（density of states）为零。作者提出该修正项对应一个具有负边界长度的复杂鞍点几何（complex saddle geometry），即内视界鞍点（inner horizon saddle），并通过Picard-Lefschetz分析和稳定性分析讨论其对态密度的贡献。尽管该鞍点违反Kontsevich-Segal-Witten (KSW)允许性判据（allowability criterion），但通过正确处理“错误符号模式”（wrong-sign modes）可描述其一圈效应，并据此提出较弱版本的谱KSW判据（spectral KSW criterion）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解带电黑洞在接近极端时Bekenstein-Hawking熵公式的修正项及其物理起源，特别是修正项对应内视界面积指数负值的半经典解释，以及该修正如何通过复杂鞍点几何得以实现。

Method: 利用JT引力标准结果进行半经典分析；基于arXiv:2402.10162的工作，将修正项对应为具有负边界长度的内视界鞍点几何；采用Picard-Lefschetz分析对逆拉普拉斯围道（inverse Laplace contour）进行解析延拓，并结合鞍点稳定性分析；通过处理错误符号模式描述一圈效应，并据此提出谱KSW判据。

Result: 修正项可半经典表达为内视界面积指数负值，其与Bekenstein-Hawking项的抵消使态密度在极端极限下趋于零。内视界鞍点违反KSW允许性判据，但一圈效应可通过正确处理错误符号模式加以描述。提出了谱KSW判据作为较弱版本。

Conclusion: 提出了一种新的复杂鞍点几何（内视界鞍点）解释带电黑洞接近极端时的态密度行为，并引入谱KSW判据以放宽对复杂引力鞍点的允许性要求，为一圈修正的可定义性提供判定依据。

Abstract: The Bekenstein-Hawking entropy formula $ρ= e^{A/4G}$ receives significant corrections for charged black holes near extremality. Using standard results in JT gravity, the correction term can semiclassically be expressed as minus the exponential of the inner horizon area, $e^{A_{\text{inner}}/4G}$, and the cancellation between these two exponentials enforces a vanishing density of states towards extremality, when the two horizons collide. Building on arXiv:2402.10162, we argue that the correction term corresponds to a complex saddle geometry of the bulk gravitational path integral. The proposed geometry has a negative boundary length and caps off at the inner horizon; we refer to it as the inner horizon saddle. We discuss how the saddle, and its accompanying minus sign, contribute to the density of states through a Picard-Lefschetz analysis of the inverse Laplace contour, together with a stability analysis of the saddle. We also address the inner horizon saddle's violation of the Kontsevich-Segal-Witten (KSW) allowability criterion for the inclusion of complex metrics. Despite this violation, which is believed to cause unphysical divergences in path integral computations, one can describe one-loop effects on the inner horizon saddle by carefully treating wrong-sign modes. Motivated by this observation, we propose a weaker version of the KSW criterion, which we call the spectral KSW criterion. Its purpose is to characterize when one-loop corrections around complex gravitational saddles are well defined.

</details>


### [16] [Charge Transport in Magnetized Holographic $\mathcal{M}$-QGP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08339)
*Shivam Singh Kushwah*

TL;DR: 该论文在具有四次曲率修正的全息M理论背景下，利用D6探针膜（probe D6 flavor branes）的狄拉克-玻恩-因费尔德（DBI）作用量，计算了热QGP类理论中的直流电导（DC conductivity）和霍尔电导（Hall conductivity），并分析了在有无外磁场下成对产生（pair production）对输运的贡献，将先前的AdS/CFT结果推广至非共形、高阶导数（higher-derivative）的设定中。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 得到了非共形、高阶导数修正下的直流电导与霍尔电导表达式；明确了在特定参数区间内，成对产生机制（pair production）主导输运过程，超越了一般电荷载流子输运（charge carrier transport）的贡献。

Conclusion: 该工作成功将先前基于AdS/CFT对偶的输运结果推广到包含四次曲率修正的非共形热QGP类理论中，拓展了全息方法在强耦合夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）研究中的应用范围。

Abstract: We investigate DC transport in a top-down construction of thermal QGP-like theories using a holographic M-theoretic background, incorporating quartic curvature corrections. The DC and Hall conductivities are computed from the Dirac-Born-Infeld (DBI) action of the corresponding type-IIA probe D6 flavor branes via the reality condition method proposed in arXiv:0708.1994 and arXiv:0705.3870. We further analyze pair-production contributions in the presence and absence of an external magnetic field and work out regimes where pair production dominates over charge carrier transport. These findings extend earlier AdS/CFT results to non-conformal, higher-derivative settings relevant to thermal QGP-like theories.

### [17] [Entanglement islands, fuzzballs and stretched horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08347)
*Dmitry S. Ageev,Anastasia N. Zueva*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于毛球启发（fuzzball-inspired）的黑洞模型，通过引入反射边界（stretched horizon）研究岛规则（island prescription）的实现。在二维模型中观察到“闪烁岛（blinking island）”效应，在更高维度和更现实的弦论毛球几何（superstrata、bubbling解）中，岛解的存在性敏感地依赖于边界条件和几何结构，且并不普遍成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索毛球模型（fuzzball models）中岛规则（island prescription）的实现方式，以理解在更现实的弦论黑洞描述下，信息悖论（information paradox）的解决是否仍然依赖于岛解（island solutions）的存在。

Method: 采用毛球启发的简化模型，将事件视界（event horizon）替换为反射边界即“拉伸视界（stretched horizon）”；在二维模型中分析纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）动力学；随后推广到更高维，考虑体（bulk）和边界对广义熵（generalized entropy）的贡献；最后在更现实的弦论毛球几何（如superstrata和bubbling解）中估计岛解的存在条件。

Result: 二维模型中边界的存在改变了岛鞍点（island saddle）的行为，在一定参数范围内观察到“闪烁岛（blinking island）”效应，这必然导致类似信息悖论（information paradox）的出现；在高维情形下，岛解的存在敏感地依赖于边界条件和拉伸视界位置，广泛参数范围内自然缺失纠缠岛（entanglement island）；在弦论毛球几何中，岛的存在取决于几何面积在帽区（cap）附近的行为，并不普遍成立。

Conclusion: 毛球模型中岛解的存在并非理所当然，而是强烈依赖于边界条件、拉伸视界位置以及毛球几何的细节。这些结果表明，在更真实的弦论黑洞描述中，信息悖论的解决可能需要岛规则之外的机制。

Abstract: We study the implementation of the island prescription in fuzzball-inspired models of black holes. As a simplified setup, we model a fuzzball by replacing the event horizon with a reflecting boundary (stretched horizon). In the framework of two-dimensional model with such boundary, we analyze the dynamics of entanglement entropy. We find that the presence of the boundary modifies the behavior of the island saddle, and for a range of parameter values we observe the effect of blinking island found in arXiv:2311.16244 which inevitably leads to the analogue of information paradox.
  We then extend the analysis to higher dimensions, incorporating both bulk and boundary contributions to the generalized entropy. The existence of island solutions is found to depend sensitively on the boundary conditions and the position of the stretched horizon, naturally leading to the absence of entanglement islands for a wide range of parameters.
  Finally, we consider more "realistic" stringy fuzzball geometries, including superstrata and bubbling solutions, and estimate whether island solutions can arise in these backgrounds. The results indicate that the existence of islands depends on the behavior of the geometric area near the cap, and is not guaranteed in general.

### [18] [Bogomol'nyi Equations in Mixed Product Chern-Simons Theories Governing Charged Vortices and Antivortices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08822)
*Aonan Xu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将乘积陈-西蒙斯（product Chern-Simons）理论推广到混合 $U(1)\times U(1)$ 模型，其中一个规范场由陈-西蒙斯项控制，另一个由麦克斯韦（Maxwell）或玻恩-因费尔德（Born-Infeld）项控制。通过选择适当的势能，能量泛函满足拓扑下界并由一阶自对偶方程饱和。由此产生的双荷（dyonic）系统可分为涡旋-涡旋和涡旋-反涡旋两类构型。在双周期域上，布拉德洛型边界（Bradlow-type bound）对两类系统有不同影响：涡旋-涡旋系统中涡旋数不能超过该边界，能量谱有界；涡旋-反涡旋系统中边界施加于涡旋数与反涡旋数之差，但各自数目可任意大，能量谱无界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 乘积陈-西蒙斯模型中已知仅有涡旋（vortex）构型，本文旨在将其扩展至包含涡旋和反涡旋（antivortex）共存的混合模型，从而丰富可解拓扑孤子系统的类型。

Method: 通过将乘积陈-西蒙斯理论扩展为混合 $U(1)\times U(1)$ 规范场论，一个规范场采用陈-西蒙斯（Chern-Simons）项，另一个采用麦克斯韦（Maxwell）或玻恩-因费尔德（Born-Infeld）项，并构造合适的势能函数，使能量泛函满足拓扑下界并由一阶自对偶（first-order self-dual）方程饱和。

Result: 推导出涡旋和反涡旋共存的双荷系统；在双周期域上建立了布拉德洛型边界，表明涡旋-涡旋系统中涡旋数有上界，能量谱有界；而涡旋-反涡旋系统中仅涡旋数与反涡旋数之差受限于该边界，各自数目可任意，能量谱无界。

Conclusion: 混合 $U(1)\times U(1)$ 模型不仅推广了乘积陈-西蒙斯理论，还揭示了涡旋-反涡旋共存系统与纯涡旋系统在拓扑边界条件和能量谱结构上的本质差异。

Abstract: We extend product Chern-Simons theory to develop several mixed $U(1)\times U(1)$ models where one gauge field is governed by a Chern-Simons term and the other by a Maxwell or Born-Infeld term. We show that, by choosing suitable potentials, the energy functional admits a topological lower bound saturated by first-order self-dual equations. The resulting dyonic systems can be divided into vortex-vortex and vortex-antivortex configurations, and the coexistence of vortices and antivortices in the latter extends the vortex-only result known in product Chern-Simons model. On a doubly periodic domain, we establish Bradlow-type bounds with distinct physical implications: for vortex-only systems, the vortex numbers stay below this bound and cannot be arbitrarily large; for vortex-antivortex systems, the bound is imposed on the difference between the vortex and antivortex numbers, while the individual numbers are arbitrary. This distinction results in a bounded energy spectrum for the former and an unbounded energy spectrum for the latter.

### [20] [Taming the infrared in de Sitter space: autonomous equations, stochastic approach, and Borel resummation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09736)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究 de Sitter 时空中无质量自相互作用标量场关联函数的发散微扰级数，利用自治方程（autonomous equations）方法得到有限时间依赖函数，并通过对 Borel-Le Roy 变换应用自治方程进行 Borel 求和（Borel resummation），显著改进了与随机图像时间演化的匹配；此外还提出了提取微扰系数的替代方案，并基于 Schwinger-Dyson 型微分方程截断给出了自治方程的新推导。

Method: 首先利用先前提出的自治方程（autonomous equations）方法得到有限时间依赖函数；然后将自治方程技术应用于 Borel-Le Roy 变换，通过求解这些方程执行 Borel 求和（Borel resummation）；此外还提出了一种提取微扰系数的替代方法，并通过截断 Schwinger-Dyson 型微分方程（Schwinger-Dyson-type differential equations）系统重新推导了自治方程。

Result: 自治方程方法得到的有限时间依赖函数能较好近似随机理论中关联函数的时间演化；对 Borel-Le Roy 变换应用自治方程后进行 Borel 求和，其结果与随机图像时间演化的匹配程度显著提高。

Conclusion: 自治方程结合 Borel 求和是处理 de Sitter 时空中无质量标量场微扰级数发散问题的有效手段，能够更精确地再现随机图像所预测的时间演化行为。

Abstract: We investigate the divergent perturbative series of correlation functions for a massless, self-interacting scalar field in de Sitter space. First, we use our previously proposed method of autonomous equations to obtain finite time-dependent functions, and show that these functions approximate the time evolution of the correlation functions of the stochastic theory reasonably well. Second, we apply the technique of autonomous equations to the Borel-Le Roy transforms of correlation functions, and use solutions of these equations to perform Borel resummation. The results match the time evolution obtained in the stochastic picture substantially better. In addition, we propose an alternative method for extracting perturbative coefficients and provide a new derivation of our autonomous equation by truncating a system of Schwinger-Dyson-type differential equations.

Abstract: We investigate Type IIB compactifications with spatially varying fluxes and dilaton profiles in the setting of dynamical cobordism. ### [23] [The Free Particle--Oscillator--Inverted Oscillator Triangle: Conformal Bridges, Metaplectic Rotations and $\mathfrak{osp}(1|2)$ Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09947)
*Andrey Alcala,Mikhail S. Plyushchay*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究自由粒子（free particle, FP）、谐振子（harmonic oscillator, HO）与反谐振子（inverted harmonic oscillator, IHO）作为同一共形/元辛结构（conformal/metaplectic structure）的抛物型、椭圆型和双曲型实现，并通过桥变换（bridge transformation）建立三者之间的非幺正等价关系，进而应用于量子霍尔鞍点散射、Schwinger型产生、Rindler/Unruh效应及近视界Hawking辐射等物理场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示自由粒子、谐振子与反谐振子这三种看似谱结构迥异的系统在共形超代数 $\mathfrak{osp}(1|2)$ 框架下的深层代数联系，并利用桥变换（bridge transformation）统一描述其态空间与动力学，从而建立连接不同物理场景（抛物型、椭圆型、双曲型）的理论桥梁。

Method: 基于共形/元辛结构（conformal/metaplectic structure）及其在超代数 $\mathfrak{osp}(1|2)$ 中的扩展，定义桥变换（bridge transformation）来关联FP、HO与IHO三种实现；采用光锥Mellin分解（light-cone Mellin decomposition）处理IHO散射数据，并利用Fourier-Mellin连接系数（Fourier-Mellin connection coefficients）导出IHO的透射与反射振幅；引入双曲型Cayley-Niederer映射（hyperbolic Cayley-Niederer map）描述含时薛定谔方程。

Result: FP的零能Jordan态映射为HO的束缚态与IHO的两支Gamow族；FP平面波映射为HO的相干态，并经光锥Mellin分解后映射为IHO的散射数据。FP-IHO桥是实元辛四分之一旋转（real metaplectic quarter-rotation），而FP-HO桥在薛定谔表象中非幺正，但在Fock-Bargmann表象中变为幺正极化变换。IHO的透射与反射振幅由Fourier-Mellin连接系数（即Weber/Stokes连接数据）给出。

Conclusion: 三种系统在共形超代数框架下可通过桥变换统一描述，双曲型扇区（IHO）的数学结构在量子霍尔鞍点散射、Schwinger型粒子产生、Rindler/Unruh效应、近视界Hawking辐射及Berry-Keating/反平方结构等物理问题中具有重要应用前景。

Abstract: We study the free particle (FP), the harmonic oscillator (HO) and the inverted harmonic oscillator (IHO) as parabolic, elliptic and hyperbolic realizations of one conformal/metaplectic structure, naturally extended to the superconformal algebra $\mathfrak{osp}(1|2)$. Since the corresponding self-adjoint Hamiltonians have different spectra, the relations between them are not ordinary unitary equivalences. They are instead bridge transformations between different realizations of the same conformal module. We show that the zero-energy Jordan states of the FP are mapped to HO bound states and to the two IHO Gamow families, while FP plane waves are mapped to HO coherent states and, after light-cone Mellin decomposition, to the IHO scattering data. The direct FP--IHO bridge is a real metaplectic quarter-rotation, in contrast with the stationary FP--HO conformal bridge, which is nonunitary in the Schrödinger representation but becomes unitary as a change of polarization to the Fock--Bargmann representation. The IHO transmission and reflection amplitudes are obtained as Fourier--Mellin connection coefficients, equivalently as Weber/Stokes connection data. We also describe the hyperbolic Cayley--Niederer map for the time-dependent Schrödinger equation, the Wigner/separatrix picture, and the coherent-state and Bogoliubov-transformation aspects of the construction. Some physical applications of the hyperbolic sector are briefly discussed, including quantum Hall saddle scattering, Schwinger-type production, Rindler/Unruh and near-horizon Hawking settings, and Berry--Keating/inverse-square structures.

</details>


### [24] [Bulk-Edge Correspondence via Higher Gauge Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10232)
*Hisham Sati,Urs Schreiber*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过有效相对高阶规范理论（effective relative higher gauge theory）重新表述分数量子霍尔（FQH）系统的体-边对应关系（bulk-edge correspondence），识别复Hopf纤维丛为主导拓扑效应的分类对象，并发现该理论可在M2/M5膜几何工程化（geometric engineering）框架下从11维超引力（11D supergravity）中自然导出，统一解释了FQH液体中$W_\infty$对称性与超对称性（supersymmetry）的共存现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用有效相对高阶规范理论（effective relative higher gauge theory）作为形式框架，以分类纤维丛（classifying fibration）的选择控制体-边对应关系；具体识别复Hopf纤维丛（complex Hopf fibration）为FQH系统的分类对象，并利用扭绞等变微分Cohomotopy（twisted equivariant differential Cohomotopy, TED Cohomotopy）实现通量量子化（flux-quantization），在11维超引力中通过M2/M5膜探测A型轨道奇点（A-type orbi-singularities）进行几何工程化（geometric engineering）。

Result: 复Hopf纤维丛产生了Floreanini-Jackiw/Wess-Zumino-Witten手性边界流（chiral edge currents）的非拉格朗日重构（non-Lagrangian reconstruction）；该高阶规范理论在M膜体系中自然实现：M2膜在M5膜上终结的M弦（M-string）工程化了FQH液体的边界。

Conclusion: 这种基于M膜的几何工程化或许能够自然阐明FQH液体长波长集体激发中$W_\infty$对称性与超对称性（supersymmetry）之间奇特组合的物理起源。

Abstract: More profound than bulk topological order of quantum materials is only its unwinding via gapless excitations along boundaries of the sample. We recast this bulk-edge correspondence -- for the experimentally relevant case of fractional quantum Hall (FQH) systems -- in terms of effective relative higher gauge theory, controlled by choices of classifying fibrations. For FQH systems, we identify the complex Hopf fibration as classifying the bulk/boundary topological effects, and find that it yields a non-Lagrangian reconstruction of Floreanini-Jackiw/Wess-Zumino-Witten chiral edge currents.
  Remarkably, the resulting effective FQH higher gauge theory turns out to be "geometrically engineered" on M2/M5-branes probing A-type orbi-singularities in 11D supergravity, globally completed by flux-quantization in twisted equivariant differential (TED) Cohomotopy: Here the M-string ends of M2-branes on M5-branes engineer the FQH liquid's boundary. This geometric engineering on M-branes might naturally elucidate the curious combination of $W_\infty$-symmetry and of super-symmetry that is known to govern the collective excitations of FQH liquids at long wavelengths.

*Stefano Bolognesi,Kenichi Konishi,Matteo Orso*

TL;DR: 本文研究了几种简单的渐近自由手征规范理论（asymptotically-free chiral gauge theories），其模型仅由规范群、Weyl费米子表示及重整化群不变标度参数决定。基于广义对称性和新型反常匹配条件等近期理论进展，并结合矢量规范理论（如QCD和超对称杨-米尔斯理论）的已有知识，揭示了这些模型在红外有效理论、重整化群流和轻谱结构上的丰富与复杂性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 模型仅以规范群、Weyl费米子表示及重整化群不变标度（renormalization-group-invariant scales）Λ_i 为自由参数，不含非平凡非阿贝尔整体对称性（nonabelian global symmetries）；分析依赖广义对称性（generalized symmetries）与新型反常匹配（anomaly-matching）条件，并借鉴矢量规范理论如QCD和超对称杨-米尔斯理论（supersymmetric Yang-Mills theories）的已知结果。

Result: 这些模型在红外有效理论（infrared effective theories）、重整化群流（RG flows）和轻谱（light spectra）方面展现出令人意外的丰富而有趣的结构。

Conclusion: 简单的手征规范理论模型可产生复杂的红外动力学，广义对称性与反常匹配分析是理解此类强耦合系统的有效工具。

Abstract: Several simple asymptotically-free chiral gauge theories are studied. The only ``free parameters'' of our models are the choice of the gauge group and the matter Weyl fermion representations, and the relative magnitudes of the renormalization-group-invariant scales $Λ_i$ associated with each gauge group. None of our models has nontrivial nonabelian global symmetries (``family''--like fermion representations). We rely on some recent theoretical developments on the dynamics of strongly--coupled chiral gauge theories, based on the generalized symmetries and associated new types of anomaly-matching consideration, but also on the solid knowledge on vectorlike gauge theories such as QCD and supersymmetric Yang-Mills theories. The structures of the infrared effective theories, the RG flows, and the light spectra found in these models are surprisingly rich and intriguing.

### [26] [Birth of Inflationary Universes via Wineglass Wormholes and their No-Boundary Relatives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10548)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解暴胀宇宙如何从已有时空中成核（nucleation）产生，以及该过程中涉及的拓扑转变机制。

Method: 通过数值方法求解欧几里得虫洞解，分别考虑轴子场和磁规范场与自相互作用标量场耦合的情形；分析尺度因子（scale factor）的局部极大值特征，并研究小电荷极限下的几何分裂行为。

Result: 成功构建了由轴子场或磁规范场与标量场共同支持的酒杯虫洞数值解，描述了尺度因子具有多个极值的更奇异解；发现小轴子或磁荷极限下，酒杯虫洞解分裂为背景时空与一个分离的无边界瞬子。

Conclusion: 详细研究了相关的拓扑转变过程，并对酒杯虫洞/无边界瞬子这一共同家族的性质及存在的疑难问题进行了广泛讨论。

Abstract: We study Euclidean wineglass wormholes, which mediate the nucleation of inflationary spacetimes from an existing spacetime with asymptotically flat or Anti-de Sitter regions. These wormholes are distinguished by the presence of a local maximum of the scale factor, which allows the analytically continued Lorentzian spacetime to expand after materialization. We present explicit numerical wormhole solutions supported either by an axionic field or a magnetic gauge field, in both cases in conjunction with a self-interacting scalar field. More exotic solutions, with multiple extrema of the scale factor, are also described. As we discovered recently, in the limit of small axionic or magnetic charge, wineglass wormhole solutions split into two separate geometries, one being the background spacetime and the other a disconnected no-boundary instanton. We study the associated topology changing transition in detail and provide an extensive discussion of both the properties and puzzles exhibited by this common family of wineglass/no-boundary instantons.

### [27] [On the Casimir effect with mixed dynamical edge mode and perfect electromagnetic conducting boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10662)
*Jarne Devroe,David Dudal,Sebbe Stouten*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了一块具有动力学边缘模式（DEM）边界条件的平板与一块完美电磁导体（PEMC）平板构成的平行板系统中的Casimir效应。通过引入新的边缘场恢复BRST不变性，将边界条件提升至作用量中，并积分掉体场得到非局域有效边界理论，进而计算Casimir能量。结果表明DEM平板与完美磁导体（PMC）平板在Casimir效应上等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨动力学边缘模式（dynamical edge mode, DEM）边界条件在平行板Casimir效应（Casimir effect）中的作用，并比较其与完美电磁导体（perfect electromagnetic conductor, PEMC）边界条件的异同，以揭示DEM平板在Casimir效应中的物理等效性。

Method: 为恢复BRST不变性（BRST invariance），在DEM平板上引入新的边缘场（edge fields）；利用拉格朗日乘子场（Lagrange multiplier fields）将边界条件提升至作用量中；积分掉体场（bulk fields）得到非局域有效边界理论（non-local effective boundary theory），并由此计算Casimir能量（Casimir energy）。

Result: 计算得到的Casimir力（Casimir force）与完美磁导体（perfect magnetic conductor, PMC）-PEMC设置中的结果完全相同，表明在Casimir效应视角下，DEM平板等价于PMC平板。

Conclusion: DEM边界条件与PMC边界条件在Casimir效应中具有等效性；同时，文中还给出了从配分函数（partition function）计算Casimir能量的一般泛函方法（general functional method）的详细推导。

Abstract: We study the Casimir effect for a parallel plate setup with one plate with dynamical edge mode (DEM) boundary conditions, and one plate with perfect electromagnetic conductor (PEMC) boundary conditions. In order to restore BRST invariance, new edge fields are introduced on the DEM plate. We then lift the boundary conditions into the action using Lagrange multiplier fields, and integrate out the bulk fields to obtain a non-local effective boundary theory from which we compute the Casimir energy. The resulting Casimir force is identical to a PMC-PEMC setup, implying that, from the point of view of the Casimir effect, a DEM plate is equivalent to a PMC plate. We also include a detailed derivation of the general functional method used to compute the Casimir energy from the partition function.

### [28] [Regularized Master-Field Approximation for Large-$N$ Reduced Matrix Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10720)
*Reishi Maeta*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于主场（master field）的数值方法，用于大N约化矩阵模型（large-N reduced matrix models）。该方法将原本无限维的主场正则化为有限维，并尽可能满足圈方程（loop equations）。该方法从根本上避免了符号问题（sign problem），因此可同时应用于欧几里得（Euclidean）和闵可夫斯基（Minkowski）型模型。在一矩阵模型和二矩阵模型的数值计算中，欧几里得情形精确再现了解析解，闵可夫斯基情形则很好地再现了微扰结果，验证了该方法的有效性，并支持了所研究的矩阵模型存在正则化主场描述的观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大N约化矩阵模型在理论研究中有重要地位，但传统数值方法常面临符号问题，尤其是在闵可夫斯基（Minkowski）型模型中，阻碍了大规模数值模拟。本文旨在开发一种无符号问题的数值方法，以适用更广泛的矩阵模型。

Method: 提出基于主场（master field）的数值方法，通过将原本无限维的主场正则化为有限维矩阵，并要求其尽可能满足圈方程（loop equations）来实现数值计算。该方法在基础层面避免了符号问题（sign problem），因此对欧几里得（Euclidean）型和闵可夫斯基（Minkowski）型模型均适用。

Result: 在一矩阵模型和二矩阵模型的数值计算中，欧几里得（Euclidean）情形下精确解得到良好复现；闵可夫斯基（Minkowski）情形下微扰结果得到良好复现。结果验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文所提出的基于主场（master field）的正则化数值方法能够有效处理大N约化矩阵模型，适用于欧几里得（Euclidean）和闵可夫斯基（Minkowski）两类模型，并支持了所研究矩阵模型存在正则化主场描述的结论。

Abstract: We propose a numerical method based on the master field for large-$N$ reduced matrix models. While the master field is originally an infinite-dimensional matrix, in this method it is regularized to a finite dimension, with the requirement that it satisfies the loop equations as much as possible. This formulation can be directly implemented for numerical computation, and since there is no sign problem at the fundamental level, the method can be applied regardless of whether the model is of Euclidean or Minkowski type. In numerical calculations for one- and two-matrix models, the exact solution is well reproduced in the Euclidean case, while perturbative results are well reproduced in the Minkowski case. This demonstrates the effectiveness of the method and supports the idea that the matrix models studied in this paper admit a regularized master-field description.

### [30] [Parafermionizing the Monster](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10902)
*Yamato Honda,Justin Kaidi,Ippo Orii*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在特定假设下，将 Monster CFT 的 parafermionization 表示为对 ℤ_p-parafermion 理论 𝒫(p) 与其对偶 𝒫(p)^∨ 的直积进行非可逆规范变换，该变换的全局对称性由 ℤ_{pA} 的中心化子（centralizer）刻画。随后通过追踪 𝒫(p)×𝒫(p)^∨ 的对称性在该规范变换下的行为来推导 Monster CFT 的对称范畴。

Abstract: We study the parafermionization of the Monster CFT with respect to its $\mathbb{Z}_{pA}$ subgroups, with $p$ an odd prime. Under certain assumptions, we show that the parafermionization is equal to a non-invertible gauging of $\mathcal{P}(p) \times \mathcal{P}(p)^\vee$, where $\mathcal{P}(p)$ is the theory of $\mathbb{Z}_p$-parafermions and $\mathcal{P}(p)^\vee$ is an appropriate dual theory, with global symmetry characterized by the centralizer of $\mathbb{Z}_{pA}$. ### [31] [Holographic complexity of conformal fields in global de Sitter spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21408)
*Sanhita Parihar,Shubho R. Roy*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过体积和作用量两种全息方案，计算了刚性全局德西特时空（de Sitter spacetime, dS$_d$）中共形量子场的全息复杂度（holographic complexity）。研究涉及两种设定：一是以全局dS$_d$叶状结构（foliations）描述的AdS$_{d+1}$时空，其共形边界上的CFT复杂度；二是嵌入AdS$_{d+1}$时空中的全局dS$_d$膜（brane）上的CFT复杂度。论文对两种结果进行了比较，并与文献中使用静态坐标或共形（庞加莱）坐标覆盖德西特时空片段的替代全息设定下的相关结果进行了对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全息复杂度（holographic complexity）是量子信息与全息对偶（holographic duality）交叉领域的重要概念，旨在通过引力理论描述边界量子场论中的计算复杂度。该论文将此框架推广至德西特时空（de Sitter spacetime）中的共形场论（CFT），探讨在全局德西特几何下全息复杂度的行为，并系统比较不同坐标覆盖和全息设定下的结果差异。

Method: 采用体积方案（volume prescription）和作用量方案（action prescription）两种全息复杂度计算方法。首先在全局dS$_d$叶状结构下构建AdS$_{d+1}$时空，计算其共形边界上CFT的复杂度；随后考虑嵌入AdS$_{d+1}$中的全局dS$_d$膜（brane）设定，计算该膜上CFT的全息复杂度。

Result: 两种设定下（全局dS$_d$共形边界与全局dS$_d$膜）的全息复杂度结果存在差异；这些结果也与文献中使用静态坐标（static coordinates）或共形（庞加莱）坐标覆盖德西特时空片段的替代全息设定得到的结果不同。

Conclusion: 全局德西特时空中的全息复杂度依赖于具体的全息设定（边界或膜）以及时空坐标覆盖方式，反映了复杂度概念在德西特背景下的非平凡几何依赖性。

Abstract: We compute the holographic complexity of conformal quantum fields in rigid global de Sitter spacetime (dS$_{d}$) using the volume and action prescriptions. First we consider AdS$_{d+1}$ spacetime in global dS$_{d}$ foliations, and compute the complexity of the CFT supported on the global dS$_{d}$ conformal boundary. Next, we consider CFT supported on a global dS$_d$ (UV) brane embedded in AdS$_{d+1}$ spacetime, and compute the holographic complexity in this brane set up. We compare and contrast the results in the two cases, as well as with related results in the literature obtained in alternative holographic set ups involving patches of de Sitter spacetime covered by static coordinates or conformal (Poincaré) coordinates.

### [32] [Self-dual solutions of a field theory model of two linked rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2311.01277)
*Neda Abbasi Taklimi,Franco Ferrari,Marcin R. Piatek*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探索了两个具有固定高斯环绕数的高分子环（形成4-辫结）模型与非相对论性任意子（anyon）统计力学之间的联系，在排除体积相互作用关闭的条件下，分析了由拓扑约束引发的熵相互作用，并推导了自对偶场方程的非平庸解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在已有工作[7, 8]建立的链接高分子环模型与任意子（anyon）统计力学之间联系的基础上，进一步探索该模型在无排除体积相互作用下的拓扑约束效应，揭示系统热涨落中维持全局拓扑性质的物理机制。

Method: 关闭排除体积相互作用，仅保留由拓扑约束产生的熵相互作用；在4-辫结（4-plat）的一个空间维度趋于无穷大的极限下，分析极小化模型能量的场方程，并从高分子视角给出物理解释。

Result: 自对偶（self-dual）贡献负责维持系统全局拓扑性质所需的长程相互作用；非自对偶部分与拓扑约束相关，描述防止高分子链断裂的局域单体相互作用。在假设半条4-辫结单体密度为常数的近似下，发现了至少两个能量极小点，并推导出非平凡的自对偶解。

Conclusion: 两个链接高分子环的能量景观相当复杂；自对偶和非自对偶部分分别对应全局拓扑保持与局域链完整性约束，揭示了拓扑约束下高分子系统的丰富相结构。

Abstract: In this work the connection established in [7, 8] between a model of two linked polymers rings with fixed Gaussian linking number forming a 4-plat and the statistical mechanics of non-relativistic anyon particles is explored. The excluded volume interactions have been switched off and only the interactions of entropic origin arising from the topological constraints are considered. An interpretation from the polymer point of view of the field equations that minimize the energy of the model in the limit in which one of the spatial dimensions of the 4-plat becomes very large is provided. It is shown that the self-dual contributions are responsible for the long-range interactions that are necessary for preserving the global topological properties of the system during the thermal fluctuations. The non self-dual part is also related to the topological constraints, and takes into account the local interactions acting on the monomers in order to prevent the breaking of the polymer lines. It turns out that the energy landscape of the two linked rings is quite complex. Assuming as a rough approximation that the monomer densities of half of the 4-plat are constant, at least two points of energy minimum are found. Classes of non-trivial self-dual solutions of the self-dual field equations are derived. ... .

</details>

# physics.flu-dyn [[Back]](#toc)

### [33] [Rare transitions between collective states in an active fluid via a weakly nonlinear reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09779)
*Yves-Marie Ducimetière,Michael J. Shelley*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究稀悬浮液（dilute suspension）中棒状颗粒在斯托克斯流（Stokes flow）中以恒定速度游动的自组织模型。当平动扩散率降低时，均匀随机取向的二维颗粒浓度场发生余维-2 叉型分岔（pitchfork bifurcation）或余维-4 霍普夫分岔（Hopf bifurcation）。利用弱非线性展开（weakly nonlinear expansion）将系统约化为低维振幅方程，并创新性地纳入时空白噪声（spatio-temporal white noise）随机激励。从约化系统与完整系统的福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation）及自适应多层分裂（Adaptive Multilevel Splitting, AMS）算法中得到的稳态与动力学统计结果高度一致，且约化系统的数值成本显著降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 悬浮颗粒在流体中自组织形成集体运动（collective motion）是活性物质物理的核心问题之一。现有理论多聚焦于确定性动力学，对于随机噪声驱动下的罕见跃迁（rare transitions）及其机制缺乏深入理解。本研究旨在通过引入随机力并与完整系统进行定量对比，检验约化模型预测罕见跃迁统计的可靠性，从而为高效模拟活性悬浊液中的罕见事件提供方法论基础。

Method: 采用弱非线性展开将原始偏微分方程约化为分岔模态振幅的低维常微分方程（amplitude equations），并将时空白噪声解析地映射到振幅方程中的随机项。利用福克-普朗克方程直接计算稳态与动力学统计量，同时应用自适应多层分裂算法（AMS）对约化系统和完整系统分别执行罕见事件模拟，通过比较两者结果验证约化模型的准确性。

Result: 在霍普夫分岔场景下，存在两个共存的稳定周期轨道（stable periodic orbits），各自对应不同的集体动力学；随机激励可驱动系统在这两个轨道之间发生罕见跃迁。基于约化系统计算出的极长平均跃迁时间及相应的非平衡路径，与完整系统的全非线性随机模拟结果在定量上高度一致，且约化系统的计算成本大幅降低。

Conclusion: 低维振幅方程能够准确捕捉完整系统的罕见跃迁统计特性，为研究活性悬浊液中的随机自发有序化提供了高效的理论框架。跃迁路径可借助低维系统的不变流形（invariant manifolds）加以理解，从而揭示跃迁机制的本质。

Abstract: We study a model for a dilute suspension of rod-like particles swimming at constant velocity in a Stokes flow. As the translational diffusivity of the particles decreases, a two-dimensional uniform concentration of randomly aligned particles undergoes either a codimension-2 pitchfork bifurcation or a codimension-4 Hopf bifurcation, depending on the particles' swimming speed. We use a weakly nonlinear expansion to reduce the system to a low-dimensional one for the amplitudes of the bifurcating eigenmodes. The originality of our calculations lies in incorporating spatio-temporal white noise forcing. The stochastic forcing terms in the amplitude equations are derived analytically from the noise acting on the original system. Past the onset of the bifurcations, the particles deterministically self-organize into steady or oscillating states of collective motion. For the Hopf bifurcation scenario, two stable periodic orbits are found to coexist, each corresponding to a distinct collective dynamics. The stochastic forcing induces rare transitions between them. Owing to the low dimensionality of amplitude equations, steady and dynamical statistics can be computed directly from the Fokker-Planck equation, or via the Adaptive Multilevel Splitting (AMS) rare-event algorithm. In particular, extremely long mean transition times and associated out-of-equilibrium paths between the periodic orbits are obtained. These paths can be understood in light of the invariant manifolds of the low-dimensional system, which brings insights into the mechanism behind the transitions. We also performed fully nonlinear stochastic simulations and used the AMS algorithm directly on the full system. The statistics are in good quantitative agreement with those computed on the reduced systems, the latter being obtained at a considerably lower numerical cost.

</details>

### [34] [Lattice Quantization of Free Fermions without Doublers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09199)
*Mario A. Serna,Paul M. Alsing*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在任意维度格点（lattice）上对自由费米子（free fermions）进行量子化（quantize）的方法，通过结合费米子的二阶描述与非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonians）的工具，在 m=0 极限下消除了倍频问题（doublers）。研究识别了二阶费米子方程的新赝厄米对称性（Pseudo-Hermitian symmetry）及其对应的 U(1) 对称性（可在定域规范理论下转化为电荷），并进行了数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 格点场论中，对费米子进行离散化时会出现倍频问题，即一个格点费米子对应多个连续费米子模式，这违背了费米子种类的物理期望。已有方法如Wilson费米子或staggered费米子虽能缓解该问题，但各有局限。本文旨在寻求一种在任意维度、零质量极限下彻底消除倍频问题的替代量子化方案。

Method: 该方法将费米子的二阶描述（second-order description）与非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonians）的形式理论相结合。具体而言，通过分析二阶费米子方程中新的赝厄米对称性（Pseudo-Hermitian symmetry），并识别与此对称性相关联的 U(1) 对称性，实现了对费米子自由度的重新量子化，从而在晶格格点化后避免出现倍频模式。

Result: 该方法在任意空间维度的格点离散化中，于零质量极限（m=0）下成功消除了倍频问题。此外，论文识别了二阶费米子方程中一种新的赝厄米对称性及其对应的 U(1) 对称性（该对称性在引入规范相互作用后将成为电荷）。数值计算结果验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文展示了一种结合二阶费米子方程与非厄米哈密顿量方法的新格点费米子量子化方案，能在无质量极限下消除倍频问题。该方案所揭示的赝厄米对称性与 U(1) 对称性，为进一步将其推广至定域规范理论（local gauge theory）提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We present a method to quantize free fermions which eliminates the doublers when implemented on the lattice in any number of dimensions and in the $m=0$ limit. The elimination of doublers is achieved by combining a second-order description of fermions, with the tools associated with non-Hermitian Hamiltonians. We identify a new Pseudo-Hermitian symmetry of the second-order fermion equation, and we identify the associated $U(1)$ symmetry which will become charge when shifted to a local gauge theory. We validated the methods numerically.

</details>

### [35] [Two-dimensional Clay Channels for Tunable Nanofluidic Memristor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08260)
*Sangeeta Yadav,Raj Kumar Gogoi,Aziz Lokhandwala,Siddhi Vinayak Pandey,Ankit Bhardwaj,Sunando DasGupta,Boya Radha*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了蛭石（vermiculite）纳米流体器件中电荷载流子在电场刺激下的动态重构产生记忆效应，通过调节离子传输路径实现了不同记忆环（memory loops）之间的切换，并在厘米至纳米尺度的通道中验证了忆阻特性，展示了突触可塑性等神经形态功能，为低成本、可扩展的纳米流体忆阻器用于神经形态计算提供了实验依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索受限离子通道（confined ion-channels）中电荷载流子在电场刺激下的动态重构所引发的记忆效应，旨在通过一种简洁、可实验验证的策略，揭示离子忆阻器（ionic memristor）的工作机制，并为其在神经形态计算（neuromorphic computing）中的实际集成提供可行路径。

Method: 利用蛭石纳米流体器件，通过改变电极配置（electrode configurations）而非修改电解质、通道表面化学或器件结构，实现极性依赖的记忆切换；采用重堆叠蛭石膜构建面内（in-plane）和面外（out-of-plane）通道配置，通道长度从厘米到微米尺度；并通过超微切片法（ultramicrotomy method）制备纳米级通道长度的器件进行小型化研究。

Result: 实现了交叉-1（crossing-1）和交叉-2（crossing-2）两种不同记忆环之间的极性依赖切换；在厘米至纳米尺度的通道中均验证了忆阻特性；展示了突触增强-抑制（synaptic potentiation-depression）和可编程记忆保持（programmable memory retention）等神经形态功能。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了通过简单的电极配置变化即可调控离子忆阻器的记忆行为，并验证了蛭石膜忆阻器在多种尺度下的可扩展性和神经形态计算潜力，为低成本、可溶液加工的纳米流体忆阻器在实际神经形态计算系统中的集成奠定了基础。

Abstract: Dynamic reconfiguration of charge carriers in confined ion-channels under electrical stimulation produces memory effects, where the internal resistance depends on history of the electric field. Vermiculite nanofluidic devices harness this effect to store and process information within a single component. We report switching between distinct memory loops by tuning ion transport pathways, governed by asymmetrical device architecture and intrinsic surface-charge. Polarity-dependent memory switching between crossing-1 and crossing-2 loops is achieved solely by altering electrode configurations, without modifying electrolyte, channel surface chemistry or device structure: providing mechanistic insights into ionic memristors through a straightforward, experimentally validated strategy. The memristive characteristics are demonstrated in both in-plane and out-of-plane channel configurations with channel lengths spanning from centimeters to micrometers length scales using re-stacked vermiculite membranes and further investigated for miniaturization with devices having nanometer scale channel lengths, fabricated via ultramicrotomy method. Furthermore, we demonstrate neuromorphic functionalities, including synaptic potentiation-depression and programmable memory retention, highlighting potential for bio-inspired computing systems. Cost-effective and scalable fabrication solution processed vermiculite membrane memristors pave the way for practical integration of nanofluidic memristors for neuromorphic computing applications.

### [36] [SLayerGen: a Crystal Generative Model for all Space and Layer Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08262)
*Rees Chang,Andrew Novick,Ryan P Adams,Elif Ertekin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出SLayerGen，一种面向体相（bulk）和二周期（diperiodic）材料的晶体生成模型，通过结合粗到细的自回归晶格生成、基于Transformer的Wyckoff位置采样以及空间群或层群等变扩散，首次将层群对称性（layer group symmetry）纳入生成过程，并在单层和双层材料数据集上取得了优于现有体相晶体生成模型的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有晶体生成模型主要针对体相周期材料，忽略了二周期材料（如二维超导体、薄膜半导体和催化表面）中起关键作用的层群对称性，而这些对称性对材料性质有重要影响。

Method: SLayerGen包含三个核心组件：粗到细的离散自回归晶格生成；基于Transformer的自回归采样，用于预测Wyckoff位置、元素及对称唯一原子数；以及空间群或层群等变扩散过程，用于生成原子坐标。此外，针对六方群在分数坐标中非正交的问题，修正了前人工作中的损失函数不一致性。

Result: 在从头生成二周期材料任务上，SLayerGen相较于体相晶体生成模型表现出持续的性能提升；在体相与二周期材料联合训练场景下，性能具有竞争力。

Conclusion: SLayerGen首次将层群对称性约束引入晶体生成，填补了二周期材料生成建模的空白；所构建的单层和双层数据集、评估指标及层群对称性表征为该领域的后续研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Crystal generative models have shown rapid progress for accelerating the discovery of bulk, periodic materials. However, many material systems such as 2D superconductors, thin film semiconductors, and catalytic surfaces are diperiodic, i.e., aperiodic along one of the lattice directions. These systems are invariant under the layer groups, which are known to influence materials properties yet not considered by existing models. In this paper, we propose SLayerGen, a generative model that produces crystals constrained to be invariant to any space or layer group. SLayerGen consists of coarse-to-fine discrete autoregressive lattice generation; transformer-based autoregressive sampling of Wyckoff positions, elements, and numbers of symmetrically unique atoms; and space or layer group equivariant diffusion of atomic coordinates. For the diffusion component, we corrected an inconsistency in the loss from prior work arising from hexagonal groups being non-orthogonal in fractional coordinates. To facilitate progress in generative modeling of diperiodic materials, we assembled and filtered datasets of monolayers and bilayers, propose relevant evaluation metrics, and developed novel representations for layer group symmetries. For de novo generation of diperiodic materials, SLayerGen achieves consistent performance gains over bulk crystal generative models and is competitive when training jointly on bulk and diperiodic materials.

</details>


### [37] [Photovoltaic Possibility of Cu2SiSe3 and Cu2SnS3 Ternary Chalcogenides- Single Junction to Tandem Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08312)
*Saptarshi Mandal,Surbhi Ramawat,Sumit Kukreti,Ambesh Dixit*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过漂移扩散模型（drift diffusion modeling）评估了基于三元铜基硫族化合物（ternary chalcogenides）Cu₂SiSe₃ 和 Cu₂SnS₃ 的光伏器件性能。优化后的单结 Cu₂SiSe₃ 器件效率达18.13%，Cu₂SnS₃ 器件效率为15.59%；进一步构建的叠层（tandem）太阳能电池效率可达24.1%，显著超越单结器件，验证了三元硫族化合物在下一代高效太阳能技术中的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三元铜基硫族化合物（ternary chalcogenides）因其相较于四元（quaternary）替代材料具有更低的复杂性，在可持续能源应用中正受到广泛关注。本文旨在评估基于 Cu₂SiSe₃ 和 Cu₂SnS₃ 的三元硫族化合物吸收层用于光伏（photovoltaics）器件的可行性。

Method: 采用漂移扩散模型（drift diffusion modeling）进行器件仿真，通过分析吸收层厚度、本征载流子浓度（intrinsic carrier concentration）、缺陷密度（defect density）以及界面结（interfacial junctions）处的能带对齐（energy band alignment）来评估器件性能指标。

Result: 优化的单结 Cu₂SiSe₃ 器件实现功率转换效率（power conversion efficiency）18.13%，短路电流密度（short circuit current density）38 mA cm⁻²，开路电压（open circuit voltage）0.64 V。Cu₂SnS₃ 器件效率达15.59%，短路电流密度48.8 mA cm⁻²，开路电压0.42 V。两终端叠层（two terminal tandem）太阳能电池（Cu₂SiSe₃ 顶电池 Eg 1.44 eV，Cu₂SnS₃ 底电池 Eg 0.91 eV）实现开路电压1.24 V、短路电流密度24.6 mA cm⁻²、填充因子（fill factor, FF）79.2%、效率24.1%，显著超过传统单结器件。

Conclusion: 研究证实了基于 Cu₂SiSe₃-Cu₂SnS₃ 吸收层的叠层太阳能电池（tandem solar cell）在下一代高效太阳能技术中的可行性，同时缓冲层（buffer layer）对器件参数的影响分析为进一步性能提升提供了新途径。

Abstract: Cu based ternary chalcogenides are gathering attention for sustainable energy applications due to their reduced complexity compared to quaternary alternatives. We used drift diffusion modeling to evaluate the feasibility of photovoltaics employing ternary chalcogenide absorbers based on Cu2SiSe3 and Cu2SnS3. The device metrics are evaluated by analyzing absorber layer thickness intrinsic carrier concentration defect density and energy band alignment at interfacial junctions. The optimized single junction Cu2SiSe3 based device configuration achieves a power conversion efficiency of 18.13 percent exhibiting a short circuit current density of 38 mA cm^-2 and an open circuit voltage of 0.64 V. The Cu2SnS3 based device achieves an efficiency of 15.59 percent with a short circuit current density of 48.8 mA cm^-2 and an open circuit voltage of 0.42 V. We examined the impact of the buffer layer on device parameters uncovering further avenues for performance improvement. Additionally we simulated a two terminal tandem solar cell using Cu2SiSe3 Eg 1.44 eV in the upper cell to capture photons from the visible spectrum and Cu2SnS3 Eg 0.91 eV in the lower cell to absorb from the infrared spectrum. The simulated tandem architecture, featuring a VOC of 1.24 V a JSC of 24.6 mA cm^-2 a fill factor (FF) of 79.2 percent and an efficiency of 24.1 percent markedly surpassed conventional single junction devices demonstrating the viability of Cu2SiSe3-Cu2SnS3 absorber-based tandem solar cells for next generation high-efficiency solar technologies.

Method: 本文采用综述性介绍的方式，首先阐述神经算子的基本概念——作为神经网络的一种离散化无关（discretization-independent）推广；随后通过三个选定的示例，演示其在材料多尺度建模中的具体应用。

Result: 通过三个选定的示例，本文展示了神经算子能够有效应用于材料的多尺度建模，表明其在跨尺度信息传递方面具有潜力。

Conclusion: 神经算子被证明是解决多尺度建模中跨尺度信息传递困难的有力工具，本文提供的介绍和示例为该领域的进一步研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Multiscale modeling is essential for understanding the complex behavior of materials. However, accurately transferring all relevant information from one scale to another has remained an outstanding challenge. Neural operators, discretization-independent generalizations of neural networks, is proving to be a powerful tool in addressing this challenge. This article provides an introduction to neural operators, and illustrates their use in multiscale modeling of materials through three selected examples.

### [39] [Bond strengths in solids computed from a Wannier-type construction of local vibrational modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08948)
*Mateusz Mojsak,Elfi Kraka,Adam A. L. Michalchuk*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Wannier形式的周期性局域振动模式理论（Wannier-type formulation of periodic local vibrational mode theory），通过波矢分辨局域模式的相干叠加构建实空间局域振动模式，无需额外的相位固定步骤，从而在周期体系中实现与分子局域模式直接对应的化学键与相互作用强度分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有局域振动模式（local vibrational mode）理论主要适用于分子体系，在晶体等周期性固体中尚缺乏一种无需复杂相位固定即可获得实空间局域化振动模式的方法，进而难以对周期体系中的化学键和相互作用强度进行直接且具有化学可解释性的定量分析。

Method: 该方法借鉴Wannier函数的思想，将波矢分辨的局域模式（wavevector-resolved local modes）进行局部相干叠加（locally coherent superpositions），构建出与单个内坐标（internal coordinates）相关联的实空间局域振动模式，从而获得平滑且规范一致的实空间表示，无需额外的相位固定过程。

Result: 该方法提供了定义明确的力常数（force constants）和频率（frequencies），可对周期体系中的键强和相互作用强度进行稳健且具有化学可解释性的度量；同时发现声子色散行为（phonon dispersion behavior）对局域振动模式理论计算的键强和相互作用强度有重要贡献。在MgO、四面体配位C、Si、SiC及两种CaCO3多晶型体系中验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 该框架建立了全周期体系与分子局域模式之间的直接类比，为晶体材料中的定量键合分析开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We introduce a Wannier-type formulation of periodic local vibrational mode theory that yields real-space-localized vibrational modes associated with individual internal coordinates in crystalline solids. These modes are constructed as locally coherent superpositions of wavevector-resolved local modes, yielding a smooth and gauge-consistent real-space representation without the need for additional phase-fixing procedures. The resulting Wannier-type local modes provide well-defined force constants and frequencies that enable robust, chemically interpretable measures of bond and interaction strengths in periodic systems. Moreover, our framework demonstrates that phonon dispersion behavior makes important contributions to the bond and interaction strengths calculated via local vibrational mode theory. We demonstrate the method for representative ionic and covalent systems, including MgO, tetrahedrally-coordinated C, Si, SiC, and two polymorphs of CaCO3. Our framework establishes a direct analog of molecular local modes for fully periodic systems and opens new avenues for quantitative bonding analysis in crystalline materials.

</details>


### [40] [CrystalREPA: Transferring Physical Priors from Universal MLIPs to Crystal Generative Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08960)
*Chengqian Zhang,Yucheng Jin,Duo Zhang,Tiejun Li,Han Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出 CrystalREPA，一种即插即用的表征对齐框架，通过在训练时对齐晶体生成模型的隐状态与预训练通用机器学习原子间势（MLIP）的表征，显著提升生成晶体的热力学稳定性、结构有效性和结构保真度，并发现 MLIP 的迁移有效性由其原子级表征空间的可区分性决定，而非其在标准排行榜上的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的晶体生成模型主要学习稳定晶体的外观特征，但缺乏对稳定性背后物理机制的显式监督。作者通过能量探针（energy probing）实验发现，当前最先进的晶体生成模型与预训练的通用机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials, MLIPs）之间存在显著的表征差距（representation gap），亟需一种方法弥合这一差距以提升生成晶体的稳定性。

Method: 提出 CrystalREPA（Crystal REPresentation Alignment）框架，采用即插即用（plug-and-play）方式，通过元素感知的对比学习目标（element-aware contrastive objective）将生成编码器的原子级隐状态（atom-wise hidden states）与冻结的 MLIP 表征进行对齐，从而以极小的训练开销（无额外推理成本）将具有稳定性意识的原子先验知识迁移至生成模型。

Result: 在三种生成框架、十种 MLIP 教师模型以及两个基准数据集上，CrystalREPA 一致提升了生成晶体的热力学稳定性（thermodynamic stability）、结构有效性（structural validity）和结构保真度（structural fidelity）。此外，研究发现 MLIP 的迁移有效性与其在标准排行榜（如 Matbench Discovery）上的精度关联较弱，而与其原子级表征空间的可区分性（distinguishability）高度相关。

Conclusion: CrystalREPA 是一种高效且通用的表征对齐方法，能够有效弥合晶体生成模型与 MLIP 之间的表征差距，显著提升生成质量。该工作还提供了一个实用且与精度无关的 MLIP 教师模型选择标准，即基于原子级表征空间的可区分性进行筛选。

Abstract: Crystal generative models mainly learn what stable crystals look like, with little explicit supervision for what makes them stable. We reveal a substantial representation gap between state-of-the-art crystal generative models and pretrained universal machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) via energy probing, and show this gap can be closed by a simple training-time alignment. We propose Crystal REPresentation Alignment (CrystalREPA), a plug-and-play framework that aligns the atom-wise hidden states of generative encoders with frozen MLIP representations through an element-aware contrastive objective, transferring stability-aware atomistic priors with marginal training overhead and no additional inference cost. Across three generative frameworks, ten MLIP teachers, and two benchmark datasets, CrystalREPA consistently improves the thermodynamic stability, structural validity, and structural fidelity of generated crystals. Equally important, we find that an MLIP's transfer effectiveness is poorly predicted by its accuracy on standard leaderboards (e.g., Matbench Discovery) but strongly predicted by the distinguishability of its atom-wise representation space, yielding a practical, accuracy-independent criterion for selecting MLIP teachers for generative transfer.

</details>

Abstract: We used angle-resolved Brillouin-Mandelstam light-scattering spectroscopy to monitor surface and bulk acoustic phonons in diamond along the <100> and <110> crystallographic directions across a temperature range from 10 K to 300 K. The frequencies and phase velocities were measured for three types of surface acoustic phonons: Rayleigh waves, shear horizontal waves, and high-frequency pseudo-longitudinal waves. All surface acoustic phonons exhibit weak temperature dependence, with the largest observed change of 1.6% across the examined temperature range.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Diamond and gallium nitride are complementary semiconductors for forming p-n junctions because of their respective doping limitations. Understanding the band alignment of grafted diamond/GaN heterojunctions is therefore essential for optimizing diode performance. In this study, the band alignment of diamond/Al2O3/GaN and diamond/Al2O3/SiNx/GaN heterostructures was determined by X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy. These results demonstrate that interfacial-layer engineering provides an effective strategy for tailoring the band alignment of grafted diamond/GaN heterojunctions, offering guidance for the design of p-n diodes with tunable rectifying characteristics.

### [43] [Universal 3:1 Scaling of Quantum-Confined Stark Spectra Revealed by a Three-Dimensional Profile](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09263)
*Sha Han,Kebei Chen,Runnan Zhang,Juemin Yi,Wentao Song,Ke Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发现量子限制斯塔克效应（quantum-confined Stark effect）光谱在电场强度增加时呈现近乎刚性的红移（rigid redshift），同时保持其特征峰间距模式不变。以InGaN为模型系统，揭示了带隙下和带隙上两个区域中与电场无关的标度律（scaling laws），其系数比接近3:1。通过三维可视化，发现该比值源于有效质量和量子阱宽度（well width）决定的标度关系，并在InGaN和GaAs系统中以及电致发光工作条件下得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子限制斯塔克效应是电光器件（electro-optic devices）的核心机制之一，但其光谱在电场变化下的行为规律尚缺乏系统的定量理解。本文旨在揭示电场强度F增加时光谱峰间距是否保持恒定，并建立其背后的普适标度律。

Method: 以InGaN作为模型系统，通过实验测量不同电场强度下的量子限制斯塔克效应光谱；提出一种新颖的三维可视化方法，将光谱数据在能量-电场-强度三维空间中呈现，从而提取峰间距的标度行为；并在InGaN和GaAs两种材料系统以及电致发光条件下进行交叉验证。

Result: 发现了两个与电场无关的标度律：带隙下（sub-bandgap）峰间距标度为$\frac{12π\hbar^2}{L^2\sqrt{m_em_h}}$，带隙上（above-bandgap）峰间距标度为$\frac{4π\hbar^2}{L^2\sqrt{m_em_h}}$，比值恰好为3:1。增加电场F仅扩展能量范围并增加峰数，而不改变峰间距。该行为在InGaN和GaAs系统中均成立。

Conclusion: 三维可视化方法不仅揭示了峰间距的3:1比值来源于量子阱宽度L和有效质量（effective mass）决定的物理机制，还为理解Tauc背景（Tauc background）、Franz-Keldysh振荡（Franz-Keldysh oscillations）和相干长度（coherence length）提供了新视角，为电光器件的设计与诊断提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We report that the quantum-confined Stark effect spectrum exhibits a nearly rigid redshift while preserving its characteristic peak spacing patterns when increasing the electric field strength F. Using InGaN as a model system, we uncover two electric-field-independent scaling laws for the spectral peaks in both the sub-bandgap and above-bandgap regions and the coefficient ratio is near 3:1. With a novel three-dimensional (3D) visualization, we reveal that the sub-bandgap peak spacings scale as $\frac{12π\hbar^2}{L^2\sqrt{m_em_h}}$ while the above-bandgap peak spacings scale as $\frac{4π\hbar^2}{L^2\sqrt{m_em_h}}$, explaining the origin of the 3:1 ratio. This scaling behavior, validated in both InGaN and GaAs systems and at electroluminescence working conditions, shows that increasing F only expands the energy range and increases the number of peaks without altering the spacing. Beyond these laws, the 3D profile offers new insights into the Tauc background, Franz-Keldysh oscillations and coherence length, providing a powerful tool for the design and diagnostics of electro-optic devices.

### [44] [First-Principles Study of the Temperature Dependence of Structural, Electronic, and Hyperfine Properties of the Cu(100) Surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09327)
