To this end, we perform here a comprehensive $\it{ab}$ $\it{initio}$ study of the Cu(100) surface reconstruction and its associated structural, electronic, and hyperfine properties as a function of temperature, not only at the outermost atomic layer (i.e., the topmost Cu atom) but also as a function of atomic depth relative to the reconstructed surface. To study the temperature dependence of the EFG, we use experimentally determined temperature-dependent lattice parameters for bulk copper in our calculations. The anisotropic relaxation that arises when bulk symmetry is broken helps unravel the potential sources of EFG temperature dependence at the surface. Studying the electron density of conduction electrons $ρ$($\bf{r}$) at the atomic scale near the Cu nucleus and the atom-resolved partial density of states at the topmost Cu atom allows us to correlate the surface effect on the EFG with the bulk value.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Olivine is the dominant mineral in Earth's upper mantle and therefore controls mantle rheology and the mechanics of plate tectonics. The constitutive laws for dislocation-mediated deformation of olivine depend on the nature, density, and arrangements of dislocations within crystals. Hence, imaging and characterizing these defects is important, albeit challenging. Traditional imaging approaches involve (1) transmission electron microscopy (TEM), which samples small areas and requires extensive preparation and (2) oxidation decoration methods that have low spatial resolution and cannot distinguish dislocations of opposite Burgers vectors. Here, we apply electron channeling contrast imaging (ECCI) to unlock insight into the deformation structures within olivine, and combined with electron backscatter diffraction (EBSD) and weighted Burgers vector (WBV) mapping as an informative route to characterize dislocation substructures in bulk materials. Specifically, we have used an ECCI workflow based on selected-area electron channeling patterns (SA-ECPs) and we apply this workflow to a single crystal of San Carlos olivine that was deformed by creep at high temperature. ECCI micrographs reveal subgrain boundaries, surface threading dislocations, and dislocation loops across representative areas. The observations demonstrate that this workflow can reliably reveal the complexity of subgrain boundaries in olivine, which can host multiple dislocation types and exhibit non-planar geometries. Despite the limited number of slip systems in olivine, subgrain boundaries can form complex, mixed assemblies. Overall, such observations can provide a variety of constraints on dislocation types, morphologies, and distributions, which are required to parameterize and calibrate models of transient and steady-state dislocation creep in olivine and other materials.

Motivation: 范德华层状材料（van der Waals layered materials）中普遍存在堆叠多态性（stacking polymorphism），该现象可显著改变材料的物理性质，但堆叠序列对热电性能的影响尚缺乏系统理解。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）结合电子输运理论（electron transport theory）和声子输运理论（phonon transport theory），对Sc₂Si₂Te₆的AA、AB、ABC三种高对称堆叠序列进行系统性计算分析。

Result: AA和AB堆叠结构与实验报道的ABC相能量近似简并（nearly degenerate），最大滑移势垒（sliding barrier）仅约10 meV/atom。三种堆叠的导带底（conduction-band minimum）高度敏感于堆叠序列，导致ABC、AA、AB的导带简并度（conduction-band degeneracy）分别为12、2和8。晶格热导率（lattice thermal conductivity）主要受三声子散射（three-phonon scattering）控制，四声子散射（four-phonon scattering）在ABC堆叠中提供额外降低。AB堆叠因更强的三声子散射和更低的声子群速度（phonon group velocity）展现出最低的晶格热导率。ABC结构取得最高热电优值ZT，AB结构紧随其后，AA结构显著降低。

Conclusion: 堆叠序列对Sc₂Si₂Te₆的热电性能具有不可忽视的影响，抑制AA堆叠的形成对于实现高热电性能至关重要。

Abstract: Stacking polymorphism is a common characteristic of van der Waals layered materials and can substantially modify their physical properties. Here, based on first-principles calculations combined with electron and phonon transport theories, we systematically investigate the thermodynamic stability, electronic structure, lattice dynamics, and thermoelectric performance of Sc_2Si_2Te_6 with three high-symmetry stacking sequences, namely, AA, AB, and ABC. We find that the AA- and AB-stacked structures are nearly degenerate in energy with the experimentally reported ABC phase, and that the maximum sliding barrier among these stacking sequences is only about 10~meV/atom, thereby accounting for the stacking faults observed experimentally. These three stacking sequences exhibit distinct electronic structures, with the conduction-band minimum being highly sensitive to the stacking sequence. As a consequence, the conduction-band degeneracies are 12, 2, and 8 for the ABC, AA, and AB stackings, respectively, leading to markedly different electronic transport properties near the band edge. The lattice thermal conductivity is governed primarily by three-phonon scattering, whereas four-phonon scattering provides an additional reduction, particularly in the ABC stacking. Among the three structures, the AB stacking exhibits the lowest lattice thermal conductivity owing to its stronger three-phonon scattering and lower phonon group velocity. As a result, the maximum thermoelectric figure of merit, ZT, is achieved in the ABC structure, followed closely by the AB structure, whereas the AA structure shows a substantially reduced value. These results demonstrate that the stacking sequence exerts a non-negligible influence on the thermoelectric performance of Sc_2Si_2Te_6 and suggest that suppressing the formation of the AA stacking is important for achieving high thermoelectric performance.

</details>


### [47] [Molecular Nitrogen Formation in Nitrogen-Implanted (100) $β-Ga_2O_3$ Revealed by Temperature-Dependent $N$ $K$-edge XANES](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09578)
*I. N. Demchenko,Y. Syryanyy,A. Shokri,Y. Melikhov,M. Chernyshova,M. Turek,A. Droździel,F. Munnik,R. Jakieła,R. Minikayev,J. Z. Domagala,A. Derkachova,M. Zając,J. Krajczewski,E. Grzanka,Z. Galazka*

Motivation: 宽禁带氧化物半导体（wide-band-gap oxide semiconductors）中p型掺杂的实现一直是一大难题；在β-Ga₂O₃中，氮虽长期被视为潜在受主掺杂剂（acceptor dopant），但始终未能获得空穴导电（hole conductivity），其微观原因尚不明确。

Method: 采用温度依赖性氮K边X射线吸收谱（temperature-dependent N K-edge x-ray absorption spectroscopy）对(100) β-Ga₂O₃中注入氮的微观构型进行表征，并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与多重散射模拟（multiple-scattering simulations）对光谱特征进行解析。

Result: 光谱显示存在显著的分子氮π*共振特征，且该特征在热退火后进一步增强；计算与模拟表明，氮原子在Ga₂O₃基体中倾向于形成N-N键合构型，尤其在离子注入产生的富缺陷环境中；结构分析还显示，注入导致近表面层出现局域β-γ类结构基元，呈现强非平衡结构环境。

Conclusion: 注入的氮优先形成分子N₂类构型而非替代位受主，这从微观上解释了β-Ga₂O₃中氮受主掺杂长期失败的原因，并揭示了“掺杂剂分子化（dopant molecularization）”这一在强非平衡注入条件下杂质掺入的新机制。

Abstract: The realization of $p$-type doping in wide-band-gap oxide semiconductors remains a major challenge, particularly in $β-Ga_2O_3$ where nitrogen has long been considered a potential acceptor dopant but has consistently failed to produce hole conductivity. Here we investigate the microscopic configuration of implanted nitrogen in (100) $β-Ga_2O_3$ using temperature-dependent $N$ $K$-edge x-ray absorption spectroscopy. The spectra reveal a pronounced $π^*$ resonance characteristic of molecular nitrogen, which becomes increasingly dominant upon thermal annealing. First-principles calculations and multiple-scattering simulations reveal a pronounced tendency for nitrogen atoms to form $N-N$ bonded configurations in the $Ga_2O_3$ matrix, particularly in defect-rich environments created by ion implantation, reproducing the characteristic spectral features observed in the $N$ $K$-edge XANES spectra. Structural analysis further indicates that implantation induces a defect-rich near-surface layer with local $β$-to-$γ$-like structural motifs, highlighting the strongly nonequilibrium structural environment in which nitrogen incorporation occurs. Reported results show that implanted nitrogen preferentially forms molecular $N_2$-like configurations rather than substitutional acceptors. Our results provide a microscopic explanation for the long-standing failure of nitrogen acceptor doping in $β-Ga_2O_3$ and reveal dopant molecularization as a previously overlooked pathway for impurity incorporation under strongly nonequilibrium implantation conditions.

Abstract: Chalcogen-terminated van der Waals MXenes (M2CX2; M = Nb, Ta; X = S, Se) provide a robust platform for exploring strong spin-orbit coupling and proximity engineering.   First-principles calculations reveal Rashba splitting up to 2.53 eV A and valley-contrasting spin polarization in monolayers. These features drive strong second-order nonlinear responses, with pristine bilayer Ta2CS2 reaching a shift current of |sigma|_max approx 5 A mA/V^2 and Nb2CS2/CrBr3 attaining |D|_max approx 18.44 A. In M2CS2/CrBr3 heterostructures, the ferromagnetic substrate induces a magnetization-reversible proximity exchange field with valley-selective conduction-band renormalization (Delta_val approx 50 meV).   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Momentum-resolved spin textures and potential valley-contrasting physical properties in the momentum space are two intriguing characteristics of noncentrosymmetric materials, and they have broad applications in spintronics and valleytronics. The realization of diverse spin textures within a single material, along with their further coupling to the valley degree of freedom, is highly desirable. Via first-principles calculations, we investigate electronic properties of Janus MP$_2$S$_3$Se$_3$ monolayers, which exhibits distinct spin textures at different valleys. While Ising-type spin textures are located at $K_\pm$ valleys, the symmetry breaking from the Janus structure brings about a coexistence of Weyl-type and Rashba-type spin textures at $Γ$ valley. In addition to valley-contrasting spin textures, valley dependence also occurs in Berry-curvature-driven anomalous Hall currents and optical selectivity. Besides, energy differences between $Γ$ and $K_\pm$, as well as band gaps, are highly tunable by applied strain. These findings present an intriguing coupling between diverse spin textures and multiple valleys, and pave the way for designing advanced electronic devices that leverage spin and valley degrees of freedom.

Method: 讨论了三种代表性体系：含过渡族金属的坎托尔型（Cantor-type）合金（Cr, Mn, Fe, Ni, Co）、难熔高熵合金（refractory high-entropy alloy）（Ti, Zr, Nb, Ta, Mo）以及结合过渡与难熔金属的多组元体系（Cu, Ni, Ti, Zr, Hf）。采用理论分析（theoretical analysis）与实验观测（experimental observations）相结合的方法。

Abstract: Even if the atoms of a multicomponent alloy occupy a common lattice, their distribution is not homogeneous, and regions with different compositions can be detected. Three representative examples will be discussed: a Cantor-type system containing transition-metal elements (Cr, Mn, Fe, Ni, and Co), a refractory high-entropy alloy (Ti, Zr, Nb, Ta, and Mo), and a multicomponent system combining transition and refractory metals (Cu, Ni, Ti, Zr, and Hf). Using a combination of theoretical analysis and experimental observations, we demonstrate that the formation of locally segregated regions can lead to a reduction in the overall energy of the system. This stabilization arises from the compensation of tensile and compressive strain fields associated with atoms of different sizes, highlighting the key role of local chemical and structural heterogeneity in determining the thermodynamic stability of multicomponent alloys.

### [53] [Parabolic-growth universality and its nucleation-driven breakdown across lithium-battery anode chemistries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10217)
*Changdeuck Bae*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SEI生长模型多为逐电池（cell-by-cell）的化学特异性封闭模型，但不同化学体系之间潜在的动力学标度（kinetic scaling）规律缺乏跨化学体系的系统检验。

Method: 汇编来自公开长循环数据集的循环解析数据，覆盖石墨（graphite）、硅复合材料（silicon composite）、锂金属（lithium metal）和无负极（anode-free）四种构型；引入累积界面损耗指数Λ_int，验证其与有效锂可用度(1 - Θ_Li)的标度关系。

Result: 三种构型中Λ_int与(1 - Θ_Li)呈抛物线关系，指数α=1/2，化学特异性前置因子A_chem跨越一个数量级；无负极构型偏离抛物线，指数α≈0.77，呈超抛物线行为。

Conclusion: SEI生长在多种化学体系中遵循扩散限制抛物线动力学，可将建模复杂度简化为每种化学体系单一速率常数；该规律为下一代电池构型提供了可证伪的检验标准。

Abstract: Solid-electrolyte interphase (SEI) growth is widely modeled cell-by-cell with chemistry-specific closures, yet its underlying kinetic scaling is rarely tested across chemistries. By compiling cycle-resolved data from public long-cycle datasets covering four anode configurations -- graphite, silicon composite, lithium metal, and anode-free -- we show that the cumulative interphase-loss index Lambda_int obeys the parabolic law Lambda_int = A_chem * sqrt(1 - Theta_Li) in three of the four chemistries, with an exponent indistinguishable from alpha = 1/2 within experimental uncertainty. The chemistry-specific prefactor A_chem spans an order of magnitude, but the diffusion-limited parabolic kinetics is preserved. The fourth chemistry, anode-free configurations, deviates with a super-parabolic exponent alpha approx 0.77, consistent with a nucleation-controlled growth regime. We rationalize the result using the Tammann-Deal-Grove parabolic-growth framework adapted to interphase formation and identify the conditions under which universality is recovered. The observed regularity reduces SEI modeling complexity to a single rate constant per chemistry and provides a sharp falsifiable test for next-generation cell formats.

### [54] [Saddle-node bifurcation in interfacial morphology selects battery degradation phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10252)
*Changdeuck Bae*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一个最小非线性闭包常微分方程（ODE），用于描述电池界面的动态活性面积因子。该方程在光滑速率随表面粗糙度饱和时表现出鞍结分岔（saddle-node bifurcation），并将四种典型阳极构型映射到该框架中。无阳极（anode-free） Li/Cu 构型仅距分岔阈值 5%，预测其运行稳定性窗口极小。三种可证伪预测与公开数据基本一致，并指出该近临界位置是成核控制沉积在非钝化衬底上的普适特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为电池界面动态活性面积因子建立一个物理上最简的非线性闭包模型，揭示其在不稳定相变前的临界行为，并解释无阳极锂金属电池稳定性极差的根本原因。

Method: 在近期单固定点闭包基础上提出最小非线性拓展 ODE：u̇ = K − u/(1 + αu²)，其中 u 为无量纲过剩活性面积，K 为无量纲驱动力，α 为饱和参数。通过解析求解鞍结分岔条件 K_c = 1/(2√α)，并将石墨、硅复合、锂金属、无阳极 Li/Cu 四种构型的循环末端稳态数据映射到该闭包，定量计算各构型的 K/K_c 比值。

Result: 四种阳极构型的 K/K_c 比值呈单调递增：石墨约 0.01，硅复合约 0.24，锂金属约 0.73，无阳极约 0.95。无阳极构型距鞍结分岔阈值仅 5%，预测其运行稳定性窗口极为狭窄。框架的三项可证伪预测（临界电流密度、临界温度位移、平均场临界慢化指数）与公开数据基本一致。

Conclusion: 无阳极构型处于近临界位置是成核控制沉积在非钝化衬底上的普适特征，该框架可解释其极小的稳定性窗口，并有望指导电池界面设计。

Abstract: We propose a minimal nonlinear closure ODE for the dynamic active-area factor of a battery interface and show that it exhibits a saddle-node bifurcation when the smoothing rate saturates with surface roughness. The closure is the simplest physically motivated extension of a recently introduced single-fixed-point closure [C. Bae, in preparation (2026)]: u = K - u/(1 + alphau^2), where u = xi - 1 is the dimensionless excess active area, K the dimensionless drive, and alpha a single saturation parameter. The bifurcation occurs at K_c = 1/(2sqrt(alpha)), separating a smooth passivating phase from a morphologically unstable phase. Mapping four canonical anode configurations -- graphite, silicon composite, lithium metal, and anode-free Li/Cu -- onto the closure via end-of-cycling steady-state xi extracted from publicly available long-cycle data populates the stable branch with monotonically increasing K/K_c ratios: graphite (~0.01), silicon composite (~0.24), lithium metal (~0.73), and anode-free (~0.95). The anode-free configuration sits within 5% of the saddle-node threshold, predicting a vanishingly small operational stability window in current density, temperature, and electrolyte composition. We test three falsifiable predictions of the framework -- a critical current density, a critical temperature shift, and a mean-field critical-slowing-down exponent -- and find them broadly consistent with publicly available data. We argue that this near-critical position is universal to nucleation-controlled deposition on non-passivating substrates.

Result: 弯曲区域内的量子发射器表现出显著增强的室温光谱纯度：德拜-沃勒因子（Debye-Waller factor）达到0.91，线宽窄于平坦区域内的发射器。光子相关测量证实了室温下的高纯度单光子发射。

Conclusion: 应变工程（strain engineering）是hBN中实现声子控制的有效途径，为在集成纳米光子平台上实现高相干性、室温工作的量子光源开辟了道路。

Abstract: Hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) hosts robust room-temperature single-photon emitters, yet their coherence is typically limited by phonon induced dephasing and spectral broadening. Here, we show that thermally induced curvature in bulk like hBN flakes provides a strain enabled route to suppress defect phonon coupling under ambient conditions. Nanoscale bubbles formed by thermal processing generate strong through thickness strain gradients, which we directly probe by infrared nano spectroscopy. These measurements reveal strain induced splitting of in-plane phonon modes, evidencing a substantial local modification of the phonon density of states. Quantum emitters localized within these curved regions exhibit markedly enhanced room temperature spectral purity, with Debye Waller factors of 0.91 and narrower line widths than emitters in flat regions. Photon correlation measurements confirm high-purity single photon emission at room temperature. Supported by first-principles calculations, we attribute this behavior to strain driven phonon redistribution, which depletes phonons in tensile regions and accumulates them in compressive regions, thereby creating locally phonon suppressed environments for defect emitters. These results establish strain engineering as an effective route for phonon control in hBN and open a pathway toward high coherence, room-temperature quantum light sources for integrated nano photonic platforms.

Those variables typically take the form of fields defined everywhere in space or macroscopic quantities when spatial inhomogeneities can be treated implicitly. The free energy is usually expressed as a Landau-like potential whose temperature-dependent minima track stable states, characteristic equilibrium fluctuations being implicitly accounted for. Further, the response of the system to external perturbations, and its relaxation toward thermal equilibrium, are described in terms of simple equations of motion governed by effective inertial and viscous-damping constants. There is considerable literature on the problem of deriving Landau free energy potentials, from either experiment or predictive atomistic simulations, including recent efforts to develop systematic machine-learning approaches that we denote ``third principles''. Much less attention has received the calculation of the effective constants controlling the nonequilibrium macroscopic or mesoscopic dynamics. Here we tackle that problem, describing a protocol that allows us to compute the temperature-dependent inertial and damping coefficients associated to the electric polarization in representative soft-mode ferroelectric PbTiO$_{3}$. Our scheme lends itself to a widespread application, although the non-trivial behaviors found in PbTiO$_{3}$ suggest that more case studies will be needed to finetune a general and robust calculation protocol. Abstract: Magnetic MAX phases are nanolaminated metals that combine ceramic-like thermal and mechanical stability with peculiar magnetic ordering, making them attractive for thin-film optoelectronics and spintronics. Here, we investigate laser-induced ultrafast demagnetization in a 40-nm-thick epitaxial film of the magnetic MAX phase (Cr0.5Mn0.5)2GaC, which magnetically orders below ~250 K, using time-resolved magneto-optical Kerr effect spectroscopy. The reconstructed spin heat capacity exhibits a weak temperature dependence, accounting for the absence of significant slowing down of demagnetization at elevated temperatures and fluences. Motivation: 位错环的几何构型在微观尺度上的变化如何影响其热力学性质与动力学行为，这一问题在文献中鲜有关注。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 首先，基于原子模拟数据训练机器学习（machine learning, ML）模型，预测任意几何复杂构型的自间隙原子位错环的形成能。其次，从ML模型评估构型微观态密度作为形成能的函数，并在可解的极限情形下推导解析表达式。利用统计力学（statistical mechanics）推导构型自由能、平均能量和热力学熵随温度的函数关系。最后，模拟不同几何构型位错环的自攀移（self-climb）动力学，计算扩散系数和有效激活能。

Result: ML模型在广泛构型范围内预测精度高，典型误差在1%范围内。分析表明，存在一个单一普适参数描述基态下位错环构型的形态不规则性（morphological irregularity），该参数同时决定了位错环的热力学性质和动力学行为。

Conclusion: 构型复杂位错环的性质和迁移率可统一由该不规则性参数描述，模拟结果展示了其随该参数变化的规律。

Abstract: We explore how the thermodynamic properties and dynamics of a self-interstitial prismatic dislocation loop are affected by microscopic-scale variations in its geometric configuration, an aspect that rarely received attention in literature. First, we develop a machine-learning (ML) model to predict the formation energy of an arbitrary geometrically complex configuration of a self-interstitial atom dislocation loop. Trained on atomistic simulation data, the ML model achieves high predictive accuracy across a broad range of configurations, with a typical error in the 1% range. Second, from the ML model, we evaluate the density of configurational microstates as a function of loop's formation energy and derive analytical expressions valid in tractable limiting cases. Using statistical mechanics, we derive the configurational free energy, the average energy, and the thermodynamic entropy of a dislocation loop as a function of temperature. Third, we simulate the dynamics of self-climb of dislocation loops with various geometries and evaluate their diffusion coefficients and effective activation energies. Our analysis shows that there is a single universal parameter describing the morphological irregularity of loop configurations in its ground state. This parameter determines the thermodynamic properties of a loop as well as its dynamics, and simulations illustrate how the properties and mobility of a configurationally complex loop vary as functions of the irregularity parameter.

</details>


### [61] [Oxygen vacancies beyond the dilute limit in doped CaMnO3 perovskites and implications for screening materials in thermochemical applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10636)
*Harender S. Dhattarwal,Colin M. Hylton-Farrington,Ian G. McKendry,Christopher Abram,Richard C. Remsing*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文指出以单氧空位形成能（OVFE）作为唯一描述符筛选钙钛矿热化学储能（TCES）材料存在根本性缺陷，因为化学计量比并非最低能量参考态。作者通过第一性原理计算建立依赖空位浓度的OVFE曲线，以平衡空位浓度为参考点，并揭示A位和B位掺杂的不同机制，最终构建包含构型熵的热力学模型，为钙钛矿TCES材料的筛选提供了超越单空位范式的新框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高通量筛选方法以单氧空位形成能（single OVFE）作为关键描述符，但该方法未考虑实际工作温度下空位固有的存在性，导致具有负单OVFE的材料被错误排除，从而可能遗漏有前景的TCES候选材料。本文旨在纠正这一参考态选择错误，建立更准确的筛选框架。

Method: 采用基于第一性原理密度泛函理论（ab initio density functional theory）计算氧空位形成能（OVFE）与空位浓度的依赖关系，确立平衡空位浓度作为正确的参考点。通过A位和B位掺杂分析空位形成景观的变化机制，并发展了一个包含构型熵（configurational entropy）的热力学模型，用于预测平衡氧化学计量比与温度和氧分压的函数关系。

Result: 以平衡空位浓度为参考的OVFE曲线与实验测量的还原焓（reduction enthalpy）一致，建立了可直接与实验对比的计算框架。A位掺杂主要通过应变弛豫（strain relaxation）和对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）影响空位形成，而B位掺杂则重塑局域氧化还原环境（redox environment）并引入强构型依赖性。热力学模型可准确预测温度和氧分压依赖的平衡氧化学计量比，并揭示Mn4+与B位掺杂离子的选择性还原可调控空位形成的起始温度。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了钙钛矿TCES材料的筛选框架，证明单OVFE作为描述符具有根本性不足；以平衡空位浓度为参考的OVFE曲线和包含构型熵的热力学模型提供了可直接与实验比较的方法，并为将高通量筛选工作流扩展到单空位范式之外提供了实用指导。

Abstract: Thermochemical energy storage (TCES) in oxide perovskites relies on reversible oxygen vacancy formation, and computational high-throughput screening of candidate materials has predominantly used the single oxygen vacancy formation energy (OVFE) as the key descriptor. We demonstrate that the OVFE is insufficient for screening cubic CaMnO3 perovskites, because the stoichiometric compound is not the minimum energy reference state; vacancies are inherently present at operating temperatures. Materials with negative single OVFEs are routinely excluded from screening datasets as unsuitable, but this reflects a mischoice of reference state rather than a genuine materials limitation, and risks discarding promising TCES candidates. We address this by computing OVFEs as a function of vacancy concentration using ab initio density functional theory, establishing the equilibrium vacancy concentration as the correct reference point. OVFE curves referenced to this minimum align with experimentally measured reduction enthalpies, providing a framework directly comparable to experiments. We further show that A-site and B-site doping modify the vacancy formation landscape through distinct mechanisms. A-site dopants act primarily through strain relaxation and symmetry breaking, while B-site dopants reshape the local redox environment and introduce strong configurational dependence. Finally, we develop a thermodynamic model incorporating configurational entropy that accurately predicts equilibrium oxygen stoichiometry as a function of temperature and oxygen partial pressure and reveals that selective reduction of Mn4+ versus B-site dopant ions can tune the onset temperature for vacancy formation. These results establish a screening framework for perovskite TCES materials and provide practical guidance for extending high-throughput workflows beyond the single-vacancy paradigm.

</details>


### [62] [Micro-environment of the Eu interstitial in $β$-SiAlON:Eu$^{2+}$ green phosphor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10665)
*Julien Bouquiaux,Samuel Poncé,Yongchao Jia,Masayoshi Mikami,Xavier Gonze*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理ΔSCF激发态方法、大超胞嵌入原子间力常数和Huang-Rhys理论，阐明了商用绿色荧光粉β-Si₆₋zAl_zO_zN₈₋z:Eu²⁺中Eu²⁺激活剂的精确原子尺度结构，证实了Eu-N₉配位模型，并解释了随Al/O浓度z增加时实验观测到的发射红移现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 商用绿色荧光粉β-Si₆₋zAl_zO_zN₈₋z:Eu²⁺中Eu²⁺激活剂周围的精确原子尺度结构一直难以确定，该结构对理解发光机制至关重要。

Method: 采用第一性原理ΔSCF激发态方法、嵌入3150~3501原子超胞的原子间力常数（interatomic force constants）、Huang-Rhys理论以及蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）探索，对涵盖不同Al/O浓度z的代表性低能结构模型进行分析。

Result: 低z最低能结构计算的光致发光谱与6 K下实验振动峰在峰位和强度上高度吻合，验证了Al、O和Eu共面受限的Eu-N₉配位模型。电子-声子耦合弱（S≈2.15），且不同Al/O排布下声子特征稳健，解释了实验上随z增加仍保持分辨的声子副本现象。随z增加零声子线（zero-phonon line）能量系统降低、Huang-Rhys因子适度增大以及构型多样性增加，共同解释了实验观测到的发射红移。

Conclusion: 研究确立了硅铝氧氮荧光粉中Eu²⁺的精确局域结构，揭示了弱电子-声子耦合和稳健声子特征是保持分辨声子副本的关键，并阐明了组分升高导致发射红移的结构与光谱机制。

Abstract: The precise atomic-scale structure around Eu$^{2+}$ activators in the $β$-Si$_{6-z}$Al$_z$O$_z$N$_{8-z}$:Eu$^{2+}$ commercial green phosphor remains elusive. We use the first-principles $Δ$SCF excited-state method, embedding of the interatomic force constants for supercells up to 3501 atoms, and Huang-Rhys theory to clarify this issue. Monte Carlo exploration is used to identify representative low-energy structural models spanning different levels of Al/O concentration $z$. For the lowest-energy structure at low $z$, our computed photoluminescence spectrum reproduces the experimental vibronic peaks at 6~K with excellent agreement in peak positions and intensities, validating the Eu-N$_9$ coordination model with Al, O, and Eu confined to the same crystallographic plane. Analysis of the low-energy structures reveals that the electron-phonon coupling is weak ($S \approx 2.15$) with a robust characteristic phonon signature across different Al/O arrangements, explaining the surprising persistence of resolved phonon replicas with increasing $z$. We explain the experimentally observed red-shift of emission with increasing $z$ through systematic trends in zero-phonon line energies, modest increases in Huang-Rhys factors, and larger configurational diversity at higher compositions.

</details>


### [63] [Optical selection rules in hexagonal Ge polytypes and their lifting by symmetry perturbation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10709)
*Martin Keller,Haichen Wang,Friedhelm Bechstedt,Jürgen Furthmüller,Silvana Botti*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，系统研究了六方锗（hexagonal germanium）多型体（2H、4H、6H-Ge）的光学性质，发现4H-Ge因能带边宇称匹配导致光学跃迁为宇称禁戒（parity-forbidden），其辐射寿命比2H-和6H-Ge长七个数量级；通过Si替代引入对称性扰动可打破该选择定则，将光学矩阵元提升两个数量级并显著缩短辐射寿命。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 六方锗多型体是用于硅基集成光电子学的有前景的直接带隙半导体（direct-gap semiconductor），但除2H相外，其它多型体的光学性质尚未被充分探索。

Method: 基于第一性原理（ab initio）计算，包括准粒子能带结构（quasiparticle band structure）、偶极跃迁矩阵元（dipole transition matrix element）以及求解贝特-萨尔皮特方程（Bethe-Salpeter equation）。通过Si原子替代引入可控的对称性扰动（symmetry perturbation）来打破晶体对称性。

Result: 三种多型体均具有直接带隙（direct band gap），带隙尺寸从2H到6H递增；4H-Ge的基态光学跃迁为宇称禁戒，辐射寿命比2H-和6H-Ge长七个数量级；Si替代扰动可将光学矩阵元提升两个数量级，并缩短所有受扰多型体的辐射寿命；计算了包括激子效应（excitonic effect）在内的吸收系数和频率依赖介电张量（dielectric tensor），覆盖能量范围至5 eV。

Conclusion: 4H-Ge因其宇称禁戒跃迁而严重限制发光能力；通过Si替代引入对称性扰动可有效解除该选择定则，为六方锗多型体在光电子学中的应用提供了理论依据和调控策略。

Abstract: Hexagonal germanium polytypes have emerged as promising direct-gap semiconductors for silicon-integrated optoelectronics, yet their optical properties remain largely unexplored beyond the well-studied 2H phase. We present a comprehensive theoretical study of optical properties of hexagonal 2H-, 4H-, and 6H-Ge polytypes through ab initio calculations of quasiparticle band structures, dipole transition matrix elements, and solution of the Bethe-Salpeter equation. While all three polytypes exhibit direct band gaps of increasing size from 2H to 6H, we reveal that the fundamental optical transition in 4H-Ge is parity-forbidden due to matching band parities at the valence and conduction band edges. This selection rule results in a radiative lifetime seven orders of magnitude longer than in 2H- and 6H-Ge, severely limiting light emission capabilities. To demonstrate that the selection rule can be lifted, we introduce controlled symmetry perturbations by substituting single Ge atoms with Si in each unit cell, breaking the crystal symmetry. This perturbation increases the optical matrix elements by up to two orders of magnitude and reduces radiative lifetimes for all perturbed polytypes. We also compute absorption coefficients and frequency-dependent dielectric tensors for both light polarizations, including excitonic effects up to 5 eV, providing complete optical characterization of ideal and symmetry-perturbed hexagonal Ge systems relevant for optoelectronic applications.

</details>

### [64] [Gravitational-wave standard sirens and application in cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08595)
*Wen Zhao,Liang-Gui Zhu,Youjun Lu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文综述了利用引力波（gravitational wave）标准汽笛（standard siren）约束宇宙学参数的基本原理与方法，重点讨论了中子星并合作为亮汽笛（bright siren）和恒星级黑洞并合作为暗汽笛（dark siren）两种途径，以及第二代、第三代地面探测器和空间探测器在测量哈勃常数（Hubble constant）和暗能量参数（dark energy parameters）方面的能力与前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW170817引力波事件及其电磁对应体的发现开启了多信使引力波天文学（multi-messenger gravitational wave astronomy）时代，引力波源可作为标准汽笛独立测量光度距离（luminosity distance），为宇宙膨胀历史和宇宙学参数约束提供全新手段。本文旨在系统梳理该方向的基本原理、方法和前景。

Method: 文章综述了利用引力波标准汽笛约束宇宙学的基本原理，包括源距离与红移（redshift）的测定方法，以及亮汽笛（双中子星并合+电磁对应体）和暗汽笛（恒星级双黑洞并合）两种类型的具体实现路径，并对比了第二代、第三代地面探测器和空间探测器的约束能力。

Result: 详细分析了亮汽笛与暗汽笛在约束宇宙学参数（特别是哈勃常数和暗能量参数）方面的能力差异；评估了不同代际地面探测器和空间探测器对参数精度的提升潜力。

Conclusion: 引力波标准汽笛为宇宙学参数测量提供了独立于传统电磁学方法（如超新星、宇宙微波背景辐射）的新途径。双中子星并合作为亮汽笛可提供精确红shift信息，而双黑洞并合作为暗汽笛虽缺乏电磁对应体，但仍可通过统计方法贡献约束力。未来更高灵敏度的探测设备将显著提升标准汽笛方法在宇宙学中的应用前景。

Abstract: The discovery of the gravitational-wave event GW170817 from a binary neutron star merger, together with its multi-wavelength electromagnetic counterparts, marks the beginning of the era of multi-messenger gravitational wave astronomy. Observations of gravitational-wave signals from compact binary mergers enable an independent measurement of the luminosity distance to the source. This implies that gravitational-wave sources can serve as standard sirens to probe the expansion history of the Universe, providing a new approach to constrain cosmological parameters. In this paper, we review the basic principles of using gravitational-wave standard sirens to constrain cosmology. We discuss various methods for determining the source distance and redshift, as well as the capabilities of second and third generation ground-based detectors and space-based detectors in constraining cosmological parameters, especially the Hubble constant and dark energy parameters. By examining two types of standard sirens, binary neutron star mergers with electromagnetic counterparts as bright sirens and stellar-mass binary black hole mergers as dark sirens, we illustrate the methodology, challenges, and future prospects of the standard siren approach.

### [65] [Einstein-Cartan pseudoscalaron inflation, reheating and nonthermal leptogenesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09571)
*Carlo Di Benedetto,Alessandro Di Marco,Emanuele Orazi,Gianfranco Pradisi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于爱因斯坦-嘉当-霍尔斯引力的伪标量暴胀（Einstein-Cartan pseudoscalaron inflation）模型与I型跷跷板（type-I seesaw）机制扩展的标准模型耦合后的暴胀后动力学，证明了非热轻子生成（nonthermal leptogenesis）是产生观测到的重子不对称性（baryon asymmetry）的必要且自洽机制。该框架在较宽Barbero-Immirzi参数γ范围内与宇宙微波背景（CMB）、重子声学振荡（BAO）、大爆炸核合成（BBN）及中微子振荡实验的约束一致，典型参数下给出标量谱指数n_s ~ 0.970，张量标量比r ~ 0.004，重子熵比n_B/s ~ 8.7×10^{-11}。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暴胀模型往往需要额外引入物质-反物质不对称生成机制，而如何在一个自洽的引力-粒子物理联合框架中同时解释宇宙早期暴胀与重子生成（baryogenesis）仍是开放问题。本文旨在探讨爱因斯坦-嘉当-霍尔斯引力框架下的伪标量暴胀模型是否能自然实现非热轻子生成，而不需要额外的外部机制。

Method: 将爱因斯坦-嘉当-霍尔斯引力伪标量暴胀模型与包含三个重右手马约拉纳中微子（right-handed Majorana neutrinos）的I型跷跷板扩展标准模型耦合，分析暴胀后动力学，特别是暴胀子（inflaton）与重马约拉纳费米子之间的普适耦合如何驱动非热轻子生成过程。

Result: 非热轻子生成是该模型中产生观测重子不对称性的必要且自洽机制；在Barbero-Immirzi参数γ ~ -1/100、最轻马约拉纳中微子质量约10^13 GeV、暴胀结束前e-fold数N_e ≲ 60的条件下，得到标量谱指数n_s ~ 0.970、张量标量比r ~ 0.004、重子熵比n_B/s ~ 8.7×10^{-11}，所有预测均与CMB、BAO、BBN及中微子振荡实验的约束一致。

Conclusion: 爱因斯坦-嘉当-霍尔斯伪标量暴胀模型在较宽的Barbero-Immirzi参数γ范围内能够同时满足宇宙学观测与中微子物理约束，其暴胀子与重马约拉纳中微子的普适耦合自然导致了非热轻子生成，从而为暴胀与重子生成提供了一个自洽的统一理论框架。

Abstract: We study the postinflationary dynamics of an Einstein-Cartan-Holst gravity-motivated inflationary scenario, known as Einstein-Cartan pseudoscalaron inflation, coupled to a type-I seesaw extension of the Standard Model with three heavy right-handed Majorana neutrinos. In particular, we show that nonthermal leptogenesis emerges as a necessary and self-consistent mechanism for generating the observed baryon asymmetry of the Universe, mainly because of the universal coupling of the inflaton to the additional heavy Majorana fermions. The resulting framework provides theoretical predictions that are fully compatible with the latest cosmological constraints from the Cosmic Microwave Background, Baryon Acoustic Oscillations, and Big Bang Nucleosynthesis, as well as with neutrino oscillation experiments, for a wide range of the fundamental Barbero-Immirzi model parameter $γ$, which controls the inflationary and postinflationary phases. In particular, for $γ\sim -1/100$ and a lightest Majorana-neutrino mass of order $10^{13}$ GeV, we find a scalar spectral index $n_s \sim 0.970$, a tensor-to-scalar ratio $r \sim 0.004$, for a number of e-folds before the end of inflation $N_e \lesssim 60$, and a baryon-to-entropy ratio $n_B/s \sim 8.7 \times 10^{-11}$.

### [66] [On the residual missing mass of the Bullet Cluster](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10022)
*Benoit Famaey*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文通过詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜（JWST）对子弹星系团（Bullet Cluster）的最新引力透镜模型，证实了在修改牛顿动力学（MOND）框架下，该星系团与其他质量相近的星系团一样，仍然存在残余的质量缺失差异（missing mass discrepancy），且该缺失质量主要集中于星系团中的星系周围，应为无碰撞物质（collisionless）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 修改牛顿动力学（MOND）在星系尺度上可以替代暗物质（dark matter）解释动力学现象，但在星系团（galaxy cluster）尺度上仍存在残余的质量缺失差异。利用更新后的JWST引力透镜数据，本研究旨在验证子弹星系团是否也表现出与其他同质量星系团类似的MOND残余质量缺失。

Method: 基于JWST最新发布的子弹星系团引力透镜模型（gravitational lens model），在MOND框架下对该星系团的残余质量缺失进行再分析，并与同质量等级的其他星系团进行比较。

Result: 确认子弹星系团在MOND框架下同样存在残余的质量缺失差异，且其程度与质量相近的其他星系团一致。此外，该缺失质量主要分布在星系团中的星系周围（centred on the galaxies），表明其主要成分为无碰撞物质（collisionless）。

Conclusion: 子弹星系团的观测结果进一步支持了MOND在星系团尺度上需要额外无碰撞物质来消除残余质量差异的结论，这与传统暗物质（dark matter）模型的要求存在根本性区别。

Abstract: Modified Newtonian Dynamics (MOND) is a paradigm that can do away with dark matter at galaxy scales, but displays a residual missing mass discrepancy in galaxy clusters. Prompted by the updated JWST-based gravitational lens model of the Bullet Cluster, I confirm here that this cluster exhibits the same residual missing mass discrepancy as other clusters of similar mass in the MOND context. Moreover, this missing mass should be mostly collisionless, since it is centred on the galaxies of the Bullet Cluster.

</details>


### [67] [Breaking Free from the Swampland of Impossible Universes through the DESI Portal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10476)
*Luis A. Anchordoqui,Dieter Lust*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文综述了过去两年中，将暗能量光谱仪（DESI）观测数据与弦论启发的暗能量模型联系起来的重要进展。DESI数据挑战了传统的Λ冷暗物质（ΛCDM）模型，暗示暗能量可能随时间演化，这或许表明常数暗能量Λ模型属于弦论"沼泽地"（swampland）而非"景观"（landscape），从而动摇了ΛCDM模型的观测有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弦论中构建稳定德西特（de Sitter）真空的持续困难，对ΛCDM模型的观测有效性提出了根本性质疑——常数暗能量Λ可能处于弦论中不一致的量子引力理论之沼泽地中。近期DESI等观测数据进一步挑战了ΛCDM模型，促使研究者审视弦论启发的替代方案。

Method: 本文采用综述（review）方法，系统总结了过去两年间将DESI重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation）测量及宇宙学巡天数据与弦论启发的暗能量模型联系起来的研究进展。

Result: DESI数据与宇宙学巡天的结合表明，暗能量可能具有动态、随时间演化的性质（在过去数十亿年间密度减少约10%），而非常数。这一结果对ΛCDM模型构成显著挑战。

Conclusion: 观测数据倾向于支持动态暗能量，这暗示常数暗能量Λ模型可能不属于弦论的景观，而应归入沼泽地。文章认为，弦论启发的暗能量模型是值得进一步探索的方向。

Abstract: The persistent challenge of creating stable de Sitter vacua within string theory undermines the observational validity of the $Λ$ cold dark matter (CDM) model. This difficulty suggests that the concordance model of cosmology, characterized by a constant dark energy $Λ$, may reside in the swampland of inconsistent quantum gravity theories rather than the string landscape of consistent ones. Recent observational data, particularly from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI), have significantly challenged $Λ$CDM cosmology. Specifically, the combination of DESI baryon acoustic oscillation measurements with cosmological surveys seem to indicate a preference for a dynamic, time-evolving dark energy rather than a constant, with roughly 10\% reduction in density over the last several billion years. This review summarizes significant advancements made over the past two years in linking DESI findings to string-inspired scenarios.

</details>


### [68] [Multifield stochastic inflation: Relevance of number of fields in statistical moments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10656)
*Tomo Takahashi,Koki Tokeshi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了d标量场驱动的多场暴胀（multifield inflation）中，O(d)对称性在随机（stochastic）效应下的破缺，并系统计算了e-折数（e-folds）的统计矩、原初功率谱（primordial power spectrum）及其尺度依赖，给出了与场数相关的解析公式，同时指出暴胀成功终结对场数存在理论上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在经典层面，O(d)对称性使多场暴胀中的场数不起作用；然而一旦引入随机（stochastic）效应，场数便具有物理重要性。论文旨在系统研究随机效应下场数对暴胀统计量的影响，并分析场数对暴胀终结条件的理论约束。

Method: 采用小噪声（small-noise）近似下的微扰计算方法，计算了e-折数的均值（mean number）和方差（variance）、原初功率谱（primordial power spectrum）及其尺度依赖等统计量。进一步推导了随机e-折数在任意微扰阶下的高阶统计矩（higher-order statistical moments）的一般公式，且保持对场数依赖的完全解析性。

Result: 给出了随机e-折数高阶统计矩在所有微扰阶下的一般解析公式，明确保留了场数依赖。发现暴胀成功终结的要求对场数施加了一个理论上界。并在多个O(d)对称模型上验证了上述一般结果。

Conclusion: 随机效应使多场暴胀中场数成为不可忽略的自由度，场数不仅影响暴胀的统计特性，还受限于暴胀终结条件。该研究为理解多场暴胀的随机动力学及其对原初扰动的贡献提供了系统框架。

Abstract: In multifield inflation driven by $d$ scalar fields, $O (d)$ symmetry renders the number of fields irrelevant at classical level. This ceases to be the case once stochastic effects are accommodated. The statistical quantities such as the mean number and the variance of $e$-folds as well as the primordial power spectrum and its scale dependence are perturbatively calculated in a small-noise regime. In particular, a general formula is derived for arbitrary higher-order statistical moments of the stochastic number of $e$-folds at all perturbative orders, keeping the dependence on the number of fields fully analytical. It is also discussed that the requirement for inflation to be successfully terminated puts a theoretical bound on the number of fields from above. Those general results are demonstrated for several $O (d)$-symmetric models.

</details>

### [69] [On Distinguishing Capability Elicitation from Capability Creation in Post-Training: A Free-Energy Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08368)
*Yuhao Li,Shengchao Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出后训练（post-training）研究应区分“能力引导”（capability elicitation）和“能力创造”（capability creation），引入“可访问支撑集”（accessible support）概念，并通过自由能（free-energy）框架统一解释监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）的作用机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前关于大语言模型（large language models, LLMs）后训练的争论常将监督微调（SFT）简单视为模仿、强化学习（RL）视为发现，这种二分法过于粗糙。本文旨在提出更精确的分析框架，区分训练过程是仅调整已有行为概率，还是改变了模型实际可达的行为范围。

Method: 引入“可访问支撑集”（accessible support）概念，定义为模型在有限预算下实际可生成的行为集合。基于自由能视角（free-energy view）统一分析后训练：SFT和RL均是对预训练参考分布（pretrained reference distribution）进行重加权，区别在于外部信号的来源——演示信号（demonstration signals）定义SFT的低能行为，奖励信号（reward signals）定义RL的低能行为。

Result: 当更新幅度接近基模型时，主要效应是局部重加权（local reweighting），而非能力创造。能力创造需要通过搜索（search）、交互（interaction）、工具使用（tool use）或纳入新信息来扩展模型的可达行为空间。

Conclusion: 后训练的核心问题不在于采用SFT还是RL框架，而在于训练过程是对已有可及行为进行重加权，还是真正扩展了模型的实际行为空间。

Abstract: Debates about large language model post-training often treat supervised fine-tuning (SFT) as imitation and reinforcement learning (RL) as discovery. But this distinction is too coarse. What matters is whether a training procedure increases the probability of behaviors the pretrained model could already produce, or whether it changes what the model can practically reach. We argue that post-training research should distinguish between capability elicitation and capability creation. We make this distinction operational by introducing the notion of accessible support: the set of behaviors that a model can practically produce under finite budgets. Post-training that reweights behaviors within this support is capability elicitation; whereas changing the support itself corresponds to capability creation. We develop this argument through a free-energy view of post-training. SFT and RL can both be seen as reweighting a pretrained reference distribution, only with different external signals. Demonstration signals define low-energy behavior for SFT, and reward signals define low-energy behavior for RL. When the update remains close to the base model, the main effect is local reweighting, not capability creation. Within this framework, the central question is no longer whether post-training is framed as SFT or RL, but whether it reweights behaviors already within reach, or instead expands the model's reachable behavioral space through search, interaction, tool use, or the incorporation of new information.

</details>

### [70] [Stochastic Dynamics of Domain Wall on a Racetrack: Impact of Line-Edge Roughness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08357)
*Anton V. Hlushchenko,Oksana L. Andrieieva,Mykhailo I. Bratchenko,Andriy M. Styervoyedov,Kostyantyn I. Polozhiy,Aleksei V. Chechkin*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究了铁磁赛道中边缘粗糙度（line-edge roughness）对电流驱动畴壁动力学的影响。将边缘无序建模为空间相关的奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克过程（Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process），发现即使最小程度的实验相关粗糙度也会引发显著的畴壁随机钉扎。这种随机性完全源于空间无序，即使在没有热涨落的情况下也会出现。畴壁到达给定位置的概率对施加电流呈现稳健的S形依赖，反映了脱钉阈值（depinning threshold）的有效分布。平均速度对时间和电流均呈现非线性依赖，而均方位移（mean-square displacement）在短时表现为弹道区，随后因钉扎位点俘获而饱和。结果表明，边缘粗糙度可提供可控的随机性来源并实现类p-bit（p-bit-like）功能，为概率计算和神经形态计算（probabilistic and neuromorphic computing）的硬件实现提供了路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究铁磁赛道中边缘粗糙度对电流驱动畴壁动力学（domain wall dynamics）的影响，并揭示空间无序本身即可产生随机钉扎效应，从而为概率计算硬件提供可控的随机性来源。

Method: 将边缘无序建模为空间相关的奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克过程（Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process），通过理论分析与数值模拟研究电流驱动下畴壁的运动行为。

Result: 实验相关的微小粗糙度即可引发显著随机钉扎；随机性纯由空间无序产生，无需热涨落；畴壁到达概率对电流呈S形依赖，反映脱钉阈值分布；平均速度对时间和电流呈非线性依赖；均方位移（mean-square displacement）先经历弹道区后因钉扎而饱和。

Conclusion: 边缘粗糙度可作为可控的随机性来源，实现类p-bit（p-bit-like）功能，为概率计算和神经形态计算（probabilistic and neuromorphic computing）的硬件实现提供可行路径。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of line-edge roughness on current-driven domain wall dynamics in ferromagnetic racetracks. Modeling the edge disorder as a spatially correlated Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process, we demonstrate that even minimal experimentally relevant roughness induces pronounced stochastic pinning of domain walls. Notably, this stochasticity of the current-driven motion arises purely from spatial disorder, even in the absence of thermal fluctuations. The probability of a domain wall to reach a given position exhibits a robust sigmoidal dependence on the applied current, reflecting an effective distribution of depinning thresholds. At the same time, the underlying dynamics is highly nontrivial: the mean velocity exhibits a nonlinear dependence on both time and current, while the mean-square displacement exhibits a ballistic regime at short times followed by saturation due to trapping at pinning sites. These results demonstrate that line-edge roughness provides a controllable source of stochasticity and enables p-bit-like functionality in racetrack systems, offering a pathway toward hardware implementations of probabilistic and neuromorphic computing.

</details>


### [71] [Microscopic origin of Boson peak in amorphous solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09436)
*Cunyuan Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一个非解析模型，基于标量动力学矩阵（scalar dynamical matrix）解释非晶固体中反常振动态密度（vibrational density of states, DOS）的微观起源——玻色峰（Boson peak, BP）。研究表明，玻色峰完全由配位数（coordination number）的涨落引起，而弹簧强度的涨落仅贡献阻尼效应，对低频DOS影响极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶固体中普遍存在的玻色峰（Boson peak, BP）——即低温比热和振动态密度（DOS）中的低频超额模式——其微观起源长期悬而未决。现有理论多依赖复杂假设，缺乏简洁直接的机制解释。

Method: 采用非解析模型（non-analytic model），基于含弹簧（springs）与节点（nodes）网络的标量动力学矩阵（scalar dynamical matrix），将无序（disorder）分解为两个独立因素：弹簧强度的涨落（fluctuation of spring strength）和配位数（coordination number）的涨落（即连接至同一节点的弹簧数量变化）。

Result: 配位数的涨落是玻色峰（BP）的唯一起源；弹簧强度的涨落仅产生阻尼（damping）效应，对低频振动态密度（low frequency DOS）的影响极其有限。

Conclusion: 该工作将复杂问题简化（converts complexity into simplicity），为非晶固体中玻色峰（BP）的微观起源提供了一个直接答案。

Abstract: We proposed a non-analytic model to explain the microscopic origin of the anomalous vibrational density of states (DOS), the Boson peak (BP), in amorphous solids based on the scalar dynamical matrix of a network with springs and nodes. We argue that disorder can be classified into two factors: fluctuation of spring strength and fluctuation of coordination numbers (the number of springs connected to a node). The results suggest that BP originates solely from fluctuation of coordination numbers, while the fluctuation of spring strength only contributes to the effect of damping and has very limited effect on low frequency DOS. This work converts complexity into simplicity and provides a direct answer to the puzzle of the microscopic origin of BP in amorphous solids.

</details>


### [72] [Attenuation of long-wavelength sound in quenched disordered media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09962)
*Bingyu Cui,Yuqi Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过解析推导和数值验证，研究了长波长极限下声波在淬火无序介质（quenched disordered media）中传播时的色散重整化（dispersion renormalization）和衰减（attenuation）行为。在弱无序条件下，基于玻恩近似（Born approximation）计算了无序诱导的自能（self-energies），发现弹性模量无序导致瑞利型衰减和声速降低，而密度无序只引起瑞利型衰减但不重整化声学色散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解声波在无序介质中的传播行为是凝聚态物理和材料科学中的基本问题。尽管实际材料普遍存在无序性，但长波长极限下无序对声波色散关系和衰减率的定量影响尚缺乏完备的解析理论，特别是区分弹性模量无序与密度无序的不同效应。

Method: 采用解析推导方法，在玻恩近似（Born approximation）框架下计算无序诱导的自能（self-energies），对弱无序条件下弹性模量和质量密度的空间涨落进行理论处理。通过分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）和一维、二维无序晶格的正则模分析（normal-mode analyses）对理论预测进行数值验证。

Result: 对于弱无序，结果仅依赖于涨落的方差，对随机分布的具体形式不敏感。空间无关联的弹性无序产生瑞利型衰减（Rayleigh-type attenuation）$\Gamma(q)\propto q^{d+1}$，同时伴随声速降低。密度无序同样产生瑞利型衰减，但在领头阶（leading order）不重整化声学色散。分子动力学模拟和正则模分析定量验证了理论预测。

Conclusion: 研究建立了淬火无序介质中声波传播的解析理论，揭示了弹性模量无序和密度无序对声波色散和衰减的不同贡献机制。理论预测与数值模拟的定量一致性表明，该解析框架能有效描述长波长极限下弱无序介质中的声学行为。

Abstract: We derive analytically, and validate numerically, the dispersion renormalization and attenuation of acoustic waves propagating through quenched disordered media in the long-wavelength limit. We consider weak spatial fluctuations in elastic moduli and/or mass density and compute the disorder-induced self-energies within the leading (Born) approximation. For sufficiently weak disorder, the results depend only on the variances of the fluctuations and are therefore insensitive to the detailed form of the underlying random distribution. For spatially uncorrelated elasticity disorder we obtain Rayleigh-type attenuation, $Γ(q)\propto q^{d+1}$ , together with a reduction of the sound speed. In contrast, density disorder produces Rayleigh-type attenuation but does not renormalize the acoustic dispersion to leading order. Molecular dynamics simulations and normal-mode analyses of disordered one- and two-dimensional lattices quantitatively confirm the theoretical predictions.

</details>


### [73] [Partial annealing and pattern decorrelation in associative neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10304)
*Linda Albanese,Andrea Alessandrelli,Adriano Barra,Silvio Franz,Federico Ricci-Tersenghi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本研究以Hopfield模型为基准案例，在二温二时间尺度框架下研究部分退火关联神经网络。通过引入实参数n（类似副本技巧中的副本数）调节快慢自由度间的耦合，利用Guerra插值方法推导自由能，发现负n值能有效去相关存储模式并将存储容量提升至理论最大值αc=1。数值模拟证实，部分退火在偏置模式等挑战性条件下恢复检索能力，优于传统去相关方法，表明部分退火是增强记忆组织和检索的自适应机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在二温二时间尺度框架下，部分退火关联神经网络中神经动力学与缓慢演化模式耦合机制对记忆存储和检索性能的影响，特别是实参数n对系统行为的作用。

Method: 以Hopfield模型为基准案例，采用二温二时间尺度（two-temperature-two-timescale）框架，将Guerra插值（Guerra's interpolation）方法适配到部分退火情景来推导自由能，无需依赖解析延拓（analytical continuation）；同时采用平均场蒙特卡洛动力学（mean field Monte Carlo dynamics）进行数值模拟验证。

Result: 负值n能诱导存储模式的渐进去相关，减少干扰并促进正交构型，使网络存储容量达到理论最大值αc=1；数值模拟证明部分退火在偏置模式等挑战性条件下能恢复检索能力，性能优于传统去相关方法。

Conclusion: 部分退火（partial annealing）可作为一种自适应机制（adaptive mechanism），在复杂系统中有效增强记忆组织和检索能力。

Abstract: Using the Hopfield model as a benchmark case, the present work focuses on the investigation of partially annealed associative neural networks, wherein neural dynamics is coupled to slowly evolving patterns within the two-temperature-two-timescale framework. This setting inherently introduces a real parameter n, reminiscent of the number of replicas in the celebrated replica trick, that tunes the separation of timescales and the effective interaction between fast (i.e. the neurons) and slow (i.e. the synapses) degrees of freedom. By adapting Guerra's interpolation to the case, we derive the free energy without relying on analytical continuation. The obtained results demonstrate that negative values of n induce a progressive decorrelation of the stored patterns, thereby effectively reducing interference, promoting orthogonal configurations and ultimately conferring to the network the maximal storage alphac=1. Numerical simulations based on a mean field Monte Carlo dynamics have been employed to confirm this scenario and prove that partial annealing restores retrieval in challenging regimes, such as in the presence of biased patterns, outperforming standard decorrelation methods. These findings underscore the notion of partial annealing as an adaptive mechanism for enhancing memory organisation and retrieval in complex systems.

</details>


### [74] [Exact Fixed-Point Constraints in Neural-ODEs with Provable Universality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10613)
*Feliciano Giuseppe Pacifico,Duccio Fanelli,Lorenzo Buffoni,Lorenzo Chicchi,Diego Febbe,Raffaele Marino*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一种在神经常微分方程（Neural-ODE）中显式嵌入预设不动点（fixed-points）的技术，使速度场在指定点处精确为零，在不改变表达能力的前提下严格约束梯度训练，并通过两个典型物理模型验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准神经常微分方程（Neural-ODE）在近似速度场（velocity field）时，无法保证在指定点处速度场精确为零，这限制了其在需要严格不动点约束的物理建模等任务中的应用。

Method: 给出一种显式构造方法，在参考多维空间中预设一组有限点集，使得速度场在这些点处精确为零，从而将梯度训练严格限制在预设假设类（hypothesis class）内，同时保持Neural-ODE的表达能力不变。方法在计算上易于实现。

Result: 严格证明了在速度场的任意局部约束下Neural-ODE的普适性（universality），并在两个经典物理模型上进行了实验测试，验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提技术能够在不损失Neural-ODE表达能力的前提下，显式植入不动点约束，为需要严格固定点的物理系统建模提供了可行的神经网络框架。

Abstract: We introduce a technique that enables Neural-ODEs to approximate arbitrary velocity fields with a priori planted fixed-points. Specifically, a recipe is given to explicitly accommodate for a finite collection of points in the reference multi-dimensional space of the Neural-ODE where the velocity field is exactly equal to zero. In this way, the gradient-based training is rigorously constrained inside the prescribed hypothesis class while leaving the expressive power of the Neural-ODE unaltered. We rigorously prove the universality of the Neural-ODE under any local constraints in the velocity field and give a computationally convenient way of imposing the fixed points. Our method is then tested on two paradigmatic physical models.

</details>


### [75] [Lyapunov Exponents as Duality-Invariant Signatures of Critical States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10746)
*Tong Liu,Gao Xianlong*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文将临界本征态（critical eigenstates）的识别从传统的波函数几何方法转向对偶空间李雅普诺夫（Lyapunov）性质，证明了傅里叶排除原理（Fourier exclusion principle），并将刘-夏条件（Liu–Xia condition）重新表述为严格的长度尺度判据，进而将其发展为跨微观结构定位临界集的精确可解性原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上临界本征态通过选定基下的波函数几何（如参与比、多重分形谱、有限尺寸标度）来识别，缺乏一种与表示（representation）无关且具有严格预测能力的统一判据。

Method: 本文将临界性（criticality）表述为对偶空间中的李雅普诺夫性质，证明了傅里叶排除原理——一种表示中的指数局域化（exponential localization）与其傅里叶对偶表示中的指数局域化不相容。据此将刘-夏条件 \(γ_x(E)=γ_m(E)=0\) 从现象学判据转化为严格的长度尺度表述。

Result: 该判据在转移矩阵的有界局域规范变换（bounded local gauge transformations）下保持不变，并与传统单空间多重分形诊断兼容。在可解析处理的准周期模型中，该条件给出了封闭形式的临界线、一个具有额外临界分支的精确有限临界区，以及非厄米非自对偶谱中的复杂临界面。

Conclusion: 刘-夏条件不仅是临界态的判据，更是一个精确的可解性原理（exact solvability principle），能够跨越不同的微观结构定位临界集。

Abstract: Critical eigenstates are usually identified through wave-function geometry in a chosen basis, such as participation ratios, multifractal spectra, or finite-size scaling. Here we formulate criticality instead as a dual-space Lyapunov property. We prove a Fourier exclusion principle: exponential localization in one representation is incompatible with exponential localization in its Fourier-dual representation. This turns the Liu--Xia condition, \(γ_x(E)=γ_m(E)=0\), from a phenomenological criterion into a rigorous length-scale statement: a critical state is characterized by the simultaneous absence of exponential confinement in real and momentum space. The criterion is invariant under bounded local gauge transformations of the transfer matrix and remains compatible with conventional single-space multifractal diagnostics. More importantly, it is exactly predictive. In analytically tractable quasiperiodic models, the same condition yields closed-form critical lines, an exact finite critical region with an additional critical branch, and a complex critical surface in a non-Hermitian non-self-dual spectrum. Thus the Liu--Xia condition provides not only a diagnostic of critical states, but an exact solvability principle for locating critical sets across distinct microscopic structures.

</details>

### [76] [Machine learning the non-radiative decay modes in photochemical processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08381)
*Debarshi Banerjee,Gonzalo Díaz Mirón,Alex Rodriguez,Ali Hassanali*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于可微信息不平衡（DII）的无监督信息论框架，用于从轨迹面跳跃（TSH）模拟中直接识别主导圆锥交叉（CI）接近的核坐标，并在多个分子系统中验证了其有效性，同时揭示了能隙与振子强度受不同模式支配的系统性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光激发分子体系中的非辐射衰变由朝向圆锥交叉（conical intersection, CI）的核运动驱动，但非绝热分子动力学（nonadiabatic molecular dynamics, NAD）模拟中识别负责接近CI的核自由度（nuclear degrees of freedom）因运动的高维性和集体性而极具挑战性。

Method: 引入基于可微信息不平衡（Differentiable Information Imbalance, DII）的无监督信息论框架，直接利用轨迹面跳跃（trajectory surface hopping, TSH）模拟数据，通过量化结构描述符与电子可观测量（能隙和振子强度）之间的相关性，对核自由度按预测相关性排序，再通过多步协议提取低维、物理可解释的模式。

Result: 在甲亚胺阳离子、呋喃、L-谷氨酰胺、L-焦谷氨酰胺-铵盐以及一种光活性分子马达等多个体系中，该方法恢复了已知的机理坐标，并揭示了多种结构畸变竞争贡献时的相对重要性。还发现一种系统性差异：能隙通常由少量局域坐标主导，而振子强度则依赖于更集体、分布更广的结构重排。

Conclusion: 该DII框架兼具预测能力和直接可解释性，为从高维非绝热动力学数据中提取机制性信息以及构建激发态动力学的降维模型提供了一种通用且可扩展的路线。

Abstract: Non-radiative decay in photoexcited molecular systems is driven by nuclear motion toward conical intersections (CIs), where electronic states become degenerate and nonadiabatic transitions occur. Identifying the nuclear degrees of freedom responsible for CI access from nonadiabatic molecular dynamics (NAD) simulations remains challenging because the underlying motions are high-dimensional and collective. Here, we introduce an unsupervised, information-theoretic framework based on Differentiable Information Imbalance (DII) to identify the nuclear coordinates governing CI access directly from trajectory surface hopping (TSH) simulations. By quantifying correlations between structural descriptors and electronic observables, including energy gaps and oscillator strengths, the method ranks nuclear degrees of freedom by predictive relevance. A multi-step protocol then extracts low-dimensional, physically interpretable modes associated with non-radiative decay. We apply the framework to the methaniminium cation, furan, L-glutamine, L-pyroglutamine-ammonium, and a photoactive molecular motor. Across all systems, the method recovers known mechanistic coordinates while revealing the relative importance of competing modes when multiple structural distortions contribute to CI access. The analysis also reveals a systematic distinction between observables: energy gaps are typically governed by a small number of localized coordinates, whereas oscillator strengths depend on more collective and distributed structural rearrangements. Overall, the DII-based framework combines predictive power with direct interpretability, providing a general and scalable route for extracting mechanistic insight from high-dimensional NAD data and constructing reduced-dimensional models of excited-state dynamics.

</details>


### [77] [Path Dependence in Alchemical Calculations of Water Chemical Potential in Aqueous Electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08617)
*Arlind Kacirani,Betül Uralcan,Amir Haji-Akbari*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过八种不同的逐步插入（staged particle insertion）热力学路径计算水在KCl水溶液中的化学势（chemical potential），发现同时激活范德华（van der Waals）与静电（electrostatic）相互作用的路径会产生化学上不合理的插入自由能（insertion free energy），而先激活短程范德华作用再激活静电作用的路径则给出更一致且合理的估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自由能及其导数的准确计算对评估分子与颗粒系统的热力学稳定性至关重要，但在强相互作用体系（如极性溶剂中的离子溶液）中，此类计算往往难以可靠进行。本文旨在考察不同的逐步插入路径对水在KCl水溶液中化学势计算结果的影响，并揭示路径设计对收敛性与结果一致性的关键作用。

Method: 使用八种不同的逐步插入（staged particle insertion）热力学路径计算水在KCl水溶液中的化学势。这些路径在范德华（van der Waals）相互作用与静电（electrostatic）相互作用的激活程度与顺序上存在差异，通过比较各路径下计算得到的插入自由能来评估路径设计的影响。

Result: 同时激活范德华与静电相互作用的路径（特别是完全耦合与部分端耦合协议）会产生化学上不合理的插入自由能。这些异常源于中间态中插入的水分子在与氯离子建立足够短程排斥之前就产生了强静电相互作用。相反，先激活短程范德华作用再激活静电作用的路径给出更一致且合理的估计。

Conclusion: 在极性及离子环境中的实际逐步插入热力学计算对路径设计高度敏感。研究结果强调了在逐步插入逐步插入（staged insertion）热力学协议中，应将短程相互作用与静电相互作用解耦（decoupling）的重要性。

Abstract: Accurate calculation of free energies and their derivatives is central to assessing the thermodynamic stability of molecular and particulate systems across length scales. Yet such quantities can be difficult to compute reliably in strongly interacting systems, such as solutions of ionic species in polar solvents. One important example is the chemical potential of water in aqueous electrolytes, which can be estimated through staged particle insertion by gradually coupling an inserted molecule to its environment. Although the resulting insertion free energy should be independent of the alchemical pathway, the order and manner in which van der Waals and electrostatic interactions are activated can strongly affect convergence and, in some cases, yield inconsistent estimates. Here, we examine this issue by calculating water's chemical potential in aqueous KCl solutions using eight alchemical insertion pathways that differ in the extent and order of van der Waals and Coulombic coupling. We find that concurrently activating these interactions, particularly in fully coupled and partially end-coupled protocols, can produce chemically implausible insertion free energies. These anomalies arise from intermediate states in which the inserted water molecule develops strong electrostatic interactions with a chloride ion before sufficient short-range repulsion has been established. In contrast, pathways that activate short-range van der Waals interactions before electrostatics yield more consistent and chemically plausible estimates. These findings demonstrate that practical alchemical calculations in polar and ionic environments can be highly sensitive to pathway design, underscoring the importance of decoupling short-range and electrostatic interactions in staged insertion alchemical protocols.

</details>


### [78] [Beyond the Black Box: An Interpretable Machine Learning Framework for Predicting Electronic Structure Microdescriptors and Structure-Performance Relationships in Fe-based Catalytic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08994)
*Oyinkansola Romiluyi*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可解释机器学习框架，结合SHAP特征重要性分析与树集成模型（随机森林和贝叶斯优化的CatBoost），用于表征Fe-沸石和氧化物负载催化剂在甲烷部分氧化（POM）中的构效关系，识别影响电子带隙（带隙）的关键热力学、结构和几何微观描述符，并在有限数据条件下实现了优于传统线性基线的预测性能（R² 0.61–0.77对0.32）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前甲烷转化等高能耗应用的催化剂发现与开发流程受限于昂贵的试错实验、不可重复的化学直觉，以及缺乏连接复杂催化设计空间与性能的框架，亟需一种系统化、可解释且高效的方法来加速催化剂筛选。

Method: 采用可解释机器学习框架，集成SHAP（SHapley Additive exPlanations）特征重要性分析（可解释人工智能）与基于树的集成方法（随机森林和贝叶斯优化的CatBoost），对Fe-沸石和氧化物负载催化剂进行表征，解码有限数据下的结构-性能关系。

Result: 非线性模型在预测电子带隙（band gap）方面达到R² 0.61–0.77，显著优于传统线性基线（R² = 0.32）。研究明确表明，热力学晶格稳定性和几何因素是电子带隙的主要驱动因素，而非整体化学计量比。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个轻量级、可推广的方法论和优先物理特征列表，可用于加速催化剂筛选；这些特征可进一步整合到微观动力学和反应工程模型中，构建复杂反应器的数字孪生（digital twin），并赋能自主研发实验室中的预测优化。

Abstract: The current catalyst discovery and development pipeline for energy-intensive applications like methane conversion remains bottlenecked by expensive trial-and-error experimentation, irreproducible chemical intuition, and a lack of frameworks linking complex catalytic design spaces to performance. This work presents an interpretable machine learning framework that integrates SHAP-based feature importance analysis (Explainable AI) with tree-based ensembles (Random Forest and Bayesian-optimized CatBoost) to characterize Fe-zeolite and oxide-supported catalysts for the partial oxidation of methane (POM). Despite limited data, the framework decodes complex structure-performance relationships by identifying and ranking thermodynamic, structural, and geometric microdescriptors that influence the electronic band gap and govern macroscale performance metrics such as selectivity, activity, and stability. This work explicitly demonstrates that thermodynamic lattice stability and geometric factors are the primary drivers of electronic band gap (a critical proxy for redox reactivity) rather than bulk stoichiometry. Non-linear models achieve an R2 of 0.61 - 0.77, significantly outperforming traditional linear baselines (R2 = 0.32). This workflow provides both a light-weight generalizable methodology and a prioritized list of physical features for accelerated catalyst screening - and these features can subsequently be integrated into microkinetic and reaction engineering models to create digital twins of complex reactor systems and to enable predictive optimization in autonomous R&D laboratories.

</details>


### [79] [Systematic Fine-Tuning of MACE Interatomic Potentials for Catalysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09394)
*Nima Karimitari,Jacob Clary,Derek Vigil-Fowler,Ravishankar Sundararaman,Gábor Csányi,Christopher Sutton*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了九种基于不同训练策略（从头训练 vs. 微调）的机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）在催化反应建模中的性能，发现微调型MLIP对采样策略不敏感且更擅长迁移到分布外反应，而从头训练模型的关键在于包含扰动的高能构型。最终，一个基于49,860个构型微调的大型MLIP在金属和金属氧化物催化剂上均表现最优，对双金属合金筛选实现了0.15 eV的反应能量平均绝对误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习原子间势（machine-learned interatomic potentials, MLIPs）在催化反应路径研究中兼具速度与精度，但其性能高度依赖于训练集的质量和采样策略。现有研究缺乏对从头训练（from-scratch training）与微调（fine-tuning）两种主流策略的系统性比较，尤其在不同类型催化反应和分布外（out-of-distribution）场景下的表现尚不明确。

Method: 作者训练了九种MLIPs，涵盖从头训练和基于大型基础模型（foundation models）的微调策略，使用了多种采样方法（分子动力学扰动、等高线探索、弛豫轨迹等）。模型在141个催化反应上评估，包括CO₂还原、丙烷脱氢、Pd上的氢插层以及分布外的金属氧化物析氧反应（oxygen evolution reaction, OER）。

Result: 从头训练模型若使用5%–10%的扰动高能构型，误差可降低两倍以上；微调MLIP对采样策略不敏感且能良好迁移到分布外反应。微调于金属催化剂的模型在IrO₂多晶型OER上达到0.30 eV的平均绝对误差（MAE），比基础模型MACE-MH-1优0.08 eV，比最优从头训练模型优0.14 eV。微调于O/OH吸附的模型对分布外Cu上的CO₂还原反应实现0.19 eV的能垒MAE。最终，在49,860构型上微调的大型MLIP在金属和金属氧化物催化剂上总体最优，对双金属合金左出集筛选实现0.15 eV的反应能量MAE，能泛化至未见的Miller指数表面（如(532)）。

Conclusion: 本研究明确了实现准确从头训练和微调MLIPs所需的训练构型条件，为催化反应建模中MLIP的构建策略提供了系统指导。

Abstract: Once trained, machine-learned interatomic potentials (MLIPs) provide a fast and accurate way to study catalytic reaction pathways, but their performance strongly depends on the training set. Here, we compare nine MLIPs trained with different data sets and strategies, including from-scratch (FS) training and fine-tuning (FT) of large foundation models. The models are evaluated on reaction energies, $E_{r}$, and reaction energy barriers, $E_{a}$, for 141 reactions, including CO$_2$ reduction to C$_2$ and C$_3$ products, propane dehydrogenation, hydrogen intercalation on Pd, and out-of-distribution oxygen evolution reaction (OER) on metal oxides. FS models trained with 5%--10% perturbed high-energy configurations from molecular dynamics or contour exploration reduce the error by more than twofold compared with models trained only on relaxation trajectories. In contrast, FT MLIPs are less sensitive to sampling and transfer well to out-of-distribution reactions. An MLIP fine-tuned on metallic catalysts achieves a 0.30 eV MAE for OER on iridium oxide polymorphs, outperforming out-of-the-box MACE-MH-1 by 0.08 eV and the best FS model by 0.14 eV. A model fine-tuned to O and OH adsorption on metal oxides gives a 0.19 eV reaction-barrier MAE for out-of-distribution CO$_2$RR on Cu, comparable to an FS model trained on in-distribution C--C bond-breaking reactions. Finally, a large MLIP fine-tuned on 49,860 configurations gives the best overall performance across metallic and metal-oxide catalysts and was used to screen a large left-out set of bimetallic alloys, achieving a 0.15 eV MAE for $E_{r}$, even for adsorbates on unseen Miller-index surfaces such as (532). This work identifies the training configurations needed for accurate FS and FT MLIPs for catalytic reaction modeling.

</details>


### [80] [Polarizable Embedding QM/MM for Periodic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09752)
*Julian Bessner,Anoop Ajaya Kumar Nair,Magnus Andreas Hilduberg Christiansen,Timo Jacob,Hannes Jónsson,Elvar Örn Jónsson*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于周期性体系的可极化嵌入（polarizable embedded, PE）量子力学/分子力学（QM/MM）方案，通过单中心多极展开（SCME）模型描述MM区域水分子，并引入近场/远场多级展开点策略实现周期相互作用的平滑高效收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有周期性体系的QM/MM方案在描述两个子体系之间的相互极化（mutual polarization）时仍存在精度与效率的挑战，需发展一种能够在远场（far-field）实现平滑收敛、并在近场（short range）防止过极化（over-polarization）的可极化嵌入方法。

Method: 将密度泛函理论（DFT）描述的QM体系与单中心多极展开（single center multipole expansion, SCME）模型耦合；SCME模型中H₂O分子具有各向异性偶极和四极极化率（anisotropic dipole and quadrupole polarizabilities）以及最高至十六极矩（hexadecapole）的永久多极矩。通过在远场引入单点和簇状多极展开点实现周期相互作用势的平滑高效收敛；在近场采用实空间各向同性阻尼函数（real-space pair-wise isotropic damping functions）筛除静电相互作用以防止过极化。两个子体系的分离采用弹性散射辅助柔性内区（elastic scattering assisted flexible inner region）方法，确保边界处径向分布函数（radial distribution）的平滑过渡。

Result: 该嵌入方案通过精心选择近场和远场势展开方式，使PE-QM/MM计算的精度与纯QM计算相匹配；在分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟中实现了两个子体系在边界处的平滑径向分布过渡。

Conclusion: 该周期性可极化嵌入QM/MM方案能够有效描述QM与MM子体系间的相互极化，在保持计算精度的同时实现了周期相互作用势的平滑收敛，为大规模周期性体系的量子力学/分子力学模拟提供了可行的极化嵌入框架。

Abstract: A general polarizable embedded (PE) quantum mechanics/molecular mechanics scheme for periodic systems is presented, describing mutual polarization of the two subsystems. The QM system, described with density functional theory (DFT), is coupled to a single center multipole expansion (SCME) model, characterising H$_2$O molecules in the MM region. In SCME the H$_2$O molecules are ascribed anisotropic dipole and quadrupole polarizabilities and permanent multipoles up to and including the hexadecapole. Our embedding scheme illustrates a smooth and efficient convergence pattern of the periodic interaction potential by introducing a single and clustered multipole expansion points in the far-field. By choosing the near- and far-field expansion of the potential carefully the PE-QM/MM calculation matches the level of accuracy of a the QM calculation. In the short range, the electrostatic interaction between the QM and MM subsystems is damped with a real-space and pair-wise isotropic damping functions - resulting in a screened interaction and preventing over-polarization. In molecular dynamics simulations the two subsystems are separated with the elastic scattering assisted flexible inner region [Kirchhoff et. al. JCTC, 2021, 17, 9, 5863] - ensuring a smooth transition in the radial distribution at the boundary between the two subsystems.

</details>

### [81] [Uncertainty in Physics and AI: Taxonomy, Quantification, and Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10378)
*Manuel Haußmann,Ramon Winterhalder,Maria Ubiali*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文系统梳理了机器学习（machine learning）在物理学应用中的不确定性量化（uncertainty quantification）方法，提出了统一的不确定性分类体系，阐明了频率学派与贝叶斯框架下预测不确定性与推断不确定性的解释，并讨论了包括覆盖率、校准、偏差检验和适当评分规则在内的原则性验证工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在物理学中，科学发现依赖于经过验证的概率性陈述，因此可靠的（reliable）不确定性量化对于机器学习在物理领域的应用至关重要。然而现有文献中不确定性量化方法多样、术语混杂，缺乏系统性的统一梳理。

Method: 本文通过结构化综述的方式，引入了一种统一的不确定性分类法（unified taxonomy of uncertainty），明确了频率学派（frequentist）与贝叶斯（Bayesian）框架下预测不确定性（predictive uncertainty）与推断不确定性（inference uncertainty）的含义与区别。同时，阐述了覆盖率（coverage）、校准（calibration）、偏差检验（bias tests）和适当评分规则（proper scoring rules）等原则性验证工具，并通过简单的回归与分类示例加以说明。

Result: 给出了一整套不确定性量化与验证的原则性方法论框架，并通过回归与分类的简单示例展示了上述工具的具体应用。

Conclusion: 该综述为物理学领域的机器学习从业者提供了关于不确定性量化的系统参考，有助于推动科学发现中概率性声明的可靠验证与标准化实践。

Abstract: Reliable uncertainty quantification is essential for the use of machine learning in physics, where scientific discoveries depend on validated probabilistic statements. We provide a structured overview of uncertainty quantification in ML for physics, introducing a unified taxonomy of uncertainty and clarifying the interpretation of predictive and inference uncertainties across frequentist and Bayesian frameworks. We discuss principled validation tools, including coverage, calibration, bias tests, and proper scoring rules, and illustrate them with simple regression and classification examples.

</details>


### [82] [Factual recall in linear associative memories: sharp asymptotics and mechanistic insights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10795)
*Alessio Giorlandino,Sebastian Goldt,Antoine Maillard*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文在线性联想记忆（linear associative memory）的最小设定下，精确刻画了神经网络存储输入-输出关联的存储容量，发现其可存储多达 p_c 个关联，满足 p_c log p_c / d^2 = 1/2，并揭示了最优解相较于朴素Hebbian学习规则的机制优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型在事实回忆方面表现出色，但神经网络存储和检索输入-输出关联的基本极限仍不清楚，尤其是在严格分离约束下存储容量难以直接刻画。

Method: 提出一个解耦模型（decoupled model），使每个输入拥有独立的竞争输出集；通过数值和解析证据证明该解耦模型在存储容量、学习权重谱和存储机制上等价于原模型；并利用统计力学（statistical mechanics）工具进行分析。

Result: 解耦模型可存储的关联数 p_c 满足 p_c log p_c / d^2 = 1/2；该结果可推广至线性两层架构；最优解通过将正确得分提升至竞争输出设定的极值阈值（extreme-value threshold）之上来提升性能，而非简单地增强输入-输出对齐的宽泛波动。

Conclusion: 这些发现给出了线性网络中事实存储的精确统计力学刻画，为理解更现实神经架构的记忆容量提供了基线。

Abstract: Large language models demonstrate remarkable ability in factual recall, yet the fundamental limits of storing and retrieving input--output associations with neural networks remain unclear. We study these limits in a minimal setting: a linear associative memory that maps $p$ input embeddings in $\mathbb{R}^d$ to their corresponding~$d$-dimensional targets via a single layer, requiring each mapped input to be well separated from all other targets. Unlike in supervised classification, this strict separation induces~$p$ constraints per association and produces strong correlations between constraints that make a direct characterisation of the storage capacity difficult. Here, we provide a precise characterisation of this capacity in the following way. We first introduce a decoupled model in which each input has its own independent set of competing outputs, and provide numerical and analytical evidence that this decoupled model is equivalent to the original model in terms of storage capacity, spectra of the learnt weights, and storage mechanism. Using tools from statistical physics, we show that the decoupled model can store up to $p_c \log p_c / d^2 = 1 / 2$ associations, and generalise the computation of $p_c$ to linear two-layer architectures. Our analysis also gives mechanistic insight into how the optimal solution improves over a naïve Hebbian learning rule: rather than boosting input-output alignments with broad fluctuations, the optimal solution raises the correct scores just above the extreme-value threshold set by the competing outputs. These findings give a sharp statistical-physics characterisation of factual storage in linear networks and provide a baseline for understanding the memory capacity of more realistic neural architectures.

</details>

### [83] [Dispersive decay bounds for the SSH model on the half-line](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08372)
*Remy Kassem,Amir Sagiv,Michael I. Weinstein*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文针对半直线上的SSH模型（一种自伴离散二聚体晶格哈密顿量），利用振荡积分技术证明了色散时间衰减估计，量化了局域初始条件下能量在晶格中的扩散，并确定了衰减率常数对哈密顿量参数的精确依赖关系。分析难点在于边界条件导致传播子表达式包含具有非可积奇异性的振荡积分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究SSH模型（Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型）的薛定谔流（Schrödinger flow），旨在理解局域初始条件下能量在晶格中的色散行为，并量化衰减率对哈密顿量参数的依赖。

Method: 采用振荡积分技术（oscillatory integral techniques）分析传播子中的振荡积分，处理由边界条件引入的非可积奇异性，推导色散时间衰减估计。

Result: 证明了色散时间衰减估计（dispersive time-decay estimates），量化了能量的扩散过程；确定了衰减率中常数对哈密顿量参数的精确依赖关系。

Conclusion: 成功建立了SSH模型在半直线上的色散衰减估计，并揭示了边界条件对传播子奇异性及衰减行为的复杂影响。

Abstract: We study the Schrödinger flow for the SSH model, a class of self-adjoint discrete dimer lattice Hamiltonians on the half-line. Using oscillatory integral techniques, we prove dispersive time-decay estimates, which quantify the spreading of energy throughout the lattice for a localized initial condition. Furthermore, we determine precise dependence of the constants in the decay rates on the parameters of the Hamiltonian. The analysis is complicated by the fact that as a consequence of the boundary condition, the expression for the propagator contains oscillatory integrals with nonintegrable singularities.

### [84] [A mathematical study of periodic band inversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08481)
*Tyler Guo,Maciej Zworski*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文对Tan–Devakul发现的二维周期势中电子与圆极化光子腔模耦合下的周期性能带反转现象进行了数学分析。在强耦合极限下推导了有效Bloch哈密顿量并证明了低能带的收敛性；在余弦势情形下解释了第一谱隙的周期性闭合与重新打开，证明了Dirac锥的存在性与一般性持久性，计算了孤立能带簇的Chern数；展示了更高孤立能带簇在弱耦合下无法持久；并通过追踪从覆盖空间到Brillouin环面的下降过程，解决了Berry曲率计算与Chern数之间的符号差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对Tan–Devakul在二维周期势电子与圆极化光子腔模耦合系统中观测到的周期性能带反转现象提供严格的数学分析，澄清已有数值结果中Berry曲率与Chern数之间的符号矛盾。

Method: 在强耦合极限下推导有效Bloch哈密顿量（effective Bloch Hamiltonian）并证明低能带的收敛性；在余弦势情形下分析第一谱隙（spectral gap）的周期性闭合与重新打开；利用拓扑能带理论证明Dirac锥（Dirac cones）的存在性与一般性持久性；计算孤立能带簇（isolated band clusters）的Chern数（Chern numbers）；通过追踪从覆盖空间（covering space）到Brillouin环面（Brillouin torus）的下降过程解决符号差异。

Result: 证明了强耦合极限下有效Bloch哈密顿量的收敛性；解释了余弦势中第一谱隙的周期性闭合与重新打开；证明了Dirac锥在隙闭合点处的存在性及其在一般参数下的持久性；计算了孤立能带簇的Chern数；发现更高孤立能带簇在弱耦合区域内无法持久；解决了Berry曲率计算与Chern数之间的符号不一致问题。

Conclusion: 该数学分析为周期性能带反转现象提供了严格的理论基础，澄清了拓扑量计算中的符号歧义，揭示了强耦合与弱耦合机制下能带结构的不同行为模式。

Abstract: We give a mathematical analysis of the periodic band inversion phenomenon observed by Tan--Devakul for an electron in a two-dimensional periodic potential coupled to a circularly polarized photon cavity mode. In the strong-coupling limit, we derive an effective Bloch Hamiltonian and prove convergence of the low-lying bands. For a cosine potential, we explain the periodic closing and reopening of the first spectral gap, prove the existence and generic persistence of Dirac cones at the gap-closing points, and compute the Chern numbers associated to isolated band clusters. We also show that higher isolated band clusters cannot persist in the small-coupling regime. Finally, we resolve an apparent sign discrepancy between Berry curvature computations and Chern numbers by tracking the descent from the covering space to the Brillouin torus.

</details>


### [85] [Quantum Relative Entropy and the Mean-Field Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08652)
*Gaoyue Guo,Hao Liang,Zhenfu Wang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于量子多体系统平均场极限的量子相对熵方法，证明了冯·诺依曼方程下N体密度矩阵与哈特里方程张量化解之间的定量稳定性估计，并将该方法推广至林德布拉德动力学下的有限维开放量子系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统平均场极限的严格定量分析是数学物理中的重要问题，现有方法在稳定性估计和推广性方面存在不足，尤其缺乏不依赖于相互作用特殊张量积分解的统一熵方法。

Method: 基于量子相对熵（quantum relative entropy）方法，构建熵产生恒等式（entropy production identity）；引入中心化两体涨落的抵消机制（cancellation mechanism）；利用组合估计（combinatorial estimate）控制剩余混合矩；结合半经典Wasserstein界（semiclassical Wasserstein bounds）以获得对普朗克常数一致的收敛估计。

Result: 在闭系统中，获得了固定边缘在迹范数（trace norm）下的混沌传播（propagation of chaos）；在联合平均场与半经典极限下得到了对普朗克常数一致的收敛估计；在开放量子系统中，对一般有界两体相互作用建立了类似的相对熵估计。

Conclusion: 该熵方法不依赖于相互作用的任何特殊张量积分解（tensor-product decomposition），具有广泛的适用性，可用于封闭与开放量子系统的平均场极限分析。

Abstract: We develop a quantum relative entropy method for the mean-field limit of quantum many-body systems. For closed systems governed by the von Neumann equation, we prove a quantitative stability estimate between the $N$-body density matrix and the tensorized solution of the Hartree equation. The argument is based on an entropy production identity, a cancellation mechanism for the centered two-body fluctuation, and a combinatorial estimate controlling the remaining mixed moments. As a consequence, we obtain propagation of chaos in trace norm for fixed marginals. We further combine the entropy estimate with known semiclassical Wasserstein bounds to derive a convergence estimate that is uniform in the Planck constant in an appropriate joint mean-field and semiclassical regime. Finally, we extend the method to finite-dimensional open quantum systems governed by Lindblad dynamics. In this setting, we establish an analogous relative entropy estimate for general bounded two-body interactions, where the mean-field potential is defined through partial trace. This shows that the entropy method does not rely on any special tensor-product decomposition of the interaction.

</details>


### [86] [Picard-Lefschetz theory and alien calculus: a case study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08867)
*Si Li,Yong Li,Xinxing Tang*

Main category: math-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为 Picard–Lefschetz 理论（一种通过复鞍点分析连接流形的方法）与复苏理论（resurgence theory，一种处理发散级数并恢复非微扰信息的形式框架）之间建立的字典提供明确的有穷维检验案例，从而深化对 Stokes 现象（Stokes phenomenon）和鞍点展开中 Borel 奇点结构的理解。

Method: 分别针对 Airy 模型、Bessel 模型和 Gamma 模型三种基本一维指数积分（exponential integral），从 Picard–Lefschetz 方面描述 Lefschetz 临界点（Lefschetz thimble）并计算 Stokes 相位（Stokes phase）下临界点之间的连接轨迹（connecting trajectories）；从复苏方面分析鞍点展开（saddle expansion）的 Borel 奇点（Borel singularity），并利用外星算子（alien operator）恢复相同的 Stokes 系数（Stokes coefficient）。

Result: 在三种模型中，Picard–Lefschetz 框架下的临界点穿墙（thimble wall-crossing）所得到的 Stokes 系数，与复苏理论中外星算子计算所得结果完全一致。

Conclusion: 三个一维指数积分实例明确验证了临界点穿墙与外星微积分（alien calculus）之间的对偶字典，为解析量子场论和弦论中更复杂的鞍点求和问题提供了严格的有限维类比。

Abstract: We compare Picard--Lefschetz theory and resurgence in three basic one-dimensional exponential integrals: the Airy model, the Bessel model, and the Gamma model. On the Picard--Lefschetz side, we describe the Lefschetz thimbles and compute the connecting trajectories between critical points appearing at Stokes phases. On the resurgent side, we analyze the Borel singularities of the saddle expansions and use alien operators to recover the same Stokes coefficients. These examples serve as explicit finite-dimensional test cases for the dictionary between thimble wall-crossing and alien calculus.
