### [87] [Scaling Symmetries and Conformal Relative Equilibria on Poisson Manifolds, with Applications to Lie--Poisson Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09062)
*Manuele Santoprete*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在具有缩放对称性的精确泊松流形（exact Poisson manifold）上研究了哈密顿系统（Hamiltonian system）的共形相对平衡（conformal relative equilibrium），通过引入共形泊松作用（conformally Poisson action）和共形动量映射（conformal momentum map），建立了增广哈密顿量形式。在非线性退化情形下，该形式还原为精确辛情形下的条件。对于李-泊松流形（Lie-Poisson manifold），推导出纯代数判据：齐次哈密顿系统存在非平凡共形相对平衡当且仅当其李代数含有双曲元素（hyperbolic element）。通过三维比安奇分类（Bianchi classification）完成完全分类，并指出$\mathfrak{so}(2,1)^*$上存在非平凡共形相对平衡，而经典自由刚体在$\mathfrak{so}(3)^*$上则严格受阻。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将共形相对平衡理论从精确辛流形（exact symplectic manifold）推广至更一般的精确泊松流形，并建立李-泊松情形下的纯代数判别条件，以统一和扩展对带有缩放对称性的哈密顿系统中平衡现象的理解。

Method: 引入共形泊松作用与共形动量映射的概念，构造增广哈密顿量形式来刻画共形相对平衡；对于李-泊松流形，利用自然缩放作用给出的精确泊松结构，将问题转化为李代数中是否存在双曲元素的纯代数条件。

Result: 建立了共形相对平衡存在的充要条件：齐次哈密顿系统存在非平凡共形相对平衡当且仅当其李代数含有双曲元素；利用比安奇分类对三维情形给出完全分类；在$\mathfrak{so}(2,1)^*$上发现非平凡共形相对平衡，而$\mathfrak{so}(3)^*$上的经典自由刚体则不存在此类平衡。

Conclusion: 共形相对平衡理论可成功从辛情形推广至泊松情形，李代数中双曲元素的存在性是该平衡存在的核心代数判据，该结果对不同李代数结构下的物理系统（如自由刚体）具有明确的区分意义。

Abstract: We investigate conformal relative equilibria for Hamiltonian systems on exact Poisson manifolds equipped with scaling symmetries. By introducing conformally Poisson actions and conformal momentum maps, we characterize these equilibria through an augmented Hamiltonian formulation; in the nondegenerate case, this recovers the conditions recently developed for the exact symplectic case.
  Specializing to Lie--Poisson manifolds, where the natural scaling action canonically provides an exact Poisson structure on the dual of any finite-dimensional Lie algebra, we establish a purely algebraic criterion: a homogeneous Hamiltonian system admits a nontrivial conformal relative equilibrium if and only if the underlying Lie algebra contains a hyperbolic element. This yields a complete classification in dimension three via the Bianchi classification. As a prominent application, we show that nontrivial conformal relative equilibria emerge in the dynamics on $\mathfrak{so}(2,1)^*$, but are strictly obstructed for the classical free rigid body on $\mathfrak{so}(3)^*$.

</details>


### [88] [An exact spacetime polymer gas for finite-temperature $\mathbb Z_N$ homological quantum code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09122)
*Nafiz Ishtiaque,Shanto Chakroborty*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过精确的量子-经典映射，将有限温度的 $P$-形式 $\mathbb Z_N$ 同调码（homological codes）转化为带有拓扑背景荷的 $(d+1)$ 维时空模型，利用缺陷聚合物（defect polymers）框架导出低活性判据，并建立了更高形式的 Kramers-Wannier 对偶性，最终在素数 $N$ 情形下与 plaquette 随机团模型（random-cluster model）耦合从而导入尖锐的相变结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究有限温度下 $P$-形式 $\mathbb Z_N$ 同调码的统计力学性质，理解其在不同背景荷下的配分函数行为以及拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的指数抑制条件。

Method: 采用精确的有限 Trotter 量子-经典映射，将量子码映射为 $(d+1)$ 维时空模型；引入电、磁拓扑背景荷，将配分函数重写为闭合缺陷聚合物的形式；利用同种硬核（hard-core）majorant 气体对复合聚合物气体进行控制；推导更高形式的 Kramers-Wannier 对偶性；对素数 $N$ 情形与 plaquette 随机团模型建立精确耦合。

Result: 得到了一个显式的低活性判据（low-activity criterion），在该判据下所有背景依赖的配分函数一致可控，且同调非平凡的聚合物在时空系统长度（systole）尺度上被指数抑制。建立了交换电、磁背景、Wilson 算符与 't Hooft 算符以及 $P$-形式与 $(d-P)$-形式理论之间的精确对偶。在素数 $N$ 的特殊几何上导入了尖锐的相变结果。

Conclusion: 本文建立的聚合物气体框架与对偶关系为有限温度拓扑量子码的统计力学分析提供了精确的工具，并可通过随机团模型连接获取更丰富的相变信息。

Abstract: We study finite-temperature $P$-form $\mathbb Z_N$ homological codes via an exact finite-Trotter quantum-to-classical map to a $(d+1)$-dimensional spacetime model with electric and magnetic topological background charges. The resulting background-resolved partition functions admit an exact reformulation in terms of closed magnetic and electric defect polymers, with opposite-species interactions governed by linking phases. By bounding this complex polymer gas by positive same-species hard-core majorant gases, we obtain an explicit low-activity criterion under which all background-dependent partition functions are uniformly controlled and homologically nontrivial polymers are exponentially suppressed on the scale of the spacetime systole. We also derive an exact higher-form Kramers-Wannier duality exchanging electric and magnetic backgrounds, Wilson and 't Hooft operators, and $P$-form and $(d-P)$-form theories. Finally, for prime $N$, we identify an exact source-free gauge-theory specialization coupled to the plaquette random-cluster model, which imports sharp phase-transition results on special geometries into the spacetime framework.

</details>


### [89] [On Conservative Statistical Riemann Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09133)
*Hanwen Liu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了信息几何（information geometry）与规范理论（gauge theory）之间的对应关系，证明归一化保守统计流形可由Tzitzéica方程的解几何生成，并给出了封闭可定向曲面上此类统计结构的模空间（moduli space）的完整参数化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在揭示信息几何与规范理论之间的深层联系，并系统刻画一类重要的统计流形——归一化保守统计结构（normalized conservative statistical structure）的几何性质与模空间结构。

Method: 首先定义了满足归一化条件与守恒场方程（conservation field equation）的统计流形；其次在可定向曲面上证明了Chebyshev 1-形式为调和形式（harmonic form），且Amari–Chentsov张量的无迹部分退化为全纯三次微分（holomorphic cubic differential）；接着证明了归一化保守统计结构可由一般线性和乐（general linear holonomy）的Higgs丛（Higgs bundle）上的标量Tzitzéica方程的解几何生成，推广了Labourie–Loftin对应；最后利用全纯向量丛对模空间进行了参数化。

Result: 在亏格至少为2的封闭可定向曲面上，归一化保守统计结构的模空间完全由Teichmüller空间上的一个全纯向量丛（holomorphic vector bundle）参数化，该向量丛由阿贝尔微分（Abelian differential）和三次微分构成。

Conclusion: 信息几何与规范理论之间存在结构性的对应关系；保守统计结构在曲面上具有丰富的几何约束，其模空间可通过Teichmüller理论上的全纯微分类对象进行完整刻画。

Abstract: We establish a correspondence between information geometry and gauge theory. First, we define an important class of statistical manifolds, that is normalized and satisfies a conservation field equation. Second, we prove that for a conservative statistical structure on an orientable surface, the Chebyshev 1-form is constrained to be harmonic, and the traceless part of the Amari--Chentsov tensor descends to a holomorphic cubic differential. Then, we demonstrate that normalized conservative statistical structures are geometrically generated by solutions to the scalar Tzitzéica equation on Higgs bundles with general linear holonomy, generalizing the Labourie-Loftin correspondence. Finally, we prove that the moduli space of normalized conservative statistical structures on a closed orientable surface of genus at least 2 is completely parameterized by a holomorphic vector bundle over the Teichmüller space, consisting of Abelian differentials and cubic differentials.

</details>


### [90] [A Bundle-Theoretic Formulation of Phonons in Crystalline Phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09323)
*Aleksey Prots*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在固定晶体学背景上，将平移序参量（translational order parameter）描述为关联环面丛（associated torus bundle）的一个截面，并利用离散结构群给出的平坦埃雷斯曼联络（flat Ehresmann connection）构造了全局定义的协变微分（covariant differential），以替代局部位移梯度（local displacement gradient），从而将声子（phonon）领域表述为一阶拉格朗日场论（first-order Lagrangian field theory）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声子通常通过局部位移场（local displacement field）引入，但该局域描述所对应的整体几何对象尚不明确。本文旨在不改变局域声学方程的前提下，在固定晶体学背景上描述平移序参量的全局位形空间，并为位移梯度提供一个全局定义。

Method: 首先将正交标架丛（orthonormal frame bundle）约化至离散点群（discrete point group）以固定晶体序的取向部分；随后将平移序参量描述为关联环面丛的一个截面。对于有对称性晶型（symmorphic crystal），点群线性作用在平移环面上；对于非对称性晶型（nonsymmorphic crystal），作用为仿射的，并记录了晶体群（crystallographic group）的扩张类。结构群的离散性在关联环面丛上导出一个平坦埃雷斯曼联络，其对应的协变微分是全局定义的对象，在局部与普通位移梯度一致。利用该协变微分将声子领域表述为一阶拉格朗日场论。

Result: 当平坦环面和乐（flat torus holonomy）固定一个平衡点时，对相应的协变常数截面（covariantly constant section）线性化可得到局部位移场。对于仅含导数项的二次弹性拉格朗日量（derivative-only quadratic elastic Lagrangian）且满足标准客观性条件（standard objectivity condition）时，理论在局部退化为线性弹性理论，并给出标准声子谱。若全局平衡截面不存在，则相同的线性理论在无缺陷的单连通区域（defect-free simply connected patches）上局域有效。

Conclusion: 本文通过纤维丛（fiber bundle）语言为声子理论提供了全局几何框架，将局部位移场嵌入到关联环面丛的协变常数截面的线性化中，并在特定条件下恢复标准线性弹性与声子谱。

Abstract: Phonons are usually introduced by choosing a local displacement field. This paper keeps that local description, but identifies the global geometric object represented by it. The aim is not to change the local acoustic equations, but to describe the global configuration space of the translational order parameter on a fixed crystallographic background and to give a globally defined replacement for the displacement gradient.
  After the orientational part of the crystalline order has been fixed by a reduction of the orthonormal frame bundle to a discrete point group, the translational order parameter is described as a section of an associated torus bundle. In a symmorphic crystal the point group acts on the translation torus linearly, whereas in a nonsymmorphic crystal the action is affine and records the extension class of the crystallographic group. Relative to the fixed point-group bundle, the discreteness of the structure group gives a canonical flat Ehresmann connection on the associated torus bundle. The corresponding covariant differential of the translational field is a globally defined object which locally coincides with the ordinary displacement gradient.
  This covariant differential is then used to formulate the phonon sector as a first-order Lagrangian field theory. When the flat torus holonomy fixes an equilibrium point, linearization about the corresponding covariantly constant section gives the usual local displacement field. For derivative-only quadratic elastic Lagrangians satisfying the standard objectivity condition, the theory reduces locally to linear elasticity and to the standard acoustic phonon spectrum. If such a global equilibrium section does not exist, the same linear theory is understood locally on defect-free simply connected patches.

</details>


### [91] [Cocycle Actions on Hidden Quantum Markov Models: Symmetry Protection and Topological Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09605)
*Abdessatar Souissi,Abdessatar Barhoumi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了适用于一维量子自旋系统和对称性保护拓扑（SPT）相的隐量子马尔可夫模型（HQMM）对称性作用框架，揭示了其与SPT相群上同调分类的直接对应，并以AKLT链为例展示了该形式如何将SPT序与随机Markov过程统一描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有隐量子马尔可夫模型（HQMM）缺乏对对称性（symmetry）和拓扑相（topological phase）的系统性描述，特别是与对称性保护拓扑（symmetry-protected topological, SPT）相分类之间的联系尚未建立。本文旨在填补这一空白，将群上同调（group cohomology）分类引入HQMM框架。

Method: 提出对称性作用框架：对称群$G$在隐（虚拟）自由度上以射影表示（projective representation）作用，在物理观测量空间上以线性表示作用，由此构造出在$G$联合作用下不变的全局HQMM态。通过群上同调$2$-上循环（$2$-cocycle）$[ω] \in H^{2}(G,\mathrm{U}(1))$对对称性作用进行分类，类比一维玻色子SPT相的标准上同调分类。以Affleck--Kennedy--Lieb--Tasaki（AKLT）链为具体实例，其隐层携带非平凡类$[ω] \in H^{2}(\mathrm{SO}(3),\mathrm{U}(1))$。

Result: HQMM的对称性作用被证明可由群上同调$2$-上循环$[ω] \in H^{2}(G,\mathrm{U}(1))$自然分类，与一维玻色子SPT相通过射影边缘表示（projective edge representation）得到的标准上同调分类直接对应。在AKLT链例子中，HQMM形式在提供隐层虚拟动力学随机Markov描述的同时，再现了已知的SPT性质。

Conclusion: HQMM为连接量子随机过程（quantum stochastic processes）、多体系统的张量网络描述（tensor-network description）和SPT序（symmetry-protected topological order）提供了自然的桥梁。

Abstract: We develop a symmetry action framework for hidden quantum Markov models (HQMMs) tailored to one-dimensional quantum spin systems and symmetry-protected topological (SPT) phases. In our setting, a symmetry group $G$ acts projectively on the hidden (virtual) degrees of freedom and linearly on the physical observation space, yielding a global HQMM state that is invariant under the combined action of $G$ for both conventional and causal (input--output) structures. We show that such symmetry actions are naturally classified by a group-cohomology $2$-cocycle $[ω] \in H^{2}(G,\mathrm{U}(1))$, in direct analogy with the standard cohomological classification of one-dimensional bosonic SPT phases via projective edge representations. As an explicit example, we apply this construction to the Affleck--Kennedy--Lieb--Tasaki (AKLT) chain, where the hidden layer carries a nontrivial class $[ω] \in H^{2}(\mathrm{SO}(3),\mathrm{U}(1))$ encoding its SPT order. In this case the HQMM formalism reproduces the known SPT properties of the AKLT state while providing a stochastic, Markovian description of the underlying virtual dynamics. Our results establish HQMMs as a natural bridge between quantum stochastic processes, tensor-network descriptions of many-body systems, and symmetry-protected topological order.

*A. D. Alhaidari*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入了一类具有双参数初值、哈密顿量可用三对角对称矩阵表示的可精确求解系统。其波函数可由正交多项式展开，这些多项式包含系统全部物理信息。尽管无法解析写出双参数势函数，但可通过数值实现。文中给出连续和离散能谱的示例，并发现当初始值中的双参数超过临界值时，纯连续谱系统（如自由粒子）中会诱导出束缚态和/或共振态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）表示为某正交基组下的三对角对称矩阵（tridiagonal symmetric matrix）；波函数（wavefunction）写作基元上逐点收敛级数（point-wise convergent series）；展开系数为正交多项式（orthogonal polynomials），满足由双参数初值（two-parameter initial values）确定的三项递推关系（three-term recursion relation）。

Result: 给出了若干连续和/或离散能谱（continuous and/or discrete energy spectra）的示例系统；发现一个有趣现象：在纯粹连续谱系统（如自由粒子（free particle））中，当两个参数超过某一临界值时，会出现束缚态（bound states）和/或共振态（resonances）。

Conclusion: 无法解析写出与双参数对应的势函数（potential function），但可在给定物理参数下通过数值方式实现。该双参数框架为在可解模型中诱导束缚态和共振态提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: We introduce two-parameter classes of exactly-solvable novel systems whose Hamiltonian operators could be represented by tridiagonal symmetric matrices in some orthonormal basis set. The associated wavefunction is written as point-wise convergent series in the basis elements. The expansion coefficients of the series are orthogonal polynomials in the energy that satisfy the resulting three-term recursion relation starting with two-parameter initial values. These polynomials contain all physical information about the system and they depend on the values of the two parameters. However, we could not write down the associated two-parameter potential function analytically but could realize them numerically for a given set of physical parameters. We give several illustrative examples of these systems with continuous and/or discrete energy spectra. Moreover, a curious phenomenon is observed where bound states and/or resonances are induced in a system with pure continuous spectrum (e.g., a free particle) if the two parameters in the initial values exceed certain critical limits.

Abstract: This paper is devoted to investigating the relation between the generalized i-boson model and boxed BUC plane partitions. We also consider the actions of neutral fermion vertex operators on state vectors in terms of the neutral fermionic Fock space. With the help of the scalar product of the generalized i-boson model, the generating function for boxed BUC plane partitions is derived which can be represented as the products of Schur Q-functions. Moreover, the generating function for BUC plane partitions with the double scaling limit is presented.

### [94] [From Noncommutative Kinematics to \(U(1)_{\star}\) Gauge Theory: A Family of Spectral Triples with Localized Gauge-induced Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10250)
*Md. Rafsanjany Jim,Tanmoy Kumar Sarkar,S. Hasibul Hassan Chowdhury*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文为非交换（noncommutative）平面系统构建了谱三元组（spectral triple）框架，该系统与运动学对称群$G_{\mathrm{NC}}$的一个固定非退化不可约酉扇区相关联，由中心参数$(\hbar_0,\vartheta_0, B_0)$标记。通过Moyal侧描述和光滑截断技术，构造了局部紧的非幺正基谱三元组，并证明了有界自伴扰动下的强预解收敛性，从而以谱三元组方式逼近极限最小耦合Dirac算子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于两参数族$(r,s)$的酉等价具体实现构造偶谱三元组（even spectral triple），其Dirac算子为等谱且具有紧预解式。利用线性Darboux归一化和Stone-von Neumann定理将光滑算子代数映射到有效Moyal侧Fr\'echet *-代数上。通过将线性规范势替换为光滑截断局部化，构造有界自伴扰动，并证明在$R\rightarrow\infty$时强预解收敛到形式最小耦合算子的闭包。

Result: 对每个星-规范参数$\varrho$，获得了局部紧的非幺正基谱三元组（base spectral triple），定义在Moyal代数$\mathcal{A}_{\vartheta_{\mathrm{eff}},\varrho}$上，其中$\vartheta_{\mathrm{eff}} =\vartheta_0/(1 -\vartheta_0 B_0/\hbar_0)$。对有界自伴扰动后的谱三元组，证明了当截断半径$R\rightarrow\infty$时的强预解收敛性。

Conclusion: 有限截断谱三元组在谱三元组层面上逼近了固定非退化$G_{\mathrm{NC}}$背景上的极限最小耦合Dirac算子，为非交换几何框架下的规范场耦合提供了严格的数学近似方案。

Abstract: We construct a spectral-triple framework for a noncommutative planar system associated with a fixed nondegenerate irreducible unitary sector of the kinematical symmetry group $G_{\mathrm{NC}}$, labelled by central parameters $(\hbar_0,\vartheta_0, B_0)$ with $\hbar_0,\vartheta_0, B_0\neq 0$ and $\hbar_0 - \vartheta_0 B_0\neq 0$. For the corresponding two-parameter family $(r,s)$ of unitarily equivalent concrete realizations, we construct even spectral triples whose Dirac operators are isospectral and have compact resolvent despite the non-unital and noncompact setting. Passing to the Moyal-side description, a linear Darboux normalization and the Stone-von Neumann theorem identify the represented smooth operator algebra with the effective Moyal-side Frechet *-algebra at $\vartheta_{\mathrm{eff}} =\vartheta_0/(1 -\vartheta_0 B_0/\hbar_0)$. For each $\varrho$, this yields locally compact non-unital base spectral triples over the involutive Moyal algebra $\mathcal{A}_{\vartheta_{\mathrm{eff}},\varrho}$, with $(r,s)$ as kinematical presentation parameters and $\varrho$ as an independent star-gauge parameter. To incorporate an external $U(1)_\star$ gauge field, we replace the linear gauge potentials by smooth cutoff localizations; the resulting bounded self-adjoint perturbations define, for every $R > 0$, locally compact non-unital spectral triples. Finally, as $R\rightarrow\infty$, we prove strong resolvent convergence to a self-adjoint limiting operator, the closure of the formal minimally coupled operator. Thus the finite-cutoff spectral triples approximate, at the level of spectral triples, the limiting minimally coupled Dirac operator over a fixed nondegenerate $G_{\mathrm{NC}}$-background.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入两条新公理：(1) 利用Tomita-Takesaki理论，对锥形区域（cone-like regions）施加Haag对偶性公理；(2) 引入反射正性（reflection positivity）公理，连接近期工作[arXiv:2510.20662]。随后在已知的所有拓扑序交换投影子模型（topologically ordered commuting projector models）上验证这两条公理的成立性。

Abstract: In our previous article [arXiv:2307.12552], we introduced local topological order (LTO) axioms for abstract quantum spin systems which allow one to access topological order via a boundary algebra construction. Using the LTO axioms, we produced a canonical pure state on the quasi-local algebra, which gives a net of von Neumann algebras associated to a poset of cones in $\mathbb{R}^n$. In this article, motivated by [arXiv:2509.23734], we introduce an axiom for LTOs which ensures Haag duality for cone-like regions using Tomita-Takesaki theory. We prove this axiom is satisfied for all known topologically ordered commuting projector models. We thus get an independent proof of Haag duality for the Levin-Wen string net models originally proved in [arXiv:2509.23734]. We also give a reflection positivity axiom for LTOs, connecting to the recent article [arXiv:2510.20662]. ### [96] [A Simplicial Approach to Higher Geometric Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10695)
*Qian Zhang*

TL;DR: 本文提出了n-plectic几何中可观测量（observables）的统一框架，通过引入度移格拉斯曼变量u将L_∞-代数从Hamiltonian (n-1)-形式扩展至所有阶的Hamiltonian形式；将k-形式可观测量解释为k维拓扑缺陷，构造出满足Kan填充性质的半单纯集sOb_bullet(M)，从而建立可观测量的n-群胚模型；并从该结构中提取上同调不变量、构造递归内积得到范畴化预-n-Hilbert空间，最终为扩展对象的几何量子化（geometric quantization）提供了系统基础。

Method: 引入一个度移格拉斯曼变量u（degree-shifting Grassmann variable u），它编码子流形的余维数（submanifold codimension），从而将L_∞-代数（L_infty-algebra）从Hamiltonian (n-1)-形式扩展至所有阶的Hamiltonian形式；将k-形式可观测量解释为k维拓扑缺陷（k-dimensional topological defects），通过递归粘合构造（recursive gluing construction）组装成半单纯集sOb_bullet(M)（semi-simplicial set），并证明其满足Kan填充性质（Kan filling property），进而提供n-群胚模型（n-groupoid model）；从半单纯视角提取上同调不变量（cohomological invariants），并构造递归内积（recursive inner product）得到范畴化预-n-Hilbert空间（categorified pre-n-Hilbert space）；利用极化的层次结构（hierarchical structure of polarizations）建立与多辛几何（multisymplectic geometry）中1-极化分类相一致的量子化方案（quantization scheme）。

Conclusion: 该框架桥接了高代数结构（higher algebraic structures）与高范畴几何（higher categorical geometry），为扩展对象（extended objects）的几何量子化建立了系统化的基础。

Abstract: This paper develops a unified framework for observables in n-plectic geometry, extending the L_infty-algebra of Hamiltonian (n-1)-forms to Hamiltonian forms of all degrees via a degree-shifting Grassmann variable u that encodes submanifold codimension. Interpreting k-form observables as k-dimensional topological defects yields a recursive gluing construction that assembles into a semi-simplicial set sOb_bullet(M), which we prove satisfies the Kan filling property, thereby providing an n-groupoid model for observables. From this semi-simplicial perspective we extract cohomological invariants and construct a recursive inner product leading to a categorified pre-n-Hilbert space. The hierarchical structure of polarizations yields a natural quantization scheme matching the 1-polarization classification of multisymplectic geometry. The resulting framework bridges higher algebraic structures with higher categorical geometry and establishes a systematic foundation for the geometric quantization of extended objects.

### [97] [Vacuum and thermal fluctuations of a scalar field with point interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10725)
*Davide Fermi,Marco Gurgoglione*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了闵可夫斯基时空中与有限个点状障碍物（由零程势建模）相互作用的中性无质量标量场的真空与热涨落，利用相对zeta函数技术推导了热力学可观测量和Casimir能量的收敛Born级数展开，并数值展示了障碍物间Casimir力的吸引力特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用自伴拉普拉斯算子（self-adjoint realizations of the Laplacian）严格描述系统，并通过相对zeta函数（relative zeta-function）技术计算重正化连通配分函数（renormalized connected partition function），推导出热力学量的显式表达式及Casimir能量的收敛Born级数展开（convergent Born series expansion）。

Result: 低温和高温行为下的热力学可观测量被显式表征；Casimir能量可分解为沿障碍物连线方向的成对贡献，但其强度依赖于整体的非局域构型；数值结果显示相同障碍物间的Casimir力始终具有吸引力（attractive）。

Conclusion: 多散射过程（multiple-scattering processes）是真空力（vacuum forces）的微观机制；在零程势近似下，相同障碍物间的Casimir力均为吸引力，且力的大小非局域地依赖于整个障碍物阵列的几何配置。

Abstract: We investigate the vacuum and thermal fluctuations of a neutral massless scalar field living in Minkowski spacetime and interacting with a finite number of point-like obstacles, modelled by zero-range potentials. The system is described rigorously in terms of self-adjoint realizations of the Laplacian, under assumptions ensuring the absence of instabilities. Using the relative zeta-function technique, we determine the renormalized connected partition function and derive explicit expressions for the thermodynamic observables, characterizing both their low- and high-temperature behaviours. Furthermore, we derive of a convergent Born series expansion for the Casimir energy, which identifies multiple-scattering processes as the mechanism underlying vacuum forces. The latter decompose into pairwise contributions directed along the lines joining the obstacles, with intensities depending non-locally on the full configuration. We also present some numerical results for identical obstacles, indicating that the Casimir forces are always attractive in this context.

</details>

Abstract: Chimera states are among the most intriguing phenomena in nonlinear dynamics, characterized by the coexistence of coherent and incoherent behavior in systems of coupled identical oscillators. Many methods have been proposed to detect chimera states and to distinguish their different types. However, such methods often suffer from important limitations that prevent sufficiently precise classification. In this work, we overcome the issue by considering a method based on Fourier analysis to determine key signal characteristics such as amplitude, phase, and frequency, jointly with an unsupervised clustering step acting on normalized total variations, measures of local spatial changes of the above-mentioned dynamical features. Abstract: The planned High Luminosity upgrade to the Large Hadron Collider at CERN aims to increase the instantaneous luminosity peak to about 7.5 x 10^{34} cm^{-2}s^{-1}. The ATLAS detector will be extensively re-designed to meet the challenges of this upgrade. This paper focuses on the use of computational fluid dynamics to characterise the thermoflow in order to model the dry nitrogen flushing scheme in the Common Environmental Monitoring and Interlock System for the ATLAS Inner Tracker as part of the upgrade process. The Technical Design Report considers the possibility for the bi-phase CO2 coolant temperature to drop to as low as -55 degrees C in the case of a fault. The specification for the highest Relative Humidity within the ITk volume is therefore equivalent to a dew point temperature at or below -60 degrees C in order to prevent condensation which could damage the detector electronics. The design accommodates for humidity monitoring to detect the onset of such events and dry nitrogen flushing to remove moisture. Therefore, it is important to thoroughly understand all consequences of atmospheric air ingress due to air-leaks and/or air-ingress from the outlets due to the over-pressure. The computational fluid dynamics model presented in this study was used to provide quantitative and qualitative insight into the various operational and failure conditions, informing engineering design changes to optimise the flushing scheme and ensure that the ITk remains dry and within the design specification of the acceptable dew point range.

### [100] [A Modular Zero-Dead-Time Data Acquisition and Real-Time GPU Processing Platform for High Throughput Physics Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08845)

Result: 平台在500 MSa/s采样率下可持续处理1 GB/s数据吞吐量；通过端到端相位连续性测试，将分数数据损失限制在10^{-12}以下；实现了持续一个月的无中断稳定运行；在WISPLC暗物质实验中以124 MSa/s运行，分辨率带宽达0.1 Hz，并通过实时频谱平均大幅降低了数据存储需求。

Furthermore, long-term system stability was demonstrated through an uninterrupted one-month data acquisition run. In its current deployment for the WISPLC dark matter experiment, the platform operates at 124 MSa/s with a resolution bandwidth of 0.1 Hz. This implementation enabled a significant reduction in data storage requirements using real-time spectral averaging. The callback-driven software architecture, multi-GPU workload distribution, and custom hardware shielding solutions are detailed, establishing this platform as a flexible and cost-effective alternative to traditional hardware-based pipelines.

### [101] [Quasiparticle Quality Factors in Superconducting Resonators: Effects of Bath Temperature and Readout Power](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08591)
*Zhenyuan Sun,S Withington,Songyuan Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于修正Rothwarf-Taylor方程的宏观模型，通过引入与微波读取功率相关的声子产生项，明确给出了超导谐振器品质因子（quality factor）与浴温度（bath temperature）及读取功率（readout power）之间的显式关系。模型在NbN微带谐振器上得到了实验验证，精确刻画了热主导损耗与微波诱导损耗之间的转变，为高Q值量子器件设计提供了预测工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导谐振器在量子技术中广泛使用，但其品质因子在低温下常常偏离标准Mattis-Bardeen理论的预测。这种偏差通常归因于微波读取功率产生的非热准粒子（nonthermal quasiparticles），限制了超导器件的灵敏度。现有理论无法准确描述这一现象，亟需一个能够同时考虑热效应和微波功率效应的预测模型。

Method: 基于修正的Rothwarf-Taylor方程（Rothwarf-Taylor equations）建立宏观模型，引入一个与功率相关的声子产生项（power-dependent phonon generation term），从而建立品质因子、浴温度和读取功率之间的显式关系。

Result: 模型与带有β-Ta端接的NbN微带谐振器在不同读取功率水平（dynamic range）下的温度扫描测量结果高度吻合，准确捕捉了从热主导损耗（thermally-dominated loss）到微波诱导损耗（microwave-induced loss）的转变区域。

Conclusion: 该框架为超导谐振器的优化提供了一个预测工具，可推动用于量子传感（quantum sensing）和量子信息处理（quantum information processing）的高Q值器件设计。

Abstract: The performance of superconducting resonators underpins a wide range of modern quantum technologies, yet their quality factor often deviates at low temperatures from standard Mattis-Bardeen predictions. This discrepancy is often attributed to nonthermal quasiparticles generated by microwave readout power, which limits the sensitivity of superconducting devices. We present a macroscopic model based on modified Rothwarf-Taylor equations that incorporates a power-dependent phonon generation term, providing an explicit relationship between quality factor, bath temperature and readout power. The model shows excellent agreement with temperature sweep measurements of NbN microstrip resonators with \b{eta}-Ta terminations over a wide dynamic range of readout power levels, accurately capturing the transition between thermally-dominated and microwave-induced loss regimes. This framework provides a predictive tool for optimizing superconducting resonators and advancing the design of high-Q devices for quantum sensing and quantum information processing.

### [102] [Hole-Doping Suppresses Competing Magnetism in High-DOS C136 Carbon Schwarzite: A Computational Route Toward Superconductivity in Negative-Curvature Carbon Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09690)
*Eugene Yashin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，系统研究了D型C136碳负曲率结构（carbon schwarzite）中磁性、掺杂与高态密度金属行为之间的竞争关系，发现空穴掺杂可以有效抑制竞争性磁性分支，同时保留高态密度金属态，为超导电性筛选提供了潜在电子条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碳负曲率结构（carbon schwarzite）作为一类具有独特电子结构的负曲率碳网络，其磁性与金属行为之间的竞争关系尚未被充分理解。本文旨在通过自旋极化的第一性原理筛选研究，揭示D型C136 schwarzite在磁性、掺杂与高态密度（high-DOS）金属行为之间的相互作用机制。

Method: 采用自旋极化（spin-polarized）的第一性原理计算方法，对D型C136碳负曲率结构进行系统筛选。通过中性及带电胞计算，分析电子-空穴不对称性（electron-hole asymmetry）；对最强空穴掺杂点h8进行自旋极化的非自洽计算（NSCF）和态密度（DOS）计算，采用4×4×4 k点网格（k-point mesh）。

Result: 中性C136具有约11.01–11.03 Bohr磁子/136原子胞的竞争性磁性分支。带电胞计算显示明显的电子-空穴不对称性：添加两个电子使总磁化强度升至12.11 Bohr磁子/胞，移除两个电子则降至9.61。进一步空穴掺杂单调抑制磁性分支，移除4、6、8个电子时分别降至8.02、6.34和4.76 Bohr磁子/胞。h8点的NSCF费米能（Fermi energy）为-0.7414 eV，与SCF值-0.7413 eV一致；在E=-0.740 eV处总DOS约为44.69 states/eV/cell，其中DOS_up=33.11、DOS_down=11.58 states/eV/cell。

Conclusion: 空穴掺杂可有效抑制C136 schwarzite中的竞争性磁性不稳定性（competing magnetic instability），同时保留高态密度金属态（high-DOS metallic state），这为进一步的超导电性（superconductivity）筛选提供了有利的电子条件。但晶格稳定性、电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）及转变温度估计等问题仍有待解决。

Abstract: Carbon schwarzites are negative-curvature carbon networks with electronic structures distinct from graphene, fullerenes, and conventional carbon allotropes. Here we report a spin-polarized first-principles screening study of D-type C136 carbon schwarzite focused on the competition between magnetism, doping, and high-DOS metallic behavior. Neutral C136 has a robust competing magnetic branch, with total magnetization of about 11.01-11.03 Bohr magnetons per 136-atom cell. Charged-cell calculations reveal a clear electron-hole asymmetry: adding two electrons per cell increases the total magnetization to 12.11 Bohr magnetons per cell, while removing two electrons reduces it to 9.61. Further hole doping suppresses the magnetic branch monotonically, giving 8.02, 6.34, and 4.76 Bohr magnetons per cell for removal of 4, 6, and 8 electrons, respectively.
  The most strongly hole-doped point, h8, was examined with spin-polarized NSCF and density-of-states calculations on a 4x4x4 k-point mesh. The NSCF Fermi energy, -0.7414 eV, agrees with the SCF value, -0.7413 eV. The DOS remains high near the Fermi level: at E = -0.740 eV, the total DOS is about 44.69 states/eV/cell, with DOS_up = 33.11 and DOS_down = 11.58 states/eV/cell. Thus h8 combines substantial suppression of the competing magnetic branch with preservation of a high-DOS metallic state.
  We do not claim superconductivity in C136. Instead, these calculations identify hole doping as a route for suppressing a competing magnetic instability while preserving electronic conditions relevant for further superconductivity screening. Lattice stability, electron-phonon coupling, and transition-temperature estimates remain open problems.

</details>


### [103] [Superconductivity Mediated Long Range Magnetic Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10139)
*Ming Yan Wang,Yi Liu,Yao Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究Rashba超导体薄膜上放置铁磁绝缘体（FI）的系统，发现铁磁绝缘体会产生环形超电流，进而导致长程磁相互作用（LRMI），其衰减服从幂律。静态下该相互作用可以是铁磁性的，与先前研究中超导体会介导指数衰减的反铁磁相互作用相反；动态下LRMI具有不同的距离依赖性。结果对超导自旋电子学有潜在应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Rashba超导体薄膜中由铁磁绝缘体（ferromagnetic insulators, FIs）引发的长程磁相互作用（long-range magnetic interactions, LRMI）的物理特性，并揭示其与传统超导介质中磁相互作用的差异。

Method: 对一个顶部放置了铁磁绝缘体（FIs）的Rashba超导体薄膜系统进行理论研究，分析铁磁绝缘体引发的环形超电流（circular super-currents）及其产生的磁相互作用。

Result: 铁磁绝缘体产生环形超电流，使长程磁相互作用（LRMI）以幂律（power law）形式衰减。静态下LRMI可以是铁磁性的，且其衰减律为幂律而非指数律；动态下LRMI的距离依赖性不同于静态情况。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了Rashba超导体薄膜中可实现长程铁磁相互作用，颠覆了传统认识中超导体仅介导指数衰减反铁磁相互作用的观点，对超导自旋电子学（superconducting spintronics）具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We study a Rashba superconductor thin film with ferromagnetic insulators (FIs) placed on top of it. We show that the ferromagnetic insulators generate circular super-currents, enabling long-range magnetic interactions (LRMI), decaying in power laws. In the static case, the long-range magnetic interaction can be ferromagnetic, in contrast to previous studies showing that superconductor mediates anti-ferromagnetic interactions decaying exponentially. Surprisingly, we find that in the dynamic case, the LRMI has a different distance dependence. Our results have potential applications in superconducting spintronics.

### [104] [Apparent double-$T_c$ from a single BKT transition in anisotropic phase-only models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10226)
*Pei-Yuan Cai,Yi Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过研究各向异性相控约瑟夫森结阵列，证明了在外界平衡下仅存在单一BKT相变，而各向异性耦合和耗散会在有限尺寸、有限电流的交叉区中产生视在的双转变温度（double-$T_c$），但临界标度分析仍与单一$T_{\mathrm{BKT}}$一致，从而为非理想各向异性基线下仍观察到的稳健分裂提供了超越经典机制的物理线索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维超导体输运实验常观测到方向依赖的超导转变温度（$T_c$），引发争论：这种“双转变温度（double-$T_c$）”是真实的热力学分裂还是输运伪影？本文旨在建立一个干净的基线模型来区分这两种可能性。

Method: 采用最小各向异性纯相位约瑟夫森结阵列（phase-only Josephson-junction array），在平衡态和阻分路结（resistively shunted junction, RSJ）动力学下施加涨落扭结边界条件（fluctuating twist boundary conditions），通过数值模拟研究有限尺寸、有限电流交叉区中的电阻-温度（$R$-$T$）曲线行为，并与Halperin-Nelson拟合、固定电阻阈值以及临界标度准则（universal exponent $α=3$和动态有限尺寸标度）进行比较。

Result: 平衡模型仅表现出单一的Berezinskii–Kosterlitz–Thouless (BKT)相变。非平衡下，各向异性约瑟夫森耦合和各向异性耗散在有限尺寸、有限电流交叉区重塑线性$R$-$T$曲线，使得基于曲线形状准则（Halperin-Nelson拟合和固定电阻阈值）的人为标准产生视在的double-$T_c$。相反，临界标度准则（universal exponent $α=3$和动态有限尺寸标度）始终与单一$T_{\mathrm{BKT}}$一致。

Conclusion: 在干净的基线各向异性模型下，double-$T_c$可由输运伪影解释，而非真实热力学分裂。若非线性临界标度中仍存在稳健的分裂（如近期KTaO$_3$界面报道的结果），则指向超越此经典各向异性基线的物理机制。

Abstract: Transport experiments on two-dimensional superconductors often yield direction-dependent transition temperatures, raising the question of whether such a ``double-$T_c$'' reflects a true thermodynamic splitting or a transport artifact. To establish a baseline, we study a minimal anisotropic phase-only Josephson-junction array in equilibrium and under resistively shunted junction dynamics with fluctuating twist boundary conditions. The equilibrium model exhibits a single Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless (BKT) transition. Out of equilibrium, anisotropic Josephson couplings and anisotropic dissipation reshape the linear $R$--$T$ curves in a finite-size, finite-current crossover regime, so that curve-shape criteria such as Halperin--Nelson fits and fixed-resistance thresholds yield an apparent double-$T_c$. In contrast, critical-scaling criteria -- the universal exponent $α=3$ and dynamic finite-size scaling -- remain consistent with the single $T_{\mathrm{BKT}}$. A robust splitting that persists in the nonlinear critical scaling, such as that recently reported at KTaO$_3$ interfaces, therefore points to physics beyond this clean anisotropic baseline.

</details>


### [105] [Layer-antisymmetric pair-phase resonance at the bonding-antibonding splitting in the AA-stacked bilayer attractive Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10387)
*Yogeshwar Prasad*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文在双层AA堆叠吸引性哈伯德蜂巢晶格（AA-stacked attractive-Hubbard honeycomb bilayer）的高斯涨落（Gaussian fluctuation）层次上，发现层反称对相位通道（layer-antisymmetric pair-phase channel）中存在一个带隙内集体极点（in-gap collective pole），其频率精确等于单粒子层间跳跃（interlayer hopping）的两倍（2t_h），即键-反键能带劈裂。该共振尺度由单粒子杂化（single-particle hybridization）而非相互作用驱动的约瑟夫森耦合（Josephson coupling）决定，并可通过冷原子层偏置实验探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层超导体系中，相对相位（relative phase）是区别于同相安德森-博戈留波夫模（Anderson-Bogoliubov mode）的独立集体自由度。理解该自由度的集体激发特性，对于揭示双层配对体系中非传统集体模式及其实验可寻性具有重要意义。

Method: 作者在AA堆叠吸引性哈伯德蜂巢双层晶格模型中进行高斯涨落层次的理论分析，结合解析推导与数值博戈留波夫-德热纳（Bogoliubov-de Gennes, BdG）计算，研究层反称对相位通道的集体激发核（kernel）结构，并考察其在不同化学势下的行为。

Result: 层反称相位通道在频率ω=2t_h处存在一个带隙内集体极点，该频率恰好等于键-反键能带劈裂。该极点来源于代数机制：在该频率下，反称相位气泡（bubble）在动量空间中逐点退化为对称相位气泡，而后者恰是产生同相戈德斯通极（Goldstone pole）的原因。该共振尺度固定于单粒子杂化（2t_h），而非传统的莱格特模（Leggett mode）中由约瑟夫森耦合主导的尺度。反称相位通道核在化学势任意时均精确为零；完整振幅-相位耦合极点在半填充时与之重合，远离半填充时也紧密追踪。该激发在拉曼（Raman）光谱中被宇称禁止，因此层奇探测更为适合。层不平衡驱动（layer-imbalance drive）与对相位扇区（pair-phase sector）具有有限的高斯级重叠，表明在典型光晶格参数下可能探测到亚千赫兹（sub-kilohertz）尺度的层偏置响应特征。

Conclusion: 双层超导体中反相对相位通道的集体激发频率由单粒子杂化（2t_h）而非相互作用决定，这一机制为莱格特模提供了一种替代图像。该模式可通过冷原子系统的层偏置实验实现探测，为实验上观测这种非传统集体激发提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The relative phase between the two pair condensates of a bilayer s-wave superconductor is a collective degree of freedom distinct from the usual in-phase Anderson-Bogoliubov mode. Working at the Gaussian fluctuation level for the AA-stacked attractive-Hubbard honeycomb bilayer, we show analytically that the layer-antisymmetric pair-phase channel hosts an in-gap collective pole at twice the single-particle interlayer hopping, $2t_h$, precisely the bonding-antibonding band splitting. The mechanism is algebraic: at this frequency, the antisymmetric phase bubble reduces pointwise in momentum space to the static symmetric phase bubble that enforces the in-phase Goldstone pole. The resulting resonance scale is therefore fixed by the single-particle hybridization, rather than by the interaction-driven Josephson coupling that controls the canonical Leggett mode. The identity is verified numerically by direct Bogoliubov-de Gennes calculations. The diagonal antisymmetric phase-channel kernel zero is exact within Gaussian theory at any chemical potential; the full coupled amplitude-phase pole coincides with it at half filling and tracks it closely away from half filling. The excitation is Raman-forbidden by inversion, which motivates layer-odd probes. We find that a layer-imbalance drive has finite Gaussian-level overlap with the pair-phase sector, suggesting a possible cold-atom layer-bias response feature near the sub-kilohertz scale for typical optical-lattice parameters.

</details>


### [106] [Ginzburg--Landau Theory for Confined Thin-Film Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10686)
*Giovanni A. Ummarino,Alessio Zaccone*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文建立了量子限域超导薄膜的Ginzburg-Landau理论，从微观BCS自由能出发推导出限域几何中的G-L系数、相干长度、穿透深度等解析表达式。核心发现是量子限域通过修正电子态密度和费米能直接重整化本征超导相干长度，同时压制相干长度并增强穿透深度，驱动超导体向更强的第二类超导行为转变。理论与Al薄膜穿透深度实验吻合，建立了量子限域与超导电动力学之间的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于表面散射的传统薄膜输运理论无法解释量子限域对超导相干长度的直接重整化效应，需要建立一套能够统一描述量子限域下超导薄膜电动力学行为的理论框架。

Method: 从微观BCS自由能出发，结合金属薄膜的限域理论，推导出Ginzburg-Landau系数、相干长度、穿透深度、电子平均自由程和Ginzburg-Landau参数在限域几何中的显式解析表达式。

Result: 量子限域通过改变电子态密度和费米能直接重整化本征超导相干长度，该效应在仅考虑表面散射的传统理论中缺失。限域同时压制相干长度并增强穿透深度，使超导体随膜厚减小而向更强的第二类超导行为（type-II behavior）演化。理论预测存在一个限域重整化超导长度尺度与输运散射强烈交织的交叉区域。与Al薄膜穿透深度测量实验的比较表明，观测到的穿透深度增强源于相干长度的限域重整化与表面及无序散射对有效平均自由程的压制之间的相互作用。

Conclusion: 该理论建立了量子限域与限域金属薄膜超导电动力学之间的直接联系，为理解超导薄膜中量子尺寸效应提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: We develop a Ginzburg--Landau theory for superconducting thin films under quantum confinement. Starting from the microscopic BCS free energy and the recently developed confinement theory of metallic thin films, explicit analytical expressions are derived for the Ginzburg--Landau coefficients, coherence length, penetration depth, electronic mean free path, and Ginzburg--Landau parameter in confined geometries. The central result is that quantum confinement directly renormalizes the intrinsic superconducting coherence length through confinement-induced modifications of the electronic density of states and Fermi energy. This effect is absent in conventional thin-film transport theories based solely on surface scattering. As a consequence, confinement simultaneously suppresses the coherence length and enhances the penetration depth, thereby driving superconductors toward progressively stronger type-II behavior with decreasing film thickness. The theory predicts a crossover regime in which confinement-induced renormalization of superconducting length scales and transport scattering become strongly intertwined. Comparison with recent penetration-depth measurements in Al thin films shows that the observed enhancement of the penetration depth originates from the interplay between confinement-induced renormalization of the coherence length and suppression of the effective mean free path by surface and disorder scattering. The results establish a direct connection between quantum confinement and superconducting electrodynamics in confined metallic films.

</details>


### [107] [Transverse Magnetic Response from Orbitally Polarized Cooper Pairs in Elemental Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10700)
*Gabor Csire,Maria Teresa Mercaldo,Balazs Ujfalussy,Carmine Ortix,Mario Cuoco*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过超导密度泛函理论（superconducting density functional theory）证明，晶体对称性降低（如应变）可使钒、铌等元素超导体实现由相同轨道角动量电子组成的自旋单态轨道极化库珀对。该轨道极化超导态在磁场下会产生垂直于外加场的轨道磁化，为超导轨道电子学（superconducting orbitronics）提供了最小材料平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索元素超导体中通过晶体对称性降低（crystal symmetry lowering）实现轨道极化库珀对（orbitally polarized Cooper pairs）的可行性，并寻找可实验观测的特征信号。

Method: 采用超导密度泛函理论（superconducting density functional theory, SCDFT）进行第一性原理计算，分析对称性从三方晶系（trigonal）降低至Cs（仅保留单一镜面）后的轨道间配对（interorbital pairing）行为，并计算相应的磁响应。

Result: 对称性降低激活了体相和(111)表面的轨道间配对，且表面效应显著增强。在破坏剩余镜面对称的面内磁场下，会产生垂直于外加场的显著轨道磁化（orbital magnetization），这是等轨道角动量库珀配对（equal-orbital-moment Cooper pairing）的直接结果。

Conclusion: 钒、铌等受应变元素超导体是实现超导轨道电子学（superconducting orbitronics）的最小材料平台，其轨道磁化效应可作为轨道极化超导态的实验可观测特征。

Abstract: We demonstrate how crystalline symmetry lowering, as for instance through strain, allows elemental superconductors such as vanadium and niobium to realize spin-singlet orbitally polarized Cooper pairs composed of electrons with identical orbital moments. Using superconducting density functional theory, we show that lowering of trigonal symmetry to $C_s$, thus keeping only a single mirror plane, activates interorbital pairing in bulk and (111) surfaces, with a pronounced surface enhancement. In a magnetic field, the resulting orbitally polarized superconducting state leads to a novel transverse magnetic response. For in--plane field orientations that break the remaining mirror symmetry, a sizable orbital magnetization emerges perpendicular to the applied field. We show that this effect is a direct consequence of equal--orbital-moment Cooper pairing, providing an experimentally accessible signature of this state. Our results establish strained elemental superconductors as a minimal material platform for superconducting orbitronics.

### [108] [Freestanding GdBa2Cu3O7 Thin Films via Optimized Buffer Layer Design: Preserving Superconducting Properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10703)
*Kazumasa Iida,Kai Walter,Takafumi Hatano,Kose Morinaga,Manuela Erbe,Hongye Gao,Satoshi Hata,Jens Hänisch*

TL;DR: 本研究利用水溶性Sr3Al2O6牺牲层结合热释放胶带制备了自支撑GdBa2Cu3O7 (GdBCO)超导薄膜，并引入非晶Al2O3覆盖层抑制剥离过程中的裂纹形成。系统研究了GdBCO与牺牲层之间缓冲层设计对结构完整性和超导性能的影响，发现LaAlO3/SrTiO3双层缓冲层对维持外延生长和约92 K的超导转变温度（Tc）至关重要，而缓冲层堆叠顺序的错误会显著抑制Tc。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 制备高质量的自支撑（freestanding）高温超导薄膜是实现柔性超导器件应用的关键步骤，但如何在剥离过程中保持薄膜的结构完整性和超导特性仍面临挑战。本研究旨在通过优化缓冲层设计来解决这一问题。

Method: 采用水溶性Sr3Al2O6 (SAO)牺牲层结合热释放胶带进行剥离；在GdBCO薄膜上方引入非晶Al2O3覆盖层以抑制裂纹形成；系统比较了不同缓冲层结构（LaAlO3/SrTiO3双层、反向SrTiO3/LaAlO3双层及单层缓冲层）对薄膜性能的影响。

Result: LaAlO3/SrTiO3双层缓冲层能够在剥离后维持外延生长（epitaxial growth）并保持约92 K的超导转变温度（Tc），与生长态薄膜相当；而反向堆叠的SrTiO3/LaAlO3双层以及单层缓冲结构均导致Tc显著下降。

Conclusion: 缓冲层设计的优化，特别是堆叠顺序的选择，是制备高质量自支撑GdBCO薄膜并保持其超导特性的关键因素。

Abstract: Freestanding GdBa2Cu3O7 (GdBCO) superconducting thin films were fabricated using a water-soluble Sr3Al2O6 (SAO) sacrificial layer in combination with thermal release tape. An amorphous Al2O3 capping layer was introduced to suppress crack formation during the lift-off process. The influence of buffer-layer design inserted between the GdBCO and SAO layers was systematically investigated with respect to structural integrity and superconducting properties after lift-off. A LaAlO3/SrTiO3 bilayer buffer was found to be essential for maintaining epitaxial growth and a superconducting transition temperature (Tc) of approximately 92 K after lift-off, comparable to that of the as-grown films. In contrast, a reversed SrTiO3/LaAlO3 bilayer and single-layer buffer structures led to a suppression of Tc, highlighting the critical role of stacking sequence. These results demonstrate that optimization of the buffer-layer design is a key factor for realizing high-quality freestanding GdBCO films while maintaining their superconducting characteristics.

### [109] [Anomalous and diode Josephson effect in junctions with inhomogeneous ferromagnetic barrier and interfacial Rashba spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10740)
*Stevan Djurdjević,Zorica Popović*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了二维平面约瑟夫森结中的反常约瑟夫森效应（anomalous Josephson effect）和二极管约瑟夫森效应（diode Josephson effect），通过对称性分析、广义Furusaki-Tsukada方法数值计算以及Andreev束缚态（ABS）谱分析，揭示了打破时间反演和空间反演对称性的最小条件，并发现通过调控交换场方向、Rashba自旋轨道耦合（SOC）及超导序参量取向，非互易性可增强超过40%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索二维平面约瑟夫森结中，在任意取向交换场和界面自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）共同作用下，反常约瑟夫森效应和二极管约瑟夫森效应的物理起源与调控机制，特别是针对d-波超导电极的情形。

Method: 采用对称性分析（symmetry analysis）研判结哈密顿量中时间反演和空间反演对称性破缺的最小条件；利用广义Furusaki-Tsukada（F-T）方法数值计算电流-相位关系（current-phase relation, CPR）；通过分析相位依赖的Andreev束缚态（Andreev bound states, ABS）谱及其对电荷输运的贡献，并与F-T方法的结果进行对比。

Result: 将约瑟夫森结分为三类，重点关注d_{x^2-y^2}与d_{xy}取向超导体之间的结；通过调控铁磁层交换场方向、界面Rashba SOC及超导序参量取向，非互易性可提升超过40%；在ABS谱出现零能交叉（zero energy crossings）时，以及d-波超导电极因超导能隙较窄甚至闭合时，连续态对电流的贡献显著增强；非互易区ABS谱呈现相对于相位反转（phase inversion）的不对称轮廓，表明零相位差下存在有限电流且正反方向临界电流不等。

Conclusion: 明确指出了反常和二极管约瑟夫森效应所需的最小对称性破缺条件，揭示了不同因素协同增强非互易性的可行路径，并阐明了ABS与连续态在不同超导配对对称性下的输运贡献差异，为基于d-波超导体的非互易约瑟夫森器件提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the anomalous and diode Josephson effects in planar two-dimensional Josephson junctions with arbitrarily oriented exchange fields in two ferromagnets within the barrier, and spin-orbit coupling at the superconductor/ferromagnet interfaces, where the superconducting electrodes can have $s$-wave or arbitrarily oriented $d$-wave order parameter lobes. We perform a systematic symmetry analysis of the junction Hamiltonian and identify the minimal conditions for breaking time-reversal and space-inversion symmetries, which are required for the emergence of anomalous and diode Josephson effects. We classify the junctions into three classes, with particular attention to those between $d_{x^2-y^2}$ and $d_{xy}$ oriented superconductors. Our symmetry analysis is supported by numerical calculations of the current-phase relation (CPR) obtained using a generalized Furusaki-Tsukada (F-T) approach. By tuning the directions of exchange fields in the ferromagnets, Rashba SOC at the interfaces and superconducting order parameter orientations, nonreciprocity can be enhanced by more than 40\%. We further analyze the phase-dependent Andreev bound states (ABS) spectrum and their contribution to charge transport, as well as their signatures in the nonreciprocal transport characteristics. By comparing the current carried by ABS with that obtained using the F-T technique, we find that the contribution from continuum states above the gap becomes pronounced in presence of zero energy crossings in the ABS spectrum, and in junctions with $d$-wave superconducting electrodes due to the narrower superconducting gap, which may become closed. In the nonreciprocal regime, the ABS spectra show an asymmetric profile with respect to phase inversion, indicating the presence of a finite current at zero phase difference and unequal critical currents in opposite directions.

### [110] [Analytical solution of traversable wormholes in the presence of positive cosmological constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08205)
*Rajesh Karmakar,Xian-Hui Ge*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用引力解耦（gravitational decoupling, GD）方法，在正宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）Λ>0 条件下，构建了一个可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole, WH）的解析解。该解基于 Ellis-Bronnikov 虫洞几何，引入了宇宙学常数诱导的变形，形成了两个喉部（throat），并验证了耀出条件（flare-out condition）和零能量条件（null energy condition, NEC）的违反，同时分析了人类安全穿越所需的潮汐力与速度约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在含宇宙学常数Λ的条件下构建可穿越虫洞面临重大挑战，会使时空几何产生非平凡修正；这项工作旨在克服这些困难，获得一个在Λ>0情形下的解析可穿越虫洞解。

Method: 采用引力解耦（gravitational decoupling, GD）方法，以Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞几何为种子解，推导由宇宙学常数项诱导的度规变形；通过该框架引入第二个宇宙学喉部，并分析其几何与物理性质。

Result: 得到的虫洞解并非渐近de Sitter（de Sitter）时空，而是呈现修正的渐近行为；两个喉部均满足耀出条件，并在其附近发现零能量条件（null energy condition, NEC）被违反；通过潮汐力计算得出人类安全穿越所需的速度约束条件。

Conclusion: 引力解耦方法能够有效构建含正宇宙学常数的可穿越虫洞解；该解具有双喉部结构及修正渐近行为，同时满足可穿越虫洞的必要条件，包括NEC违反和可行的潮汐力约束。

Abstract: The construction of traversable wormholes (WHs) with a cosmological constant, $Λ$, introduces significant challenges and leads to non-trivial modifications of the spacetime geometry. In this work, we obtain an analytical solution describing a traversable WH for $Λ>0$ by utilizing the gravitational decoupling (GD) method. In this framework, we consider the Ellis-Bronnikov WH geometry and derive the corresponding deformation induced by the cosmological constant term. In addition to modifying the standard WH throat, this contribution leads to a cosmological throat. The resulting configuration, however, is not asymptotically de Sitter, instead, it exhibits modified asymptotic behaviour. Nevertheless, we verify that the flare-out condition holds at both throats and find violation of the null energy condition in their vicinity, as required for traversable WHs. Traversability is further analyzed by evaluating tidal forces and deriving constraints on the velocity required for safe human passage.

### [111] [A Constraint-Free Formulation of Black Hole Thermodynamics from the Field Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08235)
*Geonwoo Ahn,Ijin Bae,Geunyeong Jang,Yongjoon Kwon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无约束（constraint-free）方法，推广了Padmanabhan从爱因斯坦场方程直接推导黑洞热力学第一定律的方案。通过将视界场方程乘以熵变dS而非体积变分dV，该方法无需额外约束即可同时处理多视界变化，并在更高导数引力理论中仍然有效。此外，作者在热力学态空间(M,J,Q)中直接证明，外视界上的爱因斯坦场方程可无需约束地解释为黑洞热力学第一定律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在推导多视界黑洞的热力学第一定律时，只能通过施加额外约束（constraint）将变分限制在外视界上，并通过将外视界上的场方程乘以体积变分dV来引入PdV项。然而，一般变分会同时移动内外两个视界，因此需要一种无需约束、同时考虑所有视界变化的统一方案。

Method: 作者舍弃对各视界场方程施加约束的做法，转而将视界场方程乘以熵变dS（entropy variation）而非体积变分dV，从而自然地纳入所有视界的变化。此外，作者直接在热力学态空间（thermodynamic state space）(M,J,Q)中重新表述场方程，避免了以往基于r±变分方案在处理三参数黑洞（M,J,Q）时的失效问题。

Result: 该方法在爱因斯坦引力和更高导数引力中均有效；基于r±变分的方案对于由三个独立参数表征的黑洞会系统性失效，而基于(M,J,Q)态空间的方法则能直接得到无需额外约束的第一定律形式。

Conclusion: 外视界上的爱因斯坦场方程可以在无约束的条件下直接解释为黑洞热力学第一定律，且这一解释不依赖于具体的引力理论或黑洞参数数目。

Abstract: We develop a constraint-free formulation that generalizes Padmanabhan's method for deriving the first law of black hole thermodynamics directly from the Einstein field equations. In previous studies, even for multi-horizon black holes, variations were restricted to the outer horizon by imposing an additional constraint, and the PdV term was introduced by multiplying the field equations evaluated at the outer horizon by the corresponding volume variation dV. However, since general variations of the black hole parameters shift both horizons, variations at both horizons must be taken into account. To this end, we propose multiplying the horizon field equations by the entropy variation dS under such unconstrained variations. We show that this method remains valid even in higher-derivative theories of gravity. In addition, we find that $r_{\pm}$-based variation schemes generically break down for black holes characterized by three independent parameters (M,J,Q). By working directly in the thermodynamic state space (M,J,Q), we show that the Einstein field equations evaluated at the outer horizon can be also interpreted as the first law of black hole thermodynamics for general variations without imposing any additional constraints.

</details>


### [112] [Bipartite temporal Bell inequality for squeezed coherent state of inflationary perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08428)
*Aurindam Mondal*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在原始扰动初态由Bunch-Davies真空替换为相干态时，二分时域贝尔不等式（bipartite temporal Bell inequality）在探测原始扰动量子印记中的作用，发现该场景下不存在时域贝尔违背，且时域贝尔不等式对波函数纯虚相位因子的依赖是空间贝尔不等式所不具备的特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在宇宙学场景中，观测约束通常只允许访问赝自旋算符（pseudo-spin operator）的一个分量，而空间贝尔不等式（spatial Bell inequality）需要两组不同的可观测量。本文旨在利用仅需单一分量在不同时间测量的时域贝尔不等式，探究当初始态由Bunch-Davies真空替换为相干态（coherent state）时，原始扰动（primordial perturbations）的量子印记是否可被探测。

Method: 假设相干态作为宇宙早期涨落的初始条件，推导二分时域贝尔算符期望值的解析表达式，并与压缩真空态（squeezed vacuum state）情形进行对比分析。

Result: 在相干态初始条件下，不存在时域贝尔违背（temporal Bell violation）。对于大压缩参数（squeezing parameter），压缩相干态（squeezed coherent state）的结果与压缩真空态存在细微差异。时域贝尔不等式对波函数纯虚相位因子（purely imaginary phase factor）的依赖是空间贝尔不等式所不具备的独特特征。

Conclusion: 区分原始扰动不同初始态的能力并不依赖于时域贝尔不等式的违背，而可能依赖于其他物理特征。时域贝尔不等式对波函数纯虚相位因子的独特敏感度，为区分不同初态提供了新的潜在途径。

Abstract: We investigate the role of the bipartite temporal Bell inequality, an analogue of the spatial Bell inequality, in probing the quantum imprints of primordial perturbations when the initially chosen Bunch-Davies vacuum is replaced by a coherent state. Although it is based on the same principles of locality and realism, its primary advantage lies in the fact that it does not require two distinct set of observable for its construction. Instead, measurements performed on a single component of the pseudo-spin operator at different times are sufficient. Consequently, it is particularly well suited for cosmological scenarios, where observational constraints typically allow access to only one component of the pseudo-spin operator. Assuming a coherent state as the initial condition, we derive an analytical expression for the expectation value of the bipartite temporal Bell operator and demonstrate the absence of temporal Bell violation in such a scenario. Interestingly, the results for squeezed coherent state is found to differ - albeit slightly - from those of squeezed vacuum state for large values of the squeezing parameter. This suggests that the ability to distinguish among different initial states of primordial perturbations does not rely on the violation of temporal Bell inequality. Furthermore, the dependence of the temporal Bell inequality on a purely imaginary phase factor of the wave function appears to be an unique feature, which is entirely absent in the context of spatial Bell inequalities.

### [113] [The Good, the Bad, and the Subtle: Relativistic mode sums for neutron-star tidal response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08569)
*Abhishek Hegade K. R.,K. J. Kwon,Tejaswi Venumadhav,Hang Yu,Nicolas Yunes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论框架下，针对非旋转中子星在Regge-Wheeler规范（gauge）中发展了一套实用的模式求和潮汐响应（mode-sum tidal response）方法。研究发现，主导的f模贡献与直接匹配计算吻合良好（误差约3%），但模式内积算符（inner product operator）在完整函数空间上非正定，导致模式求和截断至O(ω²)时不一定严格收敛；同时星内潮汐场存在非唯一性，但该歧义对主导f模响应影响有限。研究表明相对论模式求和的实用价值源于受控的低模描述，而非形式上的强场收敛展开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中子星晚期旋近阶段（late inspiral）中的时间依赖潮汐相互作用蕴含中子星结构的重要信息，但将牛顿力学中的模式求和图像系统性地推广到完整的广义相对论框架中并非易事。本文旨在解决该推广过程中的理论困难，发展一种实用的相对论性实现方法。

Method: 论文在Regge-Wheeler规范下，针对非旋转中子星发展了一套相对论性模式求和潮汐响应方法。具体而言，利用近区边界条件（near-zone boundary conditions）系统定义了内部潮汐场（interior tidal field）、相对论性交叠积分（relativistic overlap integrals）及相应的模式振幅（mode amplitudes）。

Result: 主导的f模贡献与直接匹配计算吻合良好，在所考虑的物态方程（equations of state）范围内误差约在3%以内。然而，控制模式内积的算符在完整Regge-Wheeler规范函数空间中并非正定（positive definite），因此截断至O(ω²)的相対论模式求和不一定会严格收敛于直接匹配解。此外，星内部的潮汐场不具有唯一性，但对于所研究的扩展类别，该歧义对主导f模响应的影响有限。

Conclusion: 研究结果确认了相对论模式求和近似的实用价值，但明确指出其预测能力源于受控的低模描述（controlled low-mode description），而非形式的强场收敛展开（formally convergent strong-field expansion）。

Abstract: Time-dependent tidal interactions during the late inspiral of binary neutron stars encode valuable information about neutron-star structure, but systematically extending the familiar Newtonian mode-sum picture into full general relativity is nontrivial. In this paper, we develop a practical relativistic implementation of mode-sum tidal response for non-rotating neutron stars in Regge-Wheeler gauge. Using near-zone boundary conditions, we systematically define the interior tidal field, the relativistic overlap integrals, and the corresponding mode amplitudes. The good is that the dominant f-mode contribution is remarkably robust, reproducing the direct matching calculation to within $\sim 3$\% across the equations of state we consider. The bad is that the operator governing mode inner product is not positive definite on the full Regge-Wheeler-gauge function space, so the relativistic mode sum truncated at ${\cal{O}}(ω^2)$ is not expected to strictly converge to the direct matching solution. The subtle is that the tidal field inside the star is not unique, although this ambiguity has only a limited impact on the dominant f-mode response for the classes of extensions studied here. Our results establish the practical utility of relativistic mode-sum approximations, while making clear that their predictive power comes from a controlled low-mode description, rather than from a formally convergent strong-field expansion.

</details>


### [114] [Black hole mass and distance from accretion disk astrophysical observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08582)
*J. R. Fernández-Moreno,A. González-Juárez,A. Herrera-Aguilar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用广义相对论（general relativity）方法描述黑洞附近发射光子的频率移动（frequency shifts），考虑两个发射体（或同一发射体在两个位置）沿观测者视线方向（line of sight, LOS）对称分布。引入红移快度（redshift rapidity）作为关键变量，推导黑洞质量与距离的独立表达式；并将结果推广至具有本动（peculiar motion）的天体物理系统。

Result: 得到了施瓦西黑洞质量、距离以及测试粒子轨道半径的解析表达式，这些表达式完全由沿整个轨道测量的可观测量定义。在存在本动运动的情况下，推导出了相应的闭合公式（closed formulas）。

Conclusion: 本文提供的解析框架允许仅基于轨道观测数据直接确定黑洞的基本参数（质量与距离），无需额外的模型假设，且可推广到存在系统本动的情况，增强了方法的实用性与普适性。

Abstract: In this work we derive novel analytical expressions for the mass and distance of a Schwarzschild black hole (BH), as well as for the orbital radius of test particles orbiting it, it terms of astrophysical observables measured throughout the entire orbit of the revolving particle. We use a general relativistic method to describe the frequency shifts of photons emitted in the vivinity of a BH by considering two emitters (or two positions of the same emitter) located symmetrically opposite to each other with respect to the observer's line of sight (LOS) when performing measurements along the orbit. Furthermore, the introduction of the redshift rapidity allows us to write independent expressions for the BH mass and its distance to Earth. We also extend our study to the case when astrophysical systems have a peculiar motion and derive the corresponding closed formulas.

### [115] [General Grad-Shafranov Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08597)

Main category: gr-qc

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无张力电动力学（force-free electrodynamics）中的Grad-Shafranov方程是描述强磁场等离子体平衡态电磁场全局结构的关键方程，广泛适用于托卡马克、日冕、地球磁层、中子星及黑洞等多种场景。然而，该方程在不同情况下的表达形式各异，推导过程也较为复杂，因此需要一种统一的通用表达式来简化这一过程。

Method: 采用微分形式（differential form）的数学语言，推导出Grad-Shafranov方程的一般形式，使其能够快速适应任意具体物理情境；此外，构建了一个标量场（scalar field）的拉格朗日密度（Lagrangian density），使得该标量场的壳上条件（on-shell condition）精确等价于Grad-Shafranov方程。

Result: 得到了一个通用的Grad-Shafranov方程表达式，该表达式可快速导出任意特定情境下的具体形式；还得到了一个拉格朗日密度，其对应的运动方程即为Grad-Shafranov方程。

Conclusion: 本文的通用表达式和拉格朗日形式为Grad-Shafranov方程在不同物理场景下的应用和进一步理论研究提供了简洁统一的框架。

Abstract: To effectively describe the plasma with strong magnetic field, the force-free electrodynamics was introduced, within which the Grad-Shafranov equation plays the key role. The Grad-Shafranov equation governs the global structure of a electromagnetic field in equilibrium with symmetries. It is widely applicable in an amount of scenarios, such as the tokamak, the solar corona, the magnetosphere of Earth, neutron star and black hole, etc. However, in different situations, the Grad-Shafranov equation is expressed differently, and the derivations might be complicated. In this work, via the language of differential form, we provide a general expression of Grad-Shafranov equation, from which the expression in any specific situation can be quickly obtained. Additionally, we present a Lagrangian density for a scalar field whose on-shell condition is precisely the Grad-Shafranov equation.

### [116] [Gravitational waveform from radial infall at the third-and-half Post-Newtonian order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08798)
*Giorgio Di Russo,Donato Bini*

Main category: gr-qc

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管径向落入运动在表面上具有一维运动的简单性，但该过程必然以粒子被黑洞捕获而告终，涉及强场效应；作者意在通过在PN近似有效区域内达到最高精度（3.5PN阶），为理解此类极端两体系统的引力波信号提供重要见解。

Method: 采用质心系（center-of-mass system）和后牛顿（post-Newtonian, PN）近似方法，计算与史瓦西黑洞中径向落入粒子相关联的引力波形，将精度推进至3.5PN阶，这同时包含了2.5PN和3.5PN阶的保守贡献（conservative contributions）和辐射反作用贡献（radiation-reaction contributions）。

Result: 得到的引力波形达到了文献中已完整展示的最高精度水平，即3.5后牛顿（3.5PN）阶，该精度涵盖了两体动力学中的保守项和辐射反作用项，以及波形中的相应效应。

Conclusion: 由于后牛顿（post-Newtonian, PN）近似本身定义的局限性，该分析无法捕捉粒子落入黑洞的最终强场阶段，但在PN近似有效区域内，该结果仍为径向落入过程提供了显著的见解。

Abstract: We compute the gravitational waveform associated with a radially infalling particle in a Schwarzschild black hole working in the center-of-mass system and in a post-Newtonian (PN) approximation. Our results reach the highest accuracy level fully displayed in the literature, namely the 3.5PN order. The latter accuracy includes both conservative and radiation-reaction contributions (at 2.5PN and 3.5PN) in the two-body dynamics, and corresponding effects in the waveform too. The apparent simplicity of the radial fall (namely, the 1-dimensional motion) contrasts with the peculiarity of the process which will end necessarily with the capture of the particle by the black hole, featuring strong field effects. In other words, our analysis being limited to the region of validity of the PN approximation, cannot capture (by definition of PN approximation) the final phase of the fall, but offers significant insights anyway.

### [117] [Late-Time Cosmic Acceleration in Ricci-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity via Gradient Descent Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08893)
*Santosh V. Lohakare,B. Mishra,S. K. Maurya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在f(R,G)引力框架下研究宇宙晚期演化，通过梯度下降法结合宇宙计时器（CC）和Pantheon+超新星数据约束模型参数，发现该模型能够自洽地解释宇宙晚期加速膨胀，且表现出类精质场（quintessence-like）行为，未穿越幻象分裂面（phantom divide）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种参数化方案（parametrization scheme），利用梯度下降法（Gradient Descent）拟合参数，约束数据来自最新的宇宙计时器（Cosmic Chronometer, CC）和Pantheon+超新星数据集。采用减速参数q、态方程参数w、能量条件分析以及Om(z)诊断工具进行一致性检验。

Result: 减速参数q和态方程参数w均显示从过去减速到当前加速膨胀的清晰转变；w保持在幻象分裂面（phantom divide, w=-1）之上，呈现类精质场（quintessence-like）行为。强能量条件被违反，弱能量条件和零能量条件保持满足。Om(z)诊断将该模型与标准宇宙学常数模型区分开，指示精质场主导的未来演化。宇宙年龄最佳拟合值与独立天体测量结果一致。

Conclusion: f(R,G)引力在结合CC与Pantheon+数据集的约束下，为宇宙晚期加速膨胀提供了一个可行且自洽的解释。

Abstract: We study the late-time evolution of the Universe within the f(R,G) gravity framework, where R is the Ricci scalar and G is the Gauss-Bonnet term. To make the model tractable, we propose a parametrization scheme and determine its parameters using Gradient Descent, with constraints coming from the latest Cosmic Chronometer (CC) and Pantheon+ supernova data. Key cosmological indicators, namely the deceleration parameter q and the equation-of-state parameter w, show a clear transition from past deceleration to the present accelerated expansion. Interestingly, the equation-of-state parameter w remains above the phantom divide, indicating quintessence-like behavior consistent with current observations. Energy-condition analysis further supports this framework: the strong energy condition is violated, consistent with models allowing cosmic acceleration, whereas both the weak and null energy conditions remain satisfied. To test consistency, we also apply the Om(z) diagnostic, which distinguishes this model from the standard cosmological constant scenario and indicates a quintessence-dominated future evolution. Using the best-fit values, we estimate the age of the Universe, obtaining good agreement with independent astrophysical measurements. Overall, the results suggest that f(R,G) gravity provides a viable and self-consistent explanation for late-time cosmic acceleration when constrained using the combined CC and Pantheon+ datasets.

### [118] [Neutron stars in a conservative $f(R,T)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09206)
*Ronaldo V. Lobato,Geanderson A. Carvalho,Carlos E. C. Montaña,Jose F. Rodriguez-Ruiz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种保守形式的 $f(R,T)$ 引力理论，通过有效能量-动量张量（effective energy-momentum tensor）重构理论，使引力作用量（gravitational action）不依赖于微观物态方程（equation of state, EoS），从而避免现有方法中引力函数依赖EoS而丧失普遍性的问题。作者导出了修正的恒星结构方程、理论一致性条件及潮汐扰动部分，并利用真实表格化EoS计算了中子星可观测量（质量-半径关系、潮汐形变能力），与来自大质量脉冲星、NICER半径测量和GW170817的当前天体物理约束进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有$f(R,T)$引力方法中，引力函数通常从所选物态方程（EoS）重构，导致引力部分依赖于EoS，破坏了理论的普遍性（universality）。本文旨在克服这一局限性，提出一种守恒形式，使引力作用量独立于微观物态方程。

Method: 将理论用有效能量-动量张量（effective energy-momentum tensor）重新表述，使守恒律由场方程（field equations）和Bianchi恒等式自然导出。推导了修正的恒星结构方程（stellar structure equations）、耦合界限（coupling bounds）和壳层奇点避免（crust-singularity avoidance）等理论一致性条件，并在潮汐扰动部分引入有效热力学变量（effective thermodynamic variables）和有效声速（effective sound speed）。

Result: 利用真实表格化EoS计算了中子星可观测量，包括质量-半径关系（mass-radius relations）和潮汐形变能力（tidal deformabilities）。将模型预测与来自大质量脉冲星（massive pulsars）、NICER半径测量以及GW170817引力波事件的天体物理约束进行了比较。

Conclusion: 所提出的守恒形式$f(R,T)$引力避免了理论对EoS的依赖性问题，且能通过中子星观测数据（质量-半径关系、潮汐形变）与现有天体物理约束进行有效检验，为修正引力理论在致密星物理中的应用提供了更具普遍性的框架。

Abstract: We investigate a conservative formulation of $f(R,T)$ gravity motivated by a key limitation of several existing approaches: the gravitational function is often reconstructed from a chosen equation of state, making the gravity sector EoS-dependent and compromising universality. To avoid this problem, we reformulate the theory in terms of an effective energy-momentum tensor, so that the conservation law follows from the field equations and Bianchi identities while the gravitational action remains independent of the microphysical EoS. We derive the modified stellar structure equations, establish theoretical consistency conditions including coupling bounds and crust-singularity avoidance, and present the tidal perturbation sector in terms of effective thermodynamic variables and an effective sound speed. We then compute neutron star observables using realistic tabulated EoSs, including mass-radius relations and tidal deformabilities, and compare the model with current astrophysical constraints from massive pulsars, NICER radius measurements, and GW170817.

### [119] [Efficient and Stable Computation of Gravitational-Wave Fluxes from Generic Kerr Orbits via a Unified HeunC Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09250)
*Changkai Chen,Zhoujian Cao,Jiliang Jing*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将角向和径向Teukolsky方程（Teukolsky equations）重新表述为合流Heun函数（confluent Heun functions）形式；采用混合解析延拓算法（hybrid analytic continuation algorithm）计算连接系数（connection coefficients），消除对辅助参数的依赖；针对一般轨道的高度振荡源被积函数，实现自适应双幂映射求积法（adaptive bi-power mapping quadrature）。

Result: 在标准双精度算术下，对168个低阶模式的总辐射通量求和，相对误差达10^{-11}量级；计算成本较现有最优包GeneralizedSasakiNakamura.jl降低2-3倍，较pybhpt降低3-10倍。

Conclusion: 本文方法在精度和效率上的提升使其成为强场微扰理论（strong-field perturbation theory）的稳健工具，为高阶自力计算（high-order self-force calculations）和快速高精度波形生成提供了数值基础。

Abstract: Modeling extreme-mass-ratio inspirals hinges on the accurate and efficient computation of gravitational-wave fluxes from generic Kerr orbits. Conventional frequency-domain techniques are often limited by costly auxiliary parameter searches and numerical instabilities in the strong-field or high-frequency regimes. We address these challenges by reformulating both the angular and radial Teukolsky equations in terms of confluent Heun functions. Employing a hybrid analytic continuation algorithm to compute the connection coefficients eliminates the dependence on auxiliary parameters, directly yielding globally convergent solutions and scattering amplitudes. To resolve the highly oscillatory source integrands for generic orbits, we implement an adaptive bi-power mapping quadrature. Comprehensive benchmarks under standard double-precision arithmetic demonstrate that, for the total radiative flux summed over 168 low-order modes, our method achieves relative errors of order $10^{-11}$, with computational costs typically reduced by factors of 2--3 and 3--10 compared to the state-of-the-art \texttt{GeneralizedSasakiNakamura.jl} and \texttt{pybhpt} packages, respectively. These demonstrated gains in precision and efficiency establish the framework as a robust tool for strong-field perturbation theory, providing the numerical foundation for high-order self-force calculations and rapid, high-precision waveform generation.

</details>


### [120] [Resonant transmission of scalar waves through rotating traversable wormhole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09426)
*Rajesh Karmakar,Bum-Hoon Lee,Wonwoo Lee*

TL;DR: 本文通过数值计算旋转可穿越虫洞（rotating traversable wormhole）中标量场的透射因子与吸收谱，发现由势阱束缚态导致的Breit-Wigner型共振峰，并证明旋转增强了共振强度，从而将其确定为虫洞几何结构的特征信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在由Teo类解描述的旋转可穿越虫洞时空中，分析无质量标量场（massless scalar field）的传播，并通过数值方法计算了宽频率范围内的透射（灰体）因子（transmission (greybody) factor）及对应的吸收谱（absorption spectrum）。

Result: 吸收谱在振幅上出现一系列尖锐峰值，被识别为Breit-Wigner型共振（Breit-Wigner-type resonances）。这些共振源于标量模被喉两侧势垒形成的势阱暂时束缚。旋转增强了共振强度。

Conclusion: 结果表明，旋转对共振效应具有塑造作用，且这些共振特征可作为虫洞几何结构的特征信号。

Abstract: The viability of traversable wormholes as exotic compact objects requires the identification of signatures that distinguish them from other compact objects. Given recent advances in observing rotating black hole signatures, identifying characteristic imprints that reflect the absence of an event horizon and the presence of a throat structure is of considerable significance. Motivated by this, in the present work, we analyze the propagation of a massless scalar field in a rotating traversable wormhole spacetime described by Teo's class of solutions. We numerically compute the transmission (greybody) factor and the corresponding absorption spectrum across a broad range of frequencies. The spectrum exhibits a series of sharp peaks in the amplitudes, which we identify as Breit-Wigner-type resonances. The emergence of such peaks can be attributed to the scalar modes temporarily trapped within the potential well formed by barriers on either side of the throat. These resonant features, previously identified in static wormhole backgrounds, persist in the rotating case. In particular, for Teo's class of wormholes, we find that rotation enhances the strength of the resonances. Overall, our results demonstrate the role of rotation in shaping the resonance effect and indicate these features as characteristic signatures of wormhole geometries.

### [121] [Multimessenger consistency tests of the Friedmann cosmological model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09660)
*Antonio Enea Romano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在弗里德曼宇宙学模型（Friedmann cosmological model）框架下，推导出独立于暗能量（dark energy）形式的多信使一致性条件（multimessenger consistency conditions），并将其用于检验宇宙曲率（curvature）和宇宙常数（cosmological constant），不依赖于暗能量状态方程（equation of state）和宇宙学密度参数（cosmological density parameters）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先，在弗里德曼模型框架下，利用引力波（gravitational wave, GW）和电磁波（electromagnetic wave, EMW）的光度距离（luminosity distance），推导出一个独立于暗能量状态方程（dark energy equation of state）的曲率参数（curvature parameter）关系式。然后，基于该关系式推导出独立于暗能量模型和宇宙学密度参数的一般性多信使一致性关系。作为特例，进一步推导出针对宇宙常数（cosmological constant）的多信使一致性检验，该检验不依赖于曲率密度和物质密度参数。

Result: 得到了一个仅用引力波和电磁波光度距离表示的曲率参数关系式，可用于独立于暗能量状态方程探测宇宙曲率；同时获得了弗里德曼模型下不依赖于暗能量模型和密度参数的一般多信使一致性条件，以及一个针对宇宙常数的、不依赖于曲率和物质密度参数的多信使一致性检验。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，多信使天文学（multimessenger astronomy）能够为检验弗里德曼宇宙学模型提供独立于暗能量形式和宇宙学密度参数的一致性条件，尤其可用于检验宇宙常数假设和宇宙曲率，具有重要的宇宙学应用价值。

Abstract: We show that within the framework of the Friedmann cosmological model it is possible to derive general multimessenger consistency conditions, independent of the form of dark energy. We first derive a general relation for the curvature parameter, uniquely in terms of the gravitational wave (GW) and the electromagnetic wave (EMW) luminosity distances, which can be used to probe the curvature of the Universe with multimessenger astronomy, independently of the dark energy equation of state. We then use this to derive a general multimessenger consistency relation for the Friedmann model, independent of the dark energy model and of cosmological density parameters. As a special case, a multimessenger consistency test for the cosmological constant is also derived, independent of the curvature and matter density parameters.

### [122] [Hawking Radiation and Greybody Factors of Test Scalar and Electromagnetic Fields on Asymptotically Flat Pure Lovelock Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09756)
*Jayden Tan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文计算了纯洛弗洛克黑洞（Pure Lovelock black holes）在临界分支 d=2N+2 上的标量和高维电磁灰体因子（greybody factors）及霍金光谱（Hawking spectra），发现其霍金温度（Hawking temperature）更低，导致总辐射功率相比相同视界半径的史瓦西-唐格里尼黑洞（Schwarzschild–Tangherlini black holes）显著降低；在 d=6 基准情形下，标量和电磁辐射功率分别降低约三个和五个数量级。此外，随洛弗洛克阶数 N 增大，霍金辐射越来越由标量型电磁扇区主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纯洛弗洛克黑洞在几何上比爱因斯坦对应物更透明，但其辐射却远弱于后者，这一反直觉现象需要定量解释；同时，高阶曲率修正对霍金辐射模式（radiation pattern）的影响尚不明确。

Method: 在临界分支 d=2N+2 上，计算标量和高维电磁场的灰体因子与霍金光谱；将这些结果与相同视界半径 r_h 的史瓦西-唐格里尼黑洞进行对比。

Result: 较小的霍金温度抵消了增强的透射率，导致净辐射功率大幅下降；在 d=6 情形下，标量辐射功率约为对应史瓦西-唐格里尼黑洞的 10^{-3}，电磁辐射功率约为 10^{-5}。随洛弗洛克阶数 N 增大，霍金辐射逐渐由标量型电磁扇区主导。

Conclusion: 纯洛弗洛克黑洞的霍金辐射远弱于同视界半径的广义相对论黑洞，且高阶曲率修正会改变辐射的扇区主导性，使得标量型电磁模式成为主要辐射通道。

Abstract: Pure Lovelock black holes are geometrically more transparent than their Einstein counterparts, but they radiate far less. We compute scalar and higher-dimensional electromagnetic greybody factors and Hawking spectra on the critical branch $d=2N+2$, compare them with Schwarzschild--Tangherlini black holes at the same horizon radius $r_h$, and show that the smaller Hawking temperature overwhelms the enhanced transmission. In the benchmark $d=6$ case, the integrated scalar and electromagnetic powers are reduced by about $10^{-3}$ and $10^{-5}$, respectively. We also find a clean higher-curvature signature: as the Lovelock order $N$ grows, Hawking radiation becomes increasingly dominated by the scalar-type electromagnetic sector.

### [123] [Quantum Maxwell Demon at the Black Hole Horizon: Thermodynamics, Information, and the Equivalence Principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09783)
*Hamed Hadi,Amin Rezaei Akbarieh,Goksel Daylan Esmer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文分析了量子麦克斯韦妖（quantum Maxwell demon）在黑洞视界附近自由下落中操控西拉德热机（Szilard engine）的过程，揭示了量子信息、热力学和时空因果性之间的相互作用。研究发现，外部恶魔因视界信息丢失而出现测量相关性退化和功提取减少，但仍遵守局域热力学和兰道尔原理（Landauer's principle）；内部恶魔则退化为平直时空情形，支持等效原理在动力学层面成立，但信息处理过程仍可提供视界存在的操作信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在黑洞背景时空中，量子信息处理、热力学定律与时空因果性（spacetime causality）三者如何共存与相互制约。具体而言，研究黑洞视界（event horizon）对量子麦克斯韦妖操控西拉德热机过程中信息获取和功提取能力的影响。

Method: 将恶魔建模为相干二能级系统（coherent two-level system），工作物质（working substance）为一维盒子中穿越视界的单粒子。当盒子跨越视界时，粒子的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）分裂为可访问和不可访问的子空间，通过对内部自由度求迹，对外部恶魔产生非幺正约化动力学（non-unitary reduced dynamics）。分别在视界外和视界内构建了测量、膨胀和移除壁面的具体协议。

Result: 外部恶魔因视界导致的量子信息丢失而出现测量相关性（measurement correlations）退化和可提取功减少，但仍服从局域热力学和兰道尔原理。内部恶魔的协议在局域上简化为平直时空情形，等效原理（equivalence principle）在动力学层面成立，但量子信息处理仍可通过可访问性降低和不可逆开放系统行为提供视界的操作信号。

Conclusion: 在黑洞时空中，信息和热力学的一致性（consistency）在外部和内部观察者视角下以不同方式呈现。外部观察者经历信息丢失和功退化，但仍满足热力学定律；内部观察者则恢复平直时空行为，支持等效原理。量子信息处理为识别黑洞视界提供了可操作的特征，有助于厘清信息、因果性和热力学在黑洞时空中如何共存。

Abstract: We analyze a quantum Maxwell demon operating a Szilard engine in free fall near a black hole horizon, where quantum information, thermodynamics, and spacetime causality intersect. The demon is modeled as a coherent two-level system, and the working substance is a single particle in a one-dimensional chamber crossing the event horizon. As the chamber crosses the horizon, the particle's Hilbert space splits into accessible and inaccessible sectors, leading to non-unitary reduced dynamics for an external demon due to tracing over interior degrees of freedom. We construct explicit measurement, expansion, and wall removal protocols for demons located outside or inside the horizon. Our results show that an external demon experiences degraded measurement correlations and reduced work extraction due to horizon-induced information loss, yet still obeys local thermodynamics and Landauer's principle. For an internal demon, the protocol reduces locally to the flat spacetime case, preserving the equivalence principle at the level of dynamics. While the equivalence principle holds dynamically, quantum information processing provides an operational signature of the horizon through reduced accessibility and irreversible open system behavior, clarifying how information, causality, and thermodynamics coexist in black-hole spacetimes.

</details>


### [124] [Gravielectric and gravimagnetic fluxes in nutty black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09786)
*Dmitri Gal'tsov,Rostom Karsanov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过引入定静态时空（stationary spacetime）中的引力电场（gravielectric field, GE）和引力磁场（gravimagnetic field, GM），利用 Komar 二形式及其对偶，将 Komar-Tomimatsu 质量公式的推导扩展至局域力线图像。研究表明，Misner 弦（Misner strings, MS）携带奇异 GE 和 GM 通量，连接视界与渐近区域，且具有横向透明性，允许场线流入和流出体区域。该机制解释了 Taub-NUT 真空中 Misner 弦周围 Komar 质量积分为负的原因：场线从视界流向弦，需计算流入（正）而非流出的 Komar 通量；流入通量经 Misner 弦折返回视界，构成无源闭合回路。因此，Misner 弦是无质量的空管，而非负质量的刚性杆。类似地，GM 场线可连接视界上的正负电荷区域，产生如 Kerr 度规的引力磁偶极矩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Komar-Tomimatsu 质量公式虽能描述定静态时空的整体质量，但缺乏对局域力线结构的细致刻画。本文旨在通过引入 GE 和 GM 场，将质量公式的推导推广至局域场线图像，并澄清 Misner 弦上负质量积分这一反直觉现象的物理本质。

Method: 在定静态时空中，利用 Komar 二形式（Komar two-form）及其对偶定义 GE 和 GM 场；借助该框架重新审视 Komar-Tomimatsu 质量公式的推导，并分析 Misner 弦上奇异通量的几何与拓扑结构。

Result: 发现 Misner 弦携带奇异的 GE 和 GM 通量，连接视界与渐近区域，且具有横向透明性（laterally transparent）。Taub-NUT 真空中 Misner 弦周围 Komar 质量积分为负，是因为场线从视界流向弦，需要计算流入（正）而非流出的 Komar 通量；该流入通量通过 Misner 弦折返回视界，形成无源闭合回路。此外，GM 场线可连接视界上的正负电荷区域，如 Kerr 度规中产生的引力磁偶极矩（gravimagnetic dipole moment）。

Conclusion: Misner 弦并非负质量的刚性杆（rigid rods of negative mass），而是无质量的空管（massless empty tubes），其负质量积分源于通量方向的选择性计算。该工作为理解定静态时空中质量与通量的局域分布提供了更清晰的几何与物理图像。

Abstract: We introduce the gravielectric (GE) and gravimagnetic (GM) fields in stationary spacetime using the Komar two-form and its dual. This opens the way to extend the Komar-Tomimatsu derivation of mass formulas to a more detailed picture in terms of the local lines of force. We show that Misner strings (MS) carry singular GE and GM fluxes connecting the horizon and the asymptotic zone. Moreover, MS are laterally transparent, so field lines can flow in and out of the bulk. This explains why the usual Komar mass integrals around the Misner strings in the Taub-NUT vacuum solution are negative: the pattern of field lines shows that they flow onto the string from the horizon, so it is necessary to calculate the incoming (positive) but not the outgoing Komar fluxes. This incoming flux is then turned back to the horizon through the Misner strings, realizing the closed circuit without sources. So Misner strings are massless empty tubes, but not rigid rods of negative mass. Similarly, GM field lines can connect positively and negatively charged regions of the horizon, generating, for example, the gravimagnetic dipole moment of the Kerr metric.

### [125] [A study on Dusty Plasma Physics and the examination of Jeans Criteria for the Milky Way](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09943)
*Tanay Gupta,Isha Shailesh,Ram Prasad Prajapati*

TL;DR: 本文综述了尘埃等离子体（dusty plasma）物理，重点回顾了宇宙射线（Cosmic Rays, CRs）、阿尔文波（Alfven Waves, AWs）及带电尘埃颗粒等关键概念；进而基于爱因斯坦-德西特模型（Einstein-de Sitter model），研究了辐射压主导的膨胀宇宙中金斯不稳定性（Jeans instability），推导了色散关系，并发现膨胀因子S(t)影响临界金斯波数，短波长扰动在暴胀期对星系形成起关键作用。

  <summary>Details</summary>
