Conclusion: 膨胀宇宙中的金斯不稳定性判据与静态情况不同，膨胀因子S(t)是决定扰动能否增长的关键参数；暴胀期产生的短波长扰动为后续宇宙结构的形成提供了初始条件。

Abstract: Since the early 1990s, there has been significant interest in the physics of dusty plasmas, which has now become a new discipline in plasma science. Dusty plasma exhibits new and unusual behaviour, and provides a possibility for modified or entirely new collective modes of oscillations, instabilities as well as coherent nonlinear structures.\\ First, a review of the important recurring terms -- The Cosmic Waves (CRs), the Alfven Waves (AWs), and the associated charged dust grains is presented. Starting from the basic composition of the CRs to their scattering mechanism, along with the different modes of scattering, is presented, along with the modes of confinement and a precise definition of each term. The paper also includes some useful diagrams and brief notes from the references. \\ Gravitation plays a significant role in the collapse of matter and the formation of cosmological structures. Unlike a static universe, this paper investigates the Jeans instability in a radiation-pressure-dominated expanding universe using the Einstein-de Sitter model for Euclidean geometry with zero curvature ($κ=0$). The fluid model for an expanding universe is constructed, and by taking small perturbations, the perturbed fluid equations are obtained. The dispersion relation of gravitational instability is derived using plane-wave solutions. In the static case (Newtonian cosmology), the classical Jeans instability criterion is revisited and modified in an expanding universe. The critical Jeans wave number of perturbations to excite Jeans instability depends upon the time-dependent expansion factor $S(t)$. It is found that short-wavelength perturbations are expected during the inflationary period of big bang cosmology, which are responsible for gravitational collapse and the formation of galaxies.

### [126] [BB plot: A Tool for Accurate Model Selection Using Bayes factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10333)
*Ankur Barsode*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种称为贝叶斯因子-贝叶斯因子关系（Bayes factor-Bayes factor relationship, BB关系）的诊断方法，通过将两个竞争假设下的贝叶斯因子分布关联起来，用于验证贝叶斯因子计算的准确性，并以引力波天文学为例展示了其应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理学和天文学中常需通过贝叶斯因子（Bayes factor）在竞争假设之间进行数据偏好判断，但贝叶斯因子计算的准确性和背景分布估计缺乏有效的验证手段。

Method: 作者推导了贝叶斯因子与其在两个竞争假设下的分布之间的关系，即BB关系，并将其表示为诊断图（diagnostic plot）。该方法还可用于以较低计算成本估计贝叶斯因子的背景分布，在某些情况下甚至可解析求解。

Result: 通过引力波天文学实例验证了BB图能够有效校验贝叶斯因子计算的准确性；将该方法应用于引力波波光学透镜效应（wave-optics lensing），从GWTC4数据外推背景分布，得出GW231123事件的统计显著性上限约为≤4.1σ。

Conclusion: BB关系为贝叶斯因子计算提供了一种实用的验证工具，并能高效估计背景分布，在引力波天文学及其他领域具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: A common task in physics and astronomy is studying which of the competing hypotheses the data prefer. This is usually done by computing the Bayes factor between the two hypotheses, and either interpreting it in terms of the posterior odds or as a ranking statistic for a frequentist p-value test. Here we describe a relationship between the Bayes factor and its distributions under the two competing hypotheses, called the Bayes factor-Bayes factor (BB) relationship, expressed as a diagnostic plot. Using examples from gravitational wave (GW) astronomy, we demonstrate how the BB plot can validate the accuracy of Bayes factor calculations. The BB relationship may also be useful for estimating background distributions of the Bayes factor at low computational cost, even analytically in some cases. We apply this technique in the context of wave-optics lensing of GWs, extrapolating the background distribution from GWTC4 to put a rough bound of $\lesssim 4.1 σ$ on the statistical significance of GW231123.

### [127] [Fifth-Force Constraints from UV-Complete Scalar-Tensor Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10338)
*Alfio M. Bonanno,Emiliano M. Glaviano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个非最小耦合到引力的O(N)标量多重态，在标量-张量理论中一个非微扰完备的重整化群（renormalization group, RG）标度区域附近的RG流。在对称性破缺相中，径向模中介了一种普适的Yukawa修正，参数化为强度α和范围λ。紫外（ultraviolet, UV）完备性约束将红外数据限制在一个有限楔形区域，对应(α,λ)平面上的一个狭窄区域，部分被排除的区域落在当前实验排除包络线之下，因此改进的第五力搜索可直接检验并可能证伪这类UV完备的标量-张量模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究标量-张量理论中非微扰UV完备的标度区域，并检验其对红外现象（如对牛顿引力的Yukawa修正）施加的约束，从而为实验检验提供理论预测。

Method: 通过研究O(N)标量多重态非最小耦合到引力的系统，追踪其在相互作用的非微扰UV完备标度区域附近的重整化群（renormalization group, RG）流。利用UV完备性条件约束红外数据，将其映射到Yukawa修正参数(α,λ)平面。

Result: UV完备性将红外数据限制为一个有限的楔形区域，对应(α,λ)平面上的一个狭窄区域；该区域之外被UV完备性单独排除。部分被排除的区域位于当前实验排除包络线之下。

Conclusion: 改进的第五力搜索实验可以直接检验并可能证伪这类UV完备的标量-张量模型，因为理论上被排除的部分区域尚未被现有实验覆盖。

Abstract: We study an $O(N)$ scalar multiplet nonminimally coupled to gravity and follow its renormalization-group (RG) flow in the vicinity of an interacting, nonperturbatively UV-complete scaling regime of scalar-tensor theory. In the broken phase, the radial mode mediates a universal Yukawa correction to Newtonian gravity, parametrized by a strength $α$ and range $λ$. Imposing UV completeness -- regular RG trajectories that reach the UV scaling regime -- restricts the infrared data to a finite wedge, which maps to a narrow region in the $(α,λ)$ plane. Its complement is, therefore, ruled out by UV completeness alone. Remarkably, part of this theory-excluded domain lies below current experimental exclusion envelopes, so improved fifth-force searches can directly test and potentially falsify this class of UV-complete scalar-tensor models.

</details>


### [128] [Quantum Correlations of Neutrinos in the Kerr-Newman Space-time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10424)
*Ze-Wen Li,Shu-Jun Rong*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究Kerr-Newman度规中中微子的量子关联（QC）特性，发现度规参数（质量M、角动量a、电荷Q）对中微子振荡概率、纠缠和非定域性具有显著调制作用，且纠缠与相干性展现出高度一致的振荡行为，为中微子作为量子信息资源提供了定量支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子因弱相互作用在量子信息（quantum information, QI）领域具有独特优势，而量子关联（quantum correlations, QCs）是中微子基量子信息的基础性质。本文旨在通过变参数Kerr-Newman度规，系统研究弯曲时空背景对中微子QCs的影响机制。

Method: 在弱场近似（weak-field approximation）下，分别考虑径向和非径向两种中微子传播模式，通过改变Kerr-Newman度规的三个参数——质量M、单位质量角动量a和电荷Q——来分析中微子振荡概率及量子关联性质的演化行为。

Result: 在Kerr-Newman度规中向内传播时，中微子振荡概率与量子关联显著不同于Schwarzschild度规。径向向外传播时，角动量a增大振荡周期，电荷Q则减小周期。非径向传播中，M和a的调制效应更明显；M增大使振荡概率维持在较高值范围，而三分体纠缠（tripartite entanglement）呈现相反趋势。纠缠与相干性（coherence）在两类传播中表现出高度一致的振荡行为。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了弯曲时空参数对中微子量子关联的定量调控规律，为中微子在量子信息领域的潜在应用提供了更广泛的定量支持。

Abstract: Thanks to feeble interactions, neutrinos show special advantages in the field of quantum information (QM). The properties of quantum correlations (QCs) are fundamental for neutrino-based QM. In this paper, we investigate the influence of the Kerr--Newman metric on QCs by varying the metric parameters, namely the mass $M$, angular momentum per unit mass $a$, and charge $Q$. Both radial and non-radial neutrino propagation are considered under the weak-field approximation. The results show that, for inward propagation in the Kerr--Newman metric, the oscillation probabilities and QCs differ significantly from those obtained in the Schwarzschild metric. In the case of radial outward propagation, the angular momentum $a$ increases the oscillation period of the neutrino survival probability $P_{ee}$, entanglement, and nonlocality, whereas the charge $Q$ decreases the corresponding periods. For non-radial propagation, the modulation effects of $M$ and $a$ on the oscillation patterns of both probabilities and QCs become more pronounced. As $M$ increases, the oscillation probability remains within a higher-value range, whereas tripartite entanglement exhibits the opposite trend. Furthermore, our results reveal that, despite differences in their variation ranges, entanglement and coherence exhibit highly consistent oscillation behaviors in both radial and non-radial propagation cases. These findings provide broader quantitative support for the potential use of neutrinos as quantum information resources.

</details>


### [129] [The Dirac field in LRS space-times: a covariant approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10620)
*Stefano Vignolo,Giuseppe De Maria,Sante Carloni,Luca Fabbri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过狄拉克场的极分解将其描述为有效自旋流体，构建了避免使用标架场和克利福德矩阵的(1+1+2)协变形式体系，并在此框架下分析了自引力狄拉克场在局部旋转对称（LRS）时空中的嵌入条件，给出了解析和数值解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作对自引力狄拉克场在LRS时空中的嵌入研究有限，且传统方法依赖标架场（tetrad fields）和克利福德矩阵（Clifford matrices），形式复杂。本文旨在构建一个更简洁的协变框架，系统地分析狄拉克场在三种类型LRS时空中的一致性嵌入条件。

Method: 首先采用狄拉克场的极分解（polar decomposition）将其描述为有效自旋流体（spinorial fluid）；随后构建不依赖标架场和克利福德矩阵的(1+1+2)协变形式体系；在此基础上，假设狄拉克场的速度场和自旋矢量场位于由类时和类空汇（congruences）逐点定义的平面内，并依此扩展前人工作，分析LRS-I、II、III型时空中的嵌入条件。

Result: 给出了自引力狄拉克场在LRS-I、II、III型时空中一致性嵌入所需满足的条件；提供了若干解析解和数值解，以说明所提出框架的适用性。

Conclusion: 本文构建的(1+1+2)协变形式体系能有效规避标架场和克利福德矩阵的复杂性，适用于自引力狄拉克场在LRS时空中的嵌入问题，解析与数值结果验证了该框架的可行性与有效性。

Abstract: We employ the polar decomposition of the Dirac field to describe it as an effective spinorial fluid. We then construct a $(1+1+2)$ covariant formalism for the Dirac field that avoids the introduction of tetrad fields and Clifford matrices. Within this framework, we analyze the conditions under which a self-gravitating Dirac field can be consistently embedded in Locally Rotationally Symmetric (LRS) space-times of types I, II, and III. In accordance with the LRS symmetry requirements, we extend a previous work by assuming that the velocity and spin vector fields of the Dirac field lie in the planes defined pointwise by the generators of the time-like and space-like congruences, which underlie the $(1+1+2)$ decomposition. We present some analytical and numerical solutions to illustrate the applicability of the proposed framework.

</details>


### [130] [Gravitational Waves in High Energy Fixed-Target Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10749)
*D. V. Fursaev,V. A. Tainov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 在线性化爱因斯坦引力（linearized Einstein gravity）框架下，研究了一个高能相对论性粒子与一个静止大质量粒子构成的两体系统的引力场。高能粒子产生一个平面波前的引力激波（plane-fronted gravitational shockwave），扰动静止粒子的引力场。该问题可视为固定靶高能碰撞，碰撞伴随引力辐射（gravitational radiation），一个新效应是初始激波击中大质量粒子时会产生次级球面引力激波（secondary spherical gravitational shockwave）。在所采用的近似下，给出了引力辐射通量及球面激波振幅的解析形式，该方法也可推广到零质量粒子被一般轮廓的平面零质量壳层替代的情形，并简要讨论了相关的天体物理含义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究两体系统（高能相对论性粒子与静止大质量粒子）在线性化爱因斯坦引力框架下的引力场，特别关注高能粒子产生的平面激波对静止粒子引力场的扰动及其引发的引力辐射，并探索该过程中可能存在的次级球面激波这一新效应。

Method: 采用线性化爱因斯坦引力理论，将问题建模为固定靶高能碰撞（fixed-target high energy collision）；利用平面引力激波扰动静止粒子引力场的图像，在近似下解析求解引力辐射通量与球面激波的振幅；并讨论了将零质量粒子推广为一般轮廓的平面零质量壳层（plane null shells）的适用性。

Result: 证实该碰撞过程伴随引力辐射，与先前高能散射的预期结果一致；发现了次级球面引力激波这一新效应，其振幅与引力辐射通量均在解析近似下给出；该方法可适用于更一般的平面零质量壳层情形。

Conclusion: 所发展的解析方法为研究高能粒子碰撞中的引力激波及引力辐射提供了有效工具，相关效应可能对天体物理过程（如高能天体碰撞事件）具有潜在意义。

Abstract: The gravitational field of two-body system, a high energetic particle and a massive particle at rest, is studied in the linearized Einstein gravity. The ultrarelativistic particle yields a plane-fronted gravitational shockwave which perturbes gravitational field of the particle at rest. The problem can be also considered as a fixed-target high energy collision. We show that this collision is accompanied by the gravitational radiation, as is expected from the earlier results on the high-energy scattering. The new effect is a secondary spherical gravitational shockwave when the initial shockwave hits the massive particle. In the considered approximation the flux of gravitational radiation and the amplitude of the spherical shockwave are found in an analytic form. The suggested approach is also applicable when the null particle is replaced by plane null shells of a general profile. Implications of these effects for astrophysics are shortly discussed.

</details>


### [131] [Cusp Formation in Merging Black Hole Horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10874)
*Shilpa Kastha,Stamatis Vretinaris,Daniel Pook-Kolb,Badri Krishnan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过研究准局部黑洞视界（quasi-local black hole horizons）在并合过程中形成的尖点（cusps），建立初始双黑洞与最终残余黑洞之间的联系，并针对两个无自旋黑洞的正面对撞情形，从数值角度详细分析了尖点的形成过程及其质量与高阶多极矩的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双黑洞并合中残余黑洞的性质（如质量、自旋、高阶多极矩以及准正则模（quasi-normal modes）的激发）与初始黑洞之间的联系是重要问题，目前主要依赖引力波信号分析，本文旨在探索一种基于准局部黑洞视界的替代方法。

Method: 本文采用数值方法，聚焦于两个无自旋黑洞的正面对撞（head-on collision）情形，详细分析黑洞视界在并合过程中如何形成尖点，并考察质量及高阶质量多极矩（higher mass multipole moments）在尖点处的行为。

Result: 展示了尖点形成过程的数值细节，揭示了质量与高阶质量多极矩在尖点处的变化规律，并提出了一个唯象模型（phenomenological model）来描述这些行为。

Conclusion: 通过准局部黑洞视界上的尖点现象，能够有效连接初始双黑洞与最终残余黑洞的状态，为理解双黑洞并合提供了一个不依赖引力波信号的新视角。

Abstract: An important question in binary black hole mergers is to connect properties of the remnant black hole to those of the two initial black holes. These properties include not only the final mass and spin of the remnant, but also higher multipoles and answers to other questions such as, for a given initial configuration, which quasi-normal modes of the final black hole are excited, and what are the amplitudes of these modes? Such questions have thus far been primarily addressed through a study of the emitted gravitational wave signal. In this paper we consider a different alternative, namely using quasi-local black hole horizons themselves to establish the link between the initial and final states. Recent work has elucidated the behavior of black hole horizons in a merger. Cusps forming in such otherwise smoothly evolving horizons have been shown to play a central role in connecting the two initially separate black holes with the final remnant. In the present work, we will discuss from a numerical perspective how such cusps form in detail for the head-on collision of two non-spinning black holes. We show how the mass and higher mass multipole moments behave at the cusp and suggest a phenomenological model.

</details>

### [132] [Polydoxon Transformations and Scientific Reward in Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08642)
*James D. Wells*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于时间依赖的Polydoxon概念（定义为特定时期经验上可行的理论结构集合）提出了一种描述性框架，用以理解物理学中的科学奖励机制。高度奖励的贡献（如重大奖项和专业荣誉）被系统地视为那些能够对该空间进行扩张、收缩、重构或赋能转换的行为。奖励强度与转换在范围、中心性、深度和未来杠杆四个维度上的幅度相关。该框架将奖励成就的分析从孤立理论成功转向可行理论景观的动态演变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对物理学中科学奖励的分析多聚焦于孤立的理论成功，缺乏一个统一且动态的理论框架来描述奖励如何与不同发现类型（理论、实验、方法论）相关联。本文旨在通过Polydoxon概念填补这一缺失。

Method: 本文采用概念分析方法，定义了时间依赖的Polydoxon作为可行理论的结构化集合，并分类了四种转换类型（扩张、收缩、重构、赋能）。进一步通过范围、中心性、深度和未来杠杆四个维度量化转换幅度，以此关联奖励程度。

Result: 给出了一个统一的描述性解释：高奖励贡献对应于对Polydoxon空间的大幅度转换，且这种转换可通过多个维度的幅度评估来系统理解。该框架适用于物理学中多样化的理论和实验发现。

Conclusion: 该框架将奖励成就的分析从孤立的成功转向可行理论景观的动态演变，为理解物理学中奖励的科学活动提供了更具统一性的描述性解释。

Abstract: We develop a descriptive account of scientific reward in physics based on the concept of the time-dependent Polydoxon, defined as the structured set of empirically viable theories at a given time. We argue that highly rewarded contributions, such as those recognized by major prizes and professional honors, can be systematically understood as those that transform this space. These transformations take the form of expansion (adding viable theories), contraction (eliminating viable theories), reconfiguration (illuminating deeper structures and relations within and between theories), and enabling moves (methodological or technological advances that enable future transformations). The analysis is further refined by emphasizing that reward correlates with the transformation's magnitude, assessed along dimensions of scope, centrality, depth, and future leverage. This framework reframes the analysis of rewarded achievement away from isolated theoretical successes and toward the dynamics of a landscape of viable theories, providing a more unified descriptive interpretation of rewarded scientific activity in physics across its diverse set of theoretical and experimental discoveries.

</details>

### [133] [LLMs with in-context learning for Algorithmic Theoretical Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08212)

Abstract: There is an increasing number of algorithmic computations in theoretical physics. These, while conceptually simple, can nevertheless be time-consuming and contain subtleties that should not be overlooked. Given the recent improvement of Large Language Models (LLM), it is natural to investigate whether LLMs equipped with a computer algebra system (CAS) runtime and sufficiently informative context can reliably carry out these algorithmic tasks. In this work, we interface Claude with Maple, and apply this framework to cosmological perturbations in modified theories of gravity. We demonstrate the current capabilities of this approach, the typical failures, and how the same can be improved. We find that a frontier LLM supplied with worked examples is able to solve most test problems.

### [134] [Geometry-free prediction of inertial lift forces in microfluidic devices using deep learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08109)
*Jesse Ward-Bond,Ali Mashadian,Timothy C. Y. Chan,Edmond W. K. Young*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种不含显式几何参数的神经网络方法，用于预测惯性微流控器件中的粒子升力，该方法在训练集上的性能与现有模型相当，但能更有效地泛化到未见过的通道几何形状，并能轻松迁移到粒子追踪仿真软件中，预测结果与文献一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了一种不含显式几何参数的新型粒子升力预测方法，使用新的参数集训练神经网络（neural network）模型。

Result: 该模型在训练集内的通道几何上性能与现有模型相当，但在未见于训练集的通道几何上具有显著更优的泛化能力。该升力模型可轻松迁移至粒子追踪仿真软件，并在多种通道设计下预测出与文献一致的粒子迁移模式。

Conclusion: 所提出的无显式几何参数方法成功解决了现有机器学习模型在泛化到新通道几何时的局限性，为惯性微流控仿真提供了一种更灵活、高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Inertial microfluidic devices (IMDs) offer low-cost, high-throughput alternative techniques for many traditional particle- (or cell-) manipulation tasks, but simulating them requires being able to predict particle migration, and thus particle lift forces, under a variety of possible channel geometries. Recent work has demonstrated that machine learning models can be used to drastically speed up these numerical simulations, but doing so required training individual models for every unique channel cross-section type (e.g., rectangular, triangular) -- shifting the burden from the simulation step to the training step. In this paper, we develop a novel approach for predicting particle lift forces that contains no explicit geometric parameters. We train a neural network model using a new parameter set and show that while it performs comparably to existing models on channel geometries in the training set, it is able to generalize to unseen channel geometries far more effectively. We show that the lift force model developed herein can be easily transferred to particle tracing simulation software, where it is capable of predicting particle migration patterns consistent with the literature across a variety of channel designs.

### [135] [Can LLMs Predict Polymer Physics Just by Reading Synthesis and Processing Prose?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08255)
*Yuchu Liu,Rui Zhu,Jingwei Xiong,Haixu Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出PolyLM，一个仅基于自然语言的聚合物性能预测框架，通过从全文文献中学习合成路线、加工历史等实验上下文信息，在22种物理与力学性能上取得高精度预测（中位R²=0.74），证明了自然语言可作为材料性能预测的可扩展接口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高分子性能预测模型仅依赖化学结构表示（如SMILES或分子图），忽略了合成路线（synthesis route）、加工历史（processing history）、形态（morphology）和测试条件（testing conditions）等关键实验上下文信息，导致名义上相同的聚合物可能表现出截然不同的性能。

Method: PolyLM是一个纯自然语言（natural-language-only）框架，直接对全文文献进行建模，绕开任何结构输入。研究团队构建了一个包含185,000篇科学论文和超过276,400个独特聚合物样本的数据集，覆盖22种物理、力学与热学性能；在此基础上使用低秩适配（Low-Rank Adaptation, LoRA）和任务级不确定性加权（task-level uncertainty weighting）对Qwen3.5-9B（90亿参数语言模型）进行微调。

Result: 在68,283个保留测试样本上，模型在22种性能目标上实现了中位R²为0.74，其中关键热学、力学和物理化学性能的预测R²经常超过0.80，在所有复杂性能上均取得了新的最优基准（state-of-the-art benchmarks）。

Conclusion: 实验结果明确表明，自然语言（natural language）是一种强大且高度可扩展的材料性能预测接口，能够有效捕捉结构表示所丢失的实验上下文信息，实现更真实的高分子材料性能预测。

Abstract: Can large language models predict physical and mechanical polymer properties simply by reading unstructured scientific prose? Polymer performance is rarely determined by chemical structure alone; identical nominal polymers can exhibit drastically different behaviors depending on their synthesis route, processing history, morphology, and testing conditions. Yet, state-of-the-art polymer property models typically rely on structure-only representations -- such as SMILES or molecular graphs -- which strip away this vital experimental context. In this work, we introduce \textbf{PolyLM}, a natural-language-only, process- and condition-aware framework that predicts materials performance directly from full-text literature. By circumventing structural inputs entirely, PolyLM preserves the nuanced, unstructured descriptions of synthesis and processing reported by domain scientists. To train this framework, we curated an unprecedented, literature-scale dataset encompassing 185,000 scientific papers and over 276,400 unique polymer samples across 22 physical, mechanical, and thermal properties. We fine-tuned a massive 9-billion-parameter language model (Qwen3.5-9B) using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) and task-level uncertainty weighting. Evaluated on 68,283 held-out observations, the model achieves remarkably high predictive accuracy, establishing new state-of-the-art benchmarks for complex properties. Across the 22 diverse targets, the model achieves a median $R^2$ of 0.74, with predictions for key thermal, mechanical, and physicochemical properties frequently surpassing an $R^2$ of 0.80. These results unequivocally demonstrate that natural language is a powerful, highly scalable interface for realistic materials performance prediction.

</details>


### [136] [Generating Symmetric Materials using Latent Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10115)
*Anmar Karmush,Cedric Mathieu Brandenburg,Soheil Ershadrad,Johanna Rosén,Michael Felsberg,Filip Ekström Kelvinius*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 SymADiT，一种基于 Wyckoff 位置表示和对称性约束的扩散 Transformer 模型，用于生成具有真实晶体对称性的稳定材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在改进已有的全原子扩散 Transformer（All-atom Diffusion Transformer, ADiT），使其在材料生成任务中能够更好地捕捉和遵守晶体固有的对称性（symmetry）约束，从而生成具有更真实对称性属性的材料。

Method: 采用基于 Wyckoff 位置（Wyckoff positions）的材料表示方法；在潜空间（latent space）中进行生成式建模；通过强制生成模型的输出遵守所生成晶体的空间群（space group）和每个原子的 Wyckoff 位置施加的对称性限制，使生成材料具有更真实的对称性。

Result: 在与对称性感知（symmetry-aware）和对称性无关（symmetry-agnostic）模型的基准测试中表现出具有竞争力的性能；能够使用简单的 Transformer 架构生成稳定且具有对称性的材料。

Conclusion: SymADiT 通过引入对称性先验（symmetry prior），有效提升了材料生成中晶体对称性的真实度，并在性能上与现有方法相比具有竞争力。

Abstract: Tackling the task of materials generation, we aim to enhance the previously proposed All-atom Diffusion Transformer (ADiT) by introducing SymADiT, a symmetry-aware variant. To do so, we use a representation of materials based on Wyckoff positions. We follow ADiT and perform generative modelling in latent space, adapted to our symmetry-aware representation. By forcing the output of the generative model to adhere to the symmetry restrictions imposed by the generated crystal's space group and each atom's Wyckoff-position, the generated materials exhibit more realistic symmetry properties. We benchmark our method against both symmetry-aware and symmetry-agnostic models for materials generation and show competitive performance, generating stable, symmetric materials with a simple Transformer architecture.

### [137] [QT-Net: Rethinking Evaluation of AI Models in Atomic Chemical Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10458)
*Pablo Martínez Crespo,Stefano Ribes,Martin Rahm,Richard Beckmann,Robert S. Jordan,Marisa Gliege,Santiago Miret,Vijay Kris Narasimhan,Rocío Mercado*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于SOAP描述符的原子级离群评估协议，用于公平比较等变与非等变模型在预测原子电荷与多极矩上的表现，并由此设计了旋转增强的非等变图神经网络QT-Net，证明其可在QM9数据集上推断原子性质并提升下游分子性质预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子性质（如部分电荷或多极矩）包含化学上有意义的信息，可用于下游分子性质预测；但由于缺乏原则性的原子级分布外（out-of-distribution）评估协议，将这些性质作为机器学习目标进行评估一直存在困难。

Method: 提出基于SOAP描述符聚类原子环境的留出评估协议（held-out evaluation protocol），仅对训练中未见过的聚类标签计算指标；采用5×5交叉验证与Tukey HSD检验进行统计严格的比较；在此基础上设计了QT-Net，一种旋转增强的非等变图神经网络（graph neural network）。

Result: QT-Net可从QM9数据集中推断训练集之外的原子的电子布居数与多极矩；推断出的原子性质作为输入特征可改善下游分子性质预测；由QT-Net逐原子输出计算的分子偶极矩与QM9报告的真实值一致。

Conclusion: 所提出的评估协议和QT-Net框架能够有效学习量子拓扑原子（QTA）性质，并将其作为归纳偏置（inductive bias）用于原子尺度的分子机器学习，代码与数据已开源以支持更广泛的应用。

Abstract: Atomic properties such as partial charges or multipoles encode chemically meaningful information that can inform downstream molecular property prediction, but their evaluation as machine learning targets has been complicated by the absence of a principled out-of-distribution evaluation protocol at the atomic level. In this work, we propose a held-out evaluation protocol that clusters atomic environments by SOAP descriptors and computes metrics accounting only for cluster labels unseen during training. Following this procedure, we use 5$\times$5 cross-validation and Tukey's HSD to run a statistically rigorous comparison of E(3)-equivariant against non-equivariant, rotationally augmented models for predicting electron populations and multipoles of H, C, N, and O atoms. Building on our results, we introduce the Quantum Topological Neural Network (QT-Net), a rotationally augmented, non-equivariant graph neural network. We show that QT-Net can be used to infer properties of atoms in molecules from QM9 outside our training set, and that these inferred properties can yield improvement when used as input features for downstream molecular property prediction. To further validate the framework, molecular dipole moments computed from QT-Net's per-atom outputs recover the ground-truth values reported in QM9. We release all code and data, including a JAX implementation of QT-Net, to support the broader use of learned QTA properties as inductive biases for atomic-scale molecular machine learning.

</details>


### [138] [Composing diffusion priors with explicit physical context via generative Gibbs sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10642)
*Weizhou Wang,Jonathan Weare,Aaron R. Dinner*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需重新训练的训练自由框架GG-PA，通过将预训练扩散模型的部分先验与显式物理上下文组合，在增强状态空间中对联合目标分布进行吉布斯采样，从而实现物理感知的生成采样。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练扩散模型虽能提供强大的学习先验，但在科学采样中，目标分布往往依赖于物理上下文，而单一生成模型无法完全表征这些上下文信息。

Method: GG-PA框架将学习到的部分先验与显式物理上下文组合，在增强状态空间（augmented state space）中对联合目标分布进行推断；推导了针对该联合目标的吉布斯采样器（Gibbs sampler），证明在扩散时间趋近于零时渐近精确，且在二次相互作用（quadratic interactions）情形下对有限扩散时间仍保持精确；进一步引入扩散时间上的副本交换（replica exchange）以加速混合。

Result: 在双阱系统、φ⁴晶格模型和原子肽系统上的实验表明，GG-PA能够在无需重新训练的条件下，仅使用部分先验恢复上下文诱导的分布偏移及相互作用系统中的涌现集体行为。

Conclusion: GG-PA提供了一种将预训练生成先验与显式物理上下文相结合的实际方法，在科学采样的多种场景中有效。

Abstract: Pretrained diffusion models provide powerful learned priors, but in scientific sampling the target distribution often depends on physical context that is not fully represented by one generative model. We introduce Generative Gibbs for Physics-Aware Sampling (GG-PA), a training-free framework that formulates the composition of learned partial priors and explicit physical context as inference over a joint target distribution in an augmented state space. We derive a Gibbs sampler for this joint target, show that it is asymptotically exact as the diffusion time approaches zero, and prove that in settings with quadratic interactions it remains exact at finite diffusion times. We further introduce replica exchange over diffusion time to accelerate mixing. Experiments on a double-well system, a $φ^4$ lattice model, and atomistic peptide systems show that GG-PA recovers context-induced distribution shifts and emergent collective behavior in interacting systems using partial priors without retraining. These results demonstrate GG-PA as a practical approach for combining pretrained generative priors with explicit physical context.

</details>


### [139] [A Random-Matrix Criterion for Initializing Gated Recurrent Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10650)
*Tommaso Fioratti,Riccardo Marcaccioli,Francesco Casola*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对循环神经网络（RNN）的权重初始化问题，推导出一种适用于多种递归架构的临界增益估计准则，该准则与门控RNN储层在混沌预测任务中达到最佳性能时的增益高度吻合，并提出该准则可作为未来初始化方案的设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 权重初始化（weight initialization）是深度学习成功的关键因素之一，在“储层计算”（reservoir computing）中尤为重要——储层权重固定，仅线性学习读出层权重，而储层动力学丰富性、稳定性和记忆性高度依赖初始权重。当权重的方差 $g^2$ 控制的有序相（ordered phase）与混沌相（chaotic phase）之间的相变（phase transition）临界点对应最优初始化，但如何为广泛递归架构估计该临界增益仍缺乏简单统一的标准。

Method: 推导出一个简洁的准则来估计临界增益 $g_c$，该准则适用于一大类循环架构（recurrent architectures）。

Result: 该准则估计的临界增益与门控RNN（gated-RNN）储层在混沌预测任务上达到峰值性能时的增益高度吻合。在无限宽极限（infinite-width limit）下，有意义的初始化处于随机初始化模型的有效临界点（critical point）。

Conclusion: 所提准则可作为未来初始化方案的设计原则（design principle）。

Abstract: Proper weight initialization prior to training has historically been one of the key factors that helped kick off the deep learning revolution. Initialization is even more crucial in "reservoir computing", where the weights of a readout layer are learned linearly while the reservoir weights are fixed and largely determine the richness, stability and memory of the resulting dynamics. In the infinite-width limit it has been shown that meaningful initializations are those sitting at an effective critical point of the randomly initialized model. The phase transition is controlled by the weight variance $g^2$ and separates an ordered phase from a chaotic one where information progressively degrades. Here we derive a simple criterion to estimate the critical $g_c$ for a broad class of recurrent architectures and we show that it closely tracks the gain at which a gated-RNN reservoir achieves peak performance on a chaotic forecasting task. Finally, we argue that our criterion can serve as a design principle for future initialization schemes.

</details>

### [140] [Nonlinear Coherent Transport in 2D Thermal Metamaterials: From Solitons and Topological Defects to Quantum Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08162)
*R. A. C. Correa,K. N. M. Sharma,P. Lolur,J. van Velzen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文针对低维和纳米结构材料中偏离傅里叶定律的热输运现象，发展了一个统一的理论框架，结合非线性晶格动力学、孤子有效场论和几何缺陷网络来解释二维热超构材料（thermal metamaterials）中的双通道热输运机制，并通过实验和计算验证了其在超低热导率、高载流子迁移率和强各向异性等特性中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维和纳米结构材料中因非简谐性（anharmonicity）、降维和长寿命相干激发（long-lived coherent excitations）导致热输运持续偏离傅里叶定律（Fourier's law），这构成了非平衡统计物理（nonequilibrium statistical physics）中的核心挑战，亟需建立统一的理论框架来解释和调控此类系统中的热输运行为。

Method: 论文发展了一个针对二维热超构材料（thermal metamaterials）的统一理论框架，融合了非线性晶格动力学（nonlinear lattice dynamics）、基于孤子（soliton）的有效场论以及几何排列的缺陷网络（defect networks）作为能量流的引导结构。同时引入了适用于受控基准测试的最小离散和连续模型。

Result: 识别出一种双通道热输运机制（two-channel transport mechanism），其中相干非线性激发与不相干流体动力学模式（hydrodynamic modes）并存。该机制对几何结构、非线性强度和温度高度敏感。理论与Stone-Wales缺陷PdSSe单层和硅声子晶体纳米结构中的实验及计算结果一致，表现出超低热导率、高载流子迁移率和强各向异性。

Conclusion: 该理论为工程化热扩散架构的设计提供了可操作的指导，并指出量子模拟（quantum simulation）可作为推进非线性热输运理论发展的变革性工具，同时建立起微观非线性、几何驱动的二维热流通道化与量子可探索性之间的严格联系。

Abstract: Understanding heat transport in low-dimensional and nano-architectured materials remains a central challenge in nonequilibrium statistical physics due to persistent deviations from Fourier's law. These deviations are driven by anharmonicity, reduced dimensionality, and the emergence of long-lived coherent excitations. In this work, we develop a unified theoretical framework for two-dimensional thermal metamaterials that combines nonlinear lattice dynamics, soliton-based effective field theories, and geometrically organized defect networks as guiding structures for energy flow. We introduce minimal discrete and continuum-inspired models suitable for controlled benchmarking of thermal transport in patterned two-dimensional architectures and identify a two-channel transport mechanism in which coherent nonlinear excitations coexist with incoherent hydrodynamic modes. The interplay between these channels is shown to be highly sensitive to geometry, nonlinearity, and temperature, offering new avenues for thermal management. We establish rigorous connections between microscopic nonlinearity, geometry-driven channeling of heat in two dimensions, and quantum-enabled exploration of both high-occupation classical regimes and genuinely quantum regimes beyond the reach of standard simulation strategies. The theoretical predictions are corroborated by recent experimental and computational results in Stone-Wales-defected PdSSe monolayers and silicon phononic crystal nanostructures, which exhibit ultra-low thermal conductivity coexisting with high carrier mobility and strong anisotropy -- direct manifestations of the two-channel mechanism. This synthesis provides actionable guidance for the design of engineered heat-spreading architectures and positions quantum simulation as a transformative tool for advancing the theory of nonlinear heat transport.

### [142] [Rashba engineering at van der Waals interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08228)
*Rahul Sharma,Soumya Mukherjee,Fatima Ibrahim,Gaétan Verdierre,Libor Vojáček,Martin Mičica,Sylvain Massabeau,Oliver Paull,Vincent Polewczyk,Nicola Marzari,Alain Marty,Isabelle Gomes de Moraes,Frédéric Bonell,Juliette Mangeney,Jérôme Tignon,Gauthier Krizman,Anupam Jana,Jun Fujii,Ivana Vobornik,Federico Mazzola,Jing Li,Leticia Melo Costa,Olivier Renault,Adrien Michon,Henri Jaffrès,Jean-Marie George,Mairbek Chshiev,Sukhdeep Dhillon,Matthieu Jamet*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文实验证明，不同二维过渡金属硫族化合物（transition metal dichalcogenide, TMD）单层之间的界面能够调控Rashba自旋劈裂（Rashba spin splitting）的强度和符号，并通过太赫兹（THz）自旋电子发射进行探测，其中优化后的HfSe₂/PtSe₂异质双层展现出超越块体TMD的自旋-电荷转换效率，为构建高效可调谐THz自旋电子发射器提供了新途径。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用太赫兹自旋电子发射（THz spintronic emission）来探测Rashba自旋劈裂，并结合自旋分辨和角分辨光电子能谱（spin- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）与密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT），揭示界面电子杂化机制。

Result: 优化后的TMD异质双层（如HfSe₂/PtSe₂）表现出增强的THz发射，其自旋-电荷转换效率超越块体TMD；不同TMD单层之间的电子杂化在界面处产生了具有强Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的扩展能隙内态（in-gap states），且通过选择TMD层可工程化调控自旋-电荷转换的符号与强度。

Conclusion: 不同TMD单层界面能够有效控制Rashba自旋劈裂，为在范德华异质双层（van der Waals heterobilayers）中设计和调控自旋-电荷转换提供了可行路径，从而为构建高效且可调谐的THz自旋电子发射器开辟了新前景。

Abstract: Two-dimensional transition metal dichalcogenide (TMD) interfaces offer a versatile platform for studying emergent quantum phenomena and enabling novel device functionalities. When distinct TMD monolayers are stacked vertically or laterally stitched, their interfaces can exhibit unique electronic band alignments, giving rise to long-lived interlayer excitons, charge transfer effects, and moiré superlattices with correlated states. Here, we demonstrate that the interface between a large variety of two different epitaxially grown TMD monolayers controls the intensity and sign of the Rashba spin splitting, which is probed using THz spintronic emission. Optimized TMD heterobilayers, such as HfSe$_2$/PtSe$_2$, show enhanced THz emission that surpass the spin-to-charge conversion efficiency of bulk TMDs, confirming the presence of Rashba states with large spin splitting at the interface. By combining spin- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy with density functional theory, we reveal that the electronic hybridization between the two different TMD monolayers gives rise to extended in-gap states with strong Rashba spin-orbit coupling. The choice of TMD layers enables to engineer the sign and strength of spin-to-charge conversion in van der Waals heterobilayers opening up perspectives to build efficient and tunable THz spintronic emitters.

</details>


### [143] [Dynamically Characterizing the Structures of Dirac Points via Wave Packets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08236)
*Dan-Dan Liang,Xin Shen,Zhi Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从波包动力学（wave packet dynamics）视角研究可控狄拉克点（Dirac point）系统中的拓扑能带结构，通过引入石墨烯模型中的第三近邻耦合产生额外狄拉克点，并利用波包动力学行为揭示混合点（hybrid point）和抛物点（parabolic point）等能带结构，同时展示了如何通过波包的质心和自旋纹理（spin texture）分别确定狄拉克点和抛物点的绕数（winding number）。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑非平庸能带结构是拓扑材料领域的核心问题，而如何通过动力学方法表征这些拓扑特征仍是开放挑战。本文旨在从波包动力学视角揭示可控狄拉克点系统中的拓扑能带结构。

Method: 在石墨烯模型基础上引入第三近邻耦合（third-nearest-neighboring coupling），从而产生额外的狄拉克点对；通过分析狄拉克点的出现与湮灭过程，研究混合点和抛物点的形成；利用波包的质心运动与自旋纹理动力学定量表征拓扑不变量。

Result: 狄拉克点的出现与湮灭会导致混合点和抛物点；在带隙混合点（gapped hybrid point）处，波包运动呈现一维颤动（Zitterbewegung）运动；狄拉克点的绕数可通过波包质心确定，抛物点的绕数可通过波包自旋纹理确定。

Conclusion: 该研究可能推动通过波包动力学表征系统拓扑特征的新型实验方法的发展，该方法也可应用于其他奇异拓扑材料系统。

Abstract: Topological non-trivial band structures are the core problem in the field of topological materials. In this paper, we investigate the topological band structure in a system with controllable Dirac points from the perspective of wave packet dynamics. By adding a third-nearest-neighboring coupling to the graphene model, additional pairs of Dirac points emerge. The emergence and annihilation of Dirac points result in hybrid and parabolic points, and we show that these band structures can be revealed by the dynamical behaviors of wave packets. Particularly, for the gapped hybrid point, the motion of the wave packet shows a one-dimensional \emph{Zitterbewegung} motion. Furthermore, we also show that the winding number associated with the Dirac point and parabolic point can be determined via the center-of-mass and spin texture of wave packets, respectively. The results of this work could motivate new experimental methods to characterize the system's topological signatures through wave packet dynamics, which may also find application in systems of other exotic topological materials.

</details>


### [144] [Antiferro-Chiral Phonons in $\mathcal{P}\mathcal{T}$-Symmetric Antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08490)
*Sanjib Kumar Das,Randy Yeh,Yafei Ren*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出$\mathcal{P}\mathcal{T}$对称反铁磁体中存在反铁手性声子（antiferro-chiral phonons, AFCPs）——总角动量为零但具有子格交错角动量的声子模式，并通过分子贝里曲率（molecular Berry curvature）产生与奈尔矢量（Néel vector）的耦合，为反铁磁序的探测与相干控制提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统手性声子（chiral phonons）携带净角动量，只能耦合于净磁化强度（net magnetization），而无法耦合于补偿性的奈尔序（Néel order）。因此，需要探索能够直接与反铁磁序耦合的新型声子模式。

Method: 通过对称性分析表明，$\mathcal{P}\mathcal{T}$对称性禁止声子携带净角动量，但允许反演相关子格上存在反向旋转的局域运动。AFCPs源于拉曼活性与红外活性声子之间的奈尔矢量锁定的耦合，该耦合在$\mathcal{P}$和$\mathcal{T}$下均为奇宇称，但保持其乘积不变。通过这种杂化，正则模式同时获得拉曼和红外特征，并携带子格交错的声子角动量，作为奈尔矢量的共轭场。该耦合的微观起源是分子贝里曲率（molecular Berry curvature），并在原型晶格模型中得以展示。

Result: 在$\mathcal{P}\mathcal{T}$对称反铁磁体中，声子模式可以具有净角动量为零但子格交错角动量非零的特性。反转奈尔矢量会反转交错的声子手性。分子贝里曲率是产生该耦合的微观机制。

Conclusion: 反铁手性声子可以作为反铁磁序的探测手段，并建议相干声子激发（coherent phonon excitation）是动态控制反铁磁序的一种可行途径。

Abstract: Chiral phonons provide a route to couple lattice motion to magnetic order, but conventional chiral phonons carry a net angular momentum and thus couple naturally to net magnetization rather than to compensated Néel order. Here we show that $\mathcal{P}\mathcal{T}$-symmetric antiferromagnets can host \emph{antiferro-chiral phonons} (AFCPs): phonon modes with vanishing total angular momentum but finite sublattice-staggered angular momentum. Symmetry enforces this distinction because $\mathcal{P}\mathcal{T}$ forbids a net phonon angular momentum while allowing counter-rotating local motion on inversion-related sublattices. AFCPs arise from a Néel-vector-locked coupling between Raman and infrared-active phonons. The coupling is odd under both $\mathcal{P}$ and $\mathcal{T}$ while preserving their product. Through this hybridization, the normal modes acquire both Raman and infrared character and carry a sublattice-staggered phonon angular momentum that acts as a conjugate field to the Néel vector. This coupling is microscopically generated by the molecular Berry curvature, which is demonstrated in a prototype lattice model. Reversing the Néel vector reverses the staggered phonon chirality. These results indicate AFCPs as probes of antiferromagnetic order and suggest coherent phonon excitation as a route to its dynamical control.

</details>


### [145] [Fokker--Planck framework for stochastic octupole moment dynamics in chiral antiferromagnet Mn3Sn](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08531)
*Siyuan Qian,Shaloo Rakheja*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对Mn3Sn中热辅助八极矩动力学的约化随机框架，通过结合约化Landau–Lifshitz–Gilbert (LLG) 方程与Fokker–Planck形式体系，并利用CUDA加速求解器实现高效计算。该模型能够准确捕捉八极矩的开关行为，并展示了在超低错误概率分析中超越传统蒙特卡洛模拟的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Mn3Sn中的八极矩（octupole moment）动力学涉及热激活过程，直接进行完全三子格（three-sublattice）模拟的计算成本高昂，尤其难以高效获取超低错误概率下的统计行为。因此，需要发展一种约化的随机框架以降低计算复杂度，同时保持对关键开关行为的准确描述。

Method: 研究将约化Landau–Lifshitz–Gilbert (LLG) 方程与Fokker–Planck形式体系相结合，构建约化的随机动力学模型。通过将约化模型与完整的三子格八极矩动力学进行基准测试，验证其准确性。进一步推导对应的Fokker–Planck方程，并采用CUDA加速的求解器进行数值实现与求解。通过平衡分布、弛豫轨迹和开关时间等指标，与蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟进行对比验证。

Result: 基准测试表明，约化模型能够以良好的精度捕捉八极矩开关行为的本质特征。分析发现，八极矩动力学对离面网格分辨率高度敏感，原因是八极矩的超快旋转受其相对于基面（basal plane）的极小偏离控制。CUDA加速求解器在平衡分布、弛豫轨迹和开关时间上均与蒙特卡洛模拟一致。在热辅助场驱动开关的应用中，该方法能够高效地获得超低错误概率，而这在直接蒙特卡洛模拟中实际难以实现。

Conclusion: 所提出的约化随机框架为Mn3Sn中热辅助八极矩动力学提供了一种高效且准确的计算方法。该方法显著扩展了可访问的概率范围，能够研究直接蒙特卡洛模拟无法触及的超低错误概率区域，为反铁磁自旋电子学（antiferromagnetic spintronics）中的器件可靠性分析提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We develop a reduced stochastic framework for thermally assisted octupole moment dynamics in Mn3Sn by combining the reduced Landau--Lifshitz--Gilbert (LLG) equation with the Fokker--Planck formalism. The reduced model is benchmarked against the complete three-sublattice octupole dynamics and is shown to capture the essential switching behavior with good accuracy. We then derive the corresponding Fokker--Planck equation, which is implemented and solved via a CUDA-accelerated solver. The analysis shows that the octupole dynamics are highly sensitive to the out-of-plane grid resolution because ultrafast rotation of the octupole is controlled by its very small deviations from the basal plane. The solver is validated against Monte Carlo simulations through equilibrium distributions, relaxation trajectories, and switching times. Finally, we apply the method to thermally assisted field-driven switching and demonstrate efficient access to ultra-low error probabilities beyond the practical reach of direct Monte Carlo simulations.

### [146] [Emergent Quantum-Geometric Equivalence of Injection and Shift Currents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08643)
*Mohammad Yahyavi,Tay-Rong Chang,Md Shafayat Hossain,Arun Bansil,Naoto Nagaosa,Guoqing Chang*

TL;DR: 本文揭示了注入电流（injection current）和移位电流（shift current）这两种非线性光学响应之间隐藏的普遍联系，该联系通过带间贝里曲率（interband Berry-curvature）和量子度量偶极子（quantum-metric dipoles）建立。在费米能级附近具有近似线性电子色散的低光子能量体系中，这种关系进一步演化为等价性，两者由相同的带间量子几何偶极子（interband quantum-geometric dipole）主导。该机制自然地体现在狄拉克半金属、外尔半金属以及应变石墨烯中，表明非线性光学实验测量的是电子波函数的统一几何性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点将注入电流和移位电流视为具有不同微观起源的两种独立非线性光学响应。本文旨在揭示两者之间此前未被注意到的深层联系，并探索量子几何（quantum geometry）作为统一原理在固体非线性光学响应中的普适作用。

Method: 通过理论分析，建立注入电流与移位电流在带间贝里曲率和量子度量偶极子框架下的数学联系。进一步在费米面附近具有近似线性电子色散（linear electronic dispersion）且光子能量较低的体系中，推导出两者趋于等价的结论，并以狄拉克半金属、外尔半金属和应变石墨烯为例进行论证。

Result: 发现了注入电流与移位电流之间存在基于带间量子几何偶极子的一般性隐藏联系；在特定条件下（近似线性色散、低光子能量），该联系演化为严格的等价关系，即两种电流均由同一量子几何偶极子控制。

Conclusion: 该结果为解释非线性光学实验提供了新框架，并暗示量子几何可能作为一种更广泛的组织原则（organizing principle），用于统一固体中看似截然不同的非线性光学响应。

Abstract: Injection and shift currents are generally regarded as distinct nonlinear optical responses with separate microscopic origins. Here, we uncover a general hidden connection between them through interband Berry-curvature and quantum-metric dipoles. In systems with approximately linear electronic dispersion near the Fermi level and at low photon energies, this relation sharpens into an emergent equivalence, with injection and shift currents governed by the same interband quantum-geometric dipole. This regime is naturally realized in Dirac and Weyl semimetals, as well as in strained graphene, where measurements of injection and shift currents probe a unified geometric property of the electronic wavefunctions rather than distinct dynamical processes. Our results establish a new framework for interpreting nonlinear optical experiments and suggest that quantum geometry may provide a broader organizing principle linking seemingly distinct nonlinear optical responses in solids.

### [147] [An ab initio approach to energy alignment and charge-state prediction of adsorbates on ultrathin insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08795)
*Kevin Lizárraga,Saba Taherpour,Cesar E. P. Villegas,Christoph Wolf*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该方法将整个过程分解为多个物理子过程：利用GW计算获取孤立吸附物的电离势（ionization potential）与电子亲和能（electron affinity）；通过基底引起的准粒子重整化（quasiparticle renormalization）量化电子带隙极化；采用整数电荷转移模型（integer charge transfer model）评估费米能级钉扎；并由静电势的局域变化确定由Pauli排斥或吸附物-金属偶极引起的功函数偏移（work function shift）。

Result: 该框架在计算效率上显著优于完整的吸附物/氧化物/金属全体系模拟，同时能够透明地揭示所有涉及的物理过程，实现了计算成本与精度的平衡。

Conclusion: 这一计算高效的理论框架为分子量子比特和有机电子界面的高通量筛选（high-throughput screening）提供了可行的路径。

Abstract: The rapid progress of electron spin resonance scanning tunneling microscopy experiments has enabled the manipulation of individual adsorbate spin states physisorbed on ultrathin oxide layers supported on metal substrates. Electron resonance requires unpaired spin density on the adsorbate, which can be achieved, for instance, through charge transfer from the supporting substrate. This requires the correct energy-level alignment between the energy levels of the adsorbate and the Fermi energy of the substrate. Experiments on molecules and single atoms adsorbed on metal-insulator systems have revealed complex phenomena, including electronic bandgap narrowing, charge transfer, Fermi-level pinning, and the re-ordering of adsorbate orbitals after charge transfer. Despite these advances, a predictive first-principles approach based on accurate methods such as quasiparticle GW, capable of capturing these effects without the prohibitive cost of full adsorbate/oxide/metal simulations, remains an open challenge. In this work, we present a theoretical approach to determine the energy-level alignment of adsorbates on oxide/metal substrates. Our method transparently exposes all physical processes and strikes a balance between computational cost and accuracy. Ionization potentials and electron affinities of the isolated adsorbates are obtained using GW calculations, electronic bandgap polarization is quantified through the quasiparticle renormalization caused by the substrate, Fermi-level pinning is evaluated within the integer charge transfer model, and work function shifts arising from Pauli pushback or from the adsorbate-metal dipole are determined from the local variations of the electrostatic potential. This computationally efficient framework paves the way for highthroughput screening of molecular qubits and organic electronic interfaces.

### [148] [Localization phase diagram of the Hexagonal Lattice with irrational magnetic flux](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09974)
*Qi Gao,Shuo Zhang,Wei Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用Avila全局理论（Avila's global theory）解析求解了六角晶格（hexagonal lattice）上具有无理磁通（irrational magnetic flux）的Hofstadter模型（Hofstadter model），得到了精确的局域化相图（localization phase diagram），并通过重整化群（renormalization group）理论和数值分析加以验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Avila的Fields奖工作已数学上解决了方晶格无理磁通Hofstadter模型，但该理论通常不适用于具有子晶格（sub-lattices）或自旋（spin）等内部自由度的晶格。本研究旨在证明六角晶格（尽管有两个子晶格）仍可通过2×2转移矩阵（transfer matrix）精确求解，从而扩展Avila理论的应用范围。

Method: 构造六角晶格仅含最近邻跳跃（nearest neighbor hopping）的Hofstadter模型，用一个2×2转移矩阵描述系统，并应用Avila全局理论进行精确求解。随后使用重整化群理论验证部分相图，对于剩余部分，通过数值计算分形维数（fractal dimension）加以确定。

Result: 得到了六角晶格无理磁通下的精确局域化相图，揭示出三种纯相（pure phases）：扩展态（extended）、局域态（localized）和临界态（critical）。由于手征对称性（chiral symmetry），系统中不存在迁移率边（mobility edge）。重整化群理论和数值分析的结果均与Avila全局理论给出的相图一致。

Conclusion: 六角晶格Hofstadter模型在无理磁通条件下可被Avila全局理论精确求解，所得相图得到了重整化群理论与数值计算的双重确认。该工作扩展了Avila理论在具有内部自由度的晶格系统中的应用。

Abstract: We study the Hofstadter model on a hexagonal lattice with irrational magnetic flux in this work. The Hofstadter model of the square lattice with irrational flux has been solved mathematically by Avila in his Fields medal work. However, this theory is usually not applicable to lattices with internal degrees of freedom, such as spin or sub-lattices. In this work, we show that for the hexagonal lattice with only nearest neighbor hopping, the system can still be characterized by a 2*2 transfer matrix and solved exactly by Avila$'$s global theory of Avila although this lattice has two sub-lattices. We obtained the exact localization phase diagram of the hexagonal lattice with irrational flux by this theory, which reveals three pure phases, that is, the extended, localized and critical states but no mobility edge due to the chiral symmetry. We used the renormalization group (RG) theory to verify these results, which can determine part of the phase diagram. We then computed the fractal dimension of the remaining part numerically. The results from both the RG theory and numerical analysis confirmed the phase diagram we get from Avila$'$s global theory.

In this paper, we theoretically propose such a tool, leveraging the magnetoelectric effect induced by a localized electric field generated by one or several charged tips. Combining complementary numerical simulations and analytical approaches, we develop a consistent theory describing the stability and dynamics of Néel-type skyrmions under the influence of the electric field from a charged tip. Specifically, we demonstrate that the electric field can create, drive, and annihilate skyrmions of both chiralities, as well as more complex textures such as skyrmioniums and target skyrmions. Finally, we discuss the feasibility of a practical device capable of controlled skyrmion manipulation based on this principle.

### [150] [Effect of spin-dependent tunneling and intervalley scattering in magnetic-semiconductor van der Waals heterostructures on exciton and trion polarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09088)

Method: 采用理论分析方法，结合磁邻近效应（magnetic proximity effect）与自洽的光致发光（PL）偏振模型，考虑自旋依赖的层间电荷转移（spin-dependent interlayer charge transfer）、激子（exciton）与三重子（trion）的谷间散射（intervalley scattering）过程，以及亮激子与暗激子之间谷间和谷内散射（intravalley scattering）的广义化处理。

Result: 揭示了电子隧穿时间尺度（electron tunneling timescale）与激子和三重子的谷间散射寿命及辐射寿命（radiative lifetimes）之间的比值关系决定了光致发光（PL）动力学行为；发现了在圆偏振激光激发下，由于准粒子动力学（quasi-particles dynamics）可实现PL偏振符号（PL polarization sign）的切换。

Conclusion: 所得结果支持对激子与三重子行为的长距离操控（long-distance manipulation），为在多层磁性-半导体范德华异质结构中实现自旋和谷赝自旋（spin and valley pseudospin）的有效控制提供了新途径。

Abstract: We present a theoretical analysis of valley pseudospin control in the transition metal dichalcogenide (TMD) monolayer by utilizing the magnetic proximity effect of 2D magnetic layer and, propose self-consistent analysis of photoluminescence (PL) polarization peculiarities in TMD/magnetic material van der Waals heterostructures. We attribute observed peculiarities to the interplay between spin-dependent interlayer charge transfer and intervalley scattering of excitons and trions. The ratio between the electron tunneling timescale and the exciton and trion intervalley scattering lifetimes and radiative lifetimes determine the PL dynamics. A possibility to switch PL polarization sign due to the quasi-particles dynamics under circularly polarized laser excitations is revealed. We also discuss generalization of the proposed model due to the careful analysis of both intervalley and intravalley scattering processes between bright and dark excitons. Obtained results allow a long-distance manipulation of exciton and trion behaviors and open the possibilities for the effective control under spin and valley pseudospin in multilayer magnetic-semiconductor van der Waals heterostructures.

</details>


### [151] [Theory and Experiment of Chirality-induced Magnetic Nonreciprocity Manifested by Coupling Phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09135)
*Jiguang Yao,Ying Yang,Chenyang Lu,Lihua Zhong,Xiaolong Fan,Desheng Xue,C. -M. Hu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，磁性相互作用（magnetic interactions）是实现非互易性最稳健且最广泛使用的方法，但现有研究缺乏对其中关键手性机制的统一理解，尤其是常规手性与合成手性之间的内在联系尚不明确。

Method: 首先考察通过特殊结构产生手性电磁场（chiral electromagnetic fields）的常规手性相互作用，随后重点分析基于行波耦合系统中非平庸相位累积（nontrivial phase accumulation）实现的合成手性。建立了一个微观理论框架，将场极化（field polarization）映射为复耦合强度（complex coupling strength）的相位，并通过系统实验加以验证。

Result: 所建立的理论框架提供了一种统一的形式化描述（consistent formalism），能够同时涵盖常规手性与合成手性。特别地，研究揭示了合成手性区别于常规非互易机制（conventional nonreciprocal mechanisms）的对称性性质（symmetry properties）与独特特征。

Conclusion: 该工作从统一的理论与实验视角阐明了磁性非互易性的手性机制，合成手性因其独特的对称性特征可能为非互易光子学（nonreciprocal photonics）提供新的设计自由度。

Abstract: Magnetic interactions have long served as the most robust and widely used approach for realizing nonreciprocity, with an externally applied magnetic field breaking time-reversal symmetry (TRS) and chiral photon-magnon interactions introducing spatial asymmetry. In this work, we investigate the chirality mechanisms essential for magnetic nonreciprocity from a unified experimental and theoretical perspective. We begin by examining conventional chiral interactions that generate chiral electromagnetic fields through specially designed structures, and then place particular emphasis on synthetic chirality enabled by nontrivial phase accumulation in traveling-wave-mediated coupling systems. We establish a microscopic theoretical framework that maps field polarization onto the phase of a complex coupling strength and validate it with systematic experiments, thereby providing a consistent formalism that describes both conventional and synthetic chirality. Notably, we highlight the symmetry properties and the unique features of synthetic chirality that distinguish it from conventional nonreciprocal mechanisms.

### [152] [Magnetization alignment in spin-transfer-torque magnetic random-access memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09201)
*Afan Terko,George Lertzman-Lepofsky,Dieter Suess,Claas Abert,Erol Girt*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过微磁学（micromagnetic）模拟，系统研究了30纳米直径的三层垂直自旋转移力矩磁随机存储器（p-STT-MRAM）纳米柱，绘制了以双线性与双二次层间交换耦合为函数的平衡态相图，发现引入合成反铁磁（SAF）参考层之间的不对称性可稳定反平行态并提高SAF翻转势垒，同时公开了4374种器件配置的仿真数据集以支持器件设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 垂直自旋转移力矩磁随机存储器（perpendicular spin-transfer-torque magnetic random-access memory, p-STT-MRAM）的可靠运行需要精确控制合成反铁磁（synthetic antiferromagnet, SAF）参考层内的磁取向。然而在纳米柱（nanopillar）尺度下，器件可能展现出在扩展薄膜中不存在的磁态，因此需要系统理解这些尺寸效应及其对器件性能的影响。

Method: 采用基于实验物性参数的微磁学（micromagnetic）模拟，对直径为30纳米的三层p-STT-MRAM纳米柱进行系统研究。通过绘制以双线性（bilinear）和双二次（biquadratic）层间交换耦合为函数的平衡态相图（phase diagram），分析SAF层在饱和磁化强度、磁各向异性及厚度方面不对称性对磁态的影响，并结合最小能量路径（minimum-energy path）计算评估翻转势垒变化。

Result: 引入SAF层间在饱和磁化强度、磁各向异性和厚度上的不对称性，可以降低稳定反平行SAF态所需的耦合强度，并抑制竞争磁构型。对于非共线反平行SAF态，增加不对称性可提高SAF翻转势垒但降低自由层势垒，形成权衡关系；而共线反平行SAF态则不存在这一权衡。杂散场（stray fields）对SAF和自由层的能量势垒均有显著影响。

Conclusion: SAF层间的不对称性设计可用于调控p-STT-MRAM器件的磁态稳定性与翻转势垒，但需注意非共线构型中SAF与自由层势垒之间的权衡。为支持具有共线或非共线反平行SAF参考态器件的设计，研究团队公开发布了涵盖4374种器件构型的仿真数据集。

Abstract: Reliable operation of perpendicular spin-transfer-torque magnetic random-access memory (p-STT-MRAM) requires control of magnetic alignment within the synthetic antiferromagnet (SAF) reference layer. At nanopillar dimensions, however, devices can exhibit magnetic states that are absent in extended thin films. We present a systematic micromagnetic study of 30 nm-diameter three-layer p-STT-MRAM nanopillars using experimentally motivated material parameters, and map equilibrium states as functions of bilinear and biquadratic interlayer exchange coupling. Phase diagrams show that introducing asymmetry between the SAF layers in saturation magnetization, anisotropy, and thickness reduces the coupling strength required to stabilize antiparallel SAF states and suppress competing configurations. Minimum-energy path calculations show that, for noncollinear antiparallel SAF states, increasing SAF asymmetry can raise SAF reversal barriers while lowering the free-layer barrier; this trade-off is absent for collinear antiparallel SAF states. Stray fields also significantly modify both SAF and free-layer energy barriers. To support the design of p-STT-MRAM devices with either collinear or noncollinear antiparallel SAF reference states, we publicly release the simulation dataset covering 4374 distinct device configurations.

</details>

We introduce spin elasticity-a framework linking spin torque to spin morpgology. This reveals a topological Hooke's law, uncovers spontaneous oscillations and resonance, and predicts a new class of collective excitations:spin stress waves. By establishing a unfied tau-D theory bridging classical elasticity and topological spin physics, this work completes the elastic picture and opens a new frontier for spintronics-spinelastronics.

### [154] [Inherent Altermagnetism on regular hyperbolic lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10602)
*Eric Petermann,Kristian Mæland,Haye Hinrichsen,Björn Trauzettel*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究将交替磁体（altermagnets）的欧几里得紧束缚模型推广到二维双曲格点（hyperbolic lattices），证明次近邻跃迁足以诱导自旋分裂，确认交替磁性是某些双曲格点的固有属性，并利用四维原子轨道对主导自旋分裂谐波进行分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交替磁体是一类动量依赖自旋分裂（momentum-dependent spin splitting）但无净磁化的新型磁性系统，此前研究主要局限于欧几里得（Euclidean）几何框架下的格点模型。探索交替磁性在非欧几何（如双曲空间）中的存在性和表现形式，有助于扩展对该现象的理解。

Method: 将欧几里得交替磁体的紧束缚模型（tight-binding models）推广到二维双曲格点，后者定义在离散化的庞加莱圆盘（Poincaré disk）上。利用双曲晶体学（hyperbolic crystallography）和双曲能带理论（hyperbolic band theory）进行分析，并通过引入次近邻跃迁（next-nearest neighbor hopping, NNN）来检验自旋分裂条件。

Result: 次近邻跃迁足以在二分双曲格点（bipartite hyperbolic lattices）中诱导自旋分裂。尽管某些双曲格点族和特殊情况仍保持反铁磁性（antiferromagnetic），但发现一个完整的格点族和一个特殊情况在该框架下表现出自旋分裂。由于双曲能带理论给出的动量空间至少是四维，因此利用四维原子轨道（four-dimensional atomic orbitals）对主导自旋分裂谐波进行了分类。

Conclusion: 交替磁性是某些双曲格点的固有属性，表明这一现象不仅限于欧几里得几何系统，在双曲几何中同样存在。四维动量空间的分析框架为未来研究双曲交替磁体的物理性质提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Altermagnets are a novel class of magnetic systems characterized by their momentum-dependent spin splitting without net magnetization. In this work, we extend established Euclidean tight-binding models of altermagnets to regular hyperbolic lattices in two spatial dimensions defined on a discretized Poincaré disk. Using hyperbolic crystallography and hyperbolic band theory, we show that the inclusion of next-nearest neighbor hopping is sufficient to induce spin splitting in bipartite hyperbolic lattices. While certain families and special cases of hyperbolic lattices remain antiferromagnetic, we identify an entire family and a special case that show spin splitting in this framework. Hence, altermagnetism is inherent to certain hyperbolic lattices. Since hyperbolic band theory yields a momentum space that is at least four-dimensional, we classify the leading spin-splitting harmonics using four-dimensional atomic orbitals.

### [155] [Coherence, long-range transport and nuclear polarization in a driven-dissipative dark exciton condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09488)
*Amit Jash,Maheswar Swar,Uri Shimon,Vladimir Umansky,Israel Bar-Joseph*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在耦合量子阱中的暗偶极激子（dark dipolar excitons）凝聚体中发现了宏观相干性的直接证据，并证明其形成遵循非平衡驱动-耗散（driven-dissipative）机制。凝聚转变由增益-损耗竞争（gain-loss competition）主导，暗激子的超长寿命使其在模式选择中占据优势。通过光致发光变暗、辐射复合通道变化以及毫米级密度（声）模式传播等实验现象揭示了凝聚体的形成。暗激子密度积累引发动态核极化（dynamic nuclear polarization），通过Overhauser场关闭暗-亮激子能隙Δ，产生显著磁滞行为。在Δ~0时能隙锁定且凝聚体损耗最小，出现第二个阈值即光致发光蓝移。通过入射与边界反射激子流之间的干涉揭示了相干性，并提取出凝聚体相干长度。这些结果将暗激子确立为驱动-耗散、强相互作用、电学可调谐条件下的相干量子流体平台，桥接了极化激元凝聚体（polariton condensates）与类物质激子系统之间的物理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗偶极激子凝聚体中的宏观相干性及其非平衡形成机制，填补极化激元凝聚体与常规激子系统之间的物理空白，为强相互作用量子流体研究提供新的可控平台。

Method: 在耦合量子阱中制备暗偶极激子凝聚体，通过光致发光（photoluminescence）光谱测量、辐射复合通道分析、毫米级距离上的密度波传播观测、动态核极化效应测量以及干涉实验等手段表征其性质。

Result: 发现凝聚转变由增益-损耗竞争主导；观察到光致发光变暗、辐射复合通道变化和毫米级长程流体动力学输运；验证了动态核极化对暗-亮激子能隙Δ的调控及其导致的磁滞行为；在Δ~0时观察到能隙锁定和第二个光致发光蓝移阈值；通过干涉实验提取出凝聚体相干长度。

Conclusion: 暗激子凝聚体是一种非平衡驱动-耗散机制下的宏观相干量子流体，具有强相互作用和电学可调谐特性，为连接极化激元凝聚体与常规激子系统提供了新的研究平台。

Abstract: We report direct evidence for macroscopic coherence in a condensate of dark dipolar excitons in coupled quantum wells and show that its formation follows a non-equilibrium, driven-dissipative mechanism. The condensation transition is governed by gain-loss competition, in which the exceptionally long lifetime of dark excitons enables their dominance in mode selection. Condensate formation is revealed by photoluminescence darkening, changes in radiative recombination channels, and the emergence of long-range hydrodynamic transport manifested by propagation of density (sound) modes over millimeter-scale distances. The buildup of dark exciton density induces dynamic nuclear polarization, which closes the dark-bright exciton gap, Δ, via the Overhauser field. This leads to nuclear spin polarization across the entire mesa, far beyond the optically excited region, and produces pronounced hysteresis behavior. At Δ~ 0 the gap is locked and the condensate loss are minimal, resulting in a second threshold manifested as a photoluminescence blueshift. Coherence is revealed through interference between incident and boundary-reflected exciton currents, producing spatial modulation of the photoluminescence from the radiative reservoir and enabling extraction of the condensate coherence length. These results establish dark excitons as a platform for coherent quantum fluids in a driven-dissipative, strongly interacting regime with electrical tunability, bridging the physics of polariton condensates and matter-like excitonic systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

### [157] [Spin Seebeck effect in magnetic junctions with a compensated ferrimagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09885)
*Xin Theng Lee,Takahiro Misawa,Mamoru Matsuo,Takeo Kato*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过四子晶格模型和非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function）方法，研究了补偿型亚铁磁体/正常金属结中的自旋塞贝克效应（spin Seebeck effect），发现各向同性的磁子劈裂（isotropic magnon splitting）可产生与标准铁磁结相当的稳健自旋流，并证明交变磁体（altermagnet）结在相同条件下自旋塞贝克效应为零，从而确立了补偿型亚铁磁体在热自旋流生成中的独特地位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 补偿型亚铁磁体（compensated ferrimagnet）具有零净磁化强度却支持类铁磁自旋输运的特性，但其热自旋流生成机制尚不明确。已有研究仅关注各向异性机制，而交换耦合不对称性（exchange-coupling asymmetry）所导致的子晶格不等效性是否也能驱动自旋塞贝克效应仍有待探索。

Method: 采用四子晶格模型（four-sublattice model），其中子晶格不等效性源自交换耦合差异而非各向异性。在非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function）框架下分析补偿型亚铁磁体/正常金属结中的自旋塞贝克效应，并与交变磁体（altermagnet）结进行对比。

Result: 各向同性的磁子劈裂（isotropic magnon splitting）可在补偿型亚铁磁体结中产生稳健的自旋流，其量级与标准铁磁结相当。在相同条件下，交变磁体结的自旋塞贝克效应完全消失。

Conclusion: 具有交换耦合不对称性的补偿型亚铁磁体可作为无杂散场自旋流源（stray-field-free spin-current source），在自旋电子学（spintronics）器件中具有应用潜力。该工作为磁补偿系统中热自旋流生成提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Compensated ferrimagnets enable ferromagnet-like spin transport without net magnetization. We study the spin Seebeck effect in a compensated ferrimagnet/normal-metal junction using a four-sublattice model in which sublattice inequivalence arises from differences in exchange couplings, in contrast to the previously studied anisotropy-based mechanism. Within the nonequilibrium Green's function framework, we show that isotropic magnon splitting generates a robust spin current with a magnitude comparable to that in standard ferromagnetic junctions. We also demonstrate that the spin Seebeck effect vanishes in altermagnet junctions under identical conditions, thereby establishing compensated ferrimagnets as uniquely suited for thermal spin-current generation among magnetically compensated systems. These results provide a theoretical basis for the applications of compensated ferrimagnets with exchange-coupling asymmetry as stray-field-free spin-current sources in spintronic devices.

</details>


### [158] [Antisymmetric linear transverse magnetization and ferroaxial moments induced by geometry-driven electric field gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09966)
*Akane Inda,Satoru Hayami*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上研究了有限系统几何形状产生的电场梯度所诱导的横向磁化（transverse magnetization）和铁轴矩（ferroaxial moments）。基于Kubo形式论（Kubo formalism）和有限梯形模型的实时数值模拟，证明这两种量在电场梯度下产生，并可通过调节腿倾斜度（leg inclination）增强。诱导的横向磁化是反对称的且与磁场线性相关，在无电场梯度时该响应被Onsager倒易关系（Onsager reciprocity）禁止。横向磁化与电场呈线性关系，而纵向磁化呈二次关系，有利于实验观测。结果确立了几何诱导电场梯度作为介观系统中实现和控制非常规横向响应的通用机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有限系统几何形状产生的电场梯度能否诱导横向磁化和铁轴矩，并揭示其物理机制与调控方式，为介观系统中非常规横向响应提供新的实现途径。

Method: 采用Kubo形式论进行理论推导，并结合有限梯形模型的实时数值模拟，分析电场梯度下横向磁化与铁轴矩的产生条件与行为。

Result: 电场梯度可诱导横向磁化和铁轴矩，且通过调节腿倾斜度可增强该效应；诱导的横向磁化是反对称的并与磁场线性相关，在无电场梯度时被Onsager倒易关系禁止；横向磁化随电场线性增长，而纵向磁化呈二次增长。

Conclusion: 几何诱导的电场梯度可作为介观系统中实现和控制非常规横向响应的通用机制，且横向磁化的线性电场依赖性为实验观测提供了优势。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the transverse magnetization and ferroaxial moments induced by electric field gradients arising from the geometry of finite systems. Based on the Kubo formalism and real-time numerical simulations for a finite trapezoidal model, we demonstrate that both quantities are generated under the electric field gradient and are enhanced by tuning the leg inclination, which controls the gradient strength. We further show that the induced transverse magnetization is antisymmetric and linear in the magnetic field; such a response is prohibited by Onsager reciprocity in the absence of an electric field gradient. In addition, we find that the total transverse magnetization scales linearly with the electric field, in contrast to the longitudinal one, which exhibits a quadratic dependence, providing an advantage for experimental observation. Our results establish geometry-induced electric field gradients as a versatile mechanism for realizing and controlling unconventional transverse responses in mesoscopic systems.

</details>


### [159] [Orbital and Spin Nernst Effects in Monolayers of Transition Metal Dichalcogenides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10033)
*Saikat Saha,Arnab Bose,Sayantika Bhowal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过解析低能谷模型和全布里渊区紧束缚计算，证明单层过渡金属二硫族化物（TMD）是观测轨道能斯特效应（orbital Nernst effect）的优异平台；该效应不依赖自旋-轨道耦合，且与自旋能斯特效应共存；同时揭示了轨道贝里曲率和自旋贝里曲率的核心作用，并通过掺杂可调控这两种能斯特响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轨道电子学效应（orbitronic effects）作为自旋电子学（spintronics）的互补方向日益受到关注，但轨道能斯特效应——即温度梯度产生横向轨道电流（orbital current）的现象——仍较少被探索。本文旨在论证单层过渡金属二硫族化物（transition metal dichalcogenides, TMDs）可作为观测该效应的理想平台，并阐明其微观机制。

Method: 基于低能谷模型（low-energy valley model）进行解析推导以揭示轨道能斯特效应的微观机制；同时，针对单层2H MoS₂和2H NbS₂两种代表性体系，采用全布里渊区紧束缚方法（full Brillouin-zone tight-binding method）对解析结果进行数值验证。

Result: 轨道能斯特效应与轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect）类似，均不依赖自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）；费米能级附近的电子态对该效应起关键作用。加入自旋-轨道耦合后产生自旋能斯特效应（spin Nernst effect），其强度与自旋-轨道耦合大小成正比。在MoS₂中，轨道和自旋能斯特电导率均需电子或空穴掺杂才出现；而在金属性NbS₂中，两者本征存在。

Conclusion: 轨道和自旋贝里曲率（orbital and spin Berry curvatures）在能斯特效应中发挥核心作用；掺杂是调控轨道和自旋能斯特响应的有效手段。本文还提出了在单层过渡金属二硫族化物中探测这些效应的实验方案。

Abstract: In recent years, orbitronic effects have attracted growing attention as complementary counterparts to the well-established spintronic phenomena. In this work, we demonstrate that monolayers of transition metal dichalcogenides provide an excellent platform for the observation of the orbital Nernst effect, a relatively less explored phenomenon describing the generation of a transverse orbital current in response to an applied temperature gradient. We show that, similar to its electrical counterpart, viz., the orbital Hall effect, the orbital Nernst effect does not require the presence of spin-orbit coupling. Analytical results based on a low-energy valley model offer key insights into the underlying mechanisms, highlighting in particular the crucial role of electronic states at the Fermi energy for the emergence of this effect. The inclusion of spin-orbit coupling further gives rise to a spin Nernst effect, which scales with the strength of spin-orbit coupling and vanishes in its absence. We substantiate our analytical findings with full Brillouin-zone tight-binding results for two representative systems, monolayer 2H MoS$_2$ and 2H NbS$_2$. Our results show that while both orbital and spin Nernst conductivities in MoS$_2$ require electron or hole doping, both effects are intrinsically present in metallic NbS$_2$. Our work reveals the central role of orbital and spin Berry curvatures, identifies doping as an effective route for tuning orbital and spin Nernst responses, and proposes a possible experimental setup for detecting these effects in monolayer transition metal dichalcogenides.

</details>


### [160] [Cascade of fractional quantum Hall states in 2D system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10147)
*Chen Zhimou,Yan Jiaojie,Zhu Yuxuan,Cui Zhe,Pfeiffer Loren N.,West Kenneth W.,Baldwin Kirk W.,Gupta Adbhut,Liu Yang,Zhu Wei,Luo Wenchen,Wu Ying-Hai,Yuan Shuai,Lin Xi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过超高迁移率GaAs/AlGaAs量子阱的极低温量子输运测量，系统研究了分数量子霍尔（FQH）效应，在填充因子17/33和15/31处观测到新的纵向电阻极小值，并基于复合费米子（composite fermion）理论框架对实验观察到的分数态进行了系统性解释和模式总结。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数量子霍尔（FQH）效应是强电子关联驱动的拓扑相，具有分数化元激发、无能隙边界态和非平凡量子纠缠等特征。随着新材料平台发展和样品质量提升，实验中不断发现新的FQH态，亟需对超高迁移率体系中的FQH态进行全面系统的研究。

Method: 采用超高迁移率（高达3.7×10^7 cm^2/V/s）的GaAs/AlGaAs量子阱样品，结合核绝热去磁和稀释制冷技术进行低至1 mK的极低温量子输运测量；通过施加面内磁场考察FQH态的变化行为。

Result: 在填充因子0<ν<2范围内观测到大量已知FQH态，并首次在填充因子17/33和15/31处发现新的纵向电阻极小值。面内磁场的施加导致不同FQH态呈现差异性的变化行为。

Conclusion: 大多数填充因子可解释为非相互作用复合费米子（composite fermion）形成的整数量子霍尔态，少数态则源于复合费米子之间的剩余相互作用导致的FQH态。研究总结了0<ν<2范围内的观测分数，并提出一个实验出现模式，为不同FQH态的相对强度提供了直观图像。

Abstract: The observation of the fractional quantum Hall (FQH) effect in 2D electron gases ushered in investigations of topological phases driven by strong electron correlations. Their remarkable features include fractionalized elementary excitations, gapless boundary states, and non-trivial quantum entanglement patterns. Thanks to persistent efforts in the building of new platforms and making higher-quality samples, a diverse plethora of FQH states have been unveiled in experiments. We report a systematic study of ultrahigh-quality GaAs/AlGaAs quantum wells with mobility up to 3.7*10^7 cm^2/V/s using quantum transport measurements in nuclear adiabatic demagnetization and dilution refrigerators down to 1 mK. In addition to many FQH states that have already been identified in previous work, new longitudinal resistance dips are observed at filling factors 17/33 and 15/31. The application of an in-plane magnetic field causes disparate variations of the FQH states. The theoretical foundation of these states is discussed in the framework of composite fermion theory. While most fractions can be explained as non-interacting composite fermions forming integer quantum Hall states, a few states correspond to FQH states of composite fermions that arise from residual interaction between them. We summarize the observed fractions in the range of 0 < ν < 2 and propose a pattern to account for their experimental appearance that provides an intuitive picture about the relative strengths of different FQH states.

*S. Z. Rakhmanov,K. P. Matchonov,A. K. Rakhimov,D. U. Matrasulov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究石墨烯纳米带中一维相对论性类氢原子模型，特别是原子核有限尺寸效应下的超临界能级与临界电荷行为，以理解受限体系对狄拉克海（Dirac sea）边界的影响。

Method: 采用一维狄拉克方程描述电子在库仑势中的运动，并考虑原子核的有限尺寸；分别求解未受限原子和盒中原子两种情形下的本征值与波函数。

Result: 受限原子的临界电荷（critical charge）大于自由原子的临界电荷；展示了两种情形下的局域态密度，并发现盒中原子体系存在强局域化（strong localization）现象。

Conclusion: 空间受限会显著影响类氢原子的相对论性电子结构，导致临界电荷增大和强局域化效应，这些特征具有实验可观测性。

Abstract: We consider a model of 1D relativistic hydrogen-like atom, formed by a Coulomb impurity in graphene nanoribbon. Describing the electron motion in terms of the one-dimensional Dirac equation for Coulomb potential taking into account the finite-size of the atomic nucleus, we compute the eigenvalues and eigenfunctions of the atomic electron. The cases of unconfined atom and atomin-box system are considered. Special focus is given calculation of supercritical energy levels and the critical charge. The latter is the value of the atomic nucleus charge, when the electronic state reaches the border of the Dirac sea. It is found that for confined atom the value of the critical charge is larger than that of free atom. Experimentally measurable characteristics, local density of states is also plotted for both cases. Existence of strong localization for atom-in-box system is shown.

### [162] [Ultra-Fast Quantum Control via Non-Adiabatic Resonance Windows: A 9x Speed-up on 127-Qubit IBM Processors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10578)
*A. M. Tishin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 在IBM 127量子比特处理器上发现了一个约4.9频率处的非绝热共振窗口（non-adiabatic resonance window），可相比传统绝热极限（adiabatic limit）将门操作时长缩短9.2倍，同时保持高保真度。跨后端同步实验验证了共振剖面的普适性（R=0.9998），但纵向分析表明该高Q窗口对亚百分比级校准漂移高度敏感，从而揭示了从静态门协议向动态共振追踪控制工具过渡的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导量子比特的标准绝热协议（adiabatic protocols）面临门速度与退相干（decoherence）之间的权衡。本文旨在突破这一权衡，探索非绝热区域中是否存在可同时实现高速和高保真的共振窗口。

Method: 使用IBM Quantum 127量子比特处理器（ibm_fez和ibm_kingston）进行实验，通过同步跨后端执行（synchronous cross-backend execution）测量共振剖面，并对高Q窗口进行纵向分析（longitudinal analysis）以评估其对校准漂移的敏感性。

Result: 在约4.9的频率处发现一个非绝热共振窗口，可实现门时长相较于传统绝热极限降低9.2倍，同时保持高保真度。跨后端实验显示共振剖面近乎完全相关（R=0.9998），证实了非绝热参数（non-adiabatic parameter）的普适性。然而，该高Q窗口对亚百分比级校准漂移敏感，系统会因此进入随机动力学区域（stochastic regime）。

Conclusion: 实现下一代量子性能需要从静态门协议向动态共振追踪控制工具（dynamic resonance-tracking control tools）的转变。本研究为超快、高性能量子架构提供了理论基础和实验证据。

Abstract: Standard adiabatic protocols for superconducting qubits often face a trade-off between gate speed and decoherence. In this work, using IBM Quantum 127-qubit processors (ibm_fez and ibm_kingston), we report the discovery of a fundamental non-adiabatic resonance window at about 4.9. This window demonstrates the potential for a 9.2-fold reduction in gate duration relative to the conventional adiabatic limit, while maintaining state high fidelities within the identified resonance windows. Through synchronous cross-backend execution, we demonstrate a near-perfect correlation (R = 0.9998) in the resonance profile, confirming the universality of the non-adiabatic parameter across independent hardware architectures. However, our longitudinal analysis reveals that these high-Q windows are sensitive to sub-percent calibration drifts, which dynamically shift the system into a stochastic regime. These findings suggest that achieving next-tier quantum performance requires a transition from static gate protocols to dynamic resonance-tracking control tools. This study provides both the theoretical foundation and the experimental evidence for such ultra-fast, high-performance quantum architectures.

</details>


### [163] [Theory of Spin-splitter Magnetoresistance in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10747)
*Tim Kokkeler,Vitaly N. Golovach,F. Sebastian Bergeret*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本论文建立了金属交替磁体（altermagnet）与铁磁绝缘体耦合体系中的角度依赖磁电阻（ADMR）理论，并提出了区分其与具有自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的传统补偿磁体的判据。自旋劈裂磁电阻（SSMR）被证明是金属体系中共线交替磁体（collinear altermagnetism）的确凿特征，其与自旋霍尔磁电阻（SMR）在响应依赖关系、符号和比例性质上有三方面关键区别，为输运实验明确识别交替磁体提供了清晰路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展金属交替磁体（altermagnet）与铁磁绝缘体（ferromagnetic insulator）耦合体系中的角度依赖磁电阻（angle-dependent magnetoresistance，ADMR）理论，并建立区分交替磁体与具有自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的传统补偿磁体（conventional compensated magnets）的明确判据。

Method: 通过构建金属交替磁体与铁磁绝缘体耦合的理论模型，推导角度依赖磁电阻（ADMR）的表达式，系统分析自旋劈裂磁电阻（spin-splitter magnetoresistance，SSMR）与自旋霍尔磁电阻（spin-Hall magnetoresistance，SMR）的差异。

Result: 发现自旋劈裂磁电阻（SSMR）仅依赖于铁磁磁化强度（ferromagnetic magnetization）与交替磁体奈尔矢量（Néel vector）的相对取向；SSMR产生符号相反的纵向ADMR响应；SSMR的纵向与横向ADMR信号之间存在直接比例关系，而自旋霍尔磁电阻（SMR）中不存在该关系。

Conclusion: 自旋劈裂磁电阻（SSMR）是金属体系中共线交替磁性（collinear altermagnetism）的确凿特征（smoking-gun signature），为在输运实验中明确识别交替磁体（altermagnet）提供了清晰路线。

Abstract: We develop a theory of angle-dependent magnetoresistance (ADMR) in metallic altermagnets coupled to ferromagnetic insulators and establish criteria that distinguish them from conventional compensated magnets with spin-orbit coupling. We show that the spin-splitter magnetoresistance (SSMR) reported by H. Chen et al. [Adv. Mater. 37, 2507764 (2025)] constitutes a smoking-gun signature of collinear altermagnetism in metallic systems. In contrast to spin-Hall magnetoresistance (SMR), SSMR exhibits three key distinctions: it depends solely on the relative orientation between the ferromagnetic magnetization and the altermagnetic Néel vector, yields a longitudinal ADMR response of opposite sign, and features a direct proportionality between longitudinal and transverse ADMR signals, absent in SMR. These results provide a clear route to unambiguously identify altermagnets in transport.

</details>
