### [164] [Non-Parametric Equation of State Reveals Non-Conformal Behavior Beyond Neutron Star Densities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08584)
*Yong-Jia Huang,Shao-Peng Tang,Yi-Zhong Fan*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出一种非参数化方法，从核壳层到渐近自由区域连续构建核物质的统计状态方程（EOS），发现大质量中子星（NS）内部存在强子-夸克相变（hadron-quark phase transition）的证据，表明非微扰夸克物质本质上是软的，与夸克星图像中的刚性情景根本不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 观测要求的中子星状态方程（equation of state, EOS）既要能支撑两倍太阳质量的中子星（neutron stars, NSs），又要使低质量NS的半径较小，这一全局热力学约束需要状态方程存在特定的刚度变化特征，促使作者寻找一种非参数化方法从核壳层到渐近自由区域连续构造EOS。

Method: 采用非参数化（non-parametric）方法，从核壳层到渐近自由（asymptotic-freedom）区域连续构造统计状态方程（statistical EOS），通过观测约束和微扰QCD（perturbative QCD, pQCD）能密度界限的反向约束，分析声速平方（$c_s^2$）和迹反常（trace anomaly）$Δ\equiv 1/3 - p/ε$的行为，并基于后验分布中非单调行为（non-monotonic behavior）的程度来推断相变证据。

Result: 声速平方$c_s^2$在大质量NS中呈现清晰峰值，随后需在较宽的密度范围内持续软化，且$c_s^2$直到约$30\,n_{\rm sat}$才趋近$1/3$；迹反常$Δ$在超过NS密度后变为正值，并从上方趋近pQCD极限；后验分析发现大质量NS核心中存在强子-夸克相变的证据。

Conclusion: 非微扰夸克物质（non-perturbative quark matter）本质上是软的，这与夸克星（quark-star）图像中夸克物质刚性（stiff）的情景根本不同；$Δ>0$的自然出现与夸克-强子混合相中的压力稀释、非共形pQCD修正或有限奇异夸克质量的对称性破缺效应等微观物理预期一致。

Abstract: We propose a non-parametric approach to construct the statistical equation of state (EOS) continuously from the nuclear crust to the asymptotic-freedom regime. Driven by the observationally required stiffening to support two-solar-mass neutron stars (NSs) with relatively small radii for low-mass NSs, this global thermodynamic constraint suggests a clear peak of squared sound speed ($c_s^2$) in massive NSs. To prevent overshooting perturbative QCD (pQCD) energy-density bounds, this early stiffening must be actively compensated by an extended density range of softening, with $c_s^2$ not approaching $1/3$ until $\sim\!30\,n_{\rm sat}$. Consistently, the trace anomaly $Δ\equiv 1/3 - p/ε$ becomes positive beyond NS densities and approaches the pQCD limit from above. This natural emergence of $Δ> 0$ organically aligns with some anticipated microphysics, likely arising from the pressure dilution in a quark-hadron mixed phase, non-conformal pQCD corrections to quark-gluon interactions, or the symmetry-breaking effects of finite strange quark mass. By measuring the degree of this non-monotonic behavior in the posterior, we find evidence for a hadron-quark phase transition in the cores of the most massive neutron stars. This indicates that the non-perturbative quark matter is intrinsically soft, fundamentally distinguishing it from the stiff scenarios associated with the quark-star picture.

</details>


### [165] [Bayesian Analysis of Massive Boson Star Models for Sagittarius A* Using Near-Infrared Astrometry Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09521)
*Xiangyu Wang,Tian-chi Ma,Minyong Guo,Hai-Qing Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过贝叶斯框架下的嵌套采样（nested sampling），对银河系中心致密源人马座A*（Sagittarius A*, Sgr~A*）分别建模为大质量玻色子星（boson star）和史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole），并利用近红外耀斑（near-infrared flare）天体测量数据进行比较。结果表明，在当前观测精度和参数范围内，两种模型的贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence）差异甚微，二者在统计上不可区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 银河系中心的致密天体Sgr~A*通常被认为是超大质量黑洞，但也有理论提出其可能为玻色子星等替代致密天体。为检验这一可能性，本文旨在利用近红外耀斑天体测量数据，定量比较玻色子星与史瓦西黑洞两种模型对观测的解释能力。

Method: 研究选取了12种离散的玻色子星构型，将耀斑建模为圆赤道轨道上的热点（hotspot）。在贝叶斯框架内采用嵌套采样方法进行参数估计，获得所有参数的边缘后验分布（marginal posterior distribution）及每种模型的贝叶斯证据。对史瓦西黑洞模型执行相同的分析流程以便对比。

Result: 玻色子星与史瓦西黑洞两种模型的贝叶斯证据值仅存在微小差异；Sgr~A*的质量（约4.296×10⁶ M☉）在各构型中均落在68%最高密度区间（highest density interval）内，且结果稳定。

Conclusion: 在当前的近红外天体测量约束和所考虑的参数范围内，大质量玻色子星与史瓦西黑洞作为银河系中心致密天体，在统计上仍然不可区分。

Abstract: Assuming that the compact source at the Galactic center, Sagittarius A*, is a massive boson star, we fit the near-infrared flare astrometry data. We consider 12 discrete boson star configurations and model the flare as a hotspot on a circular equatorial orbit. The analysis is performed in a Bayesian framework using nested sampling, yielding the marginal posterior distributions of all parameters as well as the Bayesian evidence for each model. For comparison, the same procedure is applied to a Schwarzschild black hole. The resulting Bayesian evidence values differ only marginally between the boson star and black hole cases, and the well-determined mass of Sgr~A* (${\sim}4.296\times 10^6\,M_\odot$) falls within the 68\% highest density interval in every configuration. We conclude that, under current near-infrared astrometric constraints and within the considered parameter ranges, a massive boson star and a Schwarzschild black hole remain statistically indistinguishable as the compact object at the Galactic center.

</details>


### [166] [Optical Appearance of the Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson Black Hole with a Magnetically Driven Synchrotron Emissivity Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09593)
*Zeng-Yi Zhang,Xiang-Qian Li,Hao-Peng Yan,Xiao-Jun Yue*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文采用磁驱动的同步辐射发射率（magnetically driven synchrotron emissivity）替代唯象幂律模型，结合向后光线追踪（backward ray-tracing）框架，研究了Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (Kerr-BR)黑洞在几何薄吸积盘照射下的光学外观，分析了自旋参数$a$、磁场参数$B$及观测者倾角$\theta_O$对射线分类图、红移分布和比强度图像的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统研究多采用唯象的幂律发射率模型，缺乏对黑洞周围实际电磁环境的物理刻画。本文旨在引入与局域电磁环境耦合的磁驱动同步辐射发射率，更真实地描述Kerr-BR黑洞吸积盘的辐射特性。

Method: 采用向后光线追踪框架，将磁驱动同步辐射发射率作为吸积盘的辐射源，替代传统的唯象幂律发射率模型。通过改变自旋参数$a$、磁场参数$B$和观测者倾角$\theta_O$，系统分析这些参数对射线分类图、红移分布及比强度图像的影响。

Result: ISCO位置同时受$a$和$B$修正；快速旋转的顺行（prograde）构型在磁主导近似失效时会发展出额外的模型依赖内边界（inner cutoff）。高分辨率一维强度轮廓可分离直接像、$n=1\)透镜环（lensing ring）及$n\geq 2$光子环（photon ring）子图像，并量化多普勒致亮度不对称性。逆行（retrograde）盘因ISCO外移呈现更宽的中心发射匮乏区，使高阶透镜成分更易与直接发射区分。

Conclusion: 盘内边界及磁场依赖的发射率显著影响Kerr-BR黑洞的可观测外观，表明磁驱动发射率模型对准确描述黑洞成像具有重要价值。

Abstract: We investigate the optical appearance of a Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (Kerr-BR) black hole illuminated by a geometrically and optically thin accretion disk. Instead of using a phenomenological power-law emissivity, we adopt a magnetically driven synchrotron emissivity proxy coupled to the local electromagnetic environment. With a backward ray-tracing framework, we examine the effects of the spin $a$, magnetic parameter $B$, and observer inclination $θ_O$ on the ray-classification maps, redshift distributions, and specific-intensity images. We show that the ISCO position is modified by both $a$ and $B$, and that rapidly rotating prograde configurations can develop an additional model-dependent inner cutoff when the magnetically dominated approximation underlying the emissivity prescription ceases to be applicable. High-resolution one-dimensional intensity profiles further separate the direct image, the $n=1$ lensing-ring contribution, and the higher-order $n\geq 2$ photon-ring subimages, while quantifying the Doppler-induced brightness asymmetry. Retrograde disks exhibit a wider emission-depleted central region because of the outwardly shifted ISCO, making the higher-order lensed components more clearly distinguishable from the direct emission. These results show that the disk inner boundary and the magnetic-field-dependent emissivity can substantially influence the observable appearance of Kerr-BR black holes.

</details>


### [167] [Astrons: Reissner-Nordström Primordial Naked Singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10587)
*Claudio Corianò,Paul H. Frampton,Leonardo Torcellini*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文系统性地提出了一族被称为“astrons”的原始超大质量带电致密天体（primordial ultra-massive electrically charged compact objects），并从电荷产生、饱和、介质中的电荷持久性、星际等离子体屏蔽、Reissner-Nordström几何、引力透镜效应及宇宙学后果等多个层面施加约束。研究表明，普通吸积饱和给出的电荷远低于大电荷现象学基准，等离子体屏蔽构成严峻挑战，而大电荷会将外部几何推入超极端（super-extremal）区域；在均匀FLRW描述下，带电物体的相互作用能呈a⁻⁴标度，不能产生渐近晚期加速膨胀。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一种新型原始超大质量带电致密天体（astrons）存在的理论可能性，并从多个物理层面检验其是否与已知观测和理论框架兼容。

Method: 综合运用电荷产生与饱和机制、等离子体物理中的屏蔽效应、Reissner-Nordström度规下的极端带电几何分析、引力透镜效应以及均匀Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker（FLRW）宇宙学框架中的能量标度分析，对该天体族群施加系统性的理论约束。

Result: 普通吸积饱和机制给出的电荷量远低于大电荷现象学基准（phenomenological benchmark）；星际等离子体屏蔽是严重的等离子体物理问题；大电荷可使外部几何进入超极端（super-extremal）区域；在均匀FLRW描述下，带电物体的相互作用能密度按a⁻⁴标度演化，无法产生渐近晚期加速膨胀，任何由该均匀分量引发的加速时期只能是暂态。

Conclusion: astron方案应被视为一个受严格约束的理论框架，其可行性取决于等离子体物理细节以及超越均匀近似的宇宙学处理。

Abstract: We summarize a set of constraints on a proposed population of primordial, ultra-massive, electrically charged compact objects, which we call astrons. The analysis combines charge generation, charge saturation, persistence of the charge in an ionized medium, screening by the intergalactic plasma, the Reissner--Nordström geometry of highly charged compact objects, lensing, and the cosmological implications of a sparse charged population. We also discuss the possible relation to the early structures revealed by the James Webb Space Telescope: if astrons are relevant there, they would be primordial dark seeds rather than luminous objects directly observed at high redshift. The resulting scenario is sharply constrained. Ordinary accretion saturation gives charges far below the large-charge phenomenological benchmark, screening is a serious plasma-physics issue, and a large charge can place the exterior geometry deep in the super-extremal regime. As expected at the level of a homogeneous Friedmann--Lemaître--Robertson--Walker (FLRW) description, the interaction energy of a population of charged objects scales as \(a^{-4}\), so the simplest perfect-fluid reduction does not generate asymptotically late-time acceleration; any acceleration era tied to that homogeneous component can only be transitory. The astron scenario should be regarded as a constrained framework whose viability depends on plasma physics and on a cosmological treatment beyond the homogeneous approximation.

</details>

### [168] [Well-posedness of a generalized Stokes operator on domains with cylindrical ends via layer-potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10849)
*Mirela Kohr,Victor Nistor,Wolfgang Wendland*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文在具有直圆柱端（straight cylindrical ends）的区域Ω上，利用层势方法（method of layer potentials）研究广义斯托克斯算子（generalized Stokes operator）Ξ，在适当正性假设下证明其Fredholm性及可逆性，进而建立Dirichlet边值问题的适定性（well-posedness），并最终推广到小数据情形下的广义纳维-斯托克斯系统（generalized Navier-Stokes system）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的斯托克斯算子（Stokes operator）在具有圆柱端流形上的理论尚不完整，引入势项V与V₀的广义形式需要建立相应的Fredholm性与可逆性理论，以支撑后续非线性问题的适定性分析。

Method: 采用层势方法（layer potentials），在包含Ω的流形M上构造单层势（single-layer potential）S和双层势（double-layer potential）1/2+K；通过发展极限与跳跃关系（limit and jump relations）的“代数工具包”（algebra tool kit），结合格林公式（Green formulas）和能量估计（energy estimates），并借助先前工作中建立的伪微分算子（pseudodifferential operators）理论完成分析。

Result: 在V与V₀的正性假设下，证明了广义斯托克斯算子Ξ、单层势S以及算子1/2+K的Fredholm性；在稍强假设下进一步证明了这些算子的可逆性，由此得到Dirichlet边值问题的适定性。

Conclusion: 本文建立的广义斯托克斯算子的可逆性结果直接给出了线性斯托克斯边值问题的适定性，并可作为工具用于证明小数据下具有圆柱端的区域上广义纳维-斯托克斯系统Dirichlet问题的适定性。

Abstract: We study the \emph{generalized Stokes operator} \begin{equation*} \bsXi \ede \bsXi _{V,V_0} \ede \left(\begin{array}{ccc} \bsL + V & \nabla \\ \nabla^* & -V_0 \end{array}\right) \end{equation*} on a \emph{domain with straight cylindrical ends} $Ω$ using \emph{the method of layer potentials} on $M \supset Ω$. The operator $\bsXi_{0, 0}$ is the classical Stokes operator. Under suitable positivity assumptions on $V$ and $V_{0}$, we prove that $\bsXi$ is Fredholm. This allows us then to define the single- and double-layer potentials $\bsS$ and $\frac12 + \bsK$. Under further positivity assumptions, we prove that $\bsS$ and $\frac12 + \bsK$ are also Fredholm. Under slightly stronger assumptions on $V$ and $V_{0}$, we prove \emph{the invertibility} of the operators $\bsXi$, $\bsS$, and $\frac12 + \bsK$. The invertibility of these operators leads to \emph{well-posedness results} for the associated (linear) Stokes boundary value problem with Dirichlet boundary conditions on $Ω$. The proofs of these results required us to develop many related tools. In particular, we develop an ``algebra tool kit'' to deal with \emph{limit and jump relations of layer potentials.} We also develop Green formulas and energy estimates for our generalized Stokes operator $\bsXi$ on manifolds with straight cylindrical ends, which requires a careful geometric study of the related differential operators, such as the deformation operator $\Def$. For completeness, we review suitable classes of pseudodifferential operators on manifolds with straight cylindrical ends that were studied in some previous papers of ours (including ``The Stokes operator on manifolds with cylindrical ends,'' J. Diff. Equations, 2024). As an application, we prove the well-posedness result for the Dirichlet problem for the generalized Navier-Stokes system with small data on a domain with cylindrical ends.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文通过理论和粒子模拟（particle-in-cell modeling），展示了激光辐照箔片膨胀等离子体 plume 中由 Weibel 不稳定性介导的丝状结构（filamentary structures）如何形成，并解释了在 OMEGA 和 Laser Megajoule 装置上获得的实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释激光辐照箔片膨胀等离子体 plume 中 Weibel 不稳定性介导的丝状结构的形成机制，并建立理论模型以匹配已有实验观测结果。

Result: 给出了自生磁涨落（self-generated magnetic fluctuations）的主导波长和振幅的估计值，成功解释了在 OMEGA 和 Laser Megajoule 装置上获得的实验数据。

Conclusion: Weibel 不稳定性驱动的电子电流丝（electron current filaments）在准球形膨胀等离子体 plume 中自然形成，该机制与实验观测一致。

Abstract: In light of novel and past experimental results, we demonstrate how Weibel-mediated filamentary structures can develop in the expanding plasma plume of a laser-irradiated foil. The transverse ballistic cooling that occurs during the quasi-spherical plasma expansion naturally drives an electron pressure anisotropy, resulting in the growth of electron current filaments. This effect competes with electron-ion Coulomb collisions which tend to isotropize the electron distribution function. Based on theoretical and particle-in-cell modeling, we provide estimates of the dominant wavelength and amplitude of the self-generated magnetic fluctuations, which are found to explain experimental data obtained at the OMEGA and Laser Megajoule facilities.

### [170] [Refined lattice point counting on the moduli space of Klein surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09526)
*Nitin Kumar Chidambaram,Elba Garcia-Failde,Alessandro Giacchetto,Kento Osuga*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文引入了度量Möbius图（metric Möbius graphs）的模空间，将带状图（ribbon graphs）推广到不可定向情形；通过对该模空间中的格点进行计数并取连续极限，推导出Norbury递归与Witten-Kontsevich递归的精炼版本，并给出了模空间精炼欧拉示性数（refined Euler characteristic）的几何定义与显式计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将带状图的模空间理论推广到不可定向（non-orientable）情形，并建立相应的计数与体积递归关系，进而回答Goulden、Harer与Jackson提出的关于模空间精炼欧拉示性数的问题。

Method: 定义度量Möbius图（metric Möbius graphs）的模空间，每个图配备一个不可定向性度量（measure of non-orientability）；通过对该模空间中的格点按不可定向性度量加权计数，证明Norbury递归的精炼版本；再取网格细化极限（mesh finer limit），导出欧几里得体积（Euclidean volumes）的递归，从而得到Witten-Kontsevich递归的精炼版本。

Result: 建立了Norbury递归与Witten-Kontsevich递归的精炼版本；给出了模空间精炼欧拉示性数（refined Euler characteristic）的几何定义，并完成了其显式计算公式的推导。

Conclusion: 度量Möbius图的模空间统一涵盖了黎曼曲面（Riemann surfaces）与不可定向Klein曲面（Klein surfaces）的模空间；该框架不仅推广了带状图理论，还通过精炼递归回答了模空间精炼欧拉示性数的经典问题。

Abstract: We introduce the moduli space of metric Möbius graphs, which extend ribbon graphs to the non-orientable world. This space contains both the moduli space of Riemann surfaces and the moduli space of non-orientable Klein surfaces. Each metric Möbius graph is equipped with a measure of non-orientability. We count lattice points in this moduli space, weighted by the measure of non-orientability, and prove a refined version of Norbury's recursion for this count. Taking the limit as the mesh becomes finer, we deduce a recursion for the Euclidean volumes, yielding a refined version of the Witten--Kontsevich recursion. As an application, we give a geometric definition of the refined Euler characteristic of the moduli space and compute it explicitly, thereby answering a question of Goulden, Harer, and Jackson.

</details>

### [172] [Emerging 2D Materials for Beyond von Neumann Computing: A Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09695)
*Yaser Banad*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文指出传统 Dennard 缩放（Dennard scaling）的终结以及存储带宽与算力之间的差距不断增大，使得冯·诺依曼架构（von Neumann architecture）成为结构性瓶颈。二维材料（two-dimensional materials）凭借其原子级薄几何结构、电可调载流子密度和强光学响应，为构建存算一体、事件驱动（event-driven）而非时钟周期驱动、以及将工作负载迁移至光域的设备提供了统一平台。文章综述了石墨烯与石墨烯纳米带晶体管、氧化物与二维集成忆阻器、以及硅兼容二维光子与热发射器结构这三条汇聚方向，并论证二维材料领域已用十年产出众多创纪录器件，下一个十年的胜负将取决于谁率先在单一半导体晶圆上集成其中三种器件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统 Dennard 缩放（Dennard scaling）的终结以及存储带宽与算术吞吐量之间日益扩大的差距，使得冯·诺依曼划分（von Neumann partition）从暂时性问题变为结构性瓶颈，亟需新的计算架构和材料平台来突破这一限制。

Method: 本文采用前瞻视角（perspective），沿三条汇聚方向展开综述：石墨烯与石墨烯纳米带（graphene nanoribbon）晶体管作为可扩展沟道材料、氧化物与二维集成忆阻器（memristor）用于存内模拟计算（in-memory analog compute）、以及硅兼容的二维光子（photonic）与热发射器（thermal-emitter）结构用于光学计算基元（optical computing primitives）。

Result: 文章指出二维材料领域在过去十年中已产出大量创纪录性能的器件，但真正的突破将取决于能否在单一半导体晶圆上首次集成上述三类器件。

Conclusion: 二维材料为克服冯·诺依曼瓶颈提供了统一的材料平台，未来十年的竞争焦点将从单器件性能记录转向多器件系统级集成，率先实现三种关键器件在单一晶圆上的集成者将占据主导地位。

Abstract: The end of conventional Dennard scaling and the widening gap between memory bandwidth and arithmetic throughput have made the von Neumann partition a structural bottleneck rather than a transient one. Two-dimensional (2D) materials, with atomically thin geometries, electrically tunable carrier densities, and large optical responses, offer a unified platform on which to build devices that compute where they store, process events rather than clock cycles, and shift workload into the optical domain. This perspective surveys progress along three converging thrusts, graphene and graphene nanoribbon transistors as scalable channel materials, oxide and 2D-integrated memristors for in-memory analog compute, and silicon-compatible 2D photonic and thermal-emitter structures for optical computing primitives. Our central argument is that the 2D-materials community has spent a decade producing record devices, and the next decade will be decided by who first integrates three of them on a single semiconductor wafer.

</details>

### [173] [Mirror transitions in diffusion with stochastic resetting confined on a ring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08414)
*Pedro Julián-Salgado,Pavel Castro-Villarreal,Leonardo Dagdug,Denis Boyer*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维有界环形系统（circular circumference）中粒子在随机重置（stochastic resetting）下的平均首达时间（mean first-passage time）优化问题，重点分析了多重置位点情形下最优重置率（optimal resetting rate）的相变行为，发现其可呈现一阶（abrupt）和二阶（continuous）转变，并在参数空间内存在临界点（critical point）和三临界点（tri-critical point），且所有转变均关于目标位点及其对径点呈镜像对称（mirror symmetry）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管随机重置框架已被广泛用于建模自然现象，但已有研究大多集中于无界一维域中的最优重置率。有界系统，尤其是存在多个重置位点（multiple resetting sites）时的平均首达时间优化问题，仍缺乏系统理解。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 考虑一个在圆周上扩散的粒子，固定位置设有吸收目标位点（absorbing target site），粒子可重置到由任意概率密度函数（probability density function）抽取的多个位点。利用系统的自由传播子（free propagator）计算存活概率（survival probability）的拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform），进而求解平均首达时间，并针对双重置位点构型分析最优重置率对参数的依赖关系。

Result: 重置位点与吸收目标位点之间的弧长以及剩余重置位点的权重共同决定了最优重置率的转变类型，可呈现一阶（"first order"）和二阶（"second order"）过渡。平均首达时间行为足够丰富，允许在参数空间中出现临界点和三临界点。所有转变均围绕目标位点及其对径点（diametrically opposite site）具有镜像对称性。

Conclusion: 论文揭示了有界环形系统中多重置位点下最优重置率的复杂相变行为，拓展了随机重置理论在有界几何中的应用，并为理解此类系统中的优化问题提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Diffusion with an incorporated resetting mechanism provides a reference framework for modeling a wide range of natural phenomena. Within this framework, the optimal resetting rate is a key quantity that arises from the optimization of the mean first-passage time. While substantial work has focused on the study of the optimal resetting rate in unbounded one dimensional domains, little is still known about the optimization of the mean first-passage time in bounded systems, in particular when multiple resetting sites are available. In this work, we consider a particle diffusing along a circular circumference and under resetting, with an absorbing target site at a fixed location. Using the appropriate free propagator for this system, we compute the Laplace transform of the survival probability when resetting occurs to multiple sites drawn from an arbitrary probability density function. We also calculate the mean first-passage time at the target site, and study the dependence of the optimal resetting rate in terms of the relevant parameters of the system in a two-resetting site configuration. Depending on the arc length between one of the resetting sites and the absorbing target site, and the weight of the remaining resetting site, the optimal resetting rate can exhibit abrupt ("first order'') and continuous ("second order'') transitions. Moreover, the behavior of the mean first-passage time is rich enough to allow both critical and tri-critical points to exist in the parameter space. All the transitions have "mirror symmetry'' around the selected target site and its corresponding diametrically opposite site.

</details>


### [174] [A Closer Look on the Influence of Constraints Upon the Optimization of the Nonadditive Entropic Functional $S_{q}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08860)
*Leandro Lyra Braga Dognini,Constantino Tsallis*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于非可加熵$S_q$和广义能量约束$\sum p_i^{q'}e_i/\sum p_i^{q'}=U$，推导了优化问题的存在性、正性与唯一性充分条件，并给出闭式解法。证明仅当$q'=1$或$q'=q$时优化解呈$q$-指数形式；定义有效温度$T_{q,q'}$和亥姆霍兹类自由能$F_{q,q'}$，并验证了热力学第零、第三定律在广义统计力学中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准统计力学中的正则分布通过最大化玻尔兹曼-吉布斯-冯·诺伊曼-香农熵$S_{BG}$得到，但该框架在处理长程相互作用系统、非线性动力学混沌边缘系统时存在局限。本文旨在推广该优化问题至非可加熵$S_q$框架，并系统性地分析不同约束形式下的数学性质与热力学一致性。

Method: 采用数学优化分析方法，在非可加熵$S_q$与广义能量约束$\sum p_i^{q'}e_i/\sum p_i^{q'}=U$（其中$q'>0$）下，推导概率分布存在性、严格正性与唯一性的充分条件，并给出闭式解定理。通过分析不同$q'$取值（$q'=1$、$q'=q$、$q'=2-q$）对比标准情形与新情形。利用克劳修斯关系$1/T_{q,q'}=\partial S_q/\partial U$定义有效温度，并构造亥姆霍兹类自由能$F_{q,q'}$。

Result: 证明了标准情形$q'=1$和$q'=q$是唯一能使优化概率分布呈现$q$-指数形式的约束形式。定义了有效温度$T_{q,q'}$和亥姆霍兹类自由能$F_{q,q'}=U-T_{q,q'}S_q$，前者为广义统计力学中热力学第零定律的有效性提供了基础。对于$q\in(0,1)$且线性约束$q'=1$的情形，该框架（i）保持热力学第三定律；（ii）可建模任意作用程的经典多体哈密顿系统；（iii）展现出低维非线性动力系统在混沌边缘的特征。

Conclusion: 本文在非可加熵$S_q$与广义能量约束框架下，系统解决了优化分布的存在性、唯一性与闭式求解问题，明确了$q$-指数分布出现的充要条件。通过定义有效温度与自由能，验证了广义统计力学中热力学第零、第三定律的成立。该框架为长程相互作用系统和混沌边缘动力学提供了有效的统计力学描述工具。

Abstract: The thermal-equilibrium canonical distribution is currently obtained by maximizing the Boltzmann-Gibbs-von Neumann-Shannon entropy $S_{BG}(p)=k\sum^{W}_{i=1}p_{i}\ln 1/p_{i}$ constrained to $\sum^{W}_{i=1}p_{i}=1$ and $\sum^{W}_{i=1}p_{i}\,e_{i}=U$, $e_{1}\leq\ldots\leq e_{W}$ being the energies of the $W$ possible states and $U\in[e_{1},e_{W}]$ their mean value. We revisit a generalized version of this optimization problem grounded in the nonadditive entropy $S_{q}(p)=k\,(\sum^{W}_{i=1}p_{i}^{q}-1)/(1-q)$ (frequently, though not necessarily, $q\in(0,1)$; $S_1=S_{BG}$), and the constraint $\sum^{W}_{i=1} p_{i}^{q^{\prime}}e_{i} / \sum^{W}_{i=1}p_{i}^{q^{\prime}}=U$, $q^{\prime}>0$. Sufficient conditions for existence, strict positivity, and uniqueness of solutions are derived, along with a theorem that enables their closed-form calculation. We apply these results to deepen the understanding of the two standard cases in the literature ($q^{\prime}=1$ and $q^{\prime}=q$), as well as of a new one ($q^{\prime}=2-q$). We prove that these standard cases are the only ones yielding optimizing probability distributions of $q$-exponential form. Furthermore, we define an effective temperature $T_{q,q^{\prime}}$ through a Clausius-like relation $1/T_{q,q^{\prime}}=\partial S_{q} / \partial U$ and derive a Helmholtz-like energy $F_{q,q^{\prime}}=U-T_{q,q^{\prime}}S_{q}$, with the former grounding the validity of the $0^{th}$ Principle of Thermodynamics within this generalized statistical mechanics. Finally, we show that the case with a linear constraint (i.e., $q^{\prime}=1$) with $q\in(0,1)$ (i) preserves the Third Law of Thermodynamics; (ii) can be used to model classical many-body Hamiltonian systems with arbitrarily-ranged interactions; and (iii) resembles features of low-dimensional nonlinear dynamical systems at the edge of chaos.

</details>


### [175] [Condensation Transition in Entropy-Constrained Probability Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08967)
*Bautista Arenaza,Sebastián Risau-Gusman,Inés Samengo,Damián G. Hernández*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在统计物理与信息论的交叉点上，研究了由固定香农熵定义的概率单纯形（probability simplex）上高维分布的统计特性。通过引入一种离散化策略，发现当熵低于临界值 $H_c \simeq \log K - 1 + \gamma$ 时，系统会发生凝聚相变（condensation phase transition），此时绝大多数分布处于凝聚态：一个分量占据概率质量的宏观部分，其余分量形成均匀的流体背景。该框架可解释机器学习中的过度自信预测以及生态学中优势物种涌现等现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维概率空间的组织结构是统计物理与信息论领域的交叉基础问题，现有方法尚缺乏对固定香农熵下概率单纯形上分布结构的系统性分析。

Method: 提出一种离散化策略，为不同的微观态分布分配相等的统计权重，利用这种对称性对概率单纯形进行组合分析，进而研究热力学极限下的相变行为。

Result: 发现存在一个临界熵 $H_c \simeq \log K - 1 + \gamma$：当熵 $H_0 < H_c$ 时，系统进入凝聚相，绝大多数分布呈现单分量占据宏观概率质量、其余分量构成均匀流体的结构。

Conclusion: 该框架揭示了高维流形中熵约束（entropic constraints）可自然地导致稀疏性（sparsity）的涌现，为机器学习中的过度自信预测和生态学中的优势物种形成等现象提供了统一的理论基础。

Abstract: The organization of high-dimensional probability spaces is a fundamental problem at the intersection of statistical physics and information theory. Here, we analyze the distributions populating level surfaces of the probability simplex $Δ_{K-1}$ defined by a fixed Shannon entropy. We introduce a discretization strategy that assigns equal statistical weight to distinct microstate distributions and enables a combinatorial analysis of the simplex. A condensation phase transition is shown to take place below a critical entropy that scales as $H_c \simeq \log K - 1 + γ$ in the thermodynamic limit. For entropy values $H_0 < H_c$, the overwhelming majority of distributions are found in a condensed state, in which a single component captures a macroscopic fraction of the total probability mass while the remaining components form a homogeneous fluid background. These results provide a framework for understanding phenomena such as overconfident predictions in machine learning and the emergence of dominant species in ecology, and suggest that sparsity can arise naturally from entropic constraints in high-dimensional manifolds.

### [176] [Families of planar lattices with arbitrarily high $T_{\rm c}$ for the ferromagnetic Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10017)
*Davidson Noby Joseph,Connor M. Walsh,Igor Boettcher*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过迭代三角剖分构造了具有任意高临界温度的周期性平面镶嵌晶格族，证明了经典铁磁伊辛模型下临界温度与最大配位数之间呈对数标度关系，并提出了一个猜想的最优上界函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于最近发现的精确边界条件——即高临界温度需要大的最大配位数（maximal coordination number）$q_{\rm max}$，本文旨在构造能够实现任意高临界温度的周期性平面镶嵌（periodic tessellations of the plane）晶格，并探究临界温度的上界与最优性。

Method: 通过迭代三角剖分（iterative triangulation）构造晶格族；推导出这些晶格族临界温度$T_{\rm c}$的显式表达式；引入一个关于最大配位数$q_{\rm max}$的函数$T_{\rm c}^*(q_{\rm max})$，并猜想该函数对所有周期性平面镶嵌是最优上界。

Result: 这些晶格族的临界温度渐近标度为$T_{\rm c}/J\sim A \ln q_{\rm max}$，其中普适前因子（universal prefactor）$A=2/\ln 2$；从三角晶格（Triangular lattice）通过迭代三角剖分导出的阿波罗晶格（Apollonian lattices）族饱和了上述猜想的最优界。

Conclusion: 本文所讨论的晶格对网络系统（network systems）中最优性的理论问题具有意义，未来可能通过相干伊辛机（Coherent Ising Machines）或拓扑电路（topoelectric circuits）进行实验实现。

Abstract: We construct families of periodic tessellations of the plane with arbitrarily high critical temperature, $T_{\rm c}$, for the classical ferromagnetic Ising model. Our approach is motivated by recently found exact bounds, which imply that large values of $T_{\rm c}$ require large values of the maximal coordination number of the lattice, $q_{\rm max}$. We create such lattices through iterative triangulation and derive explicit expressions for their $T_{\rm c}$. Furthermore, we show that $T_{\rm c}$ for these families scales asymptotically as $T_{\rm c}/J\sim A \ln q_{\rm max}$ with a universal prefactor $A=2/\ln 2$. We introduce a function $T_{\rm c}^*(q_{\rm max})$ that we conjecture to be optimal for all periodic tessellations of the plane. We show that the family of so-called Apollonian lattices, which are derived from the Triangular lattice through iterative triangulation, saturates this bound. The lattices discussed in this work are relevant for theoretical questions of optimality in network systems and may be realized experimentally in Coherent Ising Machines or topoelectric circuits in the future.

### [177] [Sensitivity Analysis in the Face of Rare Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09148)
*John Strahan,Todd R. Gingrich*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子马达等非平衡复杂系统的设计参数众多，需要计算动力学观测量相对于这些参数的导数（即敏感性），但系统涉及稀有事件（rare events）时，观测量及其敏感性都难以通过直接模拟估计。

Method: 将重要性采样与马尔可夫状态模型（MSM）结合：MSM分别捕捉慢的稀有事件动力学和快的局部动力学，通过链式法则（chain rule）将两部分连接起来，形成高效的敏感性估计器；并基于RiteWeight算法进行迭代重加权（iterative reweighting），大幅降低MSM粗粒化带来的近似误差。

Result: 在Müller-Brown势中的扩散问题上验证了方法，该场景下跃迁速率对势能面参数的敏感性可精确计算；随后利用敏感性优化了催化驱动分子马达的粒子基模型中的方向偏置（directional bias）。

Conclusion: 该方法为稀有事件系统中动力学观测量敏感性的高效估计提供了一条实用计算路径，并能直接用于非平衡系统的参数优化。

Abstract: Molecular motors and other complex nonequilibrium systems are controlled by large sets of design parameters, and optimizing those parameters requires computing sensitivities -- derivatives of dynamical observables with respect to the parameters. When the system's dynamics involves rare events, both the observable and its sensitivity are difficult to estimate from direct simulation. We present a practical computational pipeline that addresses both challenges by combining importance sampling with a Markov state model (MSM). The MSM separately captures the slow, rare-event dynamics and the fast, local dynamics, and the chain rule connects those two pieces to yield an efficient sensitivity estimator. An iterative reweighting procedure based on the RiteWeight algorithm substantially reduces approximation errors from the MSM coarse-graining. We validate the approach on diffusion in the Müller-Brown potential, where the sensitivity of a transition rate to landscape parameters can be computed exactly. We then use sensitivies to optimize the directional bias of a particle-based model of a catalysis-driven molecular motor.

Method: 研究采用了三圈重整化方法，对质量（mass）和两个耦合常数（coupling constants）进行了重整化计算，从而首次获得该阶数下耦合常数的完整重整化群流。

Result: 首次实现了三圈阶数下耦合常数的完整重整化群流。分析表明，交叉过程通过重整化群流向连接三临界（tricritical）和临界（critical）不动点（fixed points）的直线收敛来实现。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了普适性在该问题中的具体含义，并演示了如何从重整化群β函数（beta functions）中恢复非普适项（non-universal terms）。这一结果为理解三临界-临界交叉的场论行为提供了更精确的理论基础。

Abstract: Effective field theories provide a suitable framework for both particle physics and statistical physics. We delve deeper into the study of the effective three-dimensional scalar field theory for its application to statistical physics, especially considering the role of the sextic coupling in the tricritical-to-critical crossover. The three-loop renormalization of the mass and the two coupling constants that we perform allows us to obtain, for the first time, the complete renormalization group flow of the couplings in that order. We analyze what universality means in this problem and how we can recover non-universal terms from the renormalization group beta functions. The crossover is realized by the convergence of the renormalization group flow towards the line connecting the tricritical and critical fixed points.

### [179] [Power spectral density of trajectories of active Ornstein-Uhlenbeck particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09399)
*Yeongjin Kim,Gleb Oshanin,Jae-Hyung Jeon*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于主动Ornstein-Uhlenbeck粒子（AOUPs）模型，建立了主动扩散过程功率谱密度（PSD）的精确解析理论，揭示了自由和受限系统中PSD的丰富特征，包括双噪声源导致的双平台结构以及瞬态弹道运动引起的$f^{-4}$新标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 功率谱密度（power spectral density, PSD）是随机过程在频域的核心描述符，然而虽然布朗运动和少数反常扩散过程的PSD已有研究，主动非平衡过程的谱密度几乎未被探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，提供主动扩散系统PSD的精确解析理论。

Method: 采用主动Ornstein-Uhlenbeck粒子（active Ornstein-Uhlenbeck particles, AOUPs）模型，分别在自由空间和谐波束缚（harmonic confinement）两种条件下，对主动扩散过程的PSD进行精确解析求解。

Result: 自由空间中主动运动不改变布朗运动的$f^{-2}$标度，仅修正振幅并引入持久频率（persistence frequency）处的交叉。束缚条件下，谱呈现丰富特征：双噪声源导致的双平台结构（double-trapping mechanism）以及瞬态弹道运动引起的新的$f^{-4}$谱标度。有限时间PSD的低频平台和高频振荡对观测时间$T$的依赖性在自由与受限系统中表现不同。

Conclusion: 本文结果为主动系统的PSD分析提供了一个解析可处理的框架，可用于解释已有的主动系统实验研究。

Abstract: The power spectral density (PSD) is a central frequency-domain descriptor of stochastic processes. While PSDs have been studied for Brownian motion and a few anomalous diffusion processes, the spectral densities of active nonequilibrium processes remain almost unexplored. Here, we present an exact theory for the PSDs of active diffusion using the model of active Ornstein-Uhlenbeck particles (AOUPs). We investigate the spectral densities of AOUPs in free space and under harmonic confinement. In free space, active motion does not alter the Brownian $f^{-2}$ spectrum, but only modifies its amplitude and introduces a crossover at the persistence frequency. Under confinement, the spectrum exhibits a rich variety of features depending on the persistence, trap relaxation, and activity strength, including two characteristic signatures that are absent in both thermal systems and free AOUPs. These are a two-plateau structure from a double-trapping mechanism due to two noise sources, and the new $f^{-4}$ spectral scaling associated with transient ballistic motion. We also investigate the finite time effects through the finite-time PSD, and find that the low-frequency plateau and high frequency oscillation exhibit distinct dependences on the observation time $T$ in free and confined systems. Finally, we discuss our results in connection with previously reported experimental studies of active systems. Our results provide an analytically tractable framework for interpreting such systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统均匀晶格（如三角晶格和kagome晶格）上，Ashkin-Teller模型即使存在阻挫也只呈现一条铁磁-顺磁临界线。本文旨在探索非均匀晶格（Union Jack晶格）是否会导致更丰富的临界行为，特别是临界线分裂和中间临界相的出现。

Method: 采用Metropolis蒙特卡洛方法（Metropolis Monte Carlo method）对Union Jack晶格上的Ashkin-Teller模型进行数值模拟。通过引入磁化率$\widetildeχ = \text{d}\langle m \rangle /\text{d}J$作为关键探针，观测赝临界点$J_c(L)$的尺寸标度行为。

Result: 在Union Jack晶格上，临界线分裂为两条Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）边界，中间区域出现临界相。该临界相的特征是：磁化强度随系统尺寸呈幂律衰减，相关长度比$ξ/L$在热力学极限下保持有限；赝临界点$J_c(L)$的标度行为为$(\ln L)^{-2}$，符合BKT临界性。

Conclusion: Union Jack晶格上的Ashkin-Teller模型展现出阻挫、晶格不均匀性和两个耦合自旋自由度共同作用导致的新颖临界相。由于超流、超导和超固态等量子相均具有准长程序并属于临界相范畴，该结果可能为探索此类量子相提供启发。

Abstract: The Ashkin-Teller (AT) model is a classic spin model in statistical mechanics. For traditional homogeneous lattices like triangular and kagome lattices, even when frustration exists, the model only has one ferromagnetic-paramagnetic critical line in the $J>0$ and $K<0$ region. However, in this paper, for the Union Jack lattice, where the lattice coordination numbers are 4, 8, and 8 and which also contains a large number of small triangular units, using Metropolis Monte Carlo method, we find that, the critical line of the AT model splits into two Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless(BKT) boundaries, and a critical phase emerges in the intermediate region. This phenomenon is the combined result of frustration, lattice inhomogeneity and the two coupled spin degrees of freedom inherent to the AT model. In detail, the novel critical phase characterized by a power-law decay of magnetization with system size, where the correlation length ratio $ξ/L$ remains finite even in the thermodynamic limit. We also introduce the susceptibility $\widetildeχ = \text{d}\langle m \rangle /\text{d}J$ as a key probe, and through this probe, pseudo-critical points $J_c(L)$ are observed to scale proportionally to $(\ln L)^{-2}$, a behavior consistent with BKT criticality. Since superfluids, superconductors, and supersolids all possess quasi-long-range order and fall into the category of critical phases, our results could also inspire the exploration of such quantum phases.

</details>


### [181] [Equilibrium and non-equilibrium properties of active matter systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09743)
*Mintu Karmakar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文综述了活性物质（active matter）系统的集体行为与动力学，重点探讨了体积排斥、介质无序和自旋各向异性等因素对自推进粒子（self-propelled particles）群集转变（flocking transition）和运动诱导相分离（motility-induced phase separation）等现象的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解活性物质系统中自推进粒子的集体行为如何受到热噪声（thermal noise）、自推进速度、外场强度等系统参数的影响，以及体积排斥特征、介质无序和自旋各向异性等条件如何调控这些行为。

Method: 通过引入自旋各向异性（spin anisotropy），在非晶格域（off-lattice domains）中构建自推进粒子模型，系统性地分析体积排斥、介质无序等因素对集体动力学的影响。

Result: 展示了活性物质模型中出现的多种现象，包括堵塞（jamming）、动力学停滞（kinetic arrest）、运动诱导相分离、共存相（coexisting phases）、微相分离（microphase separation）以及各类相变。

Conclusion: 活性物质系统的集体行为受热噪声、自推进速度和外场强度等多个参数调控，这些参数共同决定群集转变和相分离等复杂涌现现象。

Abstract: Active matter systems encompass both natural and artificially created systems consisting of numerous active particles. These particles actively consume energy to propel themselves or exert mechanical forces, leading to intricate behaviors and a diverse range of collective motions from flocking transition to motility-induced phase separation. The flocking transition refers to the spontaneous alignment and coordination of individuals in a group, resembling the cohesive motion observed in flocks of birds or schools of fish. On the other hand, motility-induced phase separation refers to the segregation of active particles into distinct regions based on their differing motility levels. In this presentation, I will talk about active matter systems, specifically focusing on the collective behavior and dynamics, including the influence of volume exclusion features, the impact of disorder in the media, and the behavior of self-propelled particles in off-lattice domains by introducing spin anisotropy. The objective is to understand how the collective behavior of self-propelled particles is affected by various system parameters, including thermal noise, self-propulsion velocity, external field strength, etc. I will furthermore show the phenomena such as jamming, kinetic arrest, motility-induced phase separation, coexisting phases, microphase separation, and phase transitions within the context of active matter models.

### [182] [Computing eigenpairs of quantum many-body systems with Polfed.jl](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10191)
*Rok Pintar,Konrad Pawlik,Rafał Świętek,Miroslav Hopjan,Jan Šuntajs,Jakub Zakrzewski,Piotr Sierant,Lev Vidmar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文介绍 Polfed.jl，一个基于 Julia 语言的开源软件包，实现了多项式滤波精确对角化（POLFED）算法，用于高效计算量子多体哈密顿量中谱中部的本征对，支持 GPU 加速并在无序自旋链和费米子模型中验证了其规模与速度优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非平衡多体物理需要访问量子多体哈密顿量谱中部（mid-spectrum）的本征对（eigenpairs），但希尔伯特空间维度呈指数增长（exponential growth of Hilbert-space dimension）使得这一计算极为困难。现有对角化方法的内存成本过高，限制了可处理的系统尺寸。

Method: Polfed.jl 实现了多项式滤波精确对角化（POLFED）算法。该算法在 Lanczos 迭代（Lanczos iteration）过程中动态进行多项式谱变换（polynomial spectral transformation），在保持哈密顿量稀疏性的同时显著降低内存成本。软件包支持灵活的能量定位（energy targeting）、针对结构化哈密顿量的谱映射自动优化，以及 GPU 加速，其核心计算退化为重复的稀疏矩阵-向量乘法（sparse matrix-vector multiplications）。

Result: 在无序自旋链和费米子模型上的基准测试（benchmarks）表明，Polfed.jl 能够处理比现有方法更大的系统尺寸；CPU 与 GPU 的对比测试确认了显著的加速效果。软件还提供了量子太阳模型（quantum sun model）哈密顿量的构造代码，该模型是多体遍历性破缺转变（many-body ergodicity-breaking transition）的玩具模型。

Conclusion: Polfed.jl 是处理量子多体哈密顿量谱中部本征对计算的有效工具，在可扩展性和计算效率上优于其他对角化方法。尽管本文聚焦于多体哈密顿量，但该软件包可适用于任何大型稀疏矩阵（large sparse matrix）。

Abstract: We present Polfed.jl, an open-source Julia package implementing the Polynomially Filtered Exact Diagonalization (POLFED) algorithm for computing mid-spectrum eigenvalues and eigenvectors (shortly, eigenpairs) of quantum many-body Hamiltonians. Access to such eigenpairs is essential for studying non-equilibrium many-body physics, but is hindered by the exponential growth of Hilbert-space dimension. POLFED addresses this challenge through a polynomial spectral transformation evaluated on the fly within a Lanczos iteration, preserving Hamiltonian sparsity and substantially reducing memory costs compared to other diagonalization methods. The package supports flexible energy targeting, automatic optimization of the spectral mapping for structured Hamiltonians, and GPU acceleration, which is particularly effective since the dominant computational cost reduces to repeated sparse matrix-vector multiplications. Benchmarks on disordered spin-chain and fermionic models demonstrate access to larger system sizes than alternative approaches, and CPU--GPU comparisons confirm significant speedups. In particular, we also provide code for constructing the quantum sun model Hamiltonian, a toy model of a many-body ergodicity-breaking transition. While our focus is on many-body Hamiltonians, Polfed.jl may be applied to any large sparse matrix.

</details>


### [183] [Statistical mechanics of the $N$-queens problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10326)
*Zong-Yue Liu,Hai-Jun Liao,Lei Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从统计力学（statistical mechanics）角度将 N 皇后问题（N-queens problem）视为一种晶格气体（lattice gas）模型，通过解析推导、大规模蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟和张量网络（tensor network）方法，研究了其基态熵、高温极限能量、比热峰以及相变缺失，并通过热力学积分（thermodynamic integration）从模拟数据中独立恢复了 Simkin 常数 γ。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上 N 皇后问题被视作组合学（combinatorics）或计算机科学中的搜索问题，作者希望从统计力学视角将其重新诠释为一个具有排斥相互作用的晶格气体模型，从而揭示其热力学（thermodynamics）特征，并为组合常数 γ 提供独立于穷举计数的热力学路径。

Method: 采用解析推导获得高温极限能量和约束层次（constraint hierarchy）对熵的贡献；对 N = 8 至 1024 的系统进行大规模蒙特卡洛模拟（每温度点 10⁸ 次扫描）；利用比热收敛性进行热力学积分以提取基态熵；提出基于转移矩阵（transfer matrix）的秩-9 张量网络公式以实现精确枚举。

Result: 基态熵每皇后 s₀ ≈ ln N − γ（γ ≈ 1.944）；高温极限能量 E/N → 5/3（N → ∞）；比热每皇后 Cᵥ/N 在大 N 极限下收敛到通用函数，峰值为 Cᵥᵐᵃˣ/N ≈ 1.63，位于 T* ≈ 0.235 J，未出现发散，表明不存在热力学相变（thermodynamic phase transition）。热力学积分给出 γ_MC = 1.946 ± 0.003（N = 1024），与精确组合值 γ = 1.94400(1) 偏差在 0.1% 以内。

Conclusion: N 皇后问题的统计力学表述成功架起了组合学与热力学之间的桥梁：比热收敛性使热力学积分可行，从而可以从蒙特卡洛数据独立恢复组合常数 γ；张量网络公式则为精确计数提供了另一种路径。该工作表明，组合问题可以作为统计力学系统被有效分析，并从中提取出非平凡的解析和数值结果。

Abstract: We investigate the $N$-queens problem as a lattice gas -- a model in which $N$ queens are placed on an $N \times N$
  chessboard with pairwise repulsive interactions along shared rows, columns, and diagonals -- from the perspective of
  statistical mechanics. The ground states are exactly the $Q(N)$ solutions of the classical $N$-queens problem, with
  entropy per queen $s_0 \approx \ln N - γ$ ($γ\approx 1.944$). This entropy reflects a characteristic
  constraint hierarchy: each successive geometric constraint -- columns, then diagonals -- reduces the entropy from the
  free-placement value $\ln N$ by a definite constant. We derive the exact high-temperature energy $E/N \to 5/3$ as $N
  \to \infty$. Extensive Monte Carlo simulations with $10^8$ sweeps per temperature point for $N = 8$--$1024$ reveal
  that the specific heat per queen $C_v/N$ converges to a universal function of $T$ as $N \to \infty$. The converged
  curve features a non-divergent peak $C_v^{\max}/N \approx 1.63$ at $T^* \approx 0.235\,J$, establishing the absence of
  a thermodynamic phase transition. Combined with the trivially exact high-temperature entropy $S(\infty)/N = (1/N) \ln
  \binom{N^2}{N}$, the convergence of $C_v/N$ enables a thermodynamic integration of $C_v/T$ from $T = \infty$ to $T =
  0$ that recovers the ground-state entropy -- and hence the Simkin constant $γ$ -- purely from Monte Carlo data.
  This provides an independent thermodynamic route to a fundamental combinatorial constant. Thermodynamic integration
  yields $γ_{\rm MC} = 1.946 \pm 0.003$ at $N = 1024$, within $0.1\%$ of the precise combinatorial value $γ=
  1.94400(1)$. We further present a transfer-matrix-based tensor network formulation that encodes the non-attacking
  constraints into a rank-9 site tensor with 17 nonzero elements, providing a complementary exact-enumeration route.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过在实时域（real time）中执行粗粒化（coarse-graining），将重整化群（RG）扩展至由量子操作（quantum operations）描述的非酉（nonunitary）量子动力学。

Result: 发现退相干（decoherence）与相干动力学（coherent dynamics）之间的竞争在重整化群流（RG flow）行为中起决定性作用。当相干动力学占主导时，RG流中出现无不动点（fixed points）的混沌行为，宇称-时间相变（parity-time transition）是典型实例。测量诱导的宇称-时间相变属于一维Yang-Lee边缘奇点（Yang-Lee edge singularity）普适类（universality class）。

Conclusion: 扩展后的RG框架为理解非酉量子动力学中的相变提供了理论工具，并指出通过晶格自旋系统中的量子系统实验实现虚时场（imaginary fields）的可行性。

Abstract: The renormalization group (RG) in statistical physics focuses on ground-state properties of equilibrium systems. However, it is unclear how it should be generalized to nonunitary quantum dynamics caused by dissipation and measurement backaction, in which the notion of conserved energy is absent. Here, we extend the RG to cover nonunitary quantum dynamics governed by quantum operations. By performing coarse-graining in real time, we find that the competition between decoherence and coherent dynamics plays a decisive role in the behavior of the RG flow. In particular, we find that chaotic behavior without fixed points emerges in the RG flow when coherent dynamics is dominant, with the parity-time transition serving as a prototypical example. The measurement-induced parity-time transition belongs to the universality class of the one-dimensional Yang-Lee edge singularity, which serves as a guide for experimentally realizing imaginary fields in lattice spin systems with a quantum system.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该统计物理框架能够有效提取LLM多智能体系统的社会性从众与内在偏差的定量度量，揭示集体对齐的内在驱动力，并为多智能体共识与协作的可靠性提供模型依赖的紧凑指纹（fingerprint）诊断工具。

Abstract: We investigate the emergent collective dynamics of LLM-based multi-agent systems on a 2D square lattice and present a model-agnostic statistical-physics method to disentangle social conformity from intrinsic bias, compute critical exponents, and probe the collective behavior and possible phase transitions of multi-agent systems. In our framework, each node of an $L\!\times\!L$ lattice hosts an identical LLM agent holding a binary state ($+1$/$-1$, mapped to yes/no) and updating it by querying the model conditioned on the four nearest-neighbor states. The sampler temperature $T$ serves as the sole control parameter. Across three open-weight models (llama3.1:8b, phi4-mini:3.8b, mistral:7b), we measure magnetization and susceptibility under a global-flip protocol designed to probe $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry. All models display temperature-driven order-disorder crossovers and susceptibility peaks; finite-size scaling on even-$L$ lattices yields effective exponents $γ/ν$ whose values are model-dependent, close to but incompatible with the 2D Ising universality class ($γ/ν=7/4$). Our method enables the extraction of effective $β$-weighted couplings $\tilde{J}(T)$ and fields $\tilde{h}(T)$, which serve as a measure of social conformity and intrinsic bias. In the models we analyzed, we found that collective alignment is dominated by an intrinsic bias ($\tilde{h}\gg\tilde{J}$) rather than by cooperative neighbor coupling, producing field-driven crossovers instead of genuine phase transitions. These effective parameters vary qualitatively across models, providing compact collective-behavior fingerprints for LLM agents and a quantitative diagnostic for the reliability of multi-agent consensus and collective alignment.

### [186] [The diffusion equation for non-Markovian Gaussian stochastic processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10561)
*Alessandro Taloni,Gianni Pagnini,Aleksei Chechkin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了非马尔可夫、非平稳高斯速度过程下粒子位移概率密度函数的精确演化方程，基于维克定理（Wick's theorem）构建了几何连接收缩（geometrically connected Wick contractions）的层级结构，得到推广福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation）的封闭非马尔可夫扩散方程（non-Markovian diffusion equation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从位移特征函数（characteristic function）出发，基于维克定理构建层级方程系统；该系统通过几何连接维克收缩（geometrically connected Wick contractions）求和来描述动力学过程，最终得到封闭的非马尔可夫扩散方程。

Result: 所得到的演化方程是封闭且非马尔可夫的，它推广了传统的福克-普朗克描述；高斯性（Gaussianity）仅在该方程的无穷阶极限下得以保持。该方法无需假设速度过程的马尔可夫性或平稳性。

Conclusion: 该工作为非马尔可夫、非平稳高斯速度过程下的粒子输运提供了统一的理论框架，为研究复杂环境中（如湍流扩散、生物迁移）的异常扩散（anomalous diffusion）与记忆效应提供了严格的解析工具。

Abstract: We derive the exact evolution equation for the probability density function of particle displacements generated by arbitrary Gaussian velocity processes, when neither Markovianity and nor stationarity are assumed. Starting from the characteristic function of the density of the position, we construct a systematic hierarchy of equations based on Wick's theorem, in which the dynamics is governed by sums of geometrically connected Wick contractions. This approach yields a closed non-Markovian diffusion equation that generalizes the Fokker-Planck description and preserves Gaussianity only in the infinite-order limit.

### [187] [Susceptible-Infected-Susceptible Model with Mitigation on Scale-Free Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10644)
*João Gabriel Simões Delboni,M. O. Hase*

Motivation: 传统流行病模型通常假设均匀混合或仅关注网络拓扑，缺乏对个体行为响应及外部缓解机制的定量刻画。本文旨在通过引入一个受Malthus-Verhulst型约束启发的缓解因子，在保持模型可解析处理的同时，揭示自我限制动力学（self-limiting dynamics）对无标度网络上传染病传播的非平凡影响。

Method: 采用异质平均场方法（heterogeneous mean-field approach）处理无标度网络上的易感-感染-易感（susceptible-infected-susceptible, SIS）模型；个体异质性通过幂律分布（power-law distribution）引入；缓解因子用于刻画行为响应与外部效应对感染者传播能力的有效抑制，从而形成非线性饱和效应。

Result: 缓解因子导致连接指向感染节点的概率在有限感染率下出现最大值，而整体患病率仍随传播率单调递增。此外，在高传播率下，流行病可观测变量对度指数（degree exponent）的依赖发生反转：标准模型中较小的度指数导致更高的地方性患病率，而修正模型中较大的度指数反而产生更高的患病率与沿网络边的感染概率。

Conclusion: 引入缓解因子能显著改变无标度网络上传染病传播的定性行为，包括出现非单调的连接感染概率以及度指数依赖关系的反转。分析结果得到了随机模拟的验证，表明该模型为理解自限性传播机制提供了一种可解析处理的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate infectious disease spreading on scale-free networks using a heterogeneous mean-field approach applied to the susceptible-infected-susceptible model, incorporating a mitigation factor. Individual heterogeneity is incorporated through a power-law distribution, while a mitigation factor accounts for behavioral responses and external effects that effectively reduce transmission from infected individuals. This mechanism, inspired by Malthus-Verhulst-type constraints, introduces a nonlinear saturation effect that encodes self-limiting dynamics in a tractable way. Analytical results are supported by stochastic simulations. We find that the mitigation factor induces a nontrivial behavior in the probability that a link points to an infected node, which develops a maximum at finite infection rates. In contrast, the overall prevalence remains a monotonically increasing function of the transmission rate. Additionally, the mitigation mechanism leads to an inversion in the dependence of epidemic observables on the degree exponent at sufficiently high transmission rates. While in the standard model smaller exponents yield higher endemic prevalence, in the modified model this trend reverses, with larger exponents producing higher prevalence and increased infection probability along network links.

</details>

Method: 采用单孔径双层Canted-Cosine-Theta（CCT）六极磁体拓扑结构，使用来自两家制造商的高温超导（HTS）ReBCO带材作为导体，在低温条件下完成设计、制造与测试，并对两种带材进行了适用性验证。

Abstract: A single-aperture, two-layer Canted-Cosine-Theta (CCT) sextupole magnet using high-temperature superconducting (HTS) ReBCO tape has been developed for the short straight sections (SSS) of FCC through the FCCee-HTS4 project. The magnet was designed, manufactured and tested under cryogenic conditions. Two HTS tapes from two manufacturers have been qualified for this specific application. Design and manufacturing details and cryogenic temperature measurements are presented. This demonstrator represents the first HTS CCT magnet ever constructed.

### [189] [Crystal Fractional Graph Neural Network for Energy Prediction of High-Entropy Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08103)
*Takanori Kotama,Yang Huang*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种晶格分数图神经网络（crystal fractional graph neural network），通过整合局部原子环境与全局成分信息来预测高熵合金的能量。模型在1,049个晶体结构上训练，在198个四元结构上验证，达到了与第一性原理计算相当的RMSE精度，但在处理大晶胞时存在局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高熵合金（high-entropy alloys, HEAs）因其复杂的原子构型而展现出优异的力学和热学性能，但准确预测其能量（energy）是一个挑战。现有方法难以有效结合局部原子相互作用与全局成分信息，因此需要一种能够同时整合这两类信息的预测模型。

Method: 模型由三个子网络组成：晶体图神经网络（crystal graph neural network），利用图注意力网络（graph attention network）层学习晶格内16个位点原子的局部相互作用；分数神经网络（fractional neural network），一个全连接网络（fully connected network），用于嵌入组成元素的全局分数（fraction）；以及特征融合神经网络（feature fusion neural network），融合前两个子网络的输出以预测总晶体能量。所有超参数通过Optuna优化。

Result: 模型在1,049个晶体结构上训练，并在198个四元（quaternary）结构上验证。其RMSE与第一性原理（first-principles）计算结果相当，且对低能量构型仍保持高精度。

Conclusion: 所提出的晶格分数图神经网络能够有效预测高熵合金的能量，精度接近第一性原理方法。但模型在处理大晶胞（large crystal cells）时存在局限性，未来研究将致力于扩展其在更复杂系统上的适用性。

Abstract: High-entropy alloys (HEAs) have attracted growing attention for their exceptional mechanical and thermal properties arising from complex atomic configurations. In this paper, we propose crystal fractional graph neural network for predicting the energy of high-entropy alloys by explicitly integrating both local atomic environments and global compositional information. The model consists of three components: a crystal graph neural network, which employs graph attention network layers to learn local interactions among 16 on-site atoms within the crystal lattice; fractional neural network, a fully connected network that embeds the global fraction of constituent elements; and feature fusion neural network, which fuses the outputs of the two submodels to predict the total crystal energy. We train the model on a dataset of 1,049 crystal structures and validate it on 198 quaternary structures, optimizing all hyperparameters via Optuna. Our results show that our model achieves an RMSE comparable to first-principles calculations and maintains high accuracy even for low-energy configurations. However, the model exhibits limitations in handling large crystal cells, which we aim to address in future work to extend its applicability to more complex systems.

*Francisca Garay,Gabriel Vega,Philipp Roloff*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轻子味破坏（lepton flavor violation）的希格斯玻色子衰变是超出粒子物理标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理可能信号，研究未来对撞机对这些过程的探测能力有助于指导实验设计和搜索策略。

Method: 基于未来紧凑型直线对撞机（Compact Linear Collider, CLIC）的模拟，分析了三个轻子味破坏衰变道$h\rightarrow eμ$、$h\rightarrow τμ$和$h\rightarrow eτ$的灵敏度，考虑了两组对撞参数：质心能量$\sqrt{s}=1.4$ TeV、积分光度$4$ ab$^{-1}$，以及$\sqrt{s}=3$ TeV、积分光度$5$ ab$^{-1}$。

Result: 在未观察到任何信号的情况下，可在95%置信水平（95% CL）上将这些衰变过程的分支比（branching fraction）上限设定在$10^{-4}$到$10^{-5}$范围内。

Conclusion: CLIC对轻子味破坏的希格斯衰变具有较好的探测灵敏度，能够将分支比上限压低至$10^{-5}$量级，为检验超出标准模型的新物理提供重要实验约束。

Abstract: Lepton flavor violating Higgs decays could appear in scenarios beyond the Standard Model of particle physics. In this article, we study the sensitivity of a future Compact Linear Collider (CLIC) to such processes, namely, $h\rightarrow eμ$, $h\rightarrowτμ$, and $h\rightarrow eτ$. In the absence of any observation, 95\% CL\ upper limits in the region of $10^{-4}$ to $10^{-5}$ could be placed on the branching fractions of these processes, assuming integrated luminosities of $4$\,ab$^{-1}$ at $\sqrt{s}=1.4$ TeV and $5$\,ab$^{-1}$ at $\sqrt{s}=3$ TeV.

</details>


### [191] [Inferring identified hadron production in $pp$ collisions with physics-informed machine learning at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09022)
*Rishabh Gupta,Kangkan Goswami,Suraj Prasad,Raghunath Sahoo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural network），利用PYTHIA8模拟数据推断高能强子对撞中探测器接收度之外赝快度区域的带电强子横动量谱，并通过物理约束与超参数优化使模型在训练、插值和外推区域分别达到约1.5%、1.8%和5.83%的产额不确定度，性能优于XGBoost和LightGBM。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测器接收度局限于中央快度区（mid-rapidity），赝快度区域之外的强子谱携带粒子产生的重要信息但尚未被实验测量，因此需要发展数据驱动的推断方法填补这一观测空白。

Method: 构建一个物理信息神经网络，使用PYTHIA8在质心能量13.6 TeV下的质子-质子（$pp$）对撞数据训练模型，将粒子产额比、谱形状与平滑性等物理动机约束融入损失函数（loss function），并采用分阶段超参数优化策略保证训练稳定性。

Result: 模型在训练、插值（interpolation）和外推（extrapolation）区域分别达到约1.5%、1.8%和5.83%的产额不确定度，性能优于XGBoost与LightGBM；同时成功再现粒子产额比、横动量平均值（$\langle p_{\rm T} \rangle$）的多重数依赖性和动力学冻结参数（kinetic freeze-out parameters）等关键可观测量。

Conclusion: 该模型能够捕捉潜在的物理机制，在测量相空间之外提供可靠的预测，为高能碰撞实验中受限接收度区域的强子谱研究提供有效的替代方案。

Abstract: Machine learning has become a powerful tool in high-energy collider experiments, which enables the studies based on data-driven approaches to complex reconstruction and regression tasks. The study of identified hadron spectra in pseudorapidity regions beyond detector acceptance, which is limited to mid-rapidity regions, carries important information about particle production, yet remains unmeasured. In this work, we develop a physics-informed neural network, trained on PYTHIA8 $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV, to infer $p_{\rm T}$ spectra of $π^{\pm}$, $K^{\pm}$, $p/\bar{p}$, $Λ/\barΛ$, and $K^{0}_{\mathrm{s}}$ in different rapidity regions. Physics-motivated constraints, including particle yield ratios, spectral shape, and smoothness, are incorporated into the loss function. A staged hyperparameter optimization strategy is used to ensure stability. The model achieves yield uncertainties of ${\sim}1.5\%$, $1.8\%$, and $5.83\%$ in the training, interpolation, and extrapolation regimes, respectively, outperforming XGBoost and LightGBM. It further reproduces key observables such as particle yield ratios, the multiplicity dependence of $\langle p_{\rm T} \rangle$, and kinetic freeze-out parameters, indicating that the model captures the underlying physics and provides reliable predictions beyond the measured phase space.

</details>


### [192] [Can a Nonstandard Invisible Pair Mimic the Michel Distribution?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09140)
*Pablo Roig*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究在低能有效场论框架下，除标准模型自旋1/2中微子对之外，是否存在其他不可见粒子对（X\bar{X}）可再现与标准模型无法区分的Michel型轻子衰变分布。结论是：唯一非平凡解是无质量复标量对通过纯左手矢量流耦合，其余自旋不可见对均可被区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验观测上看似与标准模型高度吻合的轻子衰变\ell_i \to \ell_j \nu\bar\nu 的Michel分布（Michel distribution），是否可能来自完全不同的不可见扇区（invisible sector）。

Method: 在一般低能有效场论（low-energy effective field theory）框架下，分析\ell_i \to \ell_j + X\bar X衰变过程，其中X\bar X为电中性、无色单态、互为共轭的不可见粒子对，自旋最高为2；允许轻子流中存在（赝）标量、(轴)矢量和反对称张量相互作用，并取无质量极限以对应精确简并情形。基于全套可测微分分布（differential distributions）建立了不可区分性判据（indistinguishability criterion）。

Result: 除标准模型的自旋1/2中微子情况外，唯一非平凡解为：一个无质量复标量对（massless complex scalar pair）通过纯左手矢量流（purely left-handed vector current）耦合，可精确再现标准Michel分布，包括对子代轻子极化（daughter-lepton polarization）和辐射道（radiative channels）的推广。其余所有自旋情况均因高阶自旋不可见对引入额外运动学前因子（kinematic prefactors）而可被区分。

Conclusion: 这些结果隔离出在Michel型轻子衰变测量中唯一可能隐藏的非标准、非平凡不可见扇区，即无质量复标量对通过左手矢量流耦合的情形。

Abstract: We ask whether a measured Michel distribution, apparently in excellent agreement with the Standard Model interpretation of the $\ell_i \to \ell_j ν\barν$ decay, could instead arise from a different invisible sector. Within a general low-energy effective field theory, we analyze lepton decays $\ell_i \to \ell_j + X\bar X$ for electrically neutral, color-singlet, mutually conjugate invisible pairs $X\bar X$ of spin up to $2$, allowing (pseudo)scalar, (axial)vector, and antisymmetric tensor interactions in the lepton current, focusing on the massless limit relevant for exact degeneracies. We formulate a criterion for indistinguishability based on the full set of measurable differential distributions. Under these assumptions, besides the obvious spin $1/2$ case, there is a unique nontrivial solution: a massless complex scalar pair coupled through a purely left-handed vector current exactly reproduces the standard Michel pattern, including its extensions to daughter-lepton polarization and radiative channels. All other cases studied here are distinguishable, in particular because higher-spin invisible pairs produce additional kinematic prefactors. These results isolate the only nonstandard and nontrivial invisible sector that can remain hidden in Michel-type lepton decay measurements.

</details>


### [193] [Probing the nature of $D_1 K$ and $D_2 K$ molecules through $D_s^{(*)}ππ$ and $D_{s0(s1)}π$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09381)
*Xing-Meng Zhao,Liu-Lin Wang,Ying-Bo He,Xiao-Yun Wang,Xiao-Hai Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了I=0的D₁K和D₂K分子态T*_{c\bar{s}1}和T*_{c\bar{s}2}的二体和三体衰变到D_s^{(*)}介子和π的过程。三角奇异性在D*K和DK阈值附近产生D_s^*π和D_sπ不变质量谱中的窄峰。同位旋破坏的二体衰变展现出较大的部分宽度，反映了分子态的强耦合特性。这些基于重强子手征微扰论（heavy hadron chiral perturbation theory）和手征幺正方法（chiral unitary approach）的预言，为实验识别D₁K和D₂K分子提供了互补信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的实验数据和理论研究表明，可能存在由D₁K和D₂K构成的分子态（molecular states）候选者T*_{c\bar{s}1}和T*_{c\bar{s}2}，但其衰变性质尚未被充分研究。理解这些分子的衰变模式，特别是三角奇异性（triangle singularity）和同位旋破坏（isospin violation）过程，对于在实验中确认这些态至关重要。

Method: 采用重强子手征微扰论（heavy hadron chiral perturbation theory, HHChPT）和手征幺正方法（chiral unitary approach）进行理论计算。分析二体和三体衰变过程，重点考察三角奇异性（triangle singularity）在D*K和DK阈值附近对不变质量谱的影响，以及同位旋破坏衰变的部分宽度（partial widths）。

Result: 三角奇异性在D*K和DK阈值附近导致D_s^*π和D_sπ不变质量谱中出现窄峰（narrow peaks）。同位旋破坏的二体衰变T*_{c\bar{s}1}→D_{s1}(2460)π⁰、T*_{c\bar{s}2}→D_{s1}(2460)π⁰和T*_{c\bar{s}2}→D*_{s0}(2317)π⁰展现出较大的部分宽度。

Conclusion: 这些理论预言为实验上鉴别D₁K和D₂K分子态提供了互补的衰变信号（complementary signatures）。三角奇异性产生的窄峰和同位旋破坏衰变的大宽度特征，可用于区分分子态与其他可能的强子解释。

Abstract: We study the two- and three-body decays of the $I=0$ $D_1K$ and $D_2K$ molecular states $T_{c\bar{s}1}^*$ and $T_{c\bar{s}2}^*$ into $D_s^{(*)}$ mesons and pions. Triangle singularities produce narrow peaks in the $D_s^*π$ and $D_sπ$ invariant mass spectra near the $D^*K$ and $DK$ thresholds. The isospin-violating two-body decays $T_{c\bar{s}1}^*\to D_{s1}(2460)π^0$, $T_{c\bar{s}2}^*\to D_{s1}(2460)π^0$, and $T_{c\bar{s}2}^*\to D_{s0}^*(2317)π^0$ exhibit large partial widths, reflecting the strong couplings inherent to molecular states. These predictions, obtained within heavy hadron chiral perturbation theory and the chiral unitary approach, provide complementary signatures for identifying $D_1K$ and $D_2K$ molecules at experiments.

</details>


### [194] [Dissecting Jet-Tagger Through Mechanistic Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09881)
*Saurabh Rai,Sanmay Ganguly*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对基于粒子Transformer架构（Particle Transformer architecture）的顶夸克标签（Top Quark Tagging）分类器进行机械性可解释性（mechanistic interpretability）分析，识别出一个稀疏六头电路（sparse six-head circuit），该电路具有清晰的源-中继-读出（source-relay-readout）结构，能够恢复绝大部分模型性能。研究还发现残差流（residual stream）优先与能量关联子基（energy correlator basis）对齐，且模型在粒子注意力栈（particle attention stack）中已饱和分类判别信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机械性可解释性旨在通过识别最小内部组件子集来逆向工程（reverse engineer）训练好的神经网络。本文旨在对粒子Transformer架构进行机械性可解释性分析，以识别负责喷注分类（jet classification）的计算电路（computational circuit），并刻画其内部表征（internal representations）的物理内容。

Method: 采用零消融（zero ablation）、路径修补（path patching）结合两种互补的流形上扰动策略（on-manifold corruption strategies），以及对残差流进行线性探测（linear probing）。

Result: 识别出一个稀疏六头电路，包含早期层中作为主要因果源（causal source）的单个注意力头、中间层中作为中继（relay）并选择性关注硬对偶子结构（hard pairwise substructure）的注意力头簇，以及后期层中读出聚合信号（aggregated signal）的单个注意力头。残差流优先与能量关联子基对齐，且模型优先编码二支子结构（2-prong substructure）可观测量。线性探测表明，模型在第一类注意力块（first class attention block）中看似单步的分类决策，实际上是基旋转（basis rotation），判别信号在粒子注意力栈中已饱和。

Conclusion: 结果表明，为自然语言模型开发的机械性可解释性方法可用于喷注物理分类器，并说明梯度下降（gradient descent）可能在无监督条件下重新发现喷注标签（jet tagging）的物理有意义方面。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability seeks to reverse engineer a trained neural network by identifying the minimal subset of internal components. We perform a mechanistic interpretability analysis of the Particle Transformer architecture, trained on the Top Quark Tagging reference dataset, with the goal of identifying the computational circuit responsible for jet classification and characterizing the physical content of its internal representations. Combining zero ablation, path patching with two complementary on-manifold corruption strategies and linear probing of the residual stream, we identify a sparse six-head circuit that recovers the great majority of the full model performance while admitting a clean source-relay-readout interpretation. In this circuit, a single early layer head serves as the primary causal source, a cluster of middle-layer heads acts as relays selectively attending to hard pairwise substructure and a single late-layer head reads out the aggregated signal. Linear probes show that the residual stream is preferentially aligned with the energy correlator basis over the $N$-subjettiness basis. Within the energy correlator basis, the model preferentially encodes 2-prong substructure observables over the 3-prong observables. A per-layer trained probe further reveals that the apparent single step commitment of the model to a classification decision in the first class attention block is in fact a basis rotation, with the discriminating signal already saturating in the particle attention stack. These results demonstrate that mechanistic interpretability methods developed for natural language models can be used for jet physics classifiers and indicate that gradient descent may rediscover physically meaningful aspects of jet tagging without supervision.

</details>


### [195] [Revival of the Reactor Antineutrino Anomaly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10353)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反应堆反中微子反常最初于2011年以2.5σ的置信水平被发现，随后在2021年因新的通量计算被认为降至约1σ而基本解决。然而，2023年法国研究团队发布了首个包含完整不确定度预算的求和模型（summation model）通量计算，本文旨在基于这一最新计算结果重新审视该反常的现状及其物理含义。

Conclusion: 基于最新的通量计算，反应堆反中微子反常并未完全解决，而是以2.2σ的水平重新出现。活性-惰性中微子振荡作为解释方案面临主要来自镓源实验与其他数据集之间的显著张力，该张力可能源于被低估的系统不确定度（systematic uncertainties）。扩大镓数据不确定度后全局张力显著缓和，表明系统误差可能是造成矛盾的主要原因。

Abstract: The Reactor Antineutrino Anomaly refers to the deficit observed between the average event rate measured in reactor antineutrino experiments with respect to the theoretical prediction. This anomaly was first identified in 2011 ($2.5σ$) as a consequence of the Huber-Muller reactor antineutrino flux calculation. It was thought to be resolved in 2021 as a result of new reactor antineutrino flux calculations, with a reduction to about $1 σ$. In this work, we examine the latest reactor antineutrino flux calculation published in 2023 by a French research group. This work represents the first summation model to include a comprehensive uncertainty budget. The result indicates a revival of the Reactor Antineutrino Anomaly at the level of $2.2\,σ$. We also consider the usual simplest explanation of the Reactor Antineutrino Anomaly by active-sterile neutrino oscillations. We present the constraints on the oscillation parameters and we derive a tension of $3.8σ$ with the results of gallium source experiments (Gallium Anomaly) taking into account also the solar neutrino and KATRIN bounds, that of the combined short-baseline reactor spectral ratio measurements, and that of the Daya Bay search for a sub-eV sterile neutrino. Since the tension may be due to underestimated systematic uncertainties and the main tension is between the gallium data and the other data, we finally present the results of a global analysis with enlarged gallium uncertainties, which reduce the global tension to $1.3σ$.

### [196] [Distinguishing Higgs portal and neutralino dark matter via vector boson fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10699)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解暗物质（DM）的本质是粒子物理学的基本挑战，需要发展能够区分不同暗物质模型的有效实验方法。

Method: 研究聚焦于LHC上的矢量玻色子融合（VBF）过程，利用$2j+\not\!\!E_T$末态中VBF喷注的极化和运动学特征、横动量分布以及$\Delta\eta$和$\Delta\varphi$等运动学变量，并结合Kolmogorov–Smirnov检验与线性判别分析（linear discriminant analysis）进行量化区分。

Result: VBF中弱玻色子的极化显著影响标记喷注的横动量分布：希格斯门户暗物质（HPDM）场景下喷注在横向方向能量更低；$\Delta\eta$和$\Delta\varphi$在两类信号间表现出特征性差异；线性判别分析表明区分置信水平超过5σ。

Abstract: Understanding the nature of dark matter (DM) is a fundamental challenge in particle physics. In this paper, we investigate the potential of vector boson fusion (VBF) processes at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) to demonstrate, as a proof of principle, the feasibility of distinguishing between different dark matter scenarios, focusing on Higgs portal DM (HPDM) and neutralino DM in the $2j + \not\!\! E_T$ final state and exploiting the distinctive kinematic features of the VBF jets and the missing transverse energy. Our study reveals that the polarization of weak bosons in VBF plays a crucial role in shaping the transverse momentum distributions of the tagged jets, with the jets being less energetic in the transverse direction for the Higgs portal scenario compared to the neutralino scenario. In addition, the kinematic variables $Δη$ and $Δφ$ exhibit characteristic differences between the Higgs portal and neutralino DM signals, providing significant discriminating power between these scenarios. We further apply a Kolmogorov--Smirnov test using linear discriminant analysis to quantify the distinguishability of the signals and find that the Higgs portal signals can be differentiated from neutralino DM signals with a C.L. exceeding $5σ$, thereby establishing the viability of collider-based discrimination between dark matter models.

We take into account supergravity, radiative, and soft supersymmetry-breaking corrections to the tree-level potential and find that viable FHI can be realized without extrema along the inflationary trajectory for a broad region of the parameter space. TL;DR: 本文提出了一种生成函数（generating-function）框架，用于多圈费曼积分（multi-loop Feynman integrals）的符号约化。在该框架中，分部积分恒等式（integration-by-parts identities）被重写为按扇区（sector-wise）生成函数的微分方程，从而将约化问题置于一个非对易微分算子代数中进行研究，并发展出基于此代数结构的迭代算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于分部积分恒等式的多圈费曼积分约化方法主要处理单个积分之间的关系，缺乏一个统一的代数框架来系统组织符号约化规则、后代方程（descendant equations）和完备性判据。

Method: 将分部积分恒等式重写为按扇区生成函数的微分方程，将约化问题转化为非对易微分算子代数中的问题；基于该代数视角设计了一个迭代算法，依次生成候选方程、提取符号约化规则、更新活动规则集，并在积分指数格点上测试完备性。

Result: 以日落图拓扑（sunset topology）、平面与非平面无质量双盒子拓扑（planar and non-planar massless double-box topologies）及其代表性子扇区为例实现了该方法，并展示了一个顶扇区不含主积分的退化情形。

Conclusion: 该方法表明符号约化规则、后代方程和完备性判据可在同一个代数框架下统一组织。

Abstract: We develop a generating-function formulation for the symbolic reduction of multi-loop Feynman integrals. In this framework, integration-by-parts identities are rewritten as differential equations for sector-wise generating functions, so the reduction problem can be studied in a non-commutative algebra of differential operators rather than only through relations among individual integrals. This viewpoint leads to an iterative algorithm that generates candidate equations, extracts symbolic reduction rules, updates the active rule set, and tests completeness on the lattice of integral indices. We illustrate the method with the sunset topology, planar and non-planar massless double-box topologies, representative subsectors, and a degenerate example in which the top sector contains no master integral. Together, these examples show how symbolic reduction rules, descendant equations, and completeness criteria can be organized within a single algebraic framework.

Hierarchical Yukawa couplings can be obtained from the overlap integrals of wavefunctions localized in extra dimensions, allowing semi-realistic patterns of flavor structures for quarks and charged leptons. ### [200] [Controlled Penumbral Inflation from Monodromic Valleys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10197)
*Pirzada,Tianjun Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，复杂结构模空间半影区（penumbra）中的长单值谷（long monodromic valleys）的局部分支数据即可判定其是否支持受控暴胀（controlled inflation），并由此首次确定了受控半影暴胀窗口。通过引入分支偏移奇次项，给出了受控条件（Δ>0、p<2等），并识别出一个具有闭合形式谷（closed-form valley）和不变吸引子方程（invariant attractor equation）的最小解析族，为半影区提供了首个精确可解的实现，将半影从几何猜想提升为可预测的搜索原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂结构模空间（complex-structure moduli space）的半影区中存在长单值谷，但这些谷是否以及如何支持暴胀仍不清楚。本文的动机在于建立局部分支数据与可控暴胀之间的直接判定准则，从而系统性地识别半影区中的受控暴胀窗口。

Method: 在轴子—伸缩子有效理论（axion--saxion effective theory）框架下，引入一个分支偏移奇次项（branch-displacing odd term），推导了受控暴胀条件：Δ ≡ p + 2ν − q > 0 时产生平台（plateau），且协变单时钟控制（covariant single-clock control）进一步要求 p < 2，或 p = 2 且 12A_p m² / V₀ >> 1 在观测窗口内成立。在此基础上，识别了一个具有闭合形式谷和不变吸引子方程的最小解析族（minimal analytic family）。

Result: 根据局部分支数据，半影谷可被划分为三类：无平台（no plateau）、非受控平台（uncontrolled plateau）和受控平台（controlled plateau）。文中给出了首个精确可解的半影暴胀实现，该实现在下一阶半影修正下仍保持可预测性（predictive）。

Conclusion: 半影区不再仅是一个几何上的推测性概念，而被提升为一个可操作的、具有预测能力的搜索原则（predictive search principle），为系统地寻找受控弦景观暴胀模型提供了新的路径。

Abstract: Long monodromic valleys arise in the penumbra of complex-structure moduli space. We show that their local branch data already determine whether they support controlled inflation, and thereby isolate the first controlled penumbral inflationary window. In the axion--saxion effective theory given in Eq.4, a branch-displacing odd term generates a plateau when $Δ\equiv p+2ν-q>0$, while covariant single-clock control further requires $p<2$, or $p=2$ with $12A_pm^2/V_0\gg1$ over the observational window. This splits penumbral valleys into no plateau, uncontrolled plateau, and controlled plateau before global completion is attempted. We identify a minimal analytic family with a closed-form valley and an invariant attractor equation for the full two-field dynamics, providing the first exactly solvable penumbral realization that remains predictive under the next penumbral order. The penumbra is thus promoted from a geometric suggestion to a predictive search principle.

### [201] [Axial Quasi-normal Modes of Admixed Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10467)
*Hamza Boumaza,Boris Betancourt Kamenetskaia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过求解双流体Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff方程，研究由普通核物质和自相互作用玻色子暗物质混合组成的中子星（admixed neutron stars）的轴向准正则模（quasi-normal modes），发现暗物质组分会显著改变振荡频率、阻尼时间及模式层次，使环down信号从中子星型连续过渡到玻色子星型，为引力波探测暗物质提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索混合中子星中暗物质组分对轴向引力波准正则模谱的影响，旨在揭示致密星体环down引力波信号中暗物质的可观测印记，为未来引力波天文台探测暗物质（dark matter）提供理论依据。

Method: 采用耦合双流体Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff（TOV）方程组求解平衡构型；中子组分使用多个现实物态方程（equation of state），玻色子组分由强耦合区（strong-coupling regime）的排斥自相互作用复标量场描述；轴向线性扰动由Regge-Wheeler型方程（Regge-Wheeler type equation）控制；采用连分数法（continued-fraction method）计算基模和泛音w模的复本征频率。

Result: 暗物质分数增加会改变振荡频率和阻尼时间；可导致模式层次通过交叉重新排序；驱动环down行为从中子星型连续过渡到玻色子星型（boson star-like ringdown behavior）。准正则模谱依赖于暗物质粒子质量、自耦合强度以及两种流体的中心密度。

Conclusion: 致密天体并合后的环down引力波信号（ringdown gravitational-wave signal）可能编码暗物质组分的清晰印记，未来引力波天文台有望利用该特征探测暗物质（dark sector）。

Abstract: We study axial quasi-normal modes of admixed neutron stars composed of ordinary nuclear matter and a self-interacting bosonic dark matter component. The equilibrium configurations are obtained by solving the coupled two-fluid Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations, where the neutron sector is modeled with several realistic equations of state and the bosonic sector is described by a repulsively self-interacting complex scalar field in the strong-coupling regime. We analyze linear axial perturbations governed by a Regge-Wheeler type equation whose effective potential reflects the combined matter distribution. Using a continued-fraction method, we compute the complex eigenfrequencies of the fundamental and overtone $w$ modes. We obtain the quasi-normal mode spectrum and investigate its dependence on the dark matter particle mass, self-coupling, and the central densities of both fluids for several realistic neutron star equations of state. We find that increasing the dark matter fraction shifts the oscillation frequencies and damping times. It can also reorder the mode hierarchy through crossings, and it drives a continuous transition from neutron star-like to boson star-like ringdown behavior. Our results demonstrate that the ringdown gravitational-wave signal from post-merger compact objects could encode clear imprints of a dark matter component, offering a new probe of the dark sector with future gravitational-wave observatories.

### [202] [Non-equilibrium scaling across first-order transitions with relativistic scalar fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10346)
*Leon J. Sieke,Jessica Fuchs,Lorenz von Smekal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过经典统计晶格模拟，研究了相对论性Z₂对称标量场理论在线性驱动下跨越磁一级相变的非平衡动力学，发现快速驱动时系统展现出与平均场模拟相同的有限时间标度行为，慢速淬火则交叉到临界Kibble-Zurek标度行为，低温下成核与生长主导转变动力学并产生标度修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究相对论性Z₂对称标量场理论在二维和三维空间中，线性驱动下跨越磁一级相变（magnetic first-order phase transitions）时的非平衡动力学（out-of-equilibrium dynamics），特别是驱动时间尺度、温度和维度对系统行为的综合影响。

Method: 采用经典统计晶格模拟（classical-statistical lattice simulations），在二维和三维空间中对相对论性Z₂对称标量场理论实施Langevin动力学，分别在靠近临界温度Tc和远低于Tc的条件下对系统进行线性驱动。

Result: 快速驱动时系统展现出与温度、维度无关的有限时间标度行为（finite-time scaling behavior），与平均场模拟结果一致；慢速淬火靠近Tc时交叉到临界Kibble-Zurek标度行为（critical Kibble-Zurek scaling behavior）；T≪Tc时成核和生长主导转变动力学，产生标度修正；在序参量变号附近，交叉行为可由Kibble-Zurek标度的主导代数修正很好描述。

Conclusion: 在T≲Tc条件下，当驱动足够快以避免成核（nucleation）但足够慢以形成关联（correlations）时，可以观察到普适的非平衡标度行为，并计算了序参量（order parameter）对应的普适标度函数（universal scaling functions）。

Abstract: We investigate the out-of-equilibrium dynamics of a relativistic $Z_2$-symmetric scalar field theory with Langevin dynamics in two and three spatial dimensions under linear driving across magnetic first-order phase transitions, close to and far below the critical temperature $T_c$. Using classical-statistical lattice simulations, we find that if the driving timescale is sufficiently fast, the system exhibits finite-time scaling behavior independent of temperature and dimensionality, identical to that observed in mean-field simulations. In slow quenches near $T_c$ this mean-field behavior crosses over to critical Kibble-Zurek scaling behavior, while for temperatures $T \ll T_c$ nucleation and growth dominate the transition dynamics, resulting in corrections to scaling. Near the transition point where the order parameter changes sign, the crossover between mean-field and critical out-of-equilibrium dynamics is found to be well described by the leading algebraic correction to Kibble-Zurek scaling. We find that universal non-equilibrium scaling behavior can be observed for $T \lesssim T_c$, provided the driving is fast enough to avoid nucleation but slow enough for correlations to form, and compute the associated universal scaling functions for the order parameter.

</details>

### [203] [Indirect Detection of Lactate Through Voltammetry Using Glassy Carbon Microelectrodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08264)
*Amish Rohtagia,Elisa Barts,Neharika Ravichandran,Sandra Lara Galindoa,Surabhi Nimbalkara,Mantra Mittal,Samantha Omer,Sam Kassegnea*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过将乳酸氧化酶（lactate oxidase）固定在壳聚糖（chitosan）基质中，修饰于光刻图案化的玻璃碳（glassy carbon, GC）微电极上，利用酶促反应产生过氧化氢（hydrogen peroxide）这一电活性副产物，结合快速扫描循环伏安法（fast-scan cyclic voltammetry, FSCV）实现对乳酸（lactate）的间接检测，检测限低至10 nM，并将功能化电极集成在柔性神经探针阵列上，为活体应用提供了可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 玻璃碳微电极虽已广泛用于多巴胺、血清素等电活性神经递质的伏安检测，但乳酸、谷氨酸、γ-氨基丁酸（gamma-aminobutyric acid, GABA）等非电活性分子无法通过常规伏安法直接检测，需进行表面功能化修饰以拓展其检测范围。

Method: 将乳酸氧化酶固定在壳聚糖基质中，修饰于光刻图案化的玻璃碳微电极表面，通过酶催化反应将乳酸转化为过氧化氢这一电活性产物；采用快速扫描循环伏安法（FSCV）检测过氧化氢，实现乳酸的间接电化学检测；利用扫描电子显微镜（scanning electron microscopy, SEM）和傅里叶变换红外光谱（Fourier transform infrared, FTIR）对电极表面形貌和键合作用进行表征。

Result: 功能化后的玻璃碳微电极可在体外实现对乳酸的低至10 nM的间接检测；FTIR分析通过特征O-H、N-H、酰胺及C-O伸缩振动谱带确认了壳聚糖的成功沉积；过氧化氢检测呈浓度依赖性，而乳酸检测因酶动力学限制出现早期饱和现象。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了一种机械性能稳健的玻璃碳微电极平台，可用于纳摩尔级别的间接乳酸传感，并为酶基电化学检测中反应-扩散耦合（reaction-diffusion coupling）机制提供了 insight。

Abstract: Glassy carbon (GC) microelectrodes are increasingly being used for voltametric detection of electroactive neurotransmitters such as dopamine and serotonin. However, non-electroactive molecules including lactate, glutamate, and gamma-aminobutyric acid (GABA) cannot be directly detected using conventional voltammetry without surface functionalization. In this study, lactate oxidase was immobilized within a chitosan matrix on lithographically patterned GC microelectrodes to enable indirect detection of lactate via enzymatic generation of hydrogen peroxide, an electroactive byproduct. The resulting hydrogen peroxide was detected using fast-scan cyclic voltammetry (FSCV), enabling indirect in vitro detection of lactate at concentrations as low as 10 nM. The functionalized GC microelectrodes were integrated into a four channel array on a 1.6 cm flexible neural probe with potential for in vivo applications. Surface morphology and bonding interactions were characterized using scanning electron microscopy (SEM) and Fourier transform infrared (FTIR) spectroscopy. FTIR analysis confirmed successful chitosan deposition through characteristic O-H, N-H, amide, and C-O stretching bands. Hydrogen peroxide detection was concentration-dependent, while lactate detection exhibited early saturation consistent with enzyme-limited kinetics. These results demonstrate a mechanically robust GC microelectrode platform for nanomolar-level indirect lactate sensing and provide insight into the reaction-diffusion coupling governing enzyme-based electrochemical detection.
