### [204] [Dual Fear Mechanisms Shaping Stochastic Population Dynamics under the Allee Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09255)
*Özgür Gültekin,Mirza Muradli*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本文提出一个包含恐惧效应的三次方种群模型，通过两个功能通道（抑制内禀增长率和调节Holling III型功能响应的饱和结构）影响具有Allee效应的单物种种群。该模型的随机扩展基于Langevin形式与Fokker-Planck方程，解析得到了稳态概率分布，揭示了噪声诱导的相变和恐惧控制的低密度态与高密度态之间的转换。此外，通过归一化矩、Fisher信息和平均首通时间分析了统计性质和逃逸动力学。模型将恐惧视为独立控制参数，为恐惧介导的种群动态中若干矛盾的实证发现提供了自然解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统捕食者-猎物模型仅将种群变化归因于捕食效应，但越来越多的证据表明捕食诱导的恐惧（predator-induced fear）是塑造种群动态的重要因素。本文旨在构建一个定量框架，系统研究恐惧如何通过多个功能通道影响具有Allee效应（Allee effect）的单物种种群动态，并解释现有文献中相互冲突的实证发现。

Method: 构建了一个三次方种群模型（cubic population model），恐惧通过两个功能通道发挥作用：(1) 通过乘法抑制机制（multiplicative suppression mechanism）降低内禀增长率；(2) 通过重新缩放Holling III型功能响应项（Holling type III interaction term）的饱和结构来调节增长与交互动态。随机扩展采用Langevin形式（Langevin formalism），包含相关的加性和乘性高斯噪声（correlated additive and multiplicative Gaussian noise），并利用对应的Fokker-Planck方程（Fokker-Planck equation）解析求解稳态概率分布（steady state probability distribution, SSPD）。通过数值模拟验证解析解，并使用现象学分岔（phenomenological bifurcation, P-bifurcation）图和三维分布曲面分析相变。

Result: 稳态概率分布同时揭示了噪声诱导的相变（noise-induced transitions）和恐惧控制的低密度态与高密度态之间的体制转换。恐惧的双通道效应产生了结构竞争和非单调分布变化。通过归一化矩（normalized moments）、Fisher信息（Fisher information）和平均首通时间（mean first-passage time, MFPT）进一步量化了统计性质和逃逸动力学。

Conclusion: 该模型将恐惧视为一个独立控制参数（independent control parameter），为恐惧介导的种群动态中若干冲突的实证发现提供了自然解释，并为保护生物学（conservation biology）和生态系统管理（ecosystem management）提供了分析基础。

Abstract: Traditional population models that include predator-prey interactions attribute demographic changes directly to predation-related effects. However, predator-induced fear in prey has increasingly been recognised as an important factor shaping population dynamics. In this study, we propose a cubic population model in which fear acts through two distinct functional channels for a single-species population exhibiting the Allee effect. In this model, fear reduces the intrinsic growth rate through a multiplicative suppression mechanism while also playing an integrated role in modulating the growth and interaction dynamics by rescaling the saturation structure of the Holling type III interaction term. The stochastic extension of the model is described by a Langevin formalism containing correlated additive and multiplicative Gaussian noise, and the steady state probability distribution (SSPD) is analytically obtained using the corresponding Fokker-Planck equation. The analytical solution is validated by numerical simulations. The SSPD reveals both noise-induced transitions and fear-controlled regime changes between low- and high-density states, with the two-channel effect of fear producing structural competition and non-monotonic changes in the distribution. These are analysed through phenomenological bifurcation (P-bifurcation) diagrams and three-dimensional distribution surfaces. Additionally, statistical properties, parameter sensitivity, and escape dynamics are investigated through normalised moments, Fisher information, and mean first-passage time (MFPT) calculations. Notably, our model treats fear as an independent control parameter and provides a natural explanation for several conflicting empirical findings in the literature on fear-mediated population dynamics, while also offering an analytical basis for conservation biology and ecosystem management.

</details>

### [205] [Mathematical analysis and numerical methods for the computation of transport coefficients in molecular dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10507)
*Noe Blassel,Louis Carillo,Shiva Darshan,Raphael Gastaldello,Alessandra Iacobucci,Elisa Marini,Regis Santet,Xiaocheng Shang,Gabriel Stoltz,Urbain Vaes*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了分子动力学中计算输运系数（transport coefficients）的三类数值方法：非平衡方法、基于时间关联函数的平衡方法以及瞬态技术，并讨论了各类方法的数值误差估计与方差缩减技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 输运系数的数值计算在分子动力学（molecular dynamics）中具有基础重要性，但现有方法在精度和效率上仍面临挑战，亟需系统梳理与改进。

Method: 将计算方法分为三类：(i) 非平衡方法（nonequilibrium methods），通过施加外部驱动场并测量平均响应来获取线性响应系数；(ii) 基于时间关联函数（time correlation function）的平衡方法，如Green–Kubo公式和Einstein公式；(iii) 瞬态技术（transient techniques），通过监测扰动动力学回归稳态的过程来计算输运系数。

Result: 为每类方法提供了数值分析要素，用于估计或量化输运系数估计量中的数值误差；同时介绍了采用控制变量（control variates）、重要性采样（importance sampling）和耦合方法（coupling methods）等方差缩减技术的最新进展。

Conclusion: 输运系数的计算仍然具有挑战性，未来仍需要持续的研究努力。

Abstract: We review various numerical approaches to compute transport coefficients in molecular dynamics. These approaches can be broadly classified into three groups: (i) nonequilibrium methods based on applying an external driving field to the system, measuring the average response in the system, and evaluating the related linear response coefficient; (ii) approaches reformulating the transport coefficient of interest through a time correlation function for the equilibrium dynamics (the most popular instances being Green--Kubo and Einstein formulas); (iii) transient techniques, where the transport coefficient can be computed by monitoring the return to the steady state of a dynamics perturbed off its stationary distribution. For all three classes of methods, we provide elements of numerical analysis, allowing to estimate or at least quantify the level of numerical errors in the estimator of the transport coefficient; and also briefly present recent attempts to more efficiently compute transport coefficients with variance reduction approaches such as control variates, importance sampling and coupling methods. The computation of transport coefficients remains nonetheless challenging and will continue requiring research efforts in the foreseeable future.

</details>

### [206] [Scaling limits for nonlinear functionals of the discrete Gaussian free field with degenerate random conductances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10884)
*Christof F. Peter,Martin Slowik*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维随机子图（包括独立同分布超临界逾渗簇）上带遍历随机电导的离散高斯自由场的非线性泛函，证明了在几乎每个环境实现下，重整化场的非线性泛函在适当 Sobolev 空间 $H^{-s}(D)$ 中收敛到其连续极限，并建立了带 Dirichlet 边界条件的随机游走格林函数的逐点估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在随机环境中理解离散随机场（如高斯自由场（Gaussian free field））的非线性泛函的标度极限行为，是随机分析与统计力学（statistical mechanics）中的核心问题。特别地，当背景介质（由随机电导（random conductances）描述）具有遍历性和无界性时，经典方法难以直接适用，因此需要建立更一般的收敛框架。

Method: 论文考虑定义在二维随机子图（包括 i.i.d. 超临界逾渗（percolation）簇）上的离散高斯自由场，其随机电导满足可积性条件。主要技术工具是建立带有 Dirichlet 边界条件的随机游走格林函数（Green's function）的逐点有界估计，该估计对所有维度 $d \geq 2$ 均成立，并以此为基础证明非线性泛函在 Sobolev 空间 $H^{-s}(D)$ 中的收敛性。

Result: 对几乎每个随机环境的实现，经过适当标度的离散高斯自由场的非线性泛函在 Sobolev 空间 $H^{-s}(D)$（对合适的 $s > 0$）中收敛到其连续极限。此外，针对所有 $d \geq 2$ 维度的随机电导系统，建立了格林函数的逐点上界估计。

Conclusion: 该结果将离散随机场非线性泛函的标度极限理论拓展到了一类具有遍历随机电导的随机子图环境，为更一般的无序介质（disordered media）中的场论极限提供了理论保证。同时，格林函数的普适性估计（不依赖于维度和环境的具体实现）为进一步研究随机环境中的随机游走行为奠定了重要基础。

Abstract: We consider nonlinear functionals of discrete Gaussian free fields with ergodic random conductances on a class of random subgraphs of $\mathbb{Z}^{2}$, including i.i.d. supercritical percolation clusters, where the conductances are possibly unbounded but satisfy an integrability condition. As our main result, we show that, for almost every realisation of the environment, the nonlinear functionals of the rescaled field converge to their continuum counterparts in the Sobolev space $H^{-s}(D)$ for suitable $s > 0$. To obtain the latter, we establish pointwise bounds for the Green's function of the associated random walk among random conductances with Dirichlet boundary conditions, which are valid for all $d \geq 2$.

</details>

### [207] [Theory for TERS of 2D materials including out-of-plane Raman response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08387)
*Raul Corrêa,Luiz G. Cançado,Ado Jorio*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文扩展了针尖增强拉曼光谱（TERS）理论，在原有仅适用于石墨烯的面内响应模型基础上，引入了面外拉曼响应（out-of-plane Raman response），并给出了光场在针尖与样品间传播的精确解析表达式。研究表明，样品-针尖（TS）散射贡献仅当面外响应显著时才重要；TERS增强对面外响应高度敏感，而归一化针尖逼近测量对相干长度（coherence length）更敏感。通过分析石墨烯实验，验证了其面外响应可忽略且相干长度非零的结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TERS理论（Phys. Rev. X 4, 031054 (2014)）仅针对石墨烯设计，忽略了其面外（out-of-plane）拉曼响应；然而TERS可用于测量过渡金属二硫属化物（TMDs）等多种二维材料，这些材料可能存在显著的面外响应，因此需要将面外响应纳入理论框架。

Method: 在原有TERS理论中引入面外拉曼响应，推导出针尖与样品间光场传播的精确解析表达式；系统数值研究了针尖半径（tip radius）、面外响应强度、TERS相干长度（coherence length）、介质折射率等物理参数对TERS信号的影响。

Result: 样品-针尖（TS）散射贡献仅在面外响应显著时重要；TERS增强对面外拉曼响应高度敏感，而归一化针尖逼近（tip-approach）测量对相干长度更敏感；介质折射率会导致一个有效针尖增强因子$f_e$。对石墨烯实验的分析表明，其面外拉曼响应可忽略，且相干长度非零。

Conclusion: 强TERS增强是探讨不同拉曼模式之间信号差异的必要条件。该理论为基于TERS研究面外拉曼响应显著的二维材料提供了统一的解析框架和实验指导。

Abstract: Tip-Enhanced Raman Spectroscopy (TERS) can be used to make nanoscale spatial measurements of 2D materials, such as graphene and transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs). The TERS theory introduced in [Phys. Rev. X 4, 031054 (2014)], however, was tailored for graphene, whose out-of-plane Raman response is neglected. In the present work, we include the out-of-plane response in the TERS theory. In doing so, we provide an exact analytical expression for the field propagation between the tip and the sample, and show that the contribution to the TERS signal that scatters first at the sample, then at the tip (sample-tip, or TS) is important only when the out-of-plane response is significant. We extensively study the variation of TERS experimental measurements when varying physical parameters of the system, like the tip radius, the out-of-plane response, the TERS coherence length, and others. It becomes evident that the TERS enhancement is very sensitive to the out-of-plane Raman response of the phonon mode, while normalized tip-approach measurements are more sensitive to the coherence length, and we show that the medium refractive index leads to an effective tip enhancement factor $f_e$. Our results lead to the conclusion that, in general, a strong TERS enhancement is a necessary condition for investigating the physics discussed here, which here means surveying the difference in TERS signals between different Raman modes. We use our model to analyze some graphene TERS experiments, showing that they are consistent with a negligible out-of-plane Raman response and a non-zero TERS coherence length in the fitting.

</details>


### [208] [Diamond membranes: platform for photonic and opto-mechanical applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10000)
*Hsin-Hui Huang,Gediminas Seniutinas,Haoran Mu,Nguyen Hoai An Le,Eulalia Puig Vilardell,Vijayakumar Anand,Jitraporn Vongsvivut,Tomas Katkus,Meguya Ryu,Junko Morikawa,Saulius Juodkazis*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过红外反射和透射表征金刚石光栅（grating）的吸光度二色性变化；利用飞秒激光（1030 nm/200 fs）以高于0.4 J/cm²/脉冲的能量密度实现碳化（carbonization）与氧化（oxidation）两步切割；并对缩放结构进行光强分布建模，分析不同偏振下的干涉图案（interference patterns）。

Conclusion: 金刚石薄膜在红外波段具有可调控的二色性特性，结合飞秒激光微加工与偏振相关干涉效应，为设计基于金刚石的光子与量子器件提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Diamond 1 - 10 micrometers thick membranes are platform for photonic, quantum and opto-mechanic devices with applications across UV-IR spectral ranges. IR characterization of diamond gratings in reflection and transmission showed a change of the IR absorbance dichroism between positive and negative when the grating period was 1-2 wavelengths (free space) including inside the region of the intrinsic diamond absorbance. Femtosecond laser cutting of micrometers-wide and mm-long structures are demonstrated by steps of carbonization > 0.4 J/cm2/pulse (1030 nm/200 fs) and oxidation of diamond membranes. Light intensity distribution inside form-birefringent diamond structure was modeled for a scaled-down structure and wavelength to reveal characteristic interference patterns for different polarizations.

### [209] [Benchmarking a restricted Boltzmann machine on the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ Bose-Hubbard chain in the adiabatic hard-core regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09247)
*Gustavo Alejandro Avalos Valentín,Roman Josué Armenta Rico,Isaac Pérez Castillo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文利用浅层受限玻尔兹曼机（restricted Boltzmann machine）作为变分拟设（variational ansatz），通过变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）方法研究半填充时绝热硬核极限（adiabatic hard-core limit）下$\mathbb{Z}_2$玻色-哈伯德链（Bose-Hubbard chain）的基态，并成功复现了其相图结构与对称性破缺绝缘构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究$\mathbb{Z}_2$玻色-哈伯德链在绝热硬核极限下半填充时的基态，检验浅层受限玻尔兹曼机（restricted Boltzmann machine）作为神经量子态（neural quantum state）能否准确描述该模型的相图与对称性破缺绝缘构型。

Method: 采用浅层受限玻尔兹曼机作为变分拟设，结合变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）方法进行数值模拟，并与该模型已有的绝热描述（adiabatic description）进行对比。

Result: 变分结果复现了由磁化观测量（magnetization observables）获得的相图整体结构，能够区分极化（polarized）区和奈尔有序（Néel-ordered）区，并捕捉到由弱对称性破缺场（weak symmetry-breaking field）选择的交错绝缘构型中的代表性自旋模式与格点占据数。

Conclusion: 浅层受限玻尔兹曼机能够复现一维$\mathbb{Z}_2$玻色-哈伯德链的主要绝热相结构，并捕捉半填充时被选中的对称性破缺绝缘构型。

Abstract: We study the ground state of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ Bose-Hubbard chain in the adiabatic hard-core limit at half filling using variational Monte Carlo with a shallow restricted Boltzmann machine as the variational ansatz. In this context, the neural quantum state is compared with the established adiabatic description of the model. The variational results reproduce the overall structure of the phase diagram obtained from magnetization observables, distinguish the polarized and Néel-ordered regions, and capture representative spin patterns and site occupations for the staggered insulating configurations selected by a weak symmetry-breaking field. Taken together, these results show that a shallow restricted Boltzmann machine reproduces the main adiabatic phase structure of the one-dimensional $\mathbb{Z}_2$ Bose-Hubbard chain and captures the selected symmetry-broken insulating configurations at half filling.

### [210] [Local supersolid in moiré modulated Bose-Hubbard model using density-matrix renormalization group method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10238)
*Siyu Xie,Qiang Xu,Qianqian Shi,Wanzhou Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法，在一维莫尔势（moiré potential）下的玻色-哈伯德模型（Bose-Hubbard model）中系统探索了局域超固态（local supersolid, lSS）相的出现，并刻画了其区别于全局超固态的三大关键特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超固态（supersolid）相的寻找与表征是凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）的核心课题之一。受二维莫尔光学晶格中局域超流相与绝缘相实验发现的启发，本文旨在探索一维莫尔势下局域超固态相的存在性及其微观特征。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法，对受莫尔势影响的一维玻色-哈伯德模型进行数值模拟。设置最大格点占据数n_max=2以实现软核玻色子（soft-core boson）约束。研究分别在有/无最近邻排斥相互作用两种情形下的基态相图。

Result: 无最近邻排斥时，识别出常规超流相、局域超流相、莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）相及莫尔诱导绝缘体相。加入最近邻排斥后，在强莫尔区域出现局域超固态（lSS）相，其核心特征包括：孤立莫尔超胞内的局域交错密度序与局域非对角长程序共存；全局非对角关联呈指数衰减；热力学极限下全局结构因子（structure factor）为零而局域结构因子非零。

Conclusion: 局域超固态相（lSS）通过与全局超固态（SS）的对比得到清晰区分——后者具有代数衰减关联和非零全局结构因子。本研究提供了莫尔晶格中局域量子相的完整微观图像，并为在超冷原子（ultracold atoms）实验中探测lSS态给出了明确的实验可观测信号。

Abstract: The search and characterization of supersolid phases remain a central topic in condensed matter physics. Inspired by the experimental discovery of local superfluid and insulating phases in two-dimensional moiré optical lattices [Meng et al., Nature 615, 231 (2023)], we systematically explore the emergence of a local supersolid ($l$SS) phase in a one-dimensional Bose-Hubbard model subjected to a moiré potential, using the density-matrix renormalization group method. We impose a maximum site occupation $n_{\rm max}=2$ to realize the soft-core boson constraint. In the absence of nearest-neighbor repulsion, we identify the conventional superfluid, local superfluid, Mott insulator, and moiré-induced insulator phases. When the nearest-neighbor repulsion is turned on, the $l$SS phase emerges in the strong-moiré regime. This phase is uniquely characterized by three key signatures: (i) coexisting local staggered density order and local off-diagonal coherence within isolated moiré supercells; (ii) exponentially decaying global off-diagonal correlations; and (iii) a vanishing global structure factor in the thermodynamic limit, while the local structure factor remains finite. These features clearly distinguish the $l$SS from the conventional global supersolid (SS) phase, which exhibits algebraic correlations and a finite global structure factor. Our results provide a complete microscopic picture of local quantum phases in moiré lattices and offer clear experimental observables for detecting $l$SS states with ultracold atoms.

</details>


### [211] [Floquet-tuned superfluid-checkerboard competition in dipolar bosons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10254)
*Jin Yang,Yaghmorassene Hebib,Chao Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过Floquet工程实现硬核偶极玻色子在方格上的各向异性跳跃，研究其半满填充下的相图，发现各向异性增强可降低棋盘序所需的相互作用强度，并在超流-棋盘边界附近观察到弱一级相变及有限尺寸效应；在掺杂体系中，识别出各向异性超流但密度模式各向同性的棋盘超固体（checkerboard-supersolid）相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用Floquet驱动（Floquet driving）沿一维方向工程化各向异性跳跃（anisotropic hopping），以研究强运动各向异性下长程偶极相互作用导致的量子多体相变，特别是密度有序（density ordering）与超流性（superfluidity）之间的竞争。

Method: 采用高频Floquet有效描述（high-frequency Floquet effective description）导出各向异性跳跃框架；使用无符号问题虫算法量子蒙特卡洛模拟（sign-problem-free worm-algorithm quantum Monte Carlo simulations），在垂直于平面的偶极极化条件下对半满填充进行相图扫描。

Result: 运动各向异性增强系统性降低了稳定棋盘序（checkerboard order）所需的相互作用强度；在超流-棋盘边界附近，有限尺寸数据表明刚度骤降与棋盘关联锐升同时发生，且随系统尺寸增大而显著尖锐化，符合弱一级相变（weakly first-order transition）特征；在掺杂区域发现狭窄的棋盘超固体（checkerboard-supersolid）相，其中超流刚度（superfluid stiffness）各向异性而密度模式（density pattern）各向同性。

Conclusion: Floquet诱导的横向运动抑制会增强密度有序；该机制可在掺杂体系中产生各向异性超流但密度模式各向同性的棋盘超固体相，为利用周期性驱动调控量子关联物质中的有序相提供了可行途径。

Abstract: We study hard-core dipolar bosons on a square lattice subject to a unidirectional periodic drive that Floquet-engineers anisotropic hopping. Driving along one lattice direction provides a controlled way to suppress transverse tunneling, yielding a kinetically quasi-one-dimensional regime with strongly anisotropic transport within the leading-order high-frequency Floquet effective description. In this limit, the system does not reduce to decoupled chains, due to the long-range in-plane dipolar interaction remains isotropic and couples different chains. Focusing on dipoles polarized perpendicular to the plane, for which the interaction is purely repulsive and isotropic, we use sign-problem-free worm-algorithm quantum Monte Carlo simulations to map the half-filling phase diagram versus kinetic anisotropy and dipolar coupling. We find that increasing kinetic anisotropy systematically lowers the interaction strength required to stabilize checkerboard order, demonstrating that Floquet-induced suppression of transverse motion enhances density ordering. Near the superfluid--checkerboard boundary, finite-size results reveal a narrow transition region where the stiffness drops rapidly while checkerboard correlations rise sharply; Its pronounced sharpening with system size is consistent with a weakly first-order transition rounded by finite-size effects. Away from half filling, on the doped sides of the checkerboard plateau, we identify a narrow checkerboard-supersolid regime with simultaneously finite checkerboard correlations and superfluid stiffness, where the superfluid stiffness is anisotropic but the density pattern is isotropic.

### [212] [Bose-Fermi Mapping in Hubbard Models at Imaginary Chemical Potential and Phase-Induced Fermionization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10418)
*Evangelos G. Filothodoros*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文发现有限温度下具有虚化学势的吸引性Fermi-Hubbard模型与排斥性Bose-Hubbard模型之间存在精确映射，通过大N展开证明配分函数通过虚化学势的π平移相关联，从而将BCS-BEC渡越映射为玻色子的费米子化（fermion-like occupation）行为。核心机制是热核（thermal kernel）的解析延拓，以及虚化学势作为统计调节器（statistical regulator）的热力学效应，提供了一种无需无限排斥或硬核约束的新型费米子化方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索吸引性Fermi-Hubbard模型与排斥性Bose-Hubbard模型在有限温度和虚化学势下的潜在映射关系，并研究这种映射如何导致玻色子系统产生类似费米子的行为，从而提供一种不同于Tonks-Girardeau极限的新型费米子化（fermionization）机制。

Method: 利用大N展开（large N-expansion）推导两个模型的配分函数关系，证明虚化学势的π平移映射条件；通过热核（thermal kernel）g(βE, φ)的解析延拓（analytic continuation）连接玻色子和费米子扇区；推导玻色模型的能隙方程（gap equation）和数方程（number equation），分析虚化学势的统计调节作用。

Result: 发现吸引性Fermi-Hubbard模型与排斥性Bose-Hubbard模型的配分函数通过θ→θ+π的平移相关联；该映射将BCS-BEC渡越转换为玻色子的费米子化行为；识别出费米子和玻色子各自对应的特殊角（φ值），标记了普适热学窗口（universal thermal window）的边界；论证了通过虚化学势诱导的热力学效应，可在有限相互作用强度下实现费米子化。

Conclusion: 虚化学势可以作为统计调节器（statistical regulator），通过扭转热相位（thermal phase）产生类费米子行为，无需硬核约束或无限排斥作用；该机制提供了一种理解相互作用晶格系统中渡越现象的统一框架，区别于Tonks-Girardeau极限、任意子（anyonic）或Floquet工程系统中的统计转变方式。

Abstract: We find a mapping between the attractive Fermi-Hubbard model and the repulsive Bose-Hubbard model at finite temperature and at imaginary chemical potential $μ=iθ$. We show, by using a large $N$-expansion, that the partition functions of the two models are related by a simple shift $θ\to θ+ π$. This condition maps the BCS--BEC crossover of attractive fermions to a Bose--Fermi crossover (fermion-like occupation) of repulsive bosons. Central feature of this correspondence plays the thermal kernel $g(βE,φ),$ whose analytic continuation $g_B(βE,φ) = g_F(βE,φ+π)$ governs the bosonic and fermionic sectors. Interestingly, we are able to find that the special angles $φ= 2π/3,4π/3$ for fermions correspond to $φ= π/3,5π/3$ for bosons, marking the boundaries of a universal thermal window. We further argue that the present mechanism shows that fermionization can occur at finite interaction strength through a thermodynamic effect induced by the imaginary chemical potential. This suggests that it is a new way of fermionization (not a change in statistics but a fermion-like behaviour) unlike the Tonks--Girardeau limit, where fermionization arises from an infinite repulsive interaction and anyonic or Floquet-engineered systems where transmutation emerges from modified statistics or dynamics. Essentially, the phase $φ$ is a statistical parameter; by twisting the thermal phase, it generates fermion-like behaviour without hard-core constraints or infinite repulsion but only by using thermodynamics. We derive the gap equation and number equation for the bosonic model, highlighting the role of the imaginary chemical potential as a statistical regulator. Our results provide a unified framework for understanding crossovers in interacting lattice systems.

### [213] [Influence of pump size on pattern formation in exciton-polaritonic Bose-Einstein condensates in the non-Markovian regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10472)
*N. V. Kuznetsova,A. D. Alliluev,D. V. Makarov,A. A. Anisich*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过引入赝微分色散项的非马尔可夫随机Gross-Pitaevskii方程，研究了非相干泵浦下激子极化激元凝聚体的动力学，发现泵浦区域增大可导致多种空间结构出现，其性质取决于动力学记忆时长；短记忆下可形成扩展态（extended state），长记忆下则出现角向凝聚体结构（angular condensate structures）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非相干泵浦下激子极化激元凝聚体（exciton-polaritonic condensate）的动力学行为，特别是泵浦区域大小和动力学记忆时长（dynamical memory）如何影响空间结构的形成与性质。

Method: 采用带有赝微分色散项（pseudo-differential dispersion term）的非马尔可夫随机Gross-Pitaevskii方程（non-Markovian stochastic Gross-Pitaevskii equation）进行建模，该色散项对应于极化激元的下分支能量（lower energy branch of polaritons）。

Result: 短记忆时间（short memory time）下，凝聚体可形成扩展至泵浦区域以外的扩展态（extended state），此现象源于色散项导致的“交通拥堵效应”（traffic jam effect）；长记忆时间（long memory time）下，泵浦区域增大会产生角向凝聚体结构，部分抑制物质波（matter waves）从泵浦区域的发射。

Conclusion: 泵浦区域面积和动力学记忆时长共同决定了激子极化激元凝聚体的空间结构形态，扩展态的形成与色散项的特殊形式密切相关。

Abstract: Dynamics of exciton-polaritonic condensate under incoherent pumping is studied using the non-Markovian stochastic Gross-Pitaevskii equation with the pseudo-differential dispersion term. This term corresponds to the lower energy branch of polaritons. It is shown that an increasing of the pumping spot area leads to the appearance of various spatial structures whose properties depend on the duration of the dynamical memory. In the regime of short memory time, condensate can form an extended state that spans outside the pumping area. We conclude that onset of such extended states is related to the specific form of the dispersion term causing the ``traffic jam'' effect. The case of long memory time corresponds to enhanced condensate formation, when increasing of the pumping area leads to appearance of angular condensate structures which partially suppress emission of matter waves from the pumping area.

### [214] [Structural transition and fragmentation of vortex lattices in rotating tilted dipolar Bose-Einstein condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10538)
*Mamta Ale,Harsimranjit Kaur,Kuldeep Suthar*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本研究通过扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程，研究了谐波约束下准二维倾斜旋转偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（dipolar Bose-Einstein condensates）中的涡旋晶格（vortex lattices），揭示了偶极子倾斜角度接近临界角时涡旋结构由正方形晶格向三角形晶格的转变，以及Lee-Huang-Yang修正（Lee-Huang-Yang correction）在超越平均场效应（beyond mean-field effects）中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究谐波约束下准二维倾斜旋转偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中涡旋晶格的结构转变，特别是偶极子倾斜角度对晶格类型的影响，以及超越平均场效应在其中的作用。

Method: 采用旋转凝聚体的扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程（extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation）进行数值分析，并引入Lee-Huang-Yang修正以纳入超越平均场效应。

Result: 偶极子倾斜接近临界角时，涡旋晶格从正方形转变为三角形；超过魔角（magic angle）后凝聚体沿对角线伸长并失去涡旋；加入LHY修正后可恢复涡旋形成；偶极子垂直于极化轴时，LHY修正导致强旋转下凝聚体碎裂；旋转频率的淬火动力学（quench dynamics）显示强旋转淬火后凝聚体无涡旋。

Conclusion: 数值分析强调了各向异性偶极玻色子的旋转特性中的超越平均场效应，这些效应可在当前偶极量子气体实验中得到观测。

Abstract: We investigate the vortex lattices of harmonically confined quasi-two-dimensional tilted rotational dipolar Bose-Einstein condensates. By employing an extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation for a rotating condensate, we reveal the structural transformation of vortices from square to triangular lattices as the tilt of dipolar bosons relative to the polarization axis approaches a critical angle. When the tilt of the magnetic dipoles surpasses the magic angle, the condensate elongates diagonally and becomes devoid of vortices. Moreover, we include the Lee-Huang-Yang correction, which enables the formation of vortices in the elongated condensate. Additionally, when dipoles are oriented perpendicular to the polarization axis, the Lee-Huang-Yang correction results in the fragmentation of condensates under strong rotation. The quench dynamics of the rotational frequency demonstrate the development of vortex lattices; however, with a strong rotational quench, the condensate remains free of vortices. Our numerical analysis highlights the beyond mean-field effects of the rotational properties of anisotropic dipolar bosons, which can be observed in current dipolar quantum gas experiments.

Method: 基于度量图（metric graph）上的拉普拉斯算子（Laplacian）构造连续哈密顿量族，通过改变图的拓扑结构来研究哈密顿量的性质变化。

Result: 证明存在一个由度量图构造的哈密顿量族，尽管其本征函数为实值，但仍能产生非平凡的几何贝里相位（Berry's phase）。

Abstract: Laplacians on metric graphs are used to construct continuous families of Hamiltonians with different topological structure. Connections between non-trivial Berry's phase and topology change are discussed.

### [216] [Impact of the non-canonical approach to the exact solution of the ideal one-dimensional electron gas confined with an anisotropic quantum wire of oscillator-shaped profile](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08986)

Method: 采用正则与两种框架求解位置依赖质量的薛定谔方程；在正则框架中得到用拉盖尔多项式（Laguerre polynomials）表达的定态波函数及离散能谱，在非正则框架中对角度部分使用盖根鲍尔多项式（Gegenbauer polynomials）求解奇偶态波函数，并研究了极限关系与特例。

Abstract: We study an exactly solvable model that can be interpreted as an ideal one-dimensional electron gas confined with an anisotropic quantum wire potential of oscillator-shaped profile. The homogeneous nature of the quantum wire is broken by the introduction of the effective electron mass, which changes with radial distance. We solve the problem described both within the canonical and the non-canonical approach. Analytical expressions of the wavefunctions of the stationary states for both cases in terms of the Laguerre polynomials are obtained, as well as the discrete energy spectrum related to these wavefunctions. Additionally, an exact solution to the angular position part of the position-dependent mass Schrödinger equation within the non-canonical approach leads to the angular-part wavefunctions of the even and odd states expressed through the Gegenbauer polynomials. Possible limit relations and special cases are studied too.

*Karol Sajnok,Fabio Costa*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在连续基（continuous basis）上建立了量子相干性（quantum coherence）的资源理论框架，重点聚焦位置表象（position representation）。通过引入基于随机动量敲击（random momentum kicks）的消相通道（dephasing channel），定义了非相干不动点与自由操作，并提出了两种相干度量——相对熵消相损失（relative-entropy dephasing loss）与希尔伯特-施密特消相损失（Hilbert-Schmidt dephasing loss），最后以引力势中的高斯波包（Gaussian wavepacket）为例进行了说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于位置本征态（position eigenstates）是不可归一化的广义本征态（non-normalizable generalized eigenstates），标准的有限维消相映射（finite-dimensional dephasing map）无法直接推广到正常态（normal states），因此需要为连续变量系统建立一套数学自洽且物理动机明确的相干性资源理论。

Method: 提出了一种基于随机动量敲击的消相通道，该通道等价于有限分辨率位置测量（finite-resolution position measurement）的无条件反作用（unconditional back-action），从而定义了非相干性的不动点概念以及一类消相协变自由操作（dephasing-covariant free operations）。基于该通道作用构建了两个量化指标：相对熵消相损失与希尔伯特-施密特消相损失。

Result: 对于物理上相关的核函数（kernels），不动点集合中不包含任何正常态，表明连续基相干性（continuous-basis coherence）与消相扰动（dephasing disturbance）相关，而非与距非空对角态集合的距离相关。相对熵消相损失在所考虑的自由操作下满足主要资源理论性质，而希尔伯特-施密特消相损失是凸的且实验上透明，但未能满足单调性（monotonicity）和强单调性（strong monotonicity）。还提出了用于认证相干性高于有限值的阈值见证（threshold witnesses），并在双路径设置中将其与干涉可见度（interference visibility）联系起来。

Conclusion: 本文所发展的理论为连续变量系统（continuous-variable systems）中的量子相干性提供了一种数学一致且物理动机明确的处理方式。

Abstract: We develop a resource-theoretic framework for quantum coherence directly in continuous basis, with emphasis on the position representation. Since position eigenstates are non-normalizable generalized eigenstates, the standard finite-dimensional dephasing map cannot be transferred directly to normal states. We therefore introduce a physically motivated dephasing channel based on random momentum kicks, equivalently described as the unconditional back-action of a finite-resolution position measurement. This yields a fixed-point notion of incoherence and a natural class of dephasing-covariant free operations. For physically relevant kernels, however, the fixed-point set contains no normal states, showing that continuous-basis coherence is tied to dephasing disturbance rather than to distance from a nonempty set of diagonal states. We study two quantifiers built from the channel action: a relative-entropy dephasing loss and a Hilbert-Schmidt dephasing loss. The former satisfies the main resource-theoretic properties under the free operations considered, while the latter is convex and experimentally transparent but fails monotonicity and strong monotonicity. We also formulate threshold witnesses for certifying coherence above a finite value and connect them, in a two-path setting, with interference visibility. Finally, we illustrate the framework with a Gaussian wavepacket evolving in a gravitational potential. The resulting theory provides a mathematically consistent and physically motivated treatment of coherence in continuous-variable systems.

</details>


### [218] [Generalized Catability of Relativistic Quantum States Measurement in a Unified Lie-Algebraic Foldy-Wouthuysen (FW) Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08248)
*Abdelmalek Bouzenada*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个统一的李代数（Lie-algebraic）形式化框架，用于描述相对论性量子系统中任意自旋粒子的“catability”（可猫性，即叠加相干态的度量），并推广了Foldy-Wouthuysen变换以分离正负能分量，最终通过自旋-1/2费米子等实例验证了该框架的统一几何与代数处理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在相对论性量子力学框架下，现有的相干态（coherent state）度量方法缺乏统一的代数处理，无法系统描述任意自旋粒子的叠加相干性（superposition coherence）和量子干涉（quantum interference）特性。本文旨在通过李代数方法建立catability的定量度量，并将这一概念推广至相对论性系统。

Method: 首先将catability定义为叠加相干态的定量度量，并利用代数表示（algebraic representations）分析相干结构和量子干涉性质。随后在李代数框架下推导广义Foldy-Wouthuysen变换，实现相对论哈密顿量（relativistic Hamiltonian）的块对角化（block-diagonalization）与正负能量分离。引入相位敏感的catability算符（phase-sensitive catability operator），研究相对论量子动力学中的相位关联与相干效应。最后将该形式化推广至任意自旋-s场的统一几何与李代数处理。

Result: 该形式化成功应用于狄拉克自旋-1/2粒子（Dirac spin-$1/2$ particles），揭示了相对论性费米子catability与旋量结构（spinorial structures）及对称性生成元（symmetry generators）之间的关系。对于任意自旋-s场，同一代数结构框架能够支持更高自旋相对论量子态的研究。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个广义的理论平台，用于研究相对论性量子相干（relativistic quantum coherence）、叠加效应以及费米子（fermionic）和玻色子（bosonic）系统中的代数对称性（algebraic symmetries）。

Abstract: In this work, a unified Lie-algebraic formulation of catability is constructed for relativistic quantum systems with arbitrary spin within this framework. In this case, the analysis starts with constructing catability as a quantitative measure for superposed coherent states, where coherence structure and quantum interference properties are studied using algebraic representations in this framework. Also, a generalized Foldy-Wouthuysen transformation is formulated within a Lie algebraic framework, delivering a systematic procedure for block-diagonalization of relativistic Hamiltonians and separation of positive- and negative-energy components in this framework. Within this formalism, a phase-sensitive catability operator is introduced to study phase correlations and coherence effects in the relativistic quantum dynamics framework. The approach is applied to Dirac spin-$1/2$ particles, where relativistic fermionic catability is analyzed in relation to spinorial structures and symmetry generators framework. The formalism is extended through a unified geometric and Lie-algebraic treatment, establishing a consistent description of catability in a relativistic quantum mechanics framework. In this context, the generalized framework is constructed for arbitrary spin-$s$ fields, enabling investigation of higher-spin relativistic quantum states within the same algebraic structure framework. In this context, the obtained results show a generalized theoretical platform for investigating relativistic quantum coherence, superposition effects, and algebraic symmetries in the framework of fermionic and bosonic systems.

### [219] [Higher-order quantum processes respecting closed labs in a spacetime have quantum controlled causal order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08351)
*Matthias Salzger,V. Vilasini*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过基于相对论因果性（relativistic causality）原则的自上而下方法，证明在经典时空中满足闭合实验室假设的协议行为等价于具有因果序量子控制（QC-QC）的量子电路，从而明确了高阶量子过程（higher-order quantum processes）中可物理实现的精确类别，排除了更一般的非因果过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子因果性与量子信息领域中存在大量抽象量子协议，允许操作之间具有循环或非无环（non-acyclic）的因果结构，包括不定因果序（indefinite causal order）和过程矩阵（process matrices）等框架。一个长期悬而未决的问题是：哪一类抽象过程可以在不依赖后选择（post-selection）的情况下获得物理实现？本文旨在为该问题提供严格解答。

Method: 基于因果盒（causal boxes）框架——该框架刻画了与固定背景时空兼容的最一般量子信息处理协议——本文形式化了“作用一次+局域序”（Acting Once + Local Order）的额外约束，这些约束在精细时空尺度上捕捉了过程矩阵框架中的闭合实验室假设。随后证明，在经典无环时空中满足这些条件的任何协议，行为上等价于一个具有因果序量子控制（QC-QC）的量子电路。

Result: 证明了QC-QC恰好构成可在经典时空中物理实现的高阶量子过程类别（包括具有不定序的过程），在闭合实验室假设下排除了更一般的非因果过程。还开发了过程盒协议的表征技术，引出了关于时空量子协议与相对论量子实验的新因果性开放问题。

Conclusion: 该工作明确了抽象高阶过程矩阵框架与实验可及量子协议之间的关系，阐明了粗粒化循环因果结构与精细无环操作因果结构之间的相互作用。

Abstract: In quantum causality and quantum information, there is a vast landscape of abstract quantum protocols permitting cyclic or non-acyclic causal structures between operations, including frameworks for indefinite causal order and higher-order quantum processes such as process matrices. A longstanding open question is what is the largest class of abstract processes that admit physical realisations without post-selection. In this work, we provide a rigorous answer using a top-down approach grounded in relativistic causality principles. Building on the framework of causal boxes, which characterise the most general quantum information-processing protocols compatible with fixed background spacetimes, we formalise additional constraints (Acting Once + Local Order) capturing the closed-laboratory assumptions of the process matrix framework at a fine-grained spacetime level. We prove that any protocol in a classical acyclic spacetime satisfying these conditions is behaviourally equivalent to a quantum circuit with quantum control of causal order (QC-QC), providing a top-down derivation of QC-QCs from physical principles. Our results show that QC-QCs constitute precisely the class of higher-order quantum processes, including those with indefinite order, that can be physically realised within classical spacetime, ruling out more general non-causal processes under the closed-labs assumption. This clarifies the relationship between abstract higher-order process matrix frameworks and experimentally accessible quantum protocols, as well as the interplay between coarse-grained cyclic and fine-grained acyclic operational causal structures. We also develop characterisation techniques for process box protocols that lead to new causality-based open questions concerning spacetime quantum protocols and relativistic quantum experiments.

### [220] [On the KAK Decomposition and Equivalence Classes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10783)
*Dawei Ding,Yu Liu,Zi-Wen Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文为KAK分解建立了严格的数学理论基础，澄清了Cartan分解的定义歧义，并区分了双陪集等价（double coset equivalence）与投影等价（projective equivalence）两种不同的等价类概念，纠正了现有文献中关于SU(4)的Weyl chamber（Weyl chamber）表示的误判。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管KAK分解在Lie理论（Lie theory）和量子计算（quantum computing）中被广泛使用，其数学基础仍不完整，尤其缺乏对分解精确条件和乘法等价类刻画（characterization of equivalence classes）的系统研究。

Method: 针对连通紧半单Lie群（connected compact semisimple Lie groups）建立KAK分解的数学理论，厘清文献中Cartan分解（Cartan decomposition）的多种定义，并给出一般性KAK分解定理的完整证明；在此基础上，分别定义双陪集等价与投影等价，发展系统化的等价类确定与唯一性判定理论。

Result: 对于SU(4)，证明了在SU(2)⊗SU(2)乘法下的局域等价类（local equivalence classes）并非如现有文献所声称的那样由通常的Weyl chamber几何表示；只有忽略全局相位（global phases）的投影局域等价（projective-local equivalence）才能恢复Weyl chamber表示。

Conclusion: 该工作为量子门（quantum gates）与量子电路（quantum circuits）理论建立了严格的Lie理论基础，解决了KAK分类中长期存在的数学不一致问题。

Abstract: The KAK decomposition is a fundamental tool in Lie theory and quantum computing. Despite its widespread use, the mathematical foundations remain incomplete, particularly regarding the precise conditions for the decomposition and the characterization of equivalence classes under multiplication by elements of $K$. Here, we present a mathematical theory of the KAK decomposition for connected compact semisimple Lie groups and derive the decomposition for $\mathrm{SU}(4)$. In particular, we clarify the relationship between various definitions of a Cartan decomposition in the literature and give a complete proof of a general KAK decomposition theorem. We then distinguish two distinct notions of KAK equivalence classes, double coset equivalence and projective equivalence, thereby addressing mathematical inconsistencies regarding KAK classification in the literature. Specifically, for $\mathrm{SU}(4)$, we show that local equivalence classes under multiplication by $\mathrm{SU}(2)\otimes \mathrm{SU}(2)$ are geometrically represented not by the usual "Weyl chamber" as claimed in the existing literature. Instead, the "Weyl chamber" is only recovered by the projective-local equivalence which disregards global phases. We develop a systematic theory for determining equivalence and uniqueness for both notions of equivalence. Our work establishes a rigorous Lie-theoretic foundation for the theory of quantum gates and circuits.

Method: 通过切断键，定义一组态（set of states），利用这些态的度量张量的零模来识别线性相关并截断键维度；若无精确零模，则优化少量最低模的线性组合以近似零模；整个截断过程不需要预先进行规范固定。

Result: 该方法在二维有限温度Z₂格点规范理论中应用，其热态纯化由无限投影纠缠对态表示，验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 局部键优化能够更有效地利用环状张量网络中的局部关联信息进行压缩，且无需规范固定，适用于有限温度格点规范理论的张量网络模拟。

Abstract: Loopy tensor networks exhibit internal correlations that often render their compression inefficient. We show that even local bond optimization can more effectively exploit locally available information about relevant loop correlations. By cutting a bond, we define a set of states whose linear dependence can be identified through a zero mode of the states' metric tensor and used to truncate the bond dimension. In the absence of an exact zero mode, a linear combination of a small number of the lowest modes can instead be optimized to provide the optimal approximation to a zero mode. The truncation does not require prior gauge fixing. The method is applied to the two-dimensional finite-temperature $Z_2$ lattice gauge theory, whose thermal-state purification is represented by an infinite projected entangled-pair state (iPEPS).

</details>

The implementation of the measurement protocol achieves rotation-detection sensitivity beyond the Heisenberg limit. ### [227] [Clifford Ergotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09878)
*Somnath Maity,Ryusuke Hamazaki*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过引入“克利福德可提取功（Clifford ergotropy）”概念，研究封闭量子动力学中热力学与魔法资源（magic resources）之间的相互作用。论文给出了克利福德可提取功的通用上界，该上界随由无限阶滤波稳定子Rényi熵（infinite-order filtered stabilizer Rényi entropy）量化的魔法资源增加而降低，并在一量子比特和两量子比特系统中验证了该上界的有效性。研究还表明，该分析对多体系统具有非平凡推论，包括典型量子态在克利福德操作下的一种热力学第二定律形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于探索封闭量子动力学中热力学（thermodynamics）与魔法资源（magic resources）之间的交互关系，特别是在受限操作（克利福德操作）下可提取功的行为如何受到量子非稳定性（magic）的影响。

Method: 方法上，论文引入克利福德可提取功（Clifford ergotropy）作为在克利福德操作（Clifford operations）限制下可提取能量（extractable energy）的量度，并利用无限阶滤波稳定子Rényi熵（infinite-order filtered stabilizer Rényi entropy）量化魔法资源，从而推导出克利福德可提取功的通用上界（universal upper bounds）。

Result: 结果表明：(1) 克利福德可提取功存在通用上界，且该上界随魔法资源的增加而降低；(2) 在一量子比特和两量子比特系统中验证了该上界的有效性，其中两量子比特系统呈现出克利福德可提取功控制景观（control landscape）的显著转变；(3) 该分析对多体系统（many-body systems）具有非平凡后果，包括典型量子态（typical quantum states）在克利福德操作下的一种热力学第二定律形式。

Conclusion: 结论是，克利福德可提取功揭示了热力学与魔法资源之间的内在关联，并建立了魔法资源在限制性操作下对能量提取过程的约束，甚至推广至多体量子系统，提供了一种类似热力学第二定律（second law of thermodynamics）的形式。

Abstract: We discuss the interplay between thermodynamics and magic resources in closed quantum dynamics by introducing Clifford ergotropy, the amount of extractable energy under the restriction to Clifford operations. We provide universal upper bounds on Clifford ergotropy, which decrease with increasing magic as quantified by the infinite-order filtered stabilizer Rényi entropy. We demonstrate the utility of this bound for one- and two-qubit systems, with the latter exhibiting a notable transition in the control landscape of Clifford ergotropy. Finally, we show that our analysis has nontrivial consequences even for many-body systems, including a form of the second law of thermodynamics under Clifford operations for typical quantum states.

### [228] [A Single-Molecule Spin-Photon Interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10077)
*Simon Roggors,Thomas Unden,Anna Aubele,Paul Mentzel,Gregor Bayer,Alon Salhov,Jochen Scharpf,Martin B. Plenio,Alex Retzker,Fedor Jelezko,Tim R. Eichhorn,Tobias A. Schaub,Matthias Pfender,Philipp Neumann,Ilai Schwartz*

Result: 该系统展现出窄零声子线、超过一小时的光谱稳定性、自旋选择性光学跃迁以及单分子ODMR。在4.5 K温度下，通过相干控制实现了毫秒量级的动力学退耦相干时间和数十毫秒的自旋弛豫时间。

Abstract: Optical interfaces that connect long-lived spin qubits to photons are a central requirement for quantum networking and distributed quantum information processing. Currently, solid-state atomic defects are leading candidates due to their inherent spin and optical coherence. Building on these advancements, synthetically tailored molecular systems represent a fundamental change in the field, utilizing precise atomic control and consistent bottom-up assembly. However, the lack of a robust spin-photon interface combining bright fluorescence, high spectral stability, and the persistent spin lifetimes inherent to ground-state systems has prohibited the detection of individual molecular qubits. Here we show that a triplet ground state carbene molecule, embedded within a structurally matched host crystal, functions as a robust spin-photon interface with single-molecule addressability. The system exhibits narrow zero-phonon lines, spectral stability over more than an hour, spin-selective optical transitions and single-molecule optically detected magnetic resonance. Coherent control yields millisecond-scale dynamical-decoupling coherence and tens-of-milliseconds spin relaxation at a temperature of 4.5 K. These results establish molecular qubits as a viable platform for single-emitter quantum optics while preserving the advantages of bottom-up chemical design and processable materials.

### [229] [Symmetry-Enforced Non-Hermitian Jarzynski Equality in an SU(2)-Rotated Family of Hybrid $\mathcal{PT}$--$\mathcal{APT}$ Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10099)
*Zongru Yang,Teng Liu,Xiaodong Tan,Feng Zhu,Le Luo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在非厄米（non-Hermitian）动力学框架下，证明当跃迁概率满足宇称交换对称性（parity-exchange symmetry）时，后选择无量子跃迁（postselected no-quantum-jump）条件下的Jarzynski等式仍然成立；通过构造包含PT对称（parity-time symmetric）与APT对称（anti-parity-time symmetric）项的混合哈密顿量族，将对称性判据从PT端点推广至更宽的混合族，并在单个囚禁$^{171}\mathrm{Yb}^+$离子实验中对三个代表点进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Jarzynski等式是非平衡热力学（nonequilibrium thermodynamics）的核心结果，已在经典与量子厄米（Hermitian）系统中得到广泛验证，但其在非厄米动力学（non-Hermitian dynamics）中的适用性仍存在争议。本文旨在探索非厄米条件下Jarzynski等式的成立条件，并扩展其适用范围。

Method: 研究采用后选择无量子跃迁框架，构造了一族由PT对称与APT对称项线性组合而成的两能级混合哈密顿量（hybrid Hamiltonian），并运用互补的几何与代数论证，证明宇称交换对称性在整个SU(2)旋转轨道（$\mathrm{SU}(2)$-rotated orbit）上得以保持。实验上，在单个囚禁$^{171}\mathrm{Yb}^+$离子中实现了三个代表点（$θ_k = 0, π/4, π/2$），在循环协议下测量了$\Delta F = 0$时的功分布（work distributions）。

Result: 实验测量结果确认了在这三个代表点处，预测的对称性判据（symmetry criterion）成立，从而验证了条件性非厄米Jarzynski等式（conditional non-Hermitian Jarzynski equality）的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文在受限的两能级系统中，建立了非厄米条件下Jarzynski关系的对称性基础扩展，将之前局限于PT对称端点的条件性Jarzynski等式推广至更广泛的PT–APT混合族。

Abstract: The Jarzynski equality is a cornerstone of nonequilibrium thermodynamics, linking work statistics to equilibrium free-energy differences. Although it has been extensively verified in classical and quantum Hermitian settings, its status in non-Hermitian dynamics remains under debate. Here we show that, in a postselected no-quantum-jump framework, a conditional non-Hermitian Jarzynski equality holds when the transition probabilities obey a parity-exchange symmetry. We study a constructed family of two-level hybrid Hamiltonians formed as linear combinations of parity-time ($\mathcal{PT}$) and anti-parity-time ($\mathcal{APT}$) symmetric terms, and demonstrate using complementary geometric and algebraic arguments that the parity-exchange symmetry persists throughout the corresponding $\mathrm{SU}(2)$-rotated orbit. Relative to previous $\mathcal{PT}$-focused conditional Jarzynski equality results, the advance here is an extension of the symmetry criterion from the isolated $\mathcal{PT}$ endpoint to a broader $\mathcal{PT}$--$\mathcal{APT}$ hybrid family. Experimentally, we implement three representative points, $θ_k = 0, π/4, π/2$, in a single trapped $^{171}\mathrm{Yb}^+$ ion and measure the resulting work distributions under cyclic protocols with $ΔF = 0$, confirming the predicted symmetry criterion at those points. Our results establish a symmetry-based extension of the conditional non-Hermitian Jarzynski relation within this restricted two-level setting.

Here, we report a quantum reservoir processing device capable of performing both quantum and classical machine learning tasks. The implementation is realized with a programmable silicon chip excited with single photons, a highly scalable and adaptable photonics technology. We successfully implement a variety of quantum tasks, including quantum state tomography and measurement of entanglement via negativity. ### [232] [No measurement induced phase transition in the entanglement dynamics of monitored non-interacting one-dimensional fermions in a disordered or quasiperiodic potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10758)
*Can Yin,Fan Bo,Antonio M. García-García*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模数值模拟（系统尺寸L≤18000）和解析分析（映射到非线性sigma模型），证明具有U(1)对称性的一维非相互作用费米子，在准周期或无序势阱中，当占据数被零差或量子跳跃协议监测时，纠缠熵始终处于面积律相位，因此不存在测量诱导的相变（MIPT）。先前报道的MIPT源于有限尺寸效应（L~500与关联长度相当）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究声称在受监测的一维非相互作用费米子系统中存在测量诱导相变（MIPT），但该结论可能受限于较小的系统尺寸（L~500）。本文旨在通过更大规模的数值计算和解析理论，检验MIPT是否真实存在，并澄清有限尺寸效应的影响。

Method: 采用GPU加速进行大规模数值模拟，将系统尺寸扩展至L≤18000；进行细致的有限尺寸标度分析（finite size scaling analysis）。对于无序情形，将问题映射到带有附加质量项的非线性sigma模型（nonlinear sigma model, NLSM）进行解析计算。

Result: 临界监测强度一致为零，因此不存在MIPT；数值结果与NLSM解析分析完全一致。在无序情形下，弱无序极限中的关联长度比干净极限更长，且随无序强度增加而增大，该特征与NLSM中不同的对称性部分相关。

Conclusion: 受监测的一维非相互作用费米子系统（无论准周期还是无序势）始终处于面积律相位，不存在测量诱导的相变。之前的MIPT观测是有限尺寸效应造成的伪象。

Abstract: We show that the entanglement entropy (EE) of one-dimensional (1d) non-interacting fermions with $U(1)$ symmetry in the presence of a quasi-periodic or disordered potential in which the occupation number is being monitored by homodyne or quantum jump protocols is always in an area-law phase so no measurement induced phase transition (MIPT) occurs. The reason for the previously claimed MIPT in these systems was a finite size effect related to the fact that the maximum lattice size $L \sim 500$ was of the order of the correlation length. By increasing the system size up to $L \leq 18000$, employing Graphics Processing Unit (GPU), and performing a careful finite size scaling analysis, we find that the critical monitoring strength is consistent with zero so no MIPT occurs. For the disordered case, these numerical results are fully supported by an analytical calculation based on mapping the problem onto a nonlinear sigma model (NLSM) with an additional mass-like term that confirms the absence of the MIPT for any monitoring or disorder strength. Another salient feature of the disordered case, in part related to a different symmetry in the NLSM, is that the correlation length in the weak disorder limit is longer than in the clean limit and increases with the disordered strength.

### [233] [Emergence of synthetic twist defects in the surface code under local perturbation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10839)
*Paul Kairys,Phillip C. Lotshaw*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文对合成缺陷（synthetic defects）在拓扑有序量子系统中的能谱性质进行了系统研究，通过自旋（spin）和Majorana语言两种表示简化问题，并利用数值计算揭示了驱动合成缺陷涌现的量子相变（quantum phase transition）位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作提出了通过在拓扑有序量子基底（quantum substrate）上施加局域微扰来创建和操控合成缺陷的方案（You et al., 2013），但该提案中的关键要素从未被系统研究。理解有限尺寸和有限微扰系统中的能谱（energy spectrum）对于实验实现至关重要。

Method: 本文构建了合成缺陷的两种替代表示：在自旋语言中描述了约束并简化问题的涌现虚拟对称性（emergent virtual symmetries），在Majorana语言中揭示了与Kitaev的Majorana链（Majorana chain）的直接联系。利用这些简化进行了数值计算。

Result: 数值计算结果指示了驱动合成缺陷涌现的量子相变位置。

Conclusion: 本文是系统理解合成缺陷能谱性质的重要一步，作者在文末讨论了未来需要进一步开展的关键工作，以便更清晰、更完整地研究该现象。

Abstract: Topologically-ordered quantum states with Abelian excitations can host defects that obey effective non-Abelian statistics, in principle allowing for quantum information processing via defect braiding. These extrinsic defects (or twists) are typically studied as static features of the lattice. However, an alternative proposal considers how an underlying topologically ordered quantum substrate can be locally perturbed to create and manipulate synthetic defects \cite{you_synthetic_2013}. Unfortunately, while largely referenced, elements of this proposal were never systematically studied. Understanding the energy spectrum is particularly important in finite size and finitely perturbed systems, which are crucial for experimental realizations. In this work we announce a significant step in this direction by explicitly constructing, simplifying, and numerically studying the spectral properties of synthetic defects in a model system. First, we introduce two alternative representations of this problem in both spin and Majorana languages. In the former we describe emergent virtual symmetries which constrain and simplify the problem and in the latter we show a direct connection to Kitaev's well-known Majorana chain. We utilize these simplifications to perform numerical calculations to indicate the location of the quantum phase transition driving the emergence of the synthetic defects. We conclude by discussing key steps for future work to more clearly and completely study this phenomena.

</details>


### [234] [Crystallographic Symmetry Generates Phononic Holonomic Gates with Biased-Erasure Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10932)
*El Mustapha Mansouri,Keigo Arai*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用晶体学对称性（crystallographic symmetry）在应变活性Λ能级体系中构建固态量子处理器的控制层，通过对称性约束的应变相互作用实现无局部微波近场的声子Λ支路控制（phononic Lambda-leg control），并基于该流形构建超绝热回波-lune holonomic量子门。旋转框架模拟显示氮空位中心（nitrogen-vacancy center）条件平均保真度达99.88%（1.833微秒），偏置擦除模型（biased-erasure model）在XZZX码容量模拟中相比非结构化Rabi基线减少64%的数据量子比特需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态量子处理器需要控制层（control layer），其误差必须对量子纠错解码器（quantum-error-correction decoders）可读。现有方法依赖局部微波近场，在复杂控制和高保真度之间面临挑战。

Method: 通过要求投影应变张量（projected strain tensor）与Λ跃迁算子共享具有多重性一的二维不可约表示（multiplicity-one two-dimensional irreducible representation），对称性将线性应变相互作用固定为标量点积。两相位锁定机械模式合成圆形应变场，实现无需局部微波近场的复杂声子Λ支路控制。在此基础上构建超绝热回波-lune holonomic量子门，并采用共振双量子反绝热音调（resonant double-quantum counterdiabatic tone）。通过高次泛音体声波谐振器（high-overtone bulk acoustic resonator）分析将哈密顿量转化为Rabi速率、线宽和包络跟踪要求。

Result: 氮空位中心旋转框架模拟给出99.88%条件平均保真度（1.833微秒），计入泄漏后为99.40%。提取的信道具有0.47%擦除概率（erasure probability）和0.168%残余Z误差。在XZZX码容量模拟中，该偏置擦除模型相比非结构化Rabi基线名义上减少64%的数据量子比特。重复轮次探测器模型诊断（repeated-round detector-model diagnostics）保持名义距离-9代理，并识别出遗漏擦除、横向基底、泄漏/标志时序及强串扰作为验证极限。

Conclusion: 晶体学对称性是协同设计声子驱动（phononic actuation）、泄漏、噪声偏置（noise bias）和量子解码（quantum decoding）的核心原则。该方案可扩展到轨道Λ系统和亮投影声子总线诊断，为固态量子处理器控制层与量子纠错的协同设计提供新框架。

Abstract: Solid-state processors require control layers whose errors are legible to quantum-error-correction decoders. We show that crystallographic symmetry can provide such a layer in strain-active Lambda manifolds. When the projected strain tensor and Lambda-transition operators share a multiplicity-one two-dimensional irreducible representation, symmetry fixes the linear strain interaction to a scalar dot product. Two phase-locked mechanical modes synthesize a circular strain field, enabling complex phononic Lambda-leg control without local microwave near fields. On this manifold we construct a superadiabatic echo-lune holonomic gate using Lambda-leg control and a resonant double-quantum counterdiabatic tone. Rotating-frame simulations of a nitrogen-vacancy center give 99.88% conditional average fidelity in 1.833 microseconds, or 99.40% when leakage is counted as error. A resonant gigahertz high-overtone bulk acoustic resonator analysis translates the Hamiltonian into Rabi-rate, linewidth, and envelope-tracking requirements. The bright-state structure organizes noise: A2-sector perturbations are parity-filtered into an optically distinguishable auxiliary state, whereas transverse E-sector faults are echo suppressed and retained as a decoder stress axis. The extracted channel has 0.47% erasure probability and 0.168% residual Z error. In XZZX code-capacity simulations, this biased-erasure model yields a nominal 64% fit-extrapolated data-qubit reduction relative to an unstructured Rabi baseline. Repeated-round detector-model diagnostics preserve the nominal distance-9 proxy and identify missed erasures, transverse floors, leakage/flag timing, and strong crosstalk as validation limits. Extensions to orbital Lambda systems and bright-projector phonon-bus diagnostics identify crystallographic symmetry as a principle for co-designing phononic actuation, leakage, noise bias, and quantum decoding.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [235] [A study of multicavity concept applied to hexagonal coaxial haloscopes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08932)
*J. M. García-Barceló,Jose R. Navarro-Madrid,Alejandro Díaz-Morcillo*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于六边形同轴几何结构的可扩展多腔体轴子探测器架构，工作频率为30 GHz。通过从单腔体设计向双腔体和三腔体构型的过渡，以及基于内六角棱镜旋转的新型调谐机制，三腔体设计相比单腔体基线实现了3倍的性能提升。进一步探索了在25 mm径向限制下的四腔体缩放潜力，并讨论了高次系统中的模式分裂、制造公差和热管理等实际挑战。该单端口多腔体方法为增加探测器灵敏体积、在射频频段高效探索轴子暗物质参数空间提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实验磁体孔径（magnet bores）有限体积的约束下，传统单腔体轴子探测器（axion haloscope）的扫描速率（scanning rate）和灵敏度（sensitivity）不足。本文旨在通过发展可扩展的多腔体架构，在有限空间内有效增加灵敏体积，从而提升高射频段轴子暗物质的探测效率。

Method: 采用六边形同轴几何结构（hexagonal coaxial geometry）设计工作于30 GHz的多腔体架构。从单腔体基线出发，逐步过渡到双腔体和三腔体构型；引入基于一个或两个内六角棱镜（inner hexagonal prism）旋转的新型调谐机制（tuning mechanism），以稳定地移动谐振频率并保持高形式因子（form factor）和品质因子（quality factor）。同时，在25 mm严格径向约束下研究四腔体架构的缩放可行性，并通过理论分析优化壁厚以保证频率稳定性。

Result: 三腔体设计（triple-subcavity design）相比单腔体基线实现了3倍（$\times3$）的性能提升。理论分析表明，在一定径向间隙（radial clearance）内，通过战略性地优化壁厚（wall thicknesses），四腔体系统在技术上是可行的。

Conclusion: 单端口多腔体方法（one-port multicavity approach）为增加轴子探测器的灵敏体积（sensitive volume）提供了可行路径，能够更高效地在高射频段探索轴子暗物质参数空间（axion dark matter parameter space）。

Abstract: In this work, a study on the development of scalable multicavity architectures for axion haloscopes, based on a hexagonal coaxial geometry operating at $30$ GHz frequencies, is presented. To enhance the scanning rate and sensitivity within the limited volume of experimental magnet bores, the transition from a baseline single-cavity design to dual and triple-subcavity configurations is investigated. A novel tuning mechanism based on the rotation of one or two inner hexagonal prisms is implemented, providing a robust method to shift the resonant frequency while maintaining high form and quality factors. The results show that the triple-subcavity design achieves an improvement of $\times3$ over the single-cavity baseline. The scaling potential of quad-subcavity architectures under a strict radial constraint of $25$ mm is further explored. Theoretical analysis confirms that a four-subcavity system is feasible within a certain radial clearance, provided that wall thicknesses are strategically optimised to ensure frequency stability. The practical challenges associated with mode splitting, manufacturing tolerances, and thermal management in these high-order systems are also discussed. This one-port multicavity approach offers a viable path toward increasing the sensitive volume of haloscopes, enabling more efficient exploration of the axion dark matter parameter space in high-frequency regimes.

</details>

TL;DR: 利用BESIII探测器在质心能量4.128–4.226 GeV范围内收集的7.33 fb⁻¹积分亮度的正负电子对撞数据，首次观测到粲奇异介子Dₛ⁺的两个强子衰变过程：Dₛ⁺→Kₛ⁰Kₛ⁰π⁺π⁰和Dₛ⁺→Kₛ⁰K⁺π⁰π⁰，并测定了它们的衰变分支比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究粲介子（charm meson）的强子衰变（hadronic decay）是检验量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）非微扰效应和探索粲夸克（charm quark）衰变机制的重要途径，而Dₛ⁺介子的多体强子衰变目前实验信息仍十分有限。

Method: 基于BESIII探测器采集的质心能量4.128–4.226 GeV范围内的e⁺e⁻对撞数据，总积分亮度为7.33 fb⁻¹。通过分析末态粒子组合，重建候选事件并扣除本底，采用最大似然拟合提取信号产额。

Result: 首次观测到Dₛ⁺→Kₛ⁰Kₛ⁰π⁺π⁰和Dₛ⁺→Kₛ⁰K⁺π⁰π⁰两个衰变过程；测得分支比分别为(4.08±0.46_stat±0.45_syst)×10⁻³和(3.32±0.64_stat±0.31_syst)×10⁻³。

Conclusion: 该工作首次报道了这两个Dₛ⁺强子衰变过程的分支比测量结果，为理解粲奇异介子的衰变机制和检验理论模型提供了新的实验依据。

Abstract: By analyzing $e^+e^-$ collision data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 7.33~fb$^{-1}$ collected with the BESIII detector at center-of-mass energies ranging from 4.128 to 4.226~GeV, we report the observations of the hadronic decays $D^+_s\to K^0_SK^0_Sπ^+π^0$ and $D^+_s\to K^0_S K^+π^0π^0$. Their decay branching fractions are determined to be ${\mathcal B}(D^+_s\to K^0_SK^0_S π^+π^0)=(4.08\pm0.46_{\rm stat}\pm0.45_{\rm syst})\times 10^{-3}$ and ${\mathcal B}(D^+_s\to K^0_S K^+π^0π^0)=(3.32\pm0.64_{\rm stat}\pm0.31_{\rm syst})\times 10^{-3}$, where the first uncertainties are statistical and the second are systematic.

### [237] [Search for invisible decays of light mesons via $J/ψ\to VP$ $(V=ω/φ,P=η/η')$ decays at STCF](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10023)
*Zhibo Tao,Yihang Xia,Vindhyawasini Prasad,Xu Gao,Weimin Song*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究基于STCF预期每年积累的3.4×10¹² J/ψ事例，利用传统分析方法对轻介子不可见衰变进行了可行性研究，设定了ω、φ、η、η'不可见衰变分支比在90%置信水平的上限，并指出深度学习技术可进一步将这些上限提升至接近轻暗物质的理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索轻介子不可见衰变（invisible decay）是搜寻轻暗物质（light dark matter）的重要途径，但目前缺乏在STCF能区的高精度可行性研究。

Method: 采用传统解析方法，基于1.3×10⁹ J/ψ事例的包含性蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）样本，通过J/ψ→VP（V=ω/φ, P=η/η'）过程产生信号，并利用投影玩具数据（toy data）模拟STCF的预期统计量（3.4×10¹² J/ψ事例/年），在90%置信水平（confidence level, C.L.）设定分支比上限。

Result: 在90%置信水平下，设定了四种介子不可见衰变分支比的上限：ℬ(ω→invisible) < 3.7×10⁻⁷，ℬ(φ→invisible) < 8.9×10⁻⁷，ℬ(η→invisible) < 1.8×10⁻⁷，ℬ(η'→invisible) < 4.1×10⁻⁷。

Conclusion: 传统解析方法已能在STCF上给出有竞争力的轻介子不可见衰变上限；若引入深度学习（Deep Learning）等机器学习技术，上限可进一步改善，接近轻暗物质的理论预测。

Abstract: We present a preliminary feasibility study of searches for invisible decays of light mesons via $J/ψ\to VP$ $(V=ω/φ,P=η/η')$ using a traditional analytical method at the proposed Super $τ$-Charm facility (STCF) which is expected to accumulate $3.4\times10^{12}$ $J/ψ$ events per year, based on an inclusive Monte Carlo sample of $1.3 \times 10^{9}$ $J/ψ$ events. The upper limits on the invisible decay branching fractions at the 90\% confidence level are set as $\mathcal{B}(ω\to invisible) < 3.7 \times 10^{-7}$, $\mathcal{B}(φ\to invisible) < 8.9 \times 10^{-7}$, $\mathcal{B}(η\to invisible) < 1.8 \times 10^{-7}$ and $\mathcal{B}(η' \to invisible) < 4.1 \times 10^{-7}$, respectively, using a projected toy data corresponding to the expected STCF statistics. By using the machine learning technique such as Deep Learning, the upper limit may be further improved to approach theoretical predictions for light dark matter.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子的带电电流散射截面（charged-current scattering cross section）编码了弱相互作用（weak interaction）与核子结构的基本信息，但在TeV能区的测量数据极为稀少，现有测量存在关键空白。

Method: 利用超级神冈探测器在4269天内收集的3989例上行穿透缪子（upward through-going muon）事件，结合对大气中微子通量的贝叶斯拟合（Bayesian fit）与探测器模拟，在500-5000 GeV能区测得通量平均的带电电流总截面。

Result: 测得的通量平均带电电流截面为 σ/E_ν = (0.51 ± 0.11) × 10⁻³⁸ cm² GeV⁻¹，这是TeV能区迄今最高精度的测量结果，与低能加速器实验及高能对撞机实验的结果一致。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了大型地下探测器可利用大气中微子进行高精度截面测量，为多TeV能量下标准模型（Standard Model）物理研究及新物理搜寻开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Neutrinos provide a unique probe of both particle physics and the high-energy universe, traversing astronomical distances with minimal interaction. Their charged-current scattering cross section encodes fundamental information about weak interactions and nucleon structure across a vast energy range, yet measurements at TeV energies remain sparse. Here we report the first determination of the flux-averaged muon neutrino and anti-neutrino charged-current total cross section using high-energy atmospheric neutrinos observed in Super-Kamiokande. Using 3989 upward through-going muon events collected over 4269 days, together with a Bayesian fit to atmospheric flux and detector simulations, we measure the flux-averaged charged-current cross section in the 500-5000 GeV range to be $σ/E_ν=(0.51\pm 0.11)\times 10^{-38}$ cm$^2$GeV$^{-1}$, with the highest precision to date in the TeV regime. Our results are consistent with accelerator-based measurements at lower energies and collider-based measurements at higher energies, bridging a critical gap between accelerator experiments and neutrino telescopes. This work demonstrates the capability of large underground detectors to perform precision cross-section measurements with atmospheric neutrinos, opening a new window for probing Standard Model physics and potential new physics searches at multi-TeV energies.

### [239] [Electroweak physics and long-lived particles at LHCb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10243)
*Felicia Volle*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于LHCb实验收集的5.1和5.4 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，首次测量了W玻色子与顶夸克的产生截面及电荷不对称性，并讨论了针对类轴子粒子与重中性轻子的暗扇区搜索新结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用LHCb实验收集的积分亮度为5.1和5.4 fb⁻¹的质子-质子（pp）对撞数据，测量W玻色子与顶夸克（top quark）的产生截面及电荷不对称性（charge asymmetries）。

Result: 首次给出了W和t的产生截面及电荷不对称性的测量结果。由于LHCb探测器的前向覆盖（forward coverage），这些结果在部分子分布函数（parton distribution functions, PDFs）探针方面与中央快度（central rapidity）测量形成互补。

Conclusion: 所呈现的精密测量结果对电弱扇区的标准模型检验具有价值；同时讨论的BSM候选粒子（包括类轴子粒子（axion-like particles）与重中性轻子（heavy neutral leptons））搜索结果为暗扇区（dark sector）中介子模型提供了实验约束。

Abstract: Extensions of the Standard Model (SM) of Particle Physics can be probed either through precision measurements of SM observables or via direct searches for processes beyond the SM (BSM). This proceeding focuses on precision measurements in the electroweak sector, in particular the properties of the $Z$ boson, $W$ boson and top quark. Measurements of the $W$ and $t$ production cross-sections, as well as charge asymmetries, with an integrated luminosity of 5.1 and 5.4 fb$^{-1}$ of $pp$ collisions collected by the LHCb experiment, are presented for the first time. In consequence of the forward coverage of the LHCb detector, these results provide complementary probes on parton distribution functions compared to measurements performed at central rapidity. Well-motivated BSM candidates include mediators between the visible and dark sectors. In this context, recent results from searches for axion-like particles and heavy neutral leptons are also discussed.

### [240] [Heat Transfer in Phase Change Materials with Multiple Fin Insertion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08120)
*Paolo Proia,Mauro Sbragaglia,Giacomo Falcucci*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过三维数值模拟研究浮力作用下含散热鳍片（fins）的相变材料（PCM）单元的熔化性能，发现多鳍片布局相比无鳍片或单鳍片设计能更高效地利用间隙空间熔化物质，且鳍片间距过近会导致熔化区域重叠干扰，从而降低性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究浮力（buoyancy forces）作用下相变材料（phase change materials, PCM）单元中固体散热鳍片对熔化性能的影响，并评估不同鳍片数量与布局的优化策略。

Method: 采用三维数值模拟（3D numerical simulations）构建含多个固体鳍片的PCM单元模型，设置等效加热功率的无鳍片和单鳍片对照组，通过总熔化物质随时间的变化量化性能，同时改变无量纲数（non-dimensional numbers）以测试不同物理条件下的表现。

Result: 确认鳍片可提升熔化性能；单鳍片布局并非最优，多鳍片设计可利用间隙空间（interstitial spaces）实现更高效熔化；鳍片间距过近会导致熔化区域重叠（overlapping）并相互干扰。

Conclusion: 多鳍片布局优于单鳍片，但需合理设计鳍片间距以避免熔化区域的负向干涉，从而实现更优的PCM单元熔化效率。

Abstract: We leverage 3D numerical simulations to study phase change materials (PCMs) cells under the effect of buoyancy forces. The solid PCM is heated from a source boundary, triggering melting. The source features multiple solid fins that protrude into the PCM cell; the impact of the fins and their number is investigated by designing and testing equivalent (in terms of heating power) finless and single fin simulations. For each configuration, the performance is quantified via the total molten substance in time. The designs were also tested for different values of the non-dimensional numbers encoding relevant properties. We confirm that fins increase the melting performance and find that single fin configurations are sub-optimal since a layout with multiple fins takes advantage of interstitial spaces, melting the substance more efficiently. The results also indicate that fins should be properly spaced, as closeness can result in overlapping, thus interfering, molten areas.

</details>


### [241] [Dynamical geometric modes in non-Euclidean plates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09289)
*Joseph C. Roback,Carlos E. Moguel-Lehmer,Katharina A. Fransen,Christian D. Santangelo,Ryan C. Hayward*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究非欧几里得弹性壳（non-Euclidean elastic shells）中的几何零模（geometric zero modes），以Enneper极小曲面为例，通过理论和实验证明该零模的动力学行为可由阻尼摆（damped pendulum）描述，并在周期驱动下呈现共振现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续弹性壳在特定预应力下可产生几何零模——即需极低弹性能即可激发的复杂运动，但当前对其动力学性质理解甚少，亟需系统研究。

Method: 以Enneper极小曲面为度规的非欧几里得板为模型，结合解析理论（analytical theory）与实验方法，分析其几何零模的弹性动力学（elastodynamics）。

Result: 该非欧几里得板表现出理论预测的连续稳定性，但这一简并性（degeneracy）最终因老化（aging）被解除；零模仍是系统中最软的模式，其动力学等价于阻尼摆；周期驱动下该摆模呈现小振荡、稳态旋转等共振现象，并在高频下与额外的拍动模（flapping mode）混合。

Conclusion: 几何零模的动力学可简化为低维摆模型，揭示了预应力和几何耦合所带来的丰富动力学行为，为弱驱动下弹性壳的响应提供了新的理解框架。

Abstract: When subjected to specific prestresses, continuum elastic shells can exhibit geometric zero modes: complex motions that require vanishing elastic energy to excite, enabling them to be driven by weak and generic energy inputs. Despite recent interest in these modes, we understand very little about their dynamical properties. Non-Euclidean plates modeled on minimal surfaces are one example in which prestresses and geometry combine to produce a continuum of ground states that the plate can explore through a geometric zero mode. We demonstrate that a non-Euclidean plate with metric corresponding to Enneper's minimal surface exhibits the predicted continuous stability, but this degeneracy is ultimately lifted by aging. Despite developing a preferred configuration, the zero mode remains the softest mode. Using a combination of analytical theory and experiments, we show that the elastodynamics of this soft mode is captured by the dynamics of a damped pendulum. A periodic driving uncovers resonance phenomena in this pendulum mode, such as small oscillations and steady rotations, but mixes with an additional flapping mode at high frequencies.

</details>


### [242] [Orienting-Field Effects on Instability and Mode Selection in Active Nematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09501)
*I. K. Joseph,A. J. H. Houston,K. N. Kowal,N. J. Mottram*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用低雷诺数Ericksen-Leslie框架，结合活性应力（active stresses）和场诱导扭矩（field-induced torques），分析了受限活性向列相（active nematic）在取向场（orienting field）作用下的不稳定性。线性分析发现两种具有奇偶对称性的模态，其不稳定性取决于活性与场强的相互作用；非线性数值解验证了线性稳定性分析对长时间态对称性的正确识别。结果表明取向场可降低经典临界活性阈值并调控模态选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解取向场如何影响受限活性向列相（confined active nematic）的不稳定性行为，特别是探究能否通过外部场调控活性系统的失稳阈值和模式选择。

Method: 采用低雷诺数Ericksen-Leslie框架（low Reynolds number Ericksen-Leslie framework），引入活性应力和场诱导扭矩；通过线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）识别两种对称性不同的失稳模态，并解析推导稳定性边界的精确和近似形式；利用完整非线性方程（full nonlinear equations）的数值解验证线性分析结果。

Result: 垂直取向场（使指向矢垂直于基底锚定方向）可降低活性阈值，并驱动一种偶对称模态（even symmetry mode）的不稳定性；平行取向场（使指向矢平行于锚定方向）则倾向于稳定系统。线性稳定性分析正确预测了长时间态的对称性。

Conclusion: 取向场能够使系统在低于经典临界活性的条件下发生失稳，因此可用于调节不稳定性起始点和控制受限活性向列相中的模式选择。

Abstract: We examine the instabilities of a confined active nematic subjected to an orienting field using a low Reynolds number Ericksen-Leslie framework with active stresses and field-induced torques. Linear analysis reveals two distinct modes, with odd and even director symmetry, the instabilities of which depend on the interplay between activity and field strength. We derive exact and approximate analytic forms of the stability boundaries and show that an orienting field that aligns the director perpendicular to the substrate anchoring direction cooperatively lowers activity thresholds and enables a field-driven even symmetry mode instability, while an orienting field that aligns the director parallel to the substrate anchoring tends to stabilise the system. Numerical solutions of the full nonlinear equations show that the linear stability analysis correctly identifies the symmetries of long-time states. These results demonstrate how orienting fields can promote an instability below the classical critical activity and can be used to both tune the instability onset and control the mode selection in confined active nematics.

</details>


### [243] [Interparticle Interactions in Nonlocal Media: Attraction and Repulsion from Charge-Polarization Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09540)
*Ali Behjatian,Madhavi Krishnan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于非局域介电理论（nonlocal dielectric theory），考虑极化中的空间关联（spatial correlations in polarization），发现溶剂结构化和极化关联能够主导带电粒子在液体中的相互作用，产生与经典介电连续模型（dielectric-continuum model）预期截然不同的行为，如同号电荷远距离吸引、异号电荷排斥、中性物质有效电迁移及长程疏水吸引力，并可能解释悬浮物絮凝（flocculation）现象的成因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来微球相互作用的实验测量表明，标准介电连续模型无法完整描述溶液相相互作用；实验证据提示溶剂在界面处的结构化效应（solvent structuring）可能主导带电粒子的相互作用，从而引出电溶剂化（electrosolvation）概念。然而现有理论框架将流体视为由恒定介电常数描述的无结构介质，未能考虑界面极化对长程相互作用的贡献，因此有必要发展更完整的理论模型。

Method: 采用非局域介电理论（nonlocal dielectric theory），在描述溶液相互作用时纳入极化中的空间关联（spatial correlations in polarization），从而允许电荷与极化共同主导相互作用。

Result: 该模型产生对称（排斥）和反对称（吸引）相互作用的框架，发现：(i) 同号电荷表面可在长距离上相互吸引，(ii) 异号电荷物体可相互排斥，(iii) 中性物质可获得有效电迁移能力并展示长程力——可能解释长程疏水吸引力。在极化关联长度ξ=2 Å的适度条件下，同号电荷生物分子在电解质水溶液中即可发生吸引。结果还表明电溶剂化效应可能解释传统上归因于色散力（dispersion forces）的悬浮物絮凝现象。

Conclusion: 溶剂结构化和极化关联可能在流体相物理中发挥主导且复杂的角色，非局域介电理论能够揭示经典连续模型所忽略的丰富相互作用行为。

Abstract: Recent measurements of microsphere interactions in diverse media suggest that the standard dielectric-continuum models of solution-phase interactions are fundamentally incomplete. Experiments indicate that the interactions of charged particles in liquids can be dominated by solvent structuring at interfaces, thereby motivating the concept of electrosolvation. While interfacial spectroscopy and molecular simulations have established that solvent molecules can exhibit net orientation at interfaces, conventional theoretical frameworks treat the fluid as a structureless medium described by a constant dielectric permittivity. This view does not envisage a contribution of interfacial polarization to interactions at longer range. Here, we employ nonlocal dielectric theory accounting for spatial correlations in polarization to describe interactions in solution. This model permits both charge and polarization to govern interactions, leading to dramatic departures from classical expectations. Specifically, the balance between charge and polarization generates a framework of symmetric (repulsive) and antisymmetric (attractive) interactions, wherein: (i) like-charged surfaces can attract at long range, (ii) oppositely charged objects can repel, and (iii) neutral matter can acquire effective electrical mobility and display long-range forces-potentially explaining long-range hydrophobic attraction. Further, like-charged biomolecules can attract in aqueous electrolytes even for modest polarization correlation lengths ($ξ=2$ Å). Our results also suggest that electrosolvation effects may underpin flocculation in suspended matter, which has traditionally been attributed to attractive dispersion forces. These findings indicate how solvent structuring and correlations may play a dominant, complex role in fluid-phase physics.

</details>


### [244] [On the thermal properties of knotted block copolymer rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09555)
*Neda Abbasi Taklimi,Franco Ferrari,Marcin R. Piątek,Luca Tubiana*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过粗粒度格点模型和王-兰道蒙特卡洛算法（Wang-Landau Monte Carlo algorithm），系统分析了打结的二嵌段共聚物环在隐式溶剂中的热力学与结构性质，发现结拓扑、单体组成与温度之间的耦合效应会导致非单调、类重入（reentrant-like）的构象行为以及低温下结的局域化与去局域化转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究打结的二嵌段共聚物环中，结拓扑（knot topology）、单体组成（monomer composition）与温度三者如何协同影响聚合物的热力学和构象响应，尤其是小范围改变B块长度带来的非单调行为。

Method: 采用粗粒度格点模型（coarse-grained lattice model）在隐式溶剂（implicit solvent）中模拟；使用王-兰道蒙特卡洛算法（Wang-Landau Monte Carlo algorithm）在宽温度范围内分析热力学与构象响应。考察了不同结拓扑（un-knot、三叶结、八字结、五叶结）以及对称和不对称单体组成；A型单体自排斥、B型单体自吸引，A-B相互作用中性。

Result: 计算了热容（heat capacity）、回转半径（radius of gyration）及其温度导数、单体属于结区域的概率等可观测量的结果。发现结拓扑、单体组成和温度的耦合强烈影响构象；B块长度的微小变化引发随温度变化的非单调、类重入（reentrant-like）构象行为，包括低温下结的局域化与去局域化之间的转变。

Conclusion: 这些效应源于拓扑约束所造成的能量贡献（energetic contributions）与熵贡献（entropic contributions）之间的竞争。

Abstract: We investigate the thermal and structural properties of knotted diblock copolymer rings using a coarse-grained lattice model in an implicit solvent. The system is studied by means of the Wang--Landau Monte Carlo algorithm, allowing us to analyze thermodynamic and conformational responses over a wide temperature range. Different knot topologies, including the unknot, trefoil, figure-eight, and pentafoil knots, are considered for both symmetric and asymmetric monomer compositions.
  In the AB model employed here, A-type monomers are self-repulsive, B-type monomers are self-attractive, and A-B interactions are neutral, such that the solvent is effectively good for A-type monomers and poor for B-type monomers at low temperatures. We analyze several key observables, including the heat capacity, the radius of gyration, and its temperature derivative for both the entire copolymer ring and the individual blocks, and the probability that a monomer belongs to the knotted region. Our results show that the interplay between knot topology, monomer composition, and temperature strongly influences polymer conformations. Small variations in the B-block length induce nonmonotonic, reentrant-like conformational behavior as a function of temperature, including transitions between knot localization and delocalization at low temperatures. These effects arise from the competition between energetic and entropic contributions imposed by topological constraints.

</details>


### [245] [A molecular perspective on coordination, screening, and emergent length scales in lithium electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10089)
*A. Coste,E. Zunzunegui-Bru,A. van Roekeghem,I. Skarmoutsos,S. Mossa*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一多尺度框架（unified multiscale framework），将锂电解质（lithium electrolytes）中局域配位化学、介观离子组织与宏观输运整合在同一物理图像中，论证了在高浓度条件下屏蔽效应（screening）与离子输运（ionic transport）由相同的关联结构（correlated structures）所决定，而非独立现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统锂电解质描述将局域配位化学（local coordination chemistry）、静电屏蔽（electrostatic screening）与离子输运（ionic transport）视为独立概念，这种分离在稀溶液（dilute conditions）下有效，但在高浓度条件下因配位、离子配对（ion pairing）、团簇化（clustering）与集体动力学（collective dynamics）的内在耦合而失效。

Method: 通过一个统一多尺度框架（unified multiscale framework），将局域配位构型（local coordination motifs）、介观离子组织（mesoscopic ionic organization）与宏观输运（macroscopic transport）联结在同一物理图像中；并选取碳酸酯液体（carbonate liquids）、聚合物电解质（polymer electrolytes）、浓缩体系（concentrated systems）及限域体系（confinement）作为代表性示例进行分析。

Result: 随着浓度升高，体系从溶剂主导的Li⁺配位（solvent-dominated Li⁺ coordination）向离子配对、团簇化以及关联区域（correlated domains）系统演化；在该浓度区间内，屏蔽效应与离子输运不再是独立现象，而是源于同一底层关联结构。

Conclusion: 理性的电解质设计（rational electrolyte design）必须同时对短程配位（short-range coordination）、介观尺度组织（mesoscale organization）与集体静电响应（collective electrostatic response）进行协同调控。

Abstract: Lithium electrolytes are commonly described using separate conceptual frameworks for local coordination chemistry, electrostatic screening, and ionic transport. This separation is effective in dilute conditions but breaks down at higher concentration, where coordination, ion pairing, clustering, and collective dynamics become intrinsically coupled. In this Perspective, we develop a unified multiscale framework that links local coordination motifs, mesoscopic ionic organization, and macroscopic transport within a single physical picture. Through representative examples spanning carbonate liquids, polymer electrolytes, concentrated systems, and confinement, we show that increasing concentration drives a systematic evolution from solvent-dominated Li$^+$ coordination to ion pairing, clustering, and correlated domains. In this regime, screening and transport are not independent phenomena but arise from the same underlying correlated structures. This perspective implies that rational electrolyte design must simultaneously control short-range coordination, mesoscale organization, and collective electrostatic response.

</details>
